
IsandUlelo 


Mfundi othandekayo 

Ngemuva kwesikhathi eside ngiyibhala le ncwadi ngamisa 
izinsuku ezintathu engangizoyihlalela ngazo ize iphele. Lezo 
zinsuku kwakuzokuba oLwesithathu lomhla zingamashumi 
amabili kuya koLwesihlanu zingamashumi amabili nambili 
kuMasingana nonyaka (1993). 

Ngalezo zinsuku ngazama ukusifeza isifiso sami. 
NgoLwesithathu nangoLwesine, ngabhala kwakhathala amehlo 
nezandla. OlwangoLwesihlanu, ngathi olwamanqamu. Imizuzu 
isisondele ngasehoreni leshumi, ekuseni, sengizoyiphetha. Incwadi 
yamaHubo esonto bese ngiyivulile, ngiqhekeze lona kanye 
ihubo ebelizoculwa umlingiswa obezojamelana nosuku lwakhe 
lokugcina. Imizuzu isihlanganisa ihora leshumi bengiwuqhumisa 
umshini sengichaza ngaye umlingiswa esekuthithibalele 
ukubulawa. Lapho nje sengithi ngichaza ngeveni yoMfundisi 
eyayisondela, inyinyitheka, abathandazi basho bangqongqoza 
ekhaya, bezishaye ziphelele ezabo zomkhuleko. Ngishaqekile 
ngawuyeka umshini, ngabalalela becula sebenamadodakazi ami 
amabili. 

Izinyembezi zigcwale amehlo. Abazange bangibuze 


nakungibuza ukuthi ngikuphi, ngoba bathathe ngokuthi 
ngisemsebenzini. Ngesikhathi becula, mina ngimangele 
ekamelweni lokufunda, ngiguqe phansi, ngathandaza 
ngingaphimiseli. Ekwenzeni kwabo kuningi okungithinte 
umoya. Selokhu le ndlu ngaqeda ukuyakha eminyakeni emihlanu 
eyedlule, bebeqala ngqa ukungena kuyo. Okwesibili, ukuthi usuku 
engilwazi behambela ngalo imizi, ngoLwesine. Nakhu namuhla, 
beqala ngqa ukufika, bangena ngoLwesihlanu ekuseni ngesikhathi 
umphefumulo wami ukubo. 
 

Ngithinteke kakhulu lapho sebekhumbuza amadodakazi 
ukuthi uNkulunkulu ungiphe isipho sokubhala, besho nokuthi 
ngalokho wayeqonde ukukhuluma ngokusebenzisa umuntu. 
Bangiculele, bangithandazela. O, ngithule, ngingedwa, zehla kimi. 
Liphelile ihora becula, bethandaza. Sebevalelisa, baphume ngalo 
kanye leli culo ebengilivulile, endabeni yami obekuzoba yiculo 
lokugcina ebelizoculwa yikholwa ebelizobulawa. 

“Makhosikazi amane angqongqoze endlini le, ngalo mzuzu, 
ningo- Nkk. Zulu, Nkk. Mchunu, Nkk. Sithole noNkk. 
Magagula. Ukufika kwenu namuhla kungitshela ukuthi 
uNkulunkulu wazi singakazi ukuthi ngosuku oluthile siyobe 
sikuphi, senzani, senziwani, ubani. Kungitshela ukuthi noma yini 
esithi siyayenza, ayenziwa yithina, futhi asizenzeli. Kungitshela 
ukuthi, njengoba nishilo nani, uNkulunkulu uyakhuluma 
ngabantu bakhe, njengoba ekhulume ngani. Ukube lo mzamo 
ubungaphumelela ugxotshwe, bengingafisa ukuba izithombe zenu, 
niyishaye njengoba ningene niyishayile imifaniswano yenu, zivele 
kuwo. 


Usuku lonke lwanamuhla abangibuka emehlweni bangibuza 
ukuthi kade ngikhalelani. Ngiyayivala manje le ncwadi, 
ngiyiphetha ngicula njengoba nani ningene naphuma ngomculo.”  

KuNkk. Mchunu ongasekho. Alale ngokuthula. 

MATTHEW JABULANI MNGADI 
NgoLwesihlanu zingama-22 kuMasingana 1993. 


1 
 
wakhe kwakungathi akusewona owakhe. 
Wawukhathazekile, ukhandlekile, uphundlwe 
yizimbokodo zomhlaba. Noma esenyuka izitebhisi zalo 
muzi aqashe kuwo lapha eMlazi, uZwelisha Dubazana 
wayezithwele, ezihola, esemanzi nte wumjuluko ngale mini 
eyayibhadliswa yisibhabhadlolo selanga. 

Eminyakeni eyayingamashumi amane eyayedlule 
wayezalelwe kwelinye lamapulazi aseFilidi. Wayeqale 
ukukhathala khona esemncane ekhathazwa yisithupha. 
Nakhona epulazini lapho babexoshwe eseyibhobhodleyana. 
Imithwalo yakwabo yayijikwe emgwaqweni ngemuva 
kokuba yena enqaba ukuqhubeka nokushaya isithupha, 
wayeseyozifunela umsebenzi esilungwini, eThekwini. 
Ukuxoshwa kwekhaya epulazini kwakusho ukuba 
usehlasenyuka kwalo. Uyise wayempampe waze wayotholwa 
omunye womasitende baseKuphumuleni eMnambithi. 

Umzimba wakhe wawunethe ngakhona. Nalapha 

eThekwini wayefike wancishelwa umhlaba. 

Kwakufuneka izimvume zokuba khona. Ekwehleni 
kwakhe enyuka efuna umsebenzi, wayeseboshwe 
kaninginingi, esendelwa eFilidi okwakuthiwa 
yayiyinkantolo yakubo eyayibhalwe epasini. 

Namaphoyisa ayemphelezela ayefike amshiye 

enkantolo yakhona, athi akazibonele. Ayethi eqambe 
ebuya eThekwini abe engenisana naye uma ngabe 
engathelekanga kuqala kunawo. Kwakuze kwaphetha 
ngokuba ayodonsa iminyaka eMazambaneni. 

1 


Wayesehleli ekamelweni ayeqashe kulo ebambelele 
esihlathini. Wayedikibele ngakhona. Wayekhumbula 
ukuthi wayethe ebuya eMazambaneni nekhaya elalike 
laba seKuphumuleni lase laphela. UHulumeni wase 
abathutha betibula abantu baseKuphumuleni wabasa 
elokishini eZakheni. Kuyise uBheseni owayengafuni 
nakulibona ilokishi, imithwalo yayibe sobhokweni. Uye 
lowaya eyokhonza eMangweni, efika akha khona. 
 

Wayethe khovololo nje kuleli kamelo lakwaSilangwe, 
wayeze ashaye phansi nangonyawo ebala iminyaka 
eyayisele anduba ahlanganise leli shumi nanhlanu 
leminyaka. Kwakuyoba yilapho–ke eyobhalisa indlu 
ayeseyoyilinda umlibe. Efede yezimoto wayedilizwe 
eseneminyaka eyisikhombisa. Ngakho–ke wayesasele 
nesishiyagalombili seminyaka. Wayeseze waganwa 
yintokazi yakwaZondi eNkumba, eyayisize yamzalela 
indodakazi nendodana khona emqashweni. Kwakusobala 
ukuthi oMakhosazana noNkosana base beyoze bakhulele 
khona, elokhu engena ephuma. 

Yebo, ngalo Mgqibelo yayizwela iminjunju 

2 


yokukhathazeka komoya. Ezweni lapha 
wayengesakhamuzi sadolobha. Edolobheni laseFilidi 
nasesigodini senkosi ayebizwa ngayo epasini 
wayengaziwa. EMnambithi babethuthwe edonsa ejele, 
kwapasi lakhe engakaliguquleli nakhona. EThekwini 
wayesenguziyantunta. 
 

Umhlangano awuqalwanga ngehora lesibili njengoba 
wawumenyezelwe. Seligamenxe, wavulwa ngomkhuleko. 
Zaqala–ke izinkulumo ngemuva kokuba unobhala 
esechazile ukuthi wawungowokuzama ukunciphisa 
izinkinga ezazikhungethe ilokishi. Laligcwele phama 
ihholo, ziphakama ziphakamile izandla, imibono ibekwa 
ngobuvamba, izikhulumi zehluleka ukusihlaba esijwini 
lesi sihloko esasiyaluza. 

“Injongo yalo mhlangano ayizwakali kahle Sihlalo. 
Awusicacisele ukuthi sihlangene lapha nje yini eqinisweni 
ezodingidwa, noma olusha esizolutshelwa.” UMthembu 
owayebuza wayeyindoda eyayisigqigqi, iluhlaza, izinwele 
zayo ezazimnyama suce, zihlobe kancane ngezimvu 
izibhulashe yazibhekisa emuva okwayenza yanencegela 
kathekwane. 

USihlalo, uMnu. Mavimbela nekhansela elisha uMnu. 

3 


Zithulele Silas Bethule babeyizingengelezi ezazingamunwe 
ezazintanganye emashumini ayisikhombisa nambili 
eminyaka. Phezu kwesivuvu sokushisa lapha ehholo, 
bobabili babedlubhe amasudi, nezintolibhantshi zakhona, 
nezikhafu ezazimpunga njengawo amasudi. Babezesula 
bezesulile ubuso nezimpandla ezazicwebezela imijuluko. 

Zithulele Silas Bethule babeyizingengelezi ezazingamunwe 
ezazintanganye emashumini ayisikhombisa nambili 
eminyaka. Phezu kwesivuvu sokushisa lapha ehholo, 
bobabili babedlubhe amasudi, nezintolibhantshi zakhona, 
nezikhafu ezazimpunga njengawo amasudi. Babezesula 
bezesulile ubuso nezimpandla ezazicwebezela imijuluko. 

Saphakama futhi esinye isandla. 

“Ake sizwe ezakho izinduku baba.” 

USihlalo wayekhomba uhalakasha lwendoda 
eyasukuma umzimba yawuthela phansi yayisithi, 
“Engikubonayo Sihlalo, nengifikelwa yizwi ngakho 
elithi angikusho, ukuthi abantu bakithi bonke bedukile, 
babalekelene noJesu!” Yalixegisa ikhwapha, yavula 
isikhwama yakhipha iBhayibheli eyaliphakamisela 

4 


phezulu, yabhonga, yalehlisa yalishaya ngesinye isandla 
ithi, “Owu! Owu! Owu! Nakhu okubahluphayo! Bathemba 

Abafuni ukukhohlwa wumhlaba basebenzele izwe elizayo 
eliyoba noju olungapheliyo!” 

“Siyaya ezinkonzweni ngomuso!” Kwakusho uLolense 
Mthembu. “Kusemhlanganweni womphakathi lapha. 
Asinamvuselelo. Hlala phansi uyeke ukusibhedela!” 

“Ake nizwe phela bazalwane! Lalelani!” Yeneka izandla 
le ndoda yakwaSangweni, yawuxegisa futhi umzimba 
iwubuka wonke umhlangano sengathi yayiwubuza buthule 
ukuthi wawuthuleleni kodwa esinye isakhamuzi seduke 
kangaka. Yamkhombisisa uMthembu ithi, “Uzoshiswa 
wena nenzalo yakho yolayitha! Izwi lithi anginitshele 
ukuthi thina nani njengamanje siseBhabhiloni, siyasha!” 
Yaba miningi imizuzwana uSangweni ebuka uMthembu 
owayenele wezwa ukuthi wayengu–Asa wayesengeza 
ngokuthi wayeganwe wu–Asiyena. “Ukuba angikholiwe 
ngabe ngiyanxapha.” Wahlala. Wathi lacu, wasukuma 
lwadansaza utununu lakwabo izinqe seluzikhiphe 
zayinjojela luyophuma. “Ayiphele imihlangano enje, 
kwande izimvuselelo, kuthandazelwe izilahlwa!” esho 
echitha izandla eyophuma. 

Kwaphakama esinye futhi isandla. Umniniso 
wasukuma wenwaya ikhanda ethi, “Indikimba 
yomhlangano ayizwakali sihlalo. Umhlangano ubamba 
lapha uthinte laphaya, ugcine usuxabana wodwa 
ungaxazululanga nkinga. Angiqonde kufundisa, kepha 
bengicela ukuba ngaphambi kokugxila emphakathini, 
noma esizweni esedukile, nokunye, ake sibhekisise 
izidingo zomuntu kuqala, ngale kokuthi ubala lini.” 

“O, hhe!” Wazikhalela futhi uMthembu. “Safa 
abashumayeli namhlanje! Phuma nawe ndodana ulandele 

5 


indoda yeBhayibheli niyoshumayeza izimvuselelo!” 
 

Umhlangano wabumbana, kwacijiswa izindlebe abanye 
sebeqalile nokunqekuzisa amakhanda. Waqhubeka uZulu: 
“Kuthiwa ekuqaleni uMdali wadala izulu nomhlaba, 
walandelisa ngemini nobusuku. Esedale umkhathi, 
wehlukanisa umhlaba ngolwandle, walandelisa ngotshani 
nemifino. Kwabe sekulandela izinyoni nezilwane zamanzi 
nezasezweni. Esekudale konke lokhu, wenza umuntu 
ukuba amfuze, abuse umhlaba. Okwethu okwezandla. 
Siphila inhlalo ephambene nohlelo loMdali. 

“Okokuqala indawo yokuhlala ayikho. Ingane iyakhala 
esiswini. Ukwesweleka kwalezi zidingo sekudale isizwe 
esingondingasithebeni. Ake sizibuze–ke ukuthi uma 
sekunje, singenzenjani? Okokuqala nje kungeze kwasisiza 
ngalutho ukugwajaza, nokwethukana, nokuwubhandisha 
siwufihla lo mdlavuza osiphethe. Asiqale ngayo 
indawo yokuhlala. Uma ngibuka iphepha likababa 
ayekhankasela ngalo ukhetho, ezethembisweni azilobile 
kukhona nesithi uzosakhela imizi. Sihle isifiso. Kazi 
amandla ayoba khona na? 

“Esinye isikhulumi lapha ehholo sike sakhuluma kahle 
kakhulu siphatha indaba yaseBhabhiloni. Isikhulumi 
esihloniphekileyo sisuke sabona isono kuphela eBhabhiloni. 
Sikhohlwa ukusho ukuthi kudalo intuthuko yesintu 
emphakathini, ipolitiki, impucuko kanye nezomnotho 
kwadala amadolobha afana nawaseRoma, i–Athens 
kwelamaGiriki, iBhabhiloni obekukhulunywa ngayo 

6 


kanye neCarthage e–Afrika. Ngikholwa ukuthi ezinye 
zezingqinamba zaseBhabhiloni zazibangwa ukwanda 
kwabantu ndawonye edolobheni elalingenazo izimfanelo 
ezanele zobudolobha. Lapha eThekwini sesike sayibona 
enye iBhabhiloni eyayibizwa ngoMkhumbane. Maningi 
amaBhabhiloni esisazowabona uma umthetho usemi 
ekutheni izigidi zabamnyama kuleli zihlaliswa ogwadule 
lwesiqeshana sendawo engamaphesenti ayishumi 
nantathu ezweni lonke; uma abanodedangendlale 
bezindawo emapulazini beqhubeka nokuxoshana 
nabazakhele. Lusaya phezulu usizi uma uhulumeni 
esaphikelele ukusendana nabantu ebasa ezinkantolo 
ezisemapasini, umuntu abe axoshwa epulazini elikuleyo 
nkantolo; uma uhulumeni esaphikelele ukuthuthana 
nabantu ebasusa ezindaweni zabo ngempoqo. Ngaleyo 
ndlela kuhlakazeka imindeni, nedlanzana elalinemizi 
ligcine lingasenayo. Abanye bathuthwa emakhaya 
basiwe emadolobheni, wona kanye la madolobha 
uhulumeni abuye abaxoshe kuwo abasendele emakhaya. 

“Uyabona–ke lona,” kwakuhleba amadoda amabili, 

7 


“Namuhla kunamuhla kuye. Uyolala ezitokisini. 
Kuhulumeni ongesisebenzi somphakathi, kodwa 
osebenza umphakathi, alikhulunywa iqiniso. Uyalifela. 
Asithule mntanomuntu.” 

Umhlangano wagcina uphume ukwangqingetshe. 
Uma ngabe ikhambi kwakuwukuqeda ubandlululo, 
bangaki ababengazimisela ngokubamba ingonyama 
ngezandla? Babehamba nje abantu bephindela 
emakhaya, akekho nowayefuna ukuyiphatha leyo. 
Abantu babengasethembene, sebebizana ngezimpimpi 
namambuka. UBhekizizwe yena okwakubonakala 
ukuthi zazingase zimthathe noma nini wayesesatshiswa 
okomuntu owayenengxibongo, engase abathelele, 
bashaqwe naye uma bendawonye. Eseyinkomo 
eyayisihamba ngayodwana. UZwelisha Dubazana owaze 
wamphelezela. 

“Waze wazilanda izinkinga mfokababa kwaze kwaba 
sengathi ubuyifunda phansi impilo yami ebuhlungu.” 
Kwakusho yena uDubazana sebehambisana, emxoxela 
ngamapulazi ayezalelwe kuwo, ngokusendwa kwakhe, 

8 


nokuthuthwa kwabo eMnambithi, nokuganwa kwakhe 
engenamuzi, engenakuwubhalisa futhi. 
 

Base bemi ngakwaSilangwe, bethi bayavalelisana 
ngesikhathi uhuntshu lwemoto emnyama luma, 
maqondana nabo. Yayigcwele isiqhoqho sezinsizwa 
ezimhlophe nezinsundu. Esamangele uZwelisha zavuleka 
zandiza izivalo zangemuva. Zehla zigxuma izinsizwa 
ezimbili ezazimnyama, zishaye ezimnyama ukusuka 
ezicathulweni kuya emasudini, emehlweni, emahembeni, 
nasezigqokweni imbala. 

“Singamaphoyisa ezomoya Bhekizizwe. Sisafuna 
ukukuphenya lo moya obuwufaka abantu bezilungele, 
uthi abavukele uhulumeni.” 

“Angizange ngisho ukuthi abavukele uhulumeni, kepha 
ngithe abavukele ubandlululo.” 

“O, kanti ushisa ngempela! Abantu abashisayo 
bapholiswa kwalasha!” Ukuthi bamdudulela nini 
emotweni, naye akabonanga. Yasuka imoto isihamba, 
kushunqa intuthu iklwebha itiyela ngamathayi. 
UDubazana wayibuka yaze yasithela, wayesexegezela 
ethukile. Wenyuka ngezitebhisi, ukwethuka nokucasuka 
sekuyomvevezelisa ekolosaneni lekamelo ayeqashe kulo. 

9  


Ngomgqibelo selimathunzi insizwa kaDubazana ewucingo 
lakwabo olwalukhanya, inwele zimashoba, yehla esitimeleni 
esiteshini eZwelethu, yanyathela yazizwa ubusha. 
Wayekade ezibambele i–ova emsebenzini, eseshayisile, 
ezishayele elakwanokusho ijezi elalimahaqa, ezilengisele 
isikhwama ayelayishe kuso umngenandlini. Njengoba 
umuzi ayeqashe kuwo wawubudebuduze neZwelethu, 
wazishayela ngalo unyawo. Wathi esebange khona, 
igazi lavele lacwila, lashona phansi. Umcabango 
wosizi lwekamelo nokuba yisikhonzi emzini womuntu 
wambhadazelisa. 

Uma ethi memfu, kwaSilangwe, amehlo azithela 
ebunikililini, kuwubutatata egcekeni lakhona, kuliwa. 
Inhlamba yayindiza emoyeni, kubanjwana, kulanyulwa, 
kujahwana. Kunenkosikazi eyayiwuqhaqhaveyana nje 
olwaluphungwa ngapha nangapha lusho ukuthatha 
kanye ngesikhwili kumalokazana owayesebhaca 
nganoma ubani ayengase abande ngaye. 

Kule mpi eyayisinezibukeli, kunendoda eyayimangaza 
iningi. Yayikhanya nayo, inobuso obabuyindilinga 
eyayisadombolo, bunendlebhula yomlomo, namehlwana 
ayemancanyana ehlabisa okwawembodla. Yayilithwele 
ilihlephulele ikapisi, ingene ejazini elalimthubi, 
linamakhukhu ayequmbile. Yayingalamuli, ingathi 
vu, kepha ilokhu izulazula negceke. Yayifake izandla 
emakhikhini ibuye izibelethe, inikine ikhanda, ime 
izigone, ababejahana ibahlabe ngendluluza yeso, bese 
inxapha, izula negceke. 

10 


Ngokusondela kwakhe kwaSilangwe wambona 
wamazi lo malokazana owayentantiswa ibala ngomshiza. 
Wayekhona naye, eyintokazi eyayisemashumini 
amathathu nesikhombisa eminyaka, ededile egadeni, 
kanti lunjalo nje ugamfu lakwabo, lumile ngeside isitho 
esasilingene kahle, sesulekile. Kwakuwumkakhe, 
uMaZondi. Wathatha izinyawo, wazicaca eshesha 
izitebhisi. Ebaleni wazithela kule nsambatheka, 
nendodakazi yakhe eyayisineshumi nanhlanu, ikhala 
ibambe ikhanda lapho umshiza uthi awudle unina. 

Washo ngomoya ophansi uDubazana wathi, “Ngicela 
wehlise umoya mama ukuze ngizwe ukuthi kwenzenjani.” 

Indoda yekapisi, uSilangwe owayesezimele 
kude laphaya ngakufenisi, wabahlaba ngeso futhi, 
wayesewuvula isikhathi eside umlomo, noxwembe lolimi 
lwabonakala kahle lunamathela olwangeni, iludedela 
kancane, inxapha ngesineke. 

“Unesibindi sokunxapha uziphathisa okukakotshi! 
Ikhona indoda esile nje eqonywa umkamuntu indoda 
yakhe ikhona endlini, nami ngiwumkayo ngikhona?” 

Iso elipholile, elibi, nokunxapha ngesineke 
kwalandeliswa owayebizwa ngokotshi owachiza yena 
ukotshi, wazibukela kude le. 

UMaNcanana wazidodloza isifuba, wasiqhubela 
phambili ethi, “Lo muzi ngowami. Usho yena lo mfazana, 
akalali kule ndlu namhlanje. Ngisho kungayiwa 
ehhovisi, kuphenywe izincwadi ezinkulu zomthetho, 
kungafika kutholakale ukuthi kubhalwe igama lami 

11 


njengomkaSilangwe, hhayi elalo simukanandwendwe 
wakho.” Wamhahlisa ngomshiza uDubazana. “Awuqhele 
phambi kwami kengishaye lesi sonakali sakho!” Naye 
uDubazana owahlanganisa izingalo evikela umkakhe 
wamqwaqwada ekhanda ngomshiza ethi, “Suka ngingaze 
ngibhodlele kuwe!” 

“Khona ngingakuchazela uzokwenzani usuwaba 
isinaphungana nje sesinoko semithi yalo mfazana wakho 
oseqomene noSilangwe!” 

“Angiqomene mina nobaba uSilangwe!” Wayephika 
ngezwana elincane uMaZondi ethuka izanya. “Uyena 
nje ovele wangibamba isandla. Naye futhi umama, uma 
ngingaphosisi, uzwile ngimkhuza.” 

“Thula! Sengiwunyoko manje, angiseyena uzakwenu? 
Ngabe ngiyisilahlwa uma ngifana nonyoko ongazalanga 
owabola amathumbu.” 

“Ngenani endlini nina bantabami, ningalunaki 
uhlanya lolu.” Kwakusho uSilangwe ebabuka ngamehlo 
ayeyabazela. 

“Bangene kuyiphi yona indlu? Kulena yami?” 
UMaNcanana washaya phansi ngonyawo, wazaza. 
“Akwenzeki lokho. Ngiyabona seningiphuze inyongo 
kakhulu.” Weqa amangqamngqeshe eqonde endlini. 
Ngokuphazima kweso kwezwakala ubugunqugunqu 
nokuwa kwempahla, nokukhala kwezitsha. Waphuma 
endiza. Amabhodwe akwaDubazana atshingwa ngaleya 
kocingo ayozikhalela phansi emgwaqweni. Watshobela 
endlini, waphuma namaphulamastofu, nawo akhala 
emgwaqweni. Esashaqekile uDubazana, uMaNcanana 
wema ngasocingweni, ipotimende lezingubo ayelithwele 
walithululela phansi emgwaqweni. 

“Wenzani MaNcanana?” Wabuza uSilangwe 

12 


esetshekise nekhanda. 
 

“Awuzwa ukuthi uyangethuka, ungixabanisa 
nomntanami lona uma uphikelela ukuthi ngiqomisa 
umkakhe?” 

“Lokhu kwesandla kuncane. Ufuna ngiqhubeke 
ngiluhlube lonke udlubu ekhasini?” 

Yahhumuzela yodwa indoda intshalantshala yayoma 
ngemuva kwendlu. “Nina nobabili,” kusho uMaNcanana 
ekhomba oDubazana nomkakhe ngomshiza, “ngenani 
endlini lapha, niqoqe wonke amasakana enu asele, 
niphume nawo manje ngingakawafaki umlilo, nani 
ngingakaniphihlizi izingozi. Ngisizeni–ke ningihlenge 
entanjeni!” 

Ekhungathekile uDubazana, wangena, nomkakhe 
watholoza wamlandela. Bengasakhulumisani, babambisana 
ngombhede newadilobu baye bakubeka ngasesangweni. 

“We mfazi nendoda abangaziwa noma beganene 
noma omasihlalisane ini, ngithi wonke amasakana enu 
wakhipheleni ngaphandle.” 

“Xola mama.” Wancenga uDubazana. “Ngisazocela 
omakhelwane bangibambise.” Esethithiza weqela 
egcekeni lomunye womakhelwane. Nakhona 
wahlangabezana nembibizane yokuhlangulwa inkosikazi 
yakhona, idisholo eliwuMaGumede elabhenguza 
ngezingalokazi lithi, “Emuva! Emuva!” 

“Mama, ngizocela ubaba uSibiya kuba angibambise.” 

“USibiya lona uhlalele ukusiza amadoda ezigilamkhuba! 
Singomakhelwane nisifica sihleli ngokuthula, 
nizohlwanyela isihlava phakathi kwethu!” 

Eseshaya uzamthilili uDubazana, omunye 
womakhelwane, uNdlela owayeseyindoda esiqinile, 
wamzwela, wambambisa izimpahla bazeqisa ucingo 

13 

bazincikisa ngodonga lwakwakhe. 

Wabonga uDubazana, wayesema isikhathi eside 
egcekeni lakwaNdlela. Wayedidekile. Ngelikade weqela 
kwaSilangwe, wathatha amapotimende wabutha 
izingubo, konke wakubeka ngaphesheya komgwaqo. 
Kungasavumi nokuba akhulume, waqhweba umkakhe, 
wamethwesa enye impahla. Yena ngesinye isandla 
wabamba ipotimende, ngesinye umfanyana wakhe 
uNkosana owayeseminyakeni eyishumi nanye, baluqhuba 
uhambo lwabo lwakwa–Sehlasenyukanemithwalo. 

Eseze wanethwa yizimvula uDubazana ehamba 
etholoza nezingane ephuma engena efunana nekamelo 
sekuhlwile, wagcina ezithele kwaMbonambi ayentanganye 
naye, besebenza ndawonye. Lwamcacela usizi 
uMbonambi owayehlala nomkakhe, nabantababo, unina 
namadodakazi, nabazukulu, namadodana, kulalwa 
kuminyenwe. UDubazana nabakwakhe bazishutheka 
ngaphansi kwetafula ekhishini. Kwakungaxoxiswana, 
inhliziyo kaDubazana ifutha, engqondweni eboniswa 
imifanekiso yokubhidlikelwa umuzi. Amalutha engqondo 
ayesemphebeza nasekubeni abuze kumkakhe ukuthi 
ikuphi okwakuyiqiniso nokwakungaluhlaza cwe. 
Imbangela yokuzishutheka ngaphansi kwamatafula 
akwaMbonambi wayibona kuyisimilo esasintekenteke 
somkakhe. 

Kwanele kwasa, baphondla ubuso, izingane bazicelela 
okwesikhashana, baphuma inqina yekamelo. Babengena 
bephuma, kulo muzi nalowaya. Akekho owayebanika 
inhliziyo, abantu belale bezikhathalele ngoMgqibelo, 
abanye belungiselela ukuya ezinkonzweni, emaphathini 

14 


nasematshwaleni. Lafudumala, lababhadlisa emgwaqweni. 
Balamba, babhocobala, kepha phakathi kwabo akekho 
owezwakala ekhala ngokuba okungenani kebadlule 
ngasethilomu. Yilowo wayedla imicabango nentukuthelo 
yakhe. 

Ngomoya ophansi wambuza wathi, “Ngize ngibe 
udadewenu nje ngoba kwenzenjani?” 

“Ukuba wawungudadewethu ngangiyokuthanda, 
uthi noma sewenza le nkohlakalo yakho ngikweluleke 
ngingekulahle uyingane yakwethu.” 

“Ngenzeni?” 

“Awazi ukuthi wenzeni?” Wamswacela uDubazana. 
“Unesibindi sokungivusela nezinhlonze ungibuze 
esikhundleni sokuba uzenyeze! Uyabona ukuthi sihlupheka 
kanje nje kungenxa yakho?” Wambuka walizwa ligqamuka 
ilangabi lothando lapho amehlo akhe ethungelana 
nawomkakhe. UMaZondi wayemehlula ngalezi zinwele zakhe 
ezazimashoba endalo ngaphansi kweduku elalimibalabala 
yesishweshwe, nobuso obabubujana, bungamunwe, buzothile, 
buhlobe ngezingcatshana zakwaZondi. Wayenekhala 
elalimile, nezihlathi ezazifocoka lapho ehleka, nezindebe 
okwakungathi zesulwa ngoju. Ekukhuleni kwakhe 
wayenomlando wokubangwa yizinsizwa zimphonsa 
ziphonsana. 

UMaZondi wamehlisela umoya uDubazana, wathi, 
“Yise kaMakhosazana, iningi lenu madoda liyinqaba 
ngoba ngesinye isikhathi like liyikhulume nje into 

15 

lingayicabangisisanga kahle.” 

“Njengoba ngisho nje yise kaMakhosazana, thina 
bantu besifazane sisenomsebenzi omkhulu kabi wokuba 
sifundise amadodana ethu azoba amasoka nabayeni 
babanye ngomuso.” 

“Niwafundise ukuthini?” 

“Ukuba kuthi noma nini uma ebona noma ecabanga 
ngomuntu wesifazane azi ukuthi ubona isidalwa 
sikaNkulunkulu esinomphefumulo nengqondo 
yokwahlukanisa okuhle nokubi; ukwenyanya okubulalayo 
nokuphokophelela okwakhayo. Kufanele sinifundise, 
sinikhombise nangezenzo, nazi nani ukuthi umuntu 
wesifazane uyaziqhayisa ngomzimba wakhe, futhi akazisoli 
ngokuba umuntu wesifazane. Nawe–ke myeni wami 
ngiyakucela ukuba ungawelekeleli la madoda abuthaka 
egazini nasengqondweni ngokungethwesa ubuze nobuwula 
bawo. Uhlezi nje uyazi ukuthi wafika eNkumba sezingibange 
isikhathi eside izinsizwa ngingaqomile. Ngokufika kwakho 
nomshado kwaba yinhlanhla yethu sobabili nawe ukuba 
sithandane. Manje–ke wena ngoba waba nenhlanhla yokuba 
ngikuthande usubona ukuthi ngiwusimukanandwendwe?” 

Ilukuluku elase liwumlakatsha wegwebu lesihlungu 
elase lifuna ukuyicisha inhliziyo kaDubazana, lehla, 
phose laphola. Wabuza wathi, “Akazange akubambe 
uSilangwe?” 

“Ungibambile impela, kepha bengisihluthula 
isandla ngimkhombisa ukuthi angisoze ngahambisana 
nabekwenza.” 

“Waqala nini ukuzibika?” 

“Kade aqala, kepha ngokuthi bengingathandi 
ukunixabanisa, bengihlale ngikugqugquzela ukuba 

16 


ufune ikamelo kweminye imizi ukuze ngisiveze lesi 
senzo esibi singasekho khona. Yise kaMakhosazana, 
angikaze ngikusho yini lokho?” Lawo mehlo ayethambile 
engakhombisi nezincane izimpawu zonembeza okungahle 
ukuba wawumudla ngaphakathi wawaphakela umyeni 
wakhe. Izwi lakhe elimnandi lehla lathi tho, enhliziyweni 
kaDubazana samuthi ohlala zehle izinhlungu enxebeni. 

Babekade behlezi beqhelelene, kepha elokuqina 
kokhonkolo labenza bashendela ebhentshini, 
basondelana. 

“Iqiniso ukuthi ngiyakuthanda MaZondi. Nakuba 
indawo yokuhlala singenayo lapha eThekwini, ngehluleka 
ngisho ukwehlukana usuku nawe, ngikuhlalise ekhaya 
eMangweni, mina ngiyozifunela umbhede ehositela.” 

“Sithandwa sami, sekungaba ukulahlekelana 
kwethu lokho. Amahositela lawa anesandla esikhulu 
ekungaqondanini kwabesifazane nabesilisa abansundu. 
Nami engeza ngazokugana ngoba ngikuthanda ngeke 
ngakwazi ukwehlukana nawe. Yise kaMakhosazana 
noNkosana, mhlawumbe angikaze ngikutshele 
ngoba asikabi naphahla lomuzi wethu. Nokho ngoba 
ukuhlupheka sekusibeke kulesi simo, sesizotshelana 
amaqiniso othando lwethu ngaphansi kophahla lwalo 
mpheme wokulindela amabhasi.” 

“Yiyiphi le mfihlo engaka othanda ukungitshela yona 

Thuleleni?” 

17 


“Ngifuna ukuthi selokhu ngaqala ukuthandana 
nawe enhliziyweni yami kunezinsika ezinhlanu ezimise 
ubhayela kimi ovuthisa uthando lomshado wethu. 
Yiziphi–ke lezi zinsika? Okokuqala ukukubuka. 
Yize sisosizini kanje, ngokukubuka nje sengiphuze 
amanzi okuphila. Ngawaphuza ngiqala ukukubona. 
Namhla sengifa njengoJesu okuthiwa wathi eselenga 
esiphambanweni wakhala ngokoma, amanzi okugcina 
engokhala ngawo kobe kunguwena. Insika yesibili, 
ukuthintana nje kwami nawe, ungibamba ingalo, 
ungigaxa, kuba sengathi ngizwa isandla ubumnandi baso 
kumbe obungaphezu kobesikaDelilah alolozela ngaso 
uSamson. Insika yesithathu, isigubhu sendlebe. Elakho 
izwi selaba umculo engingawuzwa ngisho sesedukelene 
ehlathini. Kunezingoma engizizwa zingikhumbuze wena. 
Ngisho nokuhashazela kwamacembe ezihlahla ecula 
kungikhumbuza lezo zinsuku siseyintombi nensizwa 
phansi kwezihlahla. Insika yesine, iphunga lakho. 
Uyaye uzwe uma kuthiwa umuntu unesithandwa 
esizwakala ekhaleni? Insika yesihlanu nekungeyokugcina, 
ukunambitha nje. Ngenzenjani, ngifane nomama abaze 
bafa abanye intokozo yayo yonke le mizwa igqitshwe 
emahositela?” 

“Wangikhumbuza. Nakimi kunjalo. Ngisho ungipha 
ikhadi lezilokotho ezinhle, ngithanda ukuzizwa zilotshwe 

18 

ngesadla sakho.” 

Ekugcineni kwaze kwavela mveluvelayo owabayalela 
kwaNyokana, ngasesiteshini sesitimela kwaMnyandu. 
Yize lase lishisa sengathi lase liphezudlwana kokhakhayi, 
badonsana, banikela khona. 

19  



behla esitimeleni kwaMnyandu, bebambana 
behla ngezitebhisi bengena emgodini, qede bephumela 
emgwaqweni, ilanga lase lishisa sengathi lase libaselwe 
khona ezweni. Nofasimbe olwalukhona lwase luthatheka 
njengentuthu yalo. Banqamulela ngomendo, basheshe 
bayithola inombolo ababeyifuna. 

Umuzi ababhekana nesango lawo wawufana nje nezindlu 
zasemalokishini ezazimakamelomane. Umehluko wawo 
neminye yomakhelwane ukuthi kulolu uhla ababekulo 
iningi lase lapulasitela, lapenda, abanye sebafaka 
namafasitela amakhulu, izivalo zakwanokusho, nogesi. 
Elinye idlanzana lase lizinwebe ngisho ukuzinweba lezi 
zindlwana. Isimo sezinto emzini kaNyokana sasixoxwa 
nayigceke elalinesikhotha, namaphepha, namathayi 
ezimoto, nesikelebhu sayo esasesaphantshelwa amathayi. 
Kwakungekho nangane eyayidlala ebaleni. 

“Kwasengathi namuhla sizoziphonsa esifeni esingaphezu 
kwesiphuma kuso.” Kwakusho uDubazana evula isango, 
bengena, elivala ngemuva kwabo, qede ekhuleka. 

Nokho, owayesendlini wayengezwa njengoba 
wayegulelwa yiphulamastofu eyayigqamuka amalangabi, 
esejuluke emanzi te eyidlokodla ngenaliti qede 
igqamuke futhi. Sekunuka intuthu kaphalafini. Wake 
wayiyeka, wanikina ikhanda ezulazula nendlu yonke. 
Kwaba yilapho ebezwayo abase beyeke nokukhuleka, 
sebengqongqoza. Wabavulela. Ebabona, wanyewuka, 
wathi babengangena. Bangena bebingelelwa yiphunga 

20 

likaphalafini. 

Bezibeka kanye kanye izinqe kusofa, genu genu, 
bacwila, izinyawo zabheka phezulu. Wazimelela 
uDubazana, wasukuma, waphakamisa nomkakhe, 
bahlala ngasinqe sinye becuphe njengoba babetsheliwe. 
Yize base becishe baphoqoka imigogodla, endlini 
ababehlezi kuyo kwakuhlanzekile, naphansi umata 
wesulwe ucwebezela. Osofa ababekubo babephahle itafula 
elaliyindilinga, linezihlalo ezine nazo ezazishone phakathi. 
Odongeni kwakuncike ikhabethe lezitsha, nomsakazo 
omkhulu, igumbagumba. Kwakulenga nezithombe 
zakhe umnumzane lona owayesengale, enxashiswa 
yiphulamastofu eyayilanguka. 

Wabuya umnumzane, wadonsa isihlalo 
kwezazisetafuleni, wahlala. “Lapha ekhaya–ke, 
kukwaNyokana, kwaPhathaphatha.” Esebabingelele, 
noDubazana bazethula, base belubeka–ke usizi lwabo 
lokuntula indawo. Isicelo sabo salandelwa yikho 
okwakwejwayelekile kwabaninimizi, ukukhononda 
kokuziphatha kabi kweziqashi. “Ezinye zifika nezingane, 
zingcolise. Omunye afike ehlupheka, kube ukumcosha nje, 
aphenduke umninimuzi, aqale ukuvuka ekuseni ayavuzele 
phandle ngamaphijama lawo. Omunye uze athenge nemoto 
impela, ungenayo wena. Angazi ukuthi usuke ethi mbuke 
ngaliphi iso.” 

Wabe esezibika ubuqhathanzipho ayeyibona. 
Kwakucwebezela kunjeya nje phansi, wayezibambela 
yena mathupha, eguqa, epholisha. Nokho–ke 
wayenethemba lokuthi wayesezophumula, njengoba 

21 

kwakungase zinyanga zingaki, aganwe, esenengoduso 
emakhaya. Esaqhubeka nokuchaza, nokubalisa, wezwa 
ukuthi isitofu ngale sase sicishile. Waxolisa, wabuyela 
emsebenzini wokusidlokodla nokubhamuka kwaso. 

Ngokumncenga kwabo, bemkhalela izinyembezi, 
wehla. Wavuma ukubaqubisa esabafunda ukuthi 
babengabantu abanjani. Wabahola ebakhombisa ikamelo 
nalo elalihlanzekile, lisanda kupendwa, lingenampahla. 

“Asisale sesilikhokhela kungaze kufike soka limbe, 

likwehlule ngamazwi.” 

Wasinaza uNyokana, wayemukela imali. Enqekuzisa 
ikhanjana elalithiwe chwa, entanyaneni ende, 
wabatshela ukuthi base bengangena noma nini. 
Bavalelisa bengavalelisi, babamba indlela bengasakuzwa 
nokushisa lokho. Endleleni bafuna iveni, bayithola. 
Baqala kwaSilangwe nakwaNdlela. Abatholanga 
mpuphu nashukela, nani okuwukudla ababekushiye 
khona. Balayisha kwaNdlela, bedlulela kwaMbonambi 
uDubazana esezobonga, ethatha nabantabakhe. Lashona 
elalowo muhla bekwaPhathaphatha. 

“Kulo muzi onesibongo esingejwayelekile kangaka, 
umuntu akabange esachazelwa noma ukuthi Phathaphatha 
lokhu kusho isithakazelo sakhona yini noma igama.” 
Kwakusho uDubazana behlela impahla ekamelweni. 

Lapho beqeda ngakho kodwa nje, besakhala 
ngomphangazana, wangqongqoza umninimuzi, wabacela 
uxolo. Bamlandela kwayocushwa kosofa sebeyolandiswa 
ngemithetho yakhona. 

“Angazi ukuthi lapho enike niqashe khona kuyaye 

22

kumiswe kanjani. Kepha–ke, njengoba nazi, yilowo 
nalowo muzi unomthetho wawo. Nalapha–ke ekhaya 
kunjalo. Mina–ke, uma umuntu eqashe kwami angize 
ngingamthathisa okwesiqashi, kepha ngimthatha ngokuthi 
uyingane yakwethu. Kinina nje Dubazana nomkakho, 
sengithole umfowethu nodadewethu.” 

“Umthetho okuqhutshwa ngawo lapha ekhaya unje: 
Asiqale nje ekamelweni enihlala kulo. Njengoba nilibona 
lihlanzeke kanjeya, yinoba akuphekelwa nangengozi 
kulo. Ikhishi likhona. Okwesibili, lapha ekhaya 
asiyingeni indaba kamaziphekele. Sipheka bhodwe linye 
ngaphandle–ke mhla nipheke inyama yengulube, noma 
inhlanzi, okuwukudla esingashayisani nakho lapha 
kwaNyokana.” 

Yize uDubazana afela phakathi, lamthinta emoyeni 
elokupheka ndawonye. Kwakuzoze kuphekwe ndawonye 
nje, wayezopheka nini lo muntu owayengenamkakhe? 

“Mina–ke Dubazana ngiyazazela ukuthi isisu 
asikweletwa. Esami ngiyasikhokhela ngaphandle 
kokunanaza. Ngakho–ke angizukunihlupha. Imali 
ngizozilethela mina ningakayibizi ngisho ukuyibiza. 
Angazi–ke noma mhlawumbe zikhona yini izikhalo 
lapho?” Wababuka ngawo amehlwana akhe enyoka 
ayesabeka. 

Babezihluphekela oDubazana. Basinaza nje, 
baphelela lapho. “Okunye–ke nkosikazi engiyaye 
ngingakuthandi, kepha okuvame ukwenziwa yinina 
makhosikazi, ukuba sithi sikhokha sonke uthole kodwa 
ukuthi emapuletini lapha akulingani. Uthola ukuthi 
inkosikazi njalo nje ihlala igixabeza umyeni wayo 

23 


ngezidikadika zezibhuklabhukla zemilenze yenkukhu. 
Wena–ke ongemyeni wayo ikuzibe ngomqala nephikwana. 
Mina–ke angikuthandi impela lokho.” Washo bathi noma 
bembuka bazibonela ukuthi ngempela yayimenyelisa 
eyezibhuklabhukla zemilenze yenkukhu. 

“Sengathi kulukhuni Nyokana ukukhipha isiqiniseko 
sokuthi umuntu uyodla ehlezi ematafuleni zonke 
izinsuku. Thina siyakhahlazeka emsebenzini lapha. 
Sibuya emakhaya umuntu engasakwazi nakuhlala.” 

“Okusobala Dubazana ukuthi sewazejwayeza 
ukudla ulele njengenyoka. Lapha–ke kwaNyokana 
uzokwejwayela ukudla ngomese nemfologo, uhlezi 
njengomuntu.” Wabahola–ke eyobakhombisa ikhishi. 
Bengena nje kulo, bashaywa yizinyembezi ezindongeni. 
Lalikhala ezimnyama ezentuthu yephulamastofu. 
Impahla yayingeningi kuleli khishi. Kwakunetafula 
elalimi iphulamastofu. Ngasefasiteleni kwakunosinki 
wamanzi. Ngakolunye udonga kwakunqike ikhabethe 
alivula uNyokana wathi, “Ukudla kuhlala lapha–ke, 
hhayi ukuyobanga amaphela ngakho emakamelweni.” 

Belibuka elivulile, uDubazana walinikina kancane 
ikhanda. Lapho okwakuthiwa ukudla kwakuhlala khona, 
kwakome geqe. Kwakukhona amasosipanyana amabili, 
iketelana, nezitshana ezazingengaki. Ngokuqhubeka 
kukaNyokana evula ikhabethe, emashalofini kwakulokhu 
kushaya umoya, kungafaniswa ngisho ipheshana nje 
elalike laba ngelikashukela noma impuphu. Linye kuphela 
ishalofu athi uma elivula uNyokana kwabonakala okuthile 
kulo. Kwakunephela elilodwa elalishaye amangqeshane, 

24 

lipaquziswa yindlala. Buqamama nalo kwakunezigingqane 
zamanye amaphela. Ngokukhulu ukudabuka ayengasekho 
emhlabeni. 

Sebechazelwe ngayo yonke imithetho yekhaya, 
babuyela ekamelweni labo kumnyama amehlo. 
Wawubacacela umqansa wezingqinamba ababezowuqala 
kusukela kuleyo ntambama. 

Njengoba abakwaDubazana babengenalutho 
ababezolusa ebhodweni, kwase kudingeka ukuba bacele 
openyana bokuhlanganisa nomninimuzi. Wayethe 
wayengatshelwa, wayezibonela. 

“Asimngqongqozele ekamelweni lakhe kusaqala 
nje, ngoba sike samejwayeza, sesiyomthengela njalo.” 
Kwakusho uDubazana besabonisana nomkakhe 
ekamelweni. Bavumelana, waqonda khona ekamelweni 
uDubazana, wangqongqoza. Waqala kancane, waya 
ngokuya esiqinisa isandla. Phinde ukuphendula. 

“Mhlawumbe uhambile.” Kwakuphawula uMaZondi 
engazi ukuthi lapha ekamelweni elikhulu kuNyokana 
inkukhu yakwamakhelwane yase ingene emshinini. 
UPhathaphatha wayeyimimiliza inyama, ezowacaba 
muva amathambo. 

Bedelile abakwaDubazana, baphelezelana bobabili 
bayothenga. Babuya, kwaphekwa, uMaZondi 
esesebenzisa eyakwakhe iphulamastofu. Yekanini abantu 
besimame ngokufudumeza umuzi! Nephela lalapha 
ekhaya elalikade lishaye amankeyane akubonakalanga 
nokuthi lalivuke nini. Labonakala selehla lenyuka 

25 

lizicanasela emaphaketheni empuphu nawoshukela. 

“Awu bakithi! Sesivele sangibamba isithongo, ngalala 
wo, ngingakhokhanga namali yokudla.” Wazisola 
wazithethelela yena. “Kodwa–ke akusenani. Nangomuso 
kuseyilanga.” Waphumela phandle, waphondla 
empompini, wabuya, wahlala etafuleni. Wasidonsa isitsha 
sakhe, wasivula. Kwakuyilayisi nenyama yenkukhu, 
umkhwepha. Wathi janti, kwelikaDubazana, wafica zona 
izibhuklabhukla zemilenze. Wanikina ikhanda, wancinciza 
yedwa, belu engasabali ukuthi kulesi esakhe kwakugcwele 
isikhukhukazi esimatebhe nokuhamba nokukhala kwaso. 
Ngokuncuncuza kwakhe abakwaDubazana amehlo abo 
bawathi ne, kwawabo amapuleti. 

Beqale kuqala, besadla, bethuswa yizwi lomninimuzi 
selithi, “Angesuthanga koti.” 

Bambuka, bamthola encela iminwe, ebabuka ngalezo 
zinsungulo zakhe zamehlo ekati. 

“Kunjani, kukhona okusele ngale nina 
kaMakhosazana?” 

Wasukuma uMaZondi, wathatha izitsha, wazigeza, 
waphaka futhi ewashiya amabhodwe omile. Wabuya 
nakho wakuthi qithi, etafuleni. Wabonga uNyokana, 
wawolela umntanomuntu. Elesibili waliqeda 
bengakawaqedi awokuqala. Wabapha amehlo, bamncisha 
awabo, bawapha amapuleti. 

“Umuntu uzolala ngendlala–ke namhlanje. Uma lapha 
ekhaya kuzoqhutshekwa nokuphekwa kobala olunje, 
angiboni ukuthi sizoqhubeka nobuhlobo.” Wabashiya 

26 

wayozibhekela yena mathupha emabhodweni. Wezwakala 
enxapha yedwa ethi, “Nx, nalawa masosipani esimanje 
awasenazo nezikhokho.” Wabuyela ekamelweni lakhe, 
wazivalela. Esageza izitsha uMaZondi, iphunga lentuthu 
yomthunzi wezinkukhu lavimbanisa endlini. 

Wasala–ke uMaZondi nenkinga. Ukwenza 
kukaPhathaphatha kwasheshe kwacacisa ukuthi 
uMaZondi wayengamthathisi okwenkosikazi yesiqashi 
sakwakhe, kepha emthathisa okomkakhe. UMaZondi 
wamethuka uNyokana esemude ekamelweni lakhe, 
emtshela ukuthi wayefuna ukufudunyezelwa amanzi 
okugeza, afakelwe endishini, abekelwe endlini 
yokugezela. Kwenziwa lokho, wakhala ngebhulakufesi 
ezikhethela yena akuthandayo, njengeqanda nesibindi 
esithosiwe. Phinde kodwa ukuba uPhathaphatha 
aphathaphathe amakhukhu akhiphe imali. Noma–ke 
esezamile uMaZondi wathintitha anakho, akuphakile 
kwakufana nokuthi ukuthele enzolobeleni. Wayeshaya 
aphiphithe umuntu wakhona, akhale ngendlala. Esuka 
lapho wayengena ekamelweni lakwakhe, wawudonsa 
sengathi wayedubela kuwo umthunzi wezinkukhu. 
Angakuqondanga uMaZondi ukuthi ingabe wawumenza 
azingele zona yini izinkukhu, ngoba wabe esephuma 
endlini, ezulazula egcekeni lakwakhe. Khona manjalo 
kwezwakala isikhukhukazi sizikhalela sibaleka sibuyela 
kwabo kwamakhelwane. 

27 

“Nayizolo ngilahlekelwe yisikhukhukazi sami 
esiyimpangele. Manje kukhala esinye. Angazi Nkosi 
yami ukuthi koze kube nini umuntu elusene nokhozi 
olunamadevu!” UMaZondi ezicasukele wahleka yedwa 
ezwa inkosikazi yakwamakhelwane ithetha ikwayo. 

“Uwumyeni wami Dubazana. Uyangihluphekela, 
uyangondla. Kepha kuwe angizwa kukhathazeka 
engikuthole kule ndoda yalo muzi. Ayikhokhi senti, 
kodwa emini ifuna ukudla ngodli. Njengoba uzibonele–ke 
nawe ukuthi ayidli iyashanela, kusobala ukuthi liyothi 
liphela isonto siyobe singasenasenti. Futhi nje lo muntu 
…” 

“Waphelela lapho. Unjani?” 

“Ngisho ukuthi uma ngimbuka nje, Dubazana, 
akuphephile ukusala naye emini.” Wayezibambe esecishe 
waphahluka wamtshela ukuthi wayesihluthule kaningi 
isandla ezama ukusihlwitha. 

“O, hhe!” Wazikhalela uDubazana. “Nalapha sisedlula 
futhi?” 

“Uma kuyikhona okuphephile Dubazana, kunokuba 
ngivalelwe nemamba endlini, sisedlula. Nawe uyazi 
ukuthi emiqashweni kunjani. Kukaningi nami ngiphuma 
ngesamagundane nawe sezifuna ukungemuka wena 
izintokazi.” 

Edikibele uDubazana, sekuphele nenkumbulo, 
nothando namancoko ayethi uzoncokolisana ngawo 
nomkakhe, wazilahla embhedeni imicabango iphambana 
njengemibani ekhanda. Nomkakhe edidekile, washaya 

28 

iphulamastofu, wapheka. 

“Ulele manje umkami! Ukhathele naye!” 

“Ukhathele uma kade enzani engasebenzi nje?” 

“Nami angimvuseli ukufudumeza ukudla 
kwamabili!” 

“Anginamsebenzi nalokho! Ubomshayela umthetho 
emzini wakho! Nami kulo owami umuzi umthetho 
ngiwushayela ngisho impukane endiza khona.” 

“Emzini wakho phela, uqinisile. Nami ngikhuluma 
ngomkami, hhayi ngomkethu. Okwesibili, angihlezi 
mahhala lapha. Ngiyakhokha.” 

“O, konje zinjalo iziqashi. Uma zisengaphandle 
kwamasango, zisancengile, ziyanambuza. Uma 
sezingaphakathi zikhuluma zimise izinhlamvu.” Wathula 
isikhathi eside baze bacabanga ukuthi wayesehambile. 
Ngelikade wanxapha, wayesethi, “Ngiyakubona wena 
ucabanga ukuthi uhlakaniphile. Uzosheshe uzibone 
ubulima oyibo.” Waya ekhishini, wadumela ukudla 
akudla kubanda. Waqeda, wezwakala esebubula 
ekhononda ngokuthi yena wayephakelwa ubala. 

Waqwasha cishe kwasa uDubazana, ethatha ebeka 
ngengqondo, engatholi khambi. Engalalanga, wavukela 
emsebenzini nezinkinga zakhe, esaba ngisho ukumshiya 
umkakhe nendlondlo endlini. Ngalelo langa wasebenza 
eyinkinga nakozakwabo. Wayethukela kubo. 

UDubazana waphuma emsebenzini zisamthukuthelisile 
izenzo zikaNyokana. Wayengafuni ngisho bakhulumisane 
nangokudla lapho efika kwamabili. Ngakho waqonda 

29 

esilaheni, wathenga inyama yengulube, kwaphekwa yona. 
Yadliwa, bazishaya phansi. 

“O, namhlanje sipheke ingulube mntakaNyokana!” 
Kwakumemeza yena uDubazana ngokulahla ithemba. 

Wathula isikhathi eside futhi anduba athi, “O, 
namhlanje nipheke ucuphe uchuku?” 

“Thina sazi ukuthi nengulube ukudla.” 

“Ucuphe uchuku phela Dubazana, ngoba niyazi 
ukuthi mina angiyidli.” Wamkhankatha ebuza ethi, 
“Pho, beningangitsheli ngani ukuthi nizopheka yona, 
ngizifunele okwami ukudla ngisenethuba?” 

“Ngifike nayo ungasekho.” 

“Uyazi, ngake ngazilaya ngathi asipheke ndawonye! 
Ngidleni manje?” 

“Ingathi ngeke sikwazi impela ukukulamulela endlaleni 
njengamanje ngoba nesinakho yinhlanzi esemakopini 
esizoyipheka ngomuso njengoba nemali singasenayo 
nje!” 

“Asivele siyeke ukuxoxisana ngoba siyacasulana!” 
Wangena ekamelweni lakhe, wathuka eseyedwa 
edemelayisa, elala engalele. 

Ngomuso wavuka ethembele ekutheni uMaZondi 
wayezomphekela. Wathi ukuba amlandulele ngokuthi 
wayengenalutho ngaphandle kwenhlanzi, wamduba. 
Waziyela ezitolo lapho afike wazithengela khona 
inyama kwaShisanyama, wayosela khona, wadla 
washaya esibomvu qede wayozivalela ekamelweni 
lapho adonsa khona umthunzi wezinkukhu, 
wayesezilalela. 

Akabahluphanga ngoLwesithathu kwamabili ngoba 
babemazisile ukuthi babezopheka inhlanzi. NangoLwesine 

30 


bamlandulela ngayo. NgoLwesihlanu wabuya neyenkomo 
uDubazana, kwathoswa, kwaphekwa uNyokana 
esehambile. Balala bembekele. 

“Ungabe usakhuluma! Imali! Sheshisa!” Kwaqhuma 
impama, kwakhala isibhakela. “Thula ukuklabalasa 
siwula somfazi!” NoMaZondi bamthulisa ngesibhakela. 

UDubazana, eyibona imimese nezinkemba zimenyezela 
emisebeni yamathoshi, wakhipha imvilophu, wabanika 
eshweleza. Isandla esimnyama sayihlwitha, sayifunda 
sayibala imali. 

“Ayiphelele le mali. Uyisephi enye?” 

“Njengoba ubona nje mntakababa, amarandi ayishumi 
kuphela angekho, engithengele ngawo izingane inyama. 
Igilosa bengisazoyithenga ngomuso.” 

“Sinakanaka, ungabozithathela imali singakafiki!” 
Wamthwebula amahlombe ngentshumentshu. “Thatha 
nansi imali yamashwa uthengele izingane ukudla ekuseni!” 
Yamnika isenti elimdaka, yayisithi kweyayihamba nabo: 
“Sebenzani bafana!” 

Ababizwa ngabafana babachilizela laphaya oDubazana, 
baqala ukusebenza ngomfutho, bevula iwodilobhu, 
bezithathela amapotimende, belayisha beshiya 
ababengakudingi. Babembula abakwaDubazana, bathatha 
ngisho izingubo zokulala imbala, base bembonga ngempama 
evala amehlo uDubazana, bemshiya emnyameni. 

Kwake kwaba yisikhathi eside kuthulekile endlini, 
oDubazana besaba ngisho ukukhanyisa, ingasaphathwa 
phela eyokuyozama ukuvala ekhishini. Nengqondo 

31 

yayisalahlekile. Yathi lapho isanguluka khona, 
waphuthaza umentshisi uDubazana, wakhanyisa. 
Kwaba yila kubonakalayo ukuthi babemgcabile 
kuphela ngentshumentshu. Baya ekhishini, babuka 
isivalo. Sasingephukanga, nezabana lezo zomshudo 
zisacakathisekile kuso. 

“Wulungise mntakaDubazana,” kusho umkakhe. 
“Uyazi ukuthi emalokishini kunjani. Kusenokungena 
abanye, bayifune ngodli. Uma ulandula, bakubulale.” 

Wawulungisa uDubazana, babuyela ekamelweni 
bayoqhatha usizi. 

“Ngoba kusinde umphefumulo nje, mntakaDubazana, 
akusenani. Imali uzobuye uyisebenze.” 

“Akukho mphefumulo osindile lapha MaZondi. 
Kwakhona nje ukusakazwa ngezimpama phambi 
kwakho, nokushaywa kwakho phambi kwami 
ngikhona ngingenakukuvikela, naphambi kwezingane, 
nokwamukwa amandla ami ngisebenze isonto lonke, 
kusewukufa komphefumulo. Kunjalo MaZondi, 
ukwehliswa kwesithunzi ukubulawa komphefumulo. 
Sekuyohlala njalo ezinganeni zethu kuyisilonda ukuthi 
saqhunyiswa ngezimpama phambi kwazo.” 

Kwathuleka futhi endlini, sebethe khovololo sengathi 
babeshonelwe. 

“Nakho lokhu kubanjwa kwethu inkunzi sisendlini 
kwenza ukuba ngimdlinzele uNyokana. Yini eyenza 
ukuba izigcwelegcwele ziqonde nje ngqo, ekamelweni 
lethu, zingazami ngisho ukuwunyakazisa owekamelo 
lakhe umnyango? Zaze ngani ukuthi ukhona noma 
akekho?” 

32 

“Umbuzo impela lowo,” evunyelwa umkakhe. 
“Okusobala ukuthi lo mshudo uhlala ucakathisiwe nje 
ngoba ehlinzeka le mikhuba yakhe.” 

Wathi nya, nya, waphuma, wamemeza ekhala ngakho 
okuya ethunjini. 

“Angazi noma nisapheke yona yini ingulube 
nanamuhla bakwaDubazana?” 

“Qha, baba wekhaya besithenge eyenkomo namuhla. 
Asazi noma bayishiyile yini abafana, ngoba sikhuluma 
nje, sihlezi emanzini. Sigqekezelwe, basembula konke 
ebesinakho, besishiya singenasenti.” 

“Nigqekezelwe?” 

“Impela Nyokana.” 

“Ngabe ubani lona ongeyisa kangaka othela umuzi 
wami ngeshwa? Angizwa kahle.” Wazulazula nephasiji, 
wajika ekhishini, wabuya. “Musani ukudlala ngami! 
Ningathi ugqekezwe kanjani umuzi wami kungekho ngisho 
umshudulo okhombisayo ukuthi indoda eqashe kuwo ike 
yazama ngisho ukubashaya ngomshanelo?” 

“Bengizobashaya kanjani Nyokana sebengaphakathi 
endlini, behlomile?” 

“Abawona umoya oyingcwele labaya bantu. Bebengeke 
bangene ekamelweni lakho bengaqalanga ekhishini noma 
edangilomu. Benzenjani? Bagqekeze ifasitela?” 

“Bakhahlele umnyango wasekhishini.” 

“Umnyango wasekhishini? Musa ukudlala ngami 
wena lapha. Umnyango wasekhishini ushudiwe 
ngikhuluma nawe nje. Akukho ngisho ucezu lwawo 
oluvavekile.” 

“Ubulungiswa yimina khona manje Nyokana.” 

33 

“Ho, ho, ho!” Wahleka uNyokana. “Kulo muzi 
sekuyisiqashi kuphela esibalulekile. Umniniwo 
akaselutho.” 

“Ngisho phela ngoba uthi kugqekeziwe lapha ekamelweni 
oqashe kulo. Kuleli elihlala uNyokana akungenanga ngisho 
iphela. Okusobala ukuthi abagqekezi babone ukuthi 
angibalulekile, ngiyimpofana abangethole lutho kuyo. 
Hhayi, ngeke uyazi ingqondo yeziqashi. Mhlawumbe 
amaqhinga okungincisha inyama nje, khona uzothi 
abafana bedlule bayicosha.” 

Wayibheka lapho okwakuthiwa ikhona. Kwakungekho 
ngisho inembe epuletini. Kwakubangisane ngalo 
okungamasela, kwalikhotha kwalishiya kusengathi 
laligeziwe. 

“Kulungile, ngincishe. Sobohla Manyosi!” Wangena 
ekamelweni lakhe, wazivalela. 

Waphuma uDubazana ekamelweni, wabheka 
esitsheni ekhishini. Geqe, sasomile. Wangqongqoza 
ekamelweni likaNyokana emcela ukuba ake azobona 
ukuthi wayebelwe ini, egwazwe kanjani ukuze kumbe 
amfakazele nalapho esevula icala. 

“Konke njalo lokho kusewukweya uNyokana. 
Phela umuntu engazi mina ukuthi kufanele 
amangale umninimuzi. Kuyacaca–ke ukuthi lapha 
sekukwaDubazana.” Kwalandela iphunga nentuthu 
yomthunzi wezinkukhu. “Ngoba phela yiminyango 
yami ekhahleliwe, kodwa awusho ukuthi kufanele 
siyomangala. Hlukana nami ke! Angisayingeni le ndaba.” 

UDubazana wazijika embhedeni inhliziyo yakhe 
igqugquma, ibaneka njengezulu. Nalo–ke izulu ukuduma 
kwekhanda lakhe lakulekelela entathakusa. Laduma 

34 


laphahlazeka, liklaklabula, libaneka oluluhlaza tshwe 
unyazi. 

4 


“We makoti, ngeke ngikulambise. Kodwa le ndoda 
yakho ekuphekisa ingulube nenhlanzi ngoba iqonde 
ukungilambisa, ngeke ngiyinukise ngisho iqatha.” 
Kwakusho yena uPhathaphatha ngoMgqibelo zibuya 
inhlazane, yena ebuya esilaheni nenyama ayeyosele 
khona. Elinye iphakethe ayesethe ukulinonga ngentando 
walithi qithi phambi kukaMaZondi. 

“Ngiyabonga Nyokana. Ngizoyibeka–ke ngoba uma 
elambile uDubazana mina angilambi nakulamba.” 

“Uyazizwa ukuthi uthini?” Wambuka ngamehlwana 
ekati. “Uma kulambe yena wena awulambi?” 

“Impela kunjalo. Ngilamba uma kusuthi yena. 
Khona–ke njengoba ebanjwe nenkunzi nje, umoya wakhe 
wephukile, owami ufana nofile.” 

“Ngicela ungangidumazi. Ngikuphathele le nyama 
ngothando. Ngicela uyidle, njengamanje.” Wamjamela 
ngahlabayo. 

“Njengoba ngisho nje mfowethu, ngolamba lapho 
elambe khona, ngife lapho efa khona. Unjalo umshado. 
Thina naye siyabelana kokuncane nokuningi esikudlayo, 
esikufundayo, esikuhogelayo nesikunambithayo. 

35 

Sicozululelana enjabulweni nasosizini, endlaleni 
nasenaleni.” 

“Ngingamxhawula ngisho ukumxhawula uma angifaka 
owokuba umshado wami ngiwuthande ngize ngife. 
Ngenhlanhla–ke umendo wami uyena.” 

UPhathaphatha owayethemba ukuthi inxeba 
ayezomngena ngalo uMaZondi kwakuyindlala, wenyela 
ukwenyela. Wathi, “Kulungile–ke, sale usuyithatha 
uyoyidla naso isithixo sakho leso.” 

Wabuya ntambama uDubazana esekhiphe 
amasentshana ebhange, wazithengela ukudla izingane, 
kwaphekwa kwadliwa. UPhathaphatha okwakumkhubaza 
umphefumulo ukubona abantu abaganene bebambene 
ngothando, wababuka ngelomthakathi. Nesenzo 
sikaMaZondi sasisamhlaba enhliziyweni — ukuba ayoduba 
inyama ayemthengele yona ngemali eyayikhuthuzwe 
umyeni wakhe. 

Isonto uDubazana ayengena ngalo ekuseni ngehora 
lesithupha aphume ngelesibili ntambama, laqala 
uPhathaphatha eselibiza kubo futhi ipuleti. Usizi 
lwaya phambili ngokuhamba kwesonto kutheleka 
lapha ekhaya inkosikazi eyayithi ayibe ntanganye 
noMaZondi, kepha yona yomelele emathanjeni. Yafika 
emini kungoLwesine, esanda kuphuma nje umninimuzi, 
yazethula ngokuthi yayiwuMaDuze, ingoduso yakhe 
uNyokana. Besaxoxaxoxa noMaZondi, yasheshe yazibika 
ukungaphili, yangena ekamelweni elikhulu. 

Yize ukufika kukaMaDuze kwakumphumuzile uMaZondi 
emazwini kaNyokana ayegudla iguma, kepha kwakwengeze 
ngomunye umthwalo wesisu esasilindele ukuphakelwa. Belu 
engakhokhi uNyokana, ezazela nokuthi babekhuthuziwe, 

36 

ukudla wayelokhu ekubize njalo kuMaZondi. 
Kwakungasekho nokubalekela engulubeni nasenhlanzini, 
benqena ukuthi wayengase abaphinde ngenkunzi. 

“Yini, kwenzenjani kodwa dadewethu?” Wayebuzwa 
uMaZondi emi enamathele emnyango. 

“Mntakwethu, yilesi sigebengu sendoda. Awulunguze 
phandle ukuthi asesibuya yini, ngizokuhlebela.” 

Waphuma uMaZondi wabhekabheka, wabuya 
wathi, “Hhayi, akakabonakali ntombi. Awungitshele, 
sekwenzenjani manje usuvalelwa nje?” 

“Hho, hhe, sengiyaxoshwa, mntanomuntu. Isigebengu 
lesi sithi angihambe, asisafuni futhi nokuba ngixoxe nawe 
ngoba ngizoze ngisonele kuwe ngokudalula izimfihlo 
ezinkulu.” 

“Uzoze ube umonela kimi nje uma ngihlanganiseni 
naye?” 

“Ungayiphathi le ndaba, ngoba uma engase ayizwe 
ngabe sengifile. Bengizokuhlebela eziningi ukuba uyakwazi 
ukuzibamba.” 

“Ngitshele. Ngeke ngithi vu.” 

Wabibithela uMaDuze ethi, “Uyabona ntombi kaZondi, 
kuyangethusa ukumuzwa ekhuluma kanje, kuvele 
kuzicacele ukuthi sekuyakwenza okwake kwangenza. 
Umthetho wakhe lona uNyokana uma eseqala amacebo 
okuchitha umuzi wenye indoda, nokuyibulala. Nakimi 
wenza kanje. Ungibona nje ngangendele kwaChiliza. 
Ngangize lapha kwakhe ngokuhlupheka, ngizoqasha 
njengani nje. Ngamfica ehlezi nenye inkosikazi ayeyibiza 
ngengoduso yakhe, njengoba ubona kwenzeka nakimi. 

37 


“Okulandelayo kwaba ukuba achele amanga kubantu 

zomyeni wami. Esuka lapho wabe elokhu engiphathaphatha 
ngesandla sakhe ayesibhilile, ngoba uyaboniswa 
ngasemithini. Ngeshwa lami Nkosi yami,” wakhala 
wathi, “uma eqhubeka nokungibamba ngesandla sakhe, 
ngazizwa ngibhocobala, ngihlale ngimbuke. Ngisanda 
kumvuma ngingazi nokuthi ngivumani, aliphelanga 
isonto, wambulala umyeni wami ngendlela ayebulale 

ngayo nomyeni wenkosikazi engangimfice ehlezi nayo. 

Wayixosha, wayishaya wayiphiphitha impesheni yomyeni 
wami. Njengoba esengixosha nje uselungisela eyomyeni 
wakho.” Wasikhihla. “Wena ubengakakuphathaphathi 
isandla?” 

“Angazi ntombi ukuthi kukangaki ngisihluthula 
esesibambile.” 

“Okusho ukuthi banawe abakini. Uyawehlula lo muthi 
aqeda ngawo amakhosikazi abantu, qede awabulalele 
amadoda.” 

“Umuntu akasheshe abaleke lapha ekhaya angaze 
abone amanyala enyoka. Okwakwabani ukuyobulawelwa 
indoda! Wu dade!” 

“Ngabe wenzile. Ngendlela aseyisilwane ngayo, umzuzu 
nomzuzu sengihlala ngimesabela umyeni wakho.” 

“Uyamsongela yini?” 

“Uthi yimina nomyeni wakho esiyizithikamezo. Ngiyazi 
mina uzophumelela ukungixosha maduze nje, bese 
elungiselela khona ukukugcoba?” 

“Ukungigcoba?” 

“Ngisho ukukugcobela ubufelokazi.” 

“Nanti ishwa lami bo!” Lwamshaya lwameqa uvalo 
uMaZondi uma liqiniswa elomgcobo. 

“Ungakahambi nje, ntombi yomuntu, ngicela ungisize 

38 

ungiphonsele noma ucezu nje lwesinkwa ngefasitela. Ngafa 
yindlala. Nalokhu osiphakela khona ekuseni ungemuka 
esandleni.” 

Ngempelasonto eyalandela bagcwala umgwaqo 
nomyeni bezingela ikamelo abangalitholanga. Uvalo 
lwamshaya waxega iziketi uMaZondi ngoLwesibili 
olwalandela lapho okwasa engasafaniswa khona 
uMaDuze. Wesaba ngempela manje uMaZondi ukusala 
naye njengoba ngisho amehlo akhe ayesebukeka ekhala 
igazi, esembuka amncishe wona. Okwakuyenza inhliziyo 
yakhe igxume kakhulu ifune ukuphuma nangomlomo, 
ukuthi ngalelo sonto uDubazana wayengena ngehora 
lesibili ntambama aze abuye ebusuku ngeleshumi nanye. 
Ngokuyibona indlu iyisife kakhulu, wayeze aphume 
nezingane babhace phandle esibozini semoto aze abuye 
umyeni. 

Kuthe ngoLwesihlanu ntambama, kuyihora lesihlanu 
eziyela ezitolo, wathi lapho enyuka ngezitebhisi 
zovulande wazo, yamcela uxolo inkosikazi eyayisiqinile 
impela, ikufanele nokuba ntanganye nonina. Wema, 
wayibuka wayikhophozelela eyibona ifake ingutshana 
yokuhlupheka eyayinezimbali, igqobhokile. Ekhanda 
yayithwele ibherethi eyayike yamnyama, kepha 
isiphuphile, imhloshana. Onyaweni kwakuyizicathulo 
ezazimnyama, ziqhumile. 

Yambingelela, wavuma, yayisithi qaphu qaphu naye 
kanje: “Uyabona mntanami, awungazi, futhi angifuni 

39 

ungazi. Uza ezitolo nje, kade ngikulindele.” Yambuka 
ngobuso obabunemichidlwana eyayikake amehlo 
ayethambile ezisho ukulunga, ukwazi ukuhlupheka 
nendlala. “Bese ngibulawa wuvalo, ngithi Nkosi yami, 
lashona ngingakubonanga. Mntanami, ngithi angikutshele 
ukuba uphume uphele kulowaya muzi, manje nje 
njengoba ngikhuluma. Ungalali nangengozi khona 
namhlanje, ngoba uma uke nje walenza iphutha, walala 
khona, kusa kusasa ziyakulingana ezimnyama.” 

“Bazombulalelani?” Yabutha izinhlonze inkosikazi. 
“Bazombulalela wena impela. Phela ukuqasha lokhu 
kukulunguzisa kuyo yonke imigodi lena. Kweminye 
kuvela izindlondlo, kweminye ochakide, amankentshane 
kweminye, nani nani. Lo muntu oqashe kuye 
mntanami, alimfanele elobugebengu. Inswelaboya. 
Umbulali. Umbambi wenkunzi. Umdlwenguli. Abesilisa 
uyabakhuthuza, ababulale. Owesifazane angamazi 
uyamkhuthuza, amhlukumeze, ambulale. Oganile 
njengawe nje, eqashe kwakhe, umbulalela indoda, adle 
izimali zayo zempesheni aziqede axoshe inkosikazi. 

“Njengoba ubona sithule nje, ngabe kudala 
sakuhlebela. Ngeshwa–ke awuyena umuntu ohambayo, 
kunjalo nje angakubulala uNyokana eke wakubhadama 
uxoxa nesiqashi sakwakhe.” 

“Mdali wezulu nomhlaba!” 

“Unempi yakhe yezigebengu uNyokana, nomuthi 
wamacala. Ngisho emajajini uphuma phambili. 
Ngikholwe. Abantabethu ubabuthela kulo leli butho 
lakhe. Nokuba ngiyizwe le ndaba yomyeni wakho 
ngiyihogele kumfana wami osanda kuxebuka egengeni 
yakhe. Kumanje nje lesi sigebengu simfuna ngamnyama. 

40 


Nomfelokazi abambulalela indoda njengoba esanda 
kumxosha nje ubeselungiselela wena mfelokazi omusha.” 

“Phela mntanami umuzi wami ngabe 
sengiwubhubhisile ngoba sekungazihlalela obala 
ukuthi yimina engikulume indlebe kanti kadeni thina 
sinyamanambana ngalo mfana oqembukile.” Yaphenduka 
yathalaza inkosikazi. “Ake ngikushiye mntanami nawe 
ungaze uthwebule umfanekiso wami ungifakazise 
emacaleni azongibulalisa ngomuso.” 

Yamfulathela yanyamalala osizini imshiya ehawuza 
yedwa ethi, “Hawu, hawu, hawu …!” 

Kwahlwa lishona kuMaZondi. Nasesitolo lapho 
akabange esangena. Kuleli sonto lapho uDubazana 
ayeshayisa khona ngeleshumi kusihlwa kwamcacela 
ukuthi wayengeke adabule. Wabuyela kwaNyokana 
ehalazela. Okwakumenza ahambe sengathi wayendiza 
emoyeni yizimoto ezimnyama zezidumbu ezazithe 
chithi saka njengoba kwakungoLwesihlanu nje, zilethe 
izidumbu. Kwakungathi enye yazo wayeyibona 
isimlethele umhwashabula owawunoDubazana. 

KwaNyokana wabopha ayengakubopha, 
wayesezindezindela. Kuthe ukuba kuthi zibaba, 
walengisa izikhwama zakhe, waqhuba usapho, bangena 
indlela. Babelibangisephi? Emsebenzini eZibunge. 
Wayeseyofike afune umyeni, amtshele qede balale 
emasangweni akhona okungenani. 

Wayehamba ethuka izanya, eqalaza, uNyokana 
kuba sengathi wayemsinga emnyameni. Wayesesaba 
ngisho ukwedlula ngaphansi kogesi. Bakhwekhwetha 
ngezinqamulelayo, baqhamukela esiteshini, basho 

41 


phakathi esitimeleni. Kwaba sengathi uyaphupha esizwa 
siyiqongqotha naye enye insimbi, ewubuka uMlazi ukhanya 

kwentuthu. Kwakunamalangabi ayebonakala ebomvu 
elokishini, kungacaci kodwa ukuthi kwakushiswa utshani 
noma amathayi yini. Wanyamalala uMlazi ngokuqhubeka 
kohambo, kwavela abedolobha ogesi ababekhanya 
ngokwakuthe bha. 

Wehla eZibunge, waluqhuba usapho eyojama efemini 

yamathayi. Efika emaphoyiseni, wakhala ngomyeni. 

Abasathe abeka izaba zokuthi wayeyoze amthole 
ngazikhathi thize, wawathela ngezinyembezi. Wagcina 
elandiwe uDubazana wazojamelana nobusuku angazanga 
ukuthi babuzombuthela kuphi. Ngesikhathi umkakhe 
emzekela ayezizwile, walalela ngengqondo eyayithatha 
ibeka ingahlanganisi lutho olwalungayisiza. 

“Ngithe–ke, mntakaDubazana, ngingamane ngilale 
emapayipini nezingane zami kunokuba zibe yizintandane, 
ngibe umfelokazi. Mdali wami! Konje ngingaba yini nje?” 
Wamthela ngezinyembezi. 

“Kahle, ungakhali nina kaMakhosazana.” Wamdonsela 
buqamama nezingane. “Bengingabuye ngiphephiswe ubani 
ngingasaphephiswanga uwena? Ngiyabonga. Ngiphilela 
wena, nawe uphilela mina.” Wambamba ngesilevu, 
wamsondeza ubuso, wamanga. Wazizwa emthandisisa. 
“Engingakwazi–ke manje MaZondi ukuthi sizoquba

emsebenzini, njengoba kungoLwesihlanu nje nokusho,

Nempela njengoba kwase kuyihora 
lesishiyagalombili nje, izigcwelegcwele zase zala 
ukhasha emigwaqweni lapha, sezilahle ubuntu, 
zeswela uboya. UDubazana walushiya emaphoyiseni, 

42 

ebhentshini usapho, watholoza wayoncenga enduneni. 
Njengoba base bevele beholile, akubanga nangqinamba 
engakho. Yamvumela, wageza, wahhihlila i–ovalolo 
washaya ezakhe. Waphuma waluhola usapho. 
Zayima emthumeni esesesitobhini sebhasi, engazi 
noma kwakufanele ahlalele elaliya edolobheni noma 
elaliphinda eMlazi yini. 

Ngalobo busuku abakwaDubazana balazi ngokunye 
iTheku. Ama–ambulense ayengena engenile ekhala 
ubuhhawuhhawu. Izimoto nje ezazingema–ambulense 
zazibangisana ngesango nangeminyango yesibhedlela. 
Babeshayiwe abantu! Babegwaziwe! Babeklajiwe! 
Babehlahlelwe! Lonke unya lokuzwisa isintu 
ubuhlungu lwalwenziwe. Ukusibeka pho phansi isinqe 
kubahlengikazi! Babedonsa lolu hlaka, babambe leziya. 
Babebodwa ababephangalalela khona ezinhlakeni

Lwamshaya uDubazana uvalo, wancinciza ethi, 
“Ukuba angisheshanga ngacabanga ukuba singene 
ngaphakathi esibhedlela, ngabe singeniswa sesinje 

43 

njengoba kuyashisa phandle. Ukuba mntakaZondi 
awuzidelanga ebusuku, wazongikhipha lapha

“Lo muntu ubengeke avele azibalekele nje. Sekukhona

“Hhayi, kanti mhlawumbe ikhishwe yidlozi layo 
nje le nja. Iyophunyuka nenkosikazi enhle kanje! 
Siyoze sihlangane naye okhalweni lwezimpungushe.” 
Wayeququma yedwa uNyokana endlini, ezulazula yize 
kwase kuyihora lokuqala. Mhlawumbe wayenziwa 
nawukukhalelwa yigazi labanye ababequnyiswa 
yizinhlungu lapha esibhedlela. Abanye ababesezinhlakeni, 
abanye sebephunyelwe yimiphefumulo, babedlule

Zazilele izingane, uNkosana egonwe uDubazana,

wakhe, ozela. Entathakusa wazumeka noMaZondi, 
wabelusa uDubazana okwaze kwasa ebheke ngawayizolo. 
Kwaze kwasa gelekeqe belokhu bethelekile ababelimele, 
abanye becoshwe amaphoyisa sekusa. Kanti njalo 
abanye babebanjwe inkunzi khona ekuseni nje 
sebeya emisebenzini. Ngehora lesikhombisa baphuma 

44 


oDubazana bengazange babonwe udokotela. 

Ephaphama ngesikade uDubazana, edonsa 
amathe ebamba umlomo, amehlo akhe azithela phezu

klwi, ixegelwa yizingubo emzimbeni, yambuka ngamehlo 
ayenemithambo eyayibomvu nobuso obabuhwabhekile, 
bubomvana lokhu okuvuthiwe. 

“Kwenzenjani nalala kabi kangaka nosapho ezitobhini 
zamabhasi?” 

“O, ukuhlupheka e …” Akabe esazi noma kwakufanele 
athi mama noma athi udadewabo yini. 

“Phela mfowethu kuyahlushekwa emhlabeni lapha. 
Ngabe niphelelwe yindawo yini?” 

Wavuma uDubazana. Esadla obudala uMaZondi, baxoxa

ngokuthi wayenguMaMlambo owayendele kwaMlangeni. 
Wayezwakalisa ukubazwela. Ngenhlanhla ekamelweni

“Uma nginibuka nje, ninabo ubuntu. Mhlawumbe

wafa abantu abafika nobubi.” Waqhubeka naye ebala 
imikhuba emibi yeziqashi. 

“Idlozi lakithi ngabe lihamba nami!” Walisho elihasha 
elamaNzima elingawawezi ngazihlangu zamfula; eliwaweza

ngamazibuko.

5 
ngaseMfongosi, babamba umgwaqo owawukhonkwe

Lalijamelene nelangabi lomlilo elaliwubasela

lapha ekhaya.

bhungu. 

“Nilale kahle Myboy?” 

“Yebo gogo.” 

“Kuhle–ke mfana wami.” 

Endlini eyayimakamelo mane, ingapulasitelwe, 
ingapendiwe, idwetshwe iziphambanywana ezimnyama, 
bangena ngasekhishini. Nakhona kwakumahlikilili. 
Kwakubelethene izitsha namabhodwe phansi, ematafuleni 
naphezu kwamaphulamastofu. 

“Imihlola emhlabeni!” UMaMlambo washo ethi 
khimilili ema ephelelwa amandla. “Ngizele izintombi njalo 
ngizigcwalise indlu?” 

Enamahloni, wabedlulisela endlini yokuphumula. 
Lapha amehlo ahlangabezana nezintokazi ezintathu 
ezaziyimithambalala phansi, zibhocobele. Ngokungena 

47 


kwabo zethuka, zababuka ngamehlo ayeyigazi. Belu 
phansi zazingagingqiki zodwa. Zaziphelekezwe

ayezokhipha ibhabhalazi. 

“Nkosi yami, mama, wasithelekela nabantu 
bokuhamba sisazilalele!” Kwakusho enye yalezi zintokazi 
icikica amehlo ibuka unina. 

“Kufanele ngabe kudala nivukile Thandabani.” 

Ayembiza ngoThandabani wayeneminyaka

Kwakuyibunisile impela eyayikudla le ntokazi. Yamuthi

ke wayesezobaqubisa ekamelweni elalisanda kushiywa 

48 


uMakhathini. “Ngizocela–ke Dubazana uke ucuphe nje

“Engakaphuzi namithi pho afika nayo?” Wakhononda

elalisheshisa okombani, ebakhuza ebathethisa ngalo. 
Hoqo, yafinyela ingalo nengilazi. 

AbakwaDubazana banikwa ibhentshi, bahlala phandle 

belunyelwa amehlo, bengafisi lutho olunye ngaphandle 

kokuthatha isihlwathi. Izintokazi zavuka, zabamba

emithathu eyayisegcekeni lakwaMaMlambo, itshekile, 
yakhiwe ngodaka. Kuyo kwakuphuma kungena ubhuzane

ziphuma eminyango yemizi yabantu, balazi loluya sizi 
ukuthi lwalusho ukuthini ezimbizeni zabantababo. 

UDubazana owayesesaba ngisho ukuyilanda impahla 
yakhe kwaNyokana, waqasha imoto, waya khona 
esephelezelwa nayiveni yamaphoyisa. Wathola iwadilobhu,

Wakuthutha konke ayekuthola uDubazana wayokufaka 

49 


ekamelweni lakhe elisha, wakhokha nentela. Kwaba

Walandula.

Uwena ozosizimazisa.”

inyoka yabafazi? Noma ngiwuMaMlambo ngicela ungibize

UNtozami owayeseminyakeni eyayingamashumi 
amathathu nantathu, ekhanya, ekhulile, ubuso

nasezingilazini, wambeka eceleni kwakhe uDubazana.

abanye belambile, besayoba yinkathazo kwabanye

53 


“Sengehlisile ngamanzi. Asiqhubekeni. Konje
