umkakho. Ngicela wamukele lokhu engikutshela khona, 
ungaphikisani nalutho ngoba uma uphikisana nentando 
yami kulo muzi, uphuma ngesango. NoMlangeni ugcwele 
izintaba nje, ngakho ukungalaleli lokhu kwenu. Ngibeke 
u–a, abeke u–e; ngibeke u–i abeke u–o; ngibeke u–u 
aqhubeke abeke u–aa; ngibeke u–ee, agcine esebeka u–iii 
kubi kwethu! Engisho–ke ukuthi bathi abelungu, uma 

54 


useRoma kufanele wenze njengoba namaRoma enza, 
uphile ngokwemithetho yakhona.” 

“O, hhe, kodwa uthi ngizosikhumbula sonke lesi sizwe 
engisizele.” Wazenwaya ubuso. “Ake ngilande abazali 
babo bazozibalela bona.” Lacu, wasukuma waphephukela 
ekamelweni, wabuya nawo wonke amadodakazi akhe. 
Wahlala, wawamisa aklela phambi kwabo. 

“Konje izolo umbonile uThandabani?” Wavuma 
uDubazana. 

“Thandabani, awumtshele–ke ukuthi unezingane 
ezingaki ukuze kungabibikho ngane ekhala ngokuthi 
ayiphakelwanga ngoba bengayazi abakwaDubazana.” 

“O, mama, ezami ziyisishiyagalombili nabazukulu 
abahlanu.” 

“I!” Waquma uDubazana. 

Wambuza ngokunengwa uMaMlambo wathi, 
“Uqunyiswa yini manje?” 

“Qha, mame wekhaya ngimangazwa elabazukulu 
abahlanu uThandabani ebukeka esemncane kangaka.” 

“O, bhuti, kanti baningi nje ngoba amadodakazi 
amabili azibula ngamakhosi, enye yase yengeza 
ngomntwana oyedwa.” 

“O, okusho ukuthi ngakuwena singabala amapuleti 
ayishumi nane?” 

“Impela mfowethu,” wavuma ngokuzithoba 
uThandabani. 

“Owesibili–ke uFunani. Mtshele ezakho nawe Funani.” 

“Kungcono mama ngoba ezami aziziningi kakhulu. 
Ziyisithupha nje kuphela nabazukulu abathathu, 
mfowethu.” 

55 


“I! Okusho ukuthi singabala ishumi lamapuleti.” 

“Sesinamapuleti angamashumi amabili nanhlanu uma 
sihlanganisa nomama wekhaya. Angazi noma usekhona 
yini omunye?” 

Ngokuhluthuka kwenhliziyo uMaMlambo wathi, 
“Awusho ezakho nawe Lindeni!” 

KuLindeni zazinhlanu nomzukulu oyedwa. 

“Amapuleti asengamashumi amathathu nambili. Ake 
sizwe abanye?” 

“Awusho Ntozami?” Washo unina wabipha wabheka 
le. KuNtozami zaziyisithupha kuphela. Kulesi sithupha 
munye kuphela owayesakhulelwe. 

Waqhubeka nesibalo uDubazana. “Amapuleti 
asengamashumi amathathu nesishiyagalolunye kuphela.” 

“Swidilami, vala ngezakho.” 

Zazintathu kuphela kuSwidilami. 

“Okusho ukuthi esewonke amapuleti akwaMlangeni 
angamashumi amane nantathu. Sesisonke singamashumi 
amane nesikhombisa.” 

“Impela Dubazana.” Wabheka amadodakazi 
wathi, “Seningahamba–ke bantabami, sekulungile.” 
Wawabuyisela kuDubazana amehlo wathi, “Ngithi 
sesiqedile–ke Dubazana. Ungakhathazeki ngemali, 
sizohlanganisa.” Yashaya intwabi. “Ake ngiyokwehlisa.” 
Waphuma wabashiya bekulowo mnyama nomkakhe. 

Kuphele nayesozwaneni koDubazana, balandelana 
njengababefelwe nomkakhe, bayongena ekamelweni 
abafika kulo bahlala bathi khovololo, embhedeni, 
balinganisana. 

“Uyazi–ke, Dubazana, ngaphelelwa amandla. 
Impela uma useyisiqashi usuke ungelutho. Uma 
ngikhumbula kahle, kuwo wonke amakamelo esesike 

56 


saqasha kuwo, siyaxhashazwa. Intela esiyikhokha 
ngekamelo ingaphezulu kumbe ngokuphindiwe nentela 
yendlu yonke. Bonke bathi akuphekwe ngabhodwe 
linye bangakhokhi. Okusho ukuthi wonke amandla 
akho aphelela ekondleni abaninimizi, wena uphethe 
ungasakwazi ngisho ukwakha iqhugwane lodwa leli.” 

“Akukho phela okunye okungabuye kwenziwe Dubazana. 
Okungale kwalokho yithina esizobulawa yindlala wena 
wondla izingane zamanye amadoda.” 

Ngokwenyuka kwelanga uMaZondi wawacela 
kumninimuzi amasentshana okupheka. Sekumi 
amabhodlela ejamelene nabo bonke ababezibize 
ngabazali, uMaZondi wabukwa ngamehlo ayezingxemu, 
wanikwa iziwehle zamasenti ayemdaka ayengahlangani 
ngisho ukuthenga isinkwa sodwa lesi. Bakhipha 
eyabo noDubazana, wahamba eyothenga amaqanda 
ezethembisa ukuthi kumbe babezoshayeka. Wabuya 
waphaka waphelela emapuletini ayengamashumi 
amabili, washiya kanjalo wayodlela ekamelweni 
nabakwakhe. 

Ukuthi ubani owayedlile nowayengadlile, akabonanga. 
Nokho, wezwakala umsindo ukudla sekudonsiswana 
ngakho kubangwa abazali nabantababo. Namapuleti 
ayebangwa ayephunyuka kwabanye akhale phansi. 
Abambona kahle ebaleka ethi uyodlula emjondolo, 
umthamo ugcwele umlomo, umfanyana owayesejahwa 
yiqulu lezingane ezamkhela zamkhwelela zimndondonya. 
Ezinye zamqhoqhobala zipitshiza wona umthamo 

57 


ezazilwa nokuwukhipha. Ngemuva kwalokho zafinyelela 

Lathi liyophela isonto izintokazi zalapha ekhaya 
zonke zase zikhala ngoZwelisha sengathi kwase kwaba 
kudala zamejwayela. Nantambama zazibangisana ngaye 
zimbizela ukhasino, okwakuyisenzo esasimxhopha 
umoya uMaZondi owayengakwazi kudlala nakhasino 
lowo. Enganakile uDubazana lapha endlini waba 
umdonsiswano wesimame. Umkakhe wayemnxusa 
ukuba bazivalele ekamelweni, izintokazi zimhlabekise 
ngokumdonsela kuwo ukhasino edaningilumu. 
UMaMlambo yena wayebhoke ngevangeli lokuba 
angambizi ngoMaMlambo, kepha ngo “Sis’ uThiza.” 

Kwakungase kumdidise uDubazana empilweni yakhe 
ukuba yena yedwa kule ndlu ayothi dlwa, phakathi 
kwabesimame ababebahle bonke. Phakathi nesonto, 
uma kwenzeke utshwala ababa namandla lapha ekhaya, 
ayethi lapho esebuyisa egazini amadodakazi kumcacele 
ukuthi wonke ayeyizintokazi ngempela. Kwakungathi 
uma zithola amadoda anothando olunamandla 
okuziphephisa ophuzweni, zibe amakhosikazi emizi yawo 
owawungaziqhayisa ngawo. 

Enamahlonyana uDubazana ngokuba yimpethu 
yengxabano phakathi komkakhe nomndeni walapha, 
wazama ukuncelisa amawele. Nalapho kukhasino 
kwabuye kwahlaluka ukuthi izintokazi zakwaMlangeni 
zizodwa zazibangisana ngaye, ikakhulukazi oNtozami 
noSwidilami. UNtozami yena wayehluleka nokufihla. 
Noma nini lapho kudlalwa, eba wuphathini kaDubazana 
ayembiza ngoZweli. Kancane kancane waba uZweli 

58 


kaNtozami; waba uZwelami kuSwidilami. 

“Ntozami!” 

“Yidla Zweli! Yidla!” Wayeze agxume ambambe. Khona 
uma sebenqobile, babethakasa aze amange. 

Wayebambana nobani pho? Wayeyintokazi uNtozami. 
Engamunwe, ezothile, enobuso obabubujana, kanti nginjalo 
nje, ngimile, ngikhona. Wayenalawo mehlo akhe ayensundu 
ayemthapha uDubazana ashiye imibuzo ingaphenduliwe. 

“Zwelami!” 

“Swidilami.” 

“Kusinwa kudedelwana phela. Yimina manje 
uphathina wakho.” Wayekhanya uSwidilami, enesitho 
nomnyovu wokhalo. Bonke, njengonina, babebuka 
ngalawo mahlonyana nje. Wayewabona kahle sekudlalwa 
uDubazana, ngoba phela kukhasino kushaywana ngawo 
amehlo. 

“Zwelami bandla, yidla! Hlaba ishumi lezinkomo leli!” 

“Sengilishwabadele Swidilami!” 

Ngale ekamelweni wayesuke elalele njalo uMaZondi, 
elele engalele. Ngesikhathi bona begxuma bethi 
banqobile, eyakhe inhliziyo yayidla amalangabi. Kwala 
ngabusuku thize. Bathi besatshelana ngamehlo ukuthi 
ubani owayezokudla izinkomo zabanye etafuleni, kanti 
kade emile ebabuka noNtozami. Bethuka ngoMaZondi 
esecela umyeni wakhe uxolo qede ephenduka ebuyela 
ekamelweni. 

Walandela uDubazana, wahlala embhedeni, walithetha 
libomvu. 

“Angazi noma Dubazana, ukuhlekisa ngami yini. 
Okokuqala nje ukuthi unguyise wezingane, kodwa ubizwe 
ngoZweli noZwelami mina engingakubizi nangaye, 

59 


kusukelaphi? Okwesibili, unyoko lona uMaMlambo 
usuwuthathaphi umkhuba wokumbiza ngo ‘Sis’ uThiza’? Uze 
wazi negama lakhe nje, nisuke nitshelana nikuphi ngasese?” 

“Ungichazele ukuthi niyezwana?” Wavala amehlo 
ngezandla, wakhala mi ebalisa. “Ngithini phela mina 
uma wena izintombi zakho usuzibiza phambi kwami 
ngoNtozakho noSwidilami? Kanti mangaki amaswidi 
osunawo lapha endlini?” 

“Nina kaMakhosazana, uyazi nje nawe ukuthi uwena 
kuphela lapha emhlabeni untozami noswidilami. Laba 
oNtozami noSwidilami balapha ekhaya, oNtozami 
noSwidilami ngamagama nje kuphela.” 

“Namanje usaphinda futhi uthi oNtozakho 
noSwidilakho?” Wakhala waze wavevezela. “Mina yonke 
indawo lapho sisuka khona bengikuvikela, kodwa wena 
usudayisa ngami ezitheni zami uzibiza ngamaswidi akho 
omkhuhlane.” 

“Nkosi yami, bandla nina kaMakhosazana angizange. 
Futhi akuzona izinto zami namaswidi ami. Izinto 
zikanina namaswidi kayise abazethela wona ngingekho 
nokuba khona lapho. Uma futhi ngithi ngibabiza 
ngoNtozakho noSwidilakho bazosuke basenze inhlekisa 
kakhulu.” 

“Ngiyambona noNtozami osekubiza ngoZweli. Lokhu 
okuwuSwidilami kuze kujobelele ngokuthi Zwelami pho!” 

“Uyazi–ke, angisazi ngempela manje ukuthi kufanele 
ngenze njani?” 

“Kanti musa ukudideka ngoba usufike emzini 
onezintonjana zotshwala. Mina ngazi ukuthi thina 
nawe sibambisene osizini. Ngakho–ke hlukana 
namantombazane sihlale nawe kuleli kamelo lethu 
esiliqashele umshado.” 

60 

Ekwenzeni kwakhe konke uDubazana wayezama 
ukukugwema okwakumdonsela ekubeni achithekelwe 
umuzi. Wayezama ukwenza njengoba wayetshelwa 
umkakhe. Zathi noma sezimbizela ukhasino izintokazi, 
wabika imbiba wabika ibuzi. Okwahlala kuyinkinga 
yikho ukubiza amagama oNtozami noSwidilami. Wayeze 
azibuze uma eseyedwa uDubazana ukuthi kazi yini 
eyayenze abakwaMlangeni izingane zabo ezintathu 
zokuqala bazethe ngamagama anemibuzo, ezimbili zibe 
nayizidlaliso. Esazibuza eziphendula, nababenamagama 
ayimibuzo bawenza inkinga kuye sengathi babetshelene. 
Empeleni bona babesophe ukushaya inhliziyo yalo mkakhe 
ababecabanga ukuthi wayesehlala equviswe yisikhwele. 
Wathi ubiza uThandabani impendulo yaphuma iqhasha, 
ithi, “Wena!” 

“Ngifuna wena sithandwa sami.” 

“Lindeni!” Wasabela noLindeni ethi, “Ngilindele wena 
phela mntakwethu!” 

“Uyazizwa izinto zakho zingiqholoshela emzini 
kanina ngoba zilwa nokukwenza isigqila sokuzondlela 
lo mhlambi wazo?” Nomkakhe ngale ekamelweni 
wayebhodlela kuye. “Impela emhlabeni uma ungenamuzi 
awunasithunzi.” Wasikhihla. 

Kwakuseyize okwamagama nezimpendulo. 
Okwakusazowuzamazamisa umuzi kaDubazana 
okwenzeka kungoLwesine ngehora leshumi nanye 
kusihlwa ephuma emsebenzini. Wathi lapho engqongqoza 
ekhishini umnyango wakhona wavuleka sengathi ukhona 
owayekade emlindele. Wammemeza ehleba ethi akangene 
ngokushesha. Kwaba ukungena nje kukaDubazana 
emnyameni wekhishi, intokazi yasheshisa imuthi manqa, 
manqa ngezindebe ezihlathini nasezindebeni ihleba ithi, 

61 


“Angazi ukuthi ngenziwa yini Zweli. Nginesizungu nje 
sakho.” 

“Nk …, Nkosi yami, izinto sezajika ezweni. Amakati 
asebalekela amagundane.” Wahleba naye uNtozami 
engena egulukudela engutsheni edaningilumu. Wathi 
engena ekhishini uMaZondi, umyeni wakhe wayeseshuda 
emnyango. Waphenduka nekhandlela emholela 
ekamelweni. 

“Umuntu wafa ukuphuma ebusuku!” Wayesho 
uDubazana ehlala embhedeni ekhotha udebe lwangezansi 
qede egwinya amathe. 

“Kunjani, kunambitheka kamnanjana emlonyeni, hhe? 
Ukhotha unambithe uze ucimeze.” 

Wethuka uDubazana, wahlahla amehlo ethi, 
“Kumnanjana uma kwenzenjani?” 

Umkakhe embuka ngeso lengwe yebelwe amawundlu, 
wambuza wathi, “Dubazana, ngisacela uke ukhulume 
iqiniso kanye nje selokhu safika lapha kwaMaMlambo. 
Ubani okuvulele emnyango?” 

“Mina bengicabanga ukuthi uwena ngoba 
ngingqongqoze kuleli fasitela qede wavuleka umnyango 
wekhishi.” Walukhotha futhi udebe olungezansi. 

“Unambitha awuqedi nkunzi. Kuhlale kuthiwa 
kukhona eManzimtoti nje, namhlanje mina ngizalelwe 
undebezimtoti. Dubazana, nkosi yami bandla, ngicela 
ungitshele, ubani okuqabulile?” 

“Ongiqabulephi?” Wabutha izinhlonze wazidla udebe 
futhi. 

“Ungaze ulimunce uliqede izibithi.” Wavula isikhwama 
sakhe wabuya nesibuko, wamnika. “Mina, awuzibuke 
ukuthi unjani.” 

62 

Wasemukela uDubazana, wazibuka. Akawakholwanga 
amehlo akhe. Isigcobisamlomo sasithe bhade ezihlathini 
zakhe silobe izindebe. Nowakhe umlomo wawubomvu 
tebhu. Ngawo umlomo obomvu wakhamisa njalo ezibuka. 

“Umyalezo wenhliziyo okuphi kodwa?” Wabuza 
uDubazana ezibuka ihembe esifubeni. Wayengabonanga 
ngempela ukuthi uNtozami wayezibhadeke nini izindebe 
lapha. Nokho konke kwakwenzeke ngokuphazima kweso. 
Ehembeni lakhe elaliluhlaza, phezu kwayo impela 
inhliziyo zazithe bhade izindebe ezibomvu, intokazi ize 
yambhansela nangokumgcoba indlebe. 

“Angingabazi nakungabaza ukuthi imisebenzi 
kaNtozakho lena uma kungeyona ekaSwidilakho. 
Uma ngabe awusho ukuthi ubani, ngizohamba manje 
ngibembule izingutshana lezi abalele ngazo, ngibabuke 
imilomo.” 

“Ngicela ungakwenzi nina kaMakhosazana.” 
Wamncenga. 

“Uvuna amantombazane edlala ngami ngiyinkosikazi? 
Bahlale bekwenza kubalungela!” Wahalazelela emnyango. 

“Ngicela wehlise umoya mkami.” Wambamba ngengalo 
esethi uyaphuma. “NesiZulu siyasho sithi ithi ingahamba 
idle udaka. Sihambile thina nawe. Noma kubuhlungu 
ngicela uthalalise. Nami, ngisho noma ngabe ngiyazi 
ukuthi ubani ongiqabulile, ngeke ngimveze ngoba ngiyazi 
ukuthi inhliziyo ayiphakelwa. Ungasuke umlwise, 
siphelelwe yindawo yokuhlala khona manje kusebusuku 
nje.” 

“Uqonde ukuthi indawo yokuhlala angiyincenge 
ngokulahlekelwa yisithunzi sami nokwenziwa inhlekisa?” 

63 

“Kuyaye kube njalo uma ungenamuzi MaZondi. 
Usukhohliwe yini ukuthi nawe kwase kukaningi 
uSilangwe ezibika, ekubamba, kodwa ungifihlele ngoba 
ubona ukuthi sasingase sixabane, siphelelwe nayindawo 
yokuhlala? Thina osekusifanele ukuba sifune ikamelo 
bayosichutha phambili.” Wamehlisa ethi uyabhilita, waze 
wathamba wahlala embhedeni wakhala. 

Ewezwa la mazwi emthinta uDubazana, wathula 
ecabanga edla udebe olungezansi. Enganakile ukuthi 
ngahle ukuba wayesenza icala, wenyukela kolungenhla, 
walukhotha nalo. Wambuka umkakhe, wathi, “Mina 
Dubazana ngangiyaye ngixabane noSilangwe uma 
engibhansa. Kuwena kodwa ngibona sengathi kumnandi 
ukuqatshulwa oNtozakho noSwidilakho.” 

“Kodwa nina kaMakhosazana ungasho kanjani 
ukuthi kumnandi ukuqatshulwa yintombi unenkosikazi? 
Wadlala ngami nje! Wenziwa ukuthi awukwazi ukungena 
enhliziyweni yami uzizwele ukuthi kubuhlungu kanjani 
ngithule nje.” 

“Qha, angenziwa yilokho. Kade ngikubuka umuncana 
nodebe olungezansi. Usuwuqedile–ke lowo shatini manje, 
usukhwelele olungenhla ngoba phela nakhu amaswidi 
amnandi oSwidilakho. Noma uthi ithi ingahamba 
idle udaka nje, mina angiboni ukuthi ukudla udaka 
ukuzidlela iruji.” 

“Bese ngikhohliwe MaZondi. Ake ngiyogeza endlini 

64 

encane.” Wasukuma wavula umnyango, walunguza, 
wayesephenduka ebheka umkakhe esethi, “Ngicela 
ungiphelezele Thuleleni bangaze bangiphinde.” 

Baphelezelana bangena endlini encane. Wezwakala 
nompompi amanzi ekhala endishini esegeza 
uDubazana. Zingaphansi kwezingubo, zilalele izintokazi 
zakwaMlangeni, zaqhumuka zifa yinsini. 

65 


6 
nesonto kwaMaMlambo utshwala babuyinkinga. 
Ngezimpelasonto, kusukela ngoLwesihlanu kuze kube 
yiSonto phakathi kwamabili babuphenduka isifo. 
Inhlekelele yengozi abakwaDubazana ababeyibona 
bengakayiboni abakwaMlangeni yayidalwa abanye 
besilisa ababephuze nonina bezingane abase bezihlinzela 
ezibini. Kwase kukaningana oMaZondi noDubazana 
belamela amadoda ayeseqinile impela encike ezindongeni 
zemijondolo namadodakazi oThandabani. Ngaleso sikhathi 
ugogo nonina bezingane babesuke bengasabonisisi 
kahle. Uma izingane ngesinye isikhathi sezibonakala 
emathunzini nabanye ababaziwa bengamasoka onina, 
kwakugcina kungasaqondakali ukuthi kazi–ke kulezo 
ezase zisoleka umunwe wawukhomba bani. 

AbakwaDubazana bazizwa beqhaqhazela ngo– 
Makhosazana owayesehlosile. Bamelusa, abamvumela 
nokuba adlale nezingane zaleli khaya. Kwalokho 
kumkhipha kwabo inyumbazane, kwabenyelisa onina 
abakuthatha njengokucwasa abantababo. 

Izinga lotshwala lapha ekhaya lathi kanti selivele 

lenyukile, laqhwakela ezicongweni ngokufika komnumzane 

othile okwakuthiwa uMaqhobozela Qumbisa. Wayehamba 
ngonyonyovu locekeceke lwemoto ewuhlobo lwe–BMW 
eyayisiliva okwakumpunga, ibocoke kaningana 
emzimbeni. Yayihhudleke kudlekile. OkaQumbisa 
wayethulwe kuDubazana nguMaMlambo owayemchaze 
ngokuthi wayeyisoka lakhe elase limethembise umendo. 

66 

Ngokulanda kwakhe uQumbisa wayenebhodlelasitolo 
khona eMlazi, esanda kwehlukanisa nomkakhe. 

UMaqhobozela wayevama ukutheleka kusihlwa 
kwaMaMlambo esevalile emsebenzini. Ukuthi kwakonakele 
wawubona ngayo imoto ibhensile, ngemuva ilayishe 
amabhodlela. Wayehla uQumbisa elungise okwewundlu, 
angene kuphuzwe, kusale utshwala, kugingqike izigingqane 
phansi. Kwakuba yilapho–ke isimo ayefike eyiso 
uQumbisa esasifike siguquke khona, akhule ngemizuzu 
angabe esaba yiwundlu. Wayeba isilwanyazane. Ikhanda 
ayengene elikame kahle, wayelihlikihla, alinikine, 
alihlikize. Wayebalisa angaqedi ngezinsizi zomhlaba. 
Esikhundleni sokuba benoMaMlambo baduduzane 
ngokubhidlikelwa yimizi, babebudla qede baklolodelane. 
UQumbisa wayeze ahlale athi khovololo, abambe 
isihlathi uma esebalisa ngomkakhe uMaZamisa ayethi 
wayemkhumbulela ukumgcina ehlanzekile, engalibali 
nokuthi wayenesisu. Ehlabeka uMaMlambo naye 
wayemncoma angaconsi phansi uMlangeni ngokuthi, 
nakuba wayenenkani yesele, kodwa wayengcono ngoba 
wayengakhaliswa wutshwala. Isigcino kwakuvama ukuba 
uMaMlambo aqukulwe angeniswe ekamelweni lakhe, 
abashiye bezigingqikela edaningilumu abanye. Yebo, 
wayengenisile kwaMlangeni umfo kaQumbisa. Ukusukela 

67 

eMsombulukweni kuya eMsombulukweni babuhlala 
bungangamanzi okuphala izikhumba. 

Kwenzeka–ke ukuba kuthi ngaMgqibelo thize ebusuku, 
uDubazana abambe i–ova. Wangena kusihlwa, eyoze 
ashayise kusile. Wabaqhatha uMaqhobozela namabhodlela, 
baphuza baphelelwa yingqondo. Kwakungawo futhi lo 
Mgqibelo lapho uMakhosazana waphaphama khona 
ebusuku washiya unina ezumekile waya endlini encane. 
Wahamba umlibe. Unina wavuka wampampa emfuna — 
do. Wamthungatha endlini encane. Endlini yokuphumula 
abesilisa nabesimame wabafica bengalele, befile. Wabuza, 
waphendulwa wukuhonqa. Kwakulelwe kungavaliwe. 
Waphuma wazungeza indlu nemijondolo. Lutho. 

“Umntanami ngabe udliwe yinja uyinyama yini? 
Makhosazana!” Wamemeza esekhala eyedwana 
emnyameni. Wayesesaba nokuthi kumbe wayephume 
esebuthongweni weduka okhuhleni lokuhlwa. Eselahlela, 
watholoza wayongqongqoza ekamelweni likaMaMlambo. 
Akekho owasabela. Kuphela kwezwakala ukuhudulwa 
kwezikhumba. Wasidudula isivalo savuleka. Habe! 
Yiziga yini! UMaqhobozela wayehlezi esihlalweni 
egone uMakhosazana owayethuthumela, ehlengezela 
izinyembezi. Phansi kwakusakazeke amaphepha aluhlaza 
ayeyikhulu lamarandi. 

68 

“Hhawu, Nkosi yami! Kodwa baba umdala kangaka!” 
UMaZondi emhlonipha uQumbisa wesaba ngisho 
ukumphatha ngezandla. Wasimze wakhala wathwala 
izandla esiphundu. 

Kwaba yilapho uMakhosazana ekhala oma. Wambutha 
unina emthela ngezinyembezi naye ebuza ethi, “Ukwenzani 
Makhosazana?” 

“Ungithumbe ngiphuma endlini encane mama …” 

Wasukuma uMaqhobozela, wema watholoza ebelethe 
izandla ethi, “Mashwa mani–ke lana angehlelayo!” 

Belu uMaMlambo wayesalele obokufa, ehonqa aze 
anambithe amathe. Ngokwenyuka kwamazwi baphaphama 
nababesedaningilumu nasekhishini bayogcwala 
ekamelweni lamachilo. 

“Yini, kwenzenjani Qumbisa?” UThandabani wambuza 
ethwele amehlo ayebomvu. 

“Naba bayangisukela bayangilwisa.” Weneka izandla 
ebakhomba. 

Wathi uMaZondi, “Waphosisa kanje baba umdala. 
Sikusukela uma wenzeni?” 

“Njengoba ningethwesa icala engingalazi nje.” 

ULindeni waliphakamisa izwi ethi, “Qumbisa, khuluma 
wenzeni?” 

“Yithi abakutshele bona, mina ke ngizokuchazela.” 

Ngokukhulu ukumeya nokumnengwa uMaZondi, 
uThandabani wambuka wambuza ethi, “Nimenzani 
uQumbisa emdala kangaka kunani?” 

“Asimenzanga lutho uQumbisa. Uyena osigilela iziga 
simethemba.” UMaZondi wayilanda indaba, wadedela 
uMakhosazana owayizeka ukusuka nokuhlala. 

Amehlo abomvu kaThandabani aguqukela kuQumbisa, 

69 

ambuka awaze aqina lapho ebuza ethi, “Baqinisile 
Qumbisa?” 

“Nabo phela bathi ukwenzile.” Kwakusho uFunani. 

Enambuza uQumbisa washaya ungqimphothwe ebeka 
naye olwakhe uhlangothi lwendaba. “Ngiphume lapha 
ekamelweni ngithi ngiyochitha amanzi. Uma ngivula 
isivalo sendlu encane ngithi ngiyaphuma, uvuleke 
kancane umnyango wekamelo elihlala umalokazana lona 
osengibheca. Ngiqale ngethuswe ukungikhiphela kwakhe 
ulimi enyalizisa okwemamba. Kusenjalo, angiqhwebele 
ekamelweni lakhe. Ngimhloniphe bantabami umntanami, 
ngingene kanti sengizigwaza ngowami. Kube ukungena 
kwami nje angethele insumansumane ngimdala ngingaka. 
Ungehle ngaphezulu bantabami engibuza ukuthi yini ngibe 
yisiduphunga kangaka ngiyeke yena emuhle njengoba enje, 
imali yami ngiyidle noxamu bezidakwa. Waqhubeka esho 
nokuthi ubesezwile ukuthi ngehlukanisile, ngisele nomuzi 
ngedwa. Wathi ukuba bekuya ngaye yena ubezowulaxaza lo 
xamu wendojeyana yakhe engenamuzi, ayongigana.” 

Wakhala uMaZondi ethi, “Baba, uyangiqambela. 
Angizange ngikusho konke lokho.” 

“Mntanami, ngesikhathi uqephuza ulanda 
amanga aluhlaza angizange mina ngikunqume ulimi. 
Ngikuhloniphile nje waze wayiphetha imbenge yakho. 
Wena–ke, ngokukhulu ukungeya, ungixubha ngisadla.” 

“Kodwa …” 

“Shikh–i!” UFunani owayemkhuzisa okwenkukhu 
uMaZondi. “Awuthule wena ngcwelengcwele ndini sizwe 
ezakho!” 

70 


Esasikhihla uMaZondi waqhubeka uQumbisa ethi, 
“Umoya wami ngiwuzwe wehla uma ethi imali yami 
ngiyidla nohonani wengulube.” Washo ephenduka 
ekhomba uMaMlambo owazihudula wazisheshisa 
izikhumba eshaya namakhala. 

“Akagcinanga ngokukhuluma,” kuqhuba uQumbisa. 
“Ungichukuluza sengimdala kangaka. Uyasuka lapho 
uthi angimnike amakhulu amahlanu amarandi engithe 
uma ngenqaba wavusa le ngane. Ngokucaca kokuthi 
ubefuna ukulifela amathe igama lami laziwa kangaka 
ngibaleke angaphunyuka njengoba ngingenisane nabo 
kuleli kamelo eyifuna ngabomvu imali. Ubelokhu 
engisolile ngokudlala ngayo ngokuyidla nakade 
ebabiza ngoxovudaka abayini. Kwale sengizikhulula 
ngokumxosha ngokumnika nawa amarandi ayikhulu, 
phinde wawasakaza njengoba nizibonela nje nani.” 

Izintombi zakwaMlambo nabangane bazo, utshwala 
busagcwele igazi, azilucubungulanga udaba. Zamhlohloloza 
uMaZondi zanikezelana ngaye zimnephula ziqhakambisa 
elokwethukwa ngoxovudaka kunamanyala ayegilwe 
wuQumbisa. 

“Ake sibone ukuthi nalo ngcwelengcwele wengelosi 
yakhe ugcwelezwe njengoba usho yini.” Washo uLindeni 
elekelelana nodadewabo oThandabani noFunani. Sengathi 
babetshelene bamcaphunisa okwephepha uMakhosazana 
bamjika embhedeni, qede baneka izandla. Wanqekuzisa 
ikhanda wahleka uMaqhobozela ezwa uthotholwane 
wokukhululwa emahlazweni. 

UMaZondi esathi uphuthuma ukucosha izingubo, 
bamjikela oFunani. Wazinqaka qede wayidonsa indodakazi 
enqamula nayo naphakathi kwabesilisa ababampansa 

71 


bebaphelezela ngohleko namagama anohlalwana. 

Uyise owathi engena ekuseni ingane yayisikhale 
yaze yanesilokozane, yamthela ngemvula yezinyembezi. 
Wabasathe uDubazana uyabuza ukuthi kwakonakalephi, 
bobabili oMakhosazana nonina abakwazi ukumchazela 
amazwi eswakeme emvimbini weminjunju yenhliziyo. 
Ukuthi kwakunomonakalo owawenzekile uDubazana 
waze wezwa ngokuvutha kwezintombi zakwaMlangeni 
ezamfica ekamelweni esabuza kukhalwa. Zazishaya 
izifuba zicela ukuba aye edaningilumu ayokuzwa 
inkohlakalo eyayisale yenziwa umkakhe nendodakazi. 

UDubazana nabakwakhe bahlala bonke phansi 
edaningilumu njengoba ezihlalweni kwakugcwele 
abasekhaya nabangane. OMakhosazana nonina 
balubeka olwabo uhlangothi lwendaba. Namadodakazi 
akwaMlangeni akubeka ayekuzwe ngoMaqhoboza, 
emkhomba emkhombile uMaZondi ngezinhlamba 
okwakuthiwa wayezithuke ngazo nonina. 
NaMaqhobozela lowo wayengasabonwa, enyenye ngovivi 
lokusa. Nokho, ayesasele emaningi amabhodlela obhiya 
nogologo ayefike nawo ngayizolo. Kwakukhulunywa nje 
kuphuzwa. 

UMaMlambo yena wayehlezi njengesihambi 
kusofa, ethe khovololo, ebambe isihlathi ngesandla 
esasivevezela. Wayeyeshwama yonke le ndaba. Noma 
kunjalo, wayethule nje, wayebilela ngaphakathi. 
Lalimngqangqisa elikahonqani wengulube. 

“Kodwa ingane ayilandi njengoba nilanda. Ingikhalela 

72 


ngokuthi ibigetshengwa umkhulu wayo.” Wayebeka 
ngomoya ophansi uDubazana ethonya intukuthelo 
nakuye. 

“Yebo Funani.” 

“Nisifunani nalo mkakho?” Wambuka isikhathi eside 
waze wahlengezela izinyembezi. “Wena sonke isikhathi 
uyehlulwa yilo mfazana wakho osewakudlisa ngazo zonke 
izinsila zakhe. Ubomnika imali emenelisayo ukuze apheze 
ukukhuthuza amadoda abanye. Mina sengikhathele 
uyena.” Wazesula zaminineka futhi. “Naphandle lapha 
sengizwile ukuthi uhamba esibiza ngezilambi ezondliwa 
umyeni wakhe. Umbona esephuma ibhodwe lakhe yedwa 
nje ngoba nakhu lezi zilambi eziyithi ziyakukhuthuza. 
Kungcono khona ukuba nivele niphume ngesango nisishiye 
nokuhlupheka kwethu.” 

“Mina usengiphakele ngazesutha izinhlamba zakhe.” 
Kwakugaxela uLindeni owayesanda kuyibeka phansi 
eyakhe ingilazi eyayisenegwebu. 

“Mina Dubazana bengithi ngiqashise umntanami 
lapha ekhaya. Bengingazi impela ukuthi ngifuye umna 
… umna …” Yabhilita intwabi. “Ngihlezi nomnakwethu 
ongibangisa kubantu abangizamela umuzi. Kunokuba–ke 
ngehlukane noMaqhobozela okumanje nje kuthokozwa 
ngaye lapha endlini, angehlukane nomuzi wakho mfana 
wami. Ngisize–ke mntanami uphume uphele naye lo 
mfazana wakho singakabambani nje ngezihluthu.” 

“Ngiphume kanjalo nje mama nengane 
ngingasamangalanga nakumangala emthethweni?” 

“Uyomangala phela kowakho umuzi mfana 

73 


wami, hhayi kulona wami!” Wasukuma wafingqa 

la magceke wangifica ngimsulwa. Ukuba umhambuma 

kwakho akungabi yisiqalekiso sami!” 

“Nomkani ashaywe abe mabokoboko kanje ngibe yitshe 
elingezwa buhlungu?” 

“Akashayangwa yimina umkakho mntanami. Ushaywe 
yinkohlakalo yakhe yokusethuka nokuyenga umuntu 
womuntu.” 

Baqala phansi futhi ubuwelewele, amadodakazi 
amathathu ayenamagama ayeyimibuzo nonina besho 
ababelithanda bashiye ababengalithandi kuMaZondi 
nenkosazana yakwakhe. Sekumnyama amehlo 
uDubazana wasukuma wababamba ngezingalo, wabahola 
wayozivalela nabo ekamelweni. Kwaba yisikhathi 
eside bemkhalela, naye ethule ebambe izinyembezi 
ngezinkophe. Ngale kwagcina kuxokozelwa, kuhlekwa, 
kuphuzwa. 

Kwakusemini enkulu lapho uDubazana 
owayenqekuzisa ikhanda ehlezi embhedeni elizwa 
sengathi wayesemaphusheni izwi lendoda eyayikhuleka. 
Isingenisiwe, wayizwa ibika usizi lwayo lokulala 
emigwaqweni, ikhulekela ikamelo, noma inxiwa nje 

74 

elalilingene umbhede. Wamuzwa noFunani ehleka 
olwezintombi emfuleni qede ethi, “Uyazi, mntanomuntu, 
unenhlanhla! Kodwa uphalaza ngonjani?” 

“Ngisho ngoba umuntu obenqwahe nekamelo lapha 
ekhaya uyaqoqa ngikhuluma nje. Lizoba liphume nobomvu 
mama. Akakhokhe ahambe ayolanda izimpahla.” 

OMaMlambo nala madodakazi akhe amathathu 
belekelelwa abangani. Bonke sebekhuluma 
beshwashwatha, bebuka ngayendwazile, nobala 
sebelukhotha belukhothile, bavumelana ngokuba 
baxoshwe abakwaDubazana. Nempela uFunani 
owayesehamba ebambelela ngezindonga wamlanda 
uDubazana. Waziswa nangaleyo ngqomondo yendoda 
yakwaQwabe eyayimhlikwe, ibuhwanqa buzidlubha. 
Watshelwa nokuthi uyena–ke okaQwabe nomndeni 
ababezolala ekamelweni ngokuhlwa okwakuza. 
Wakhokha washeshisa phambi kwakhe uQwabe. 
Wabasathe uyancenga uDubazana kwaba uyadulela nje. 

“Sengiyolanda izimpahla. Ngiyethemba–ke ukuthi 
nsizwa yakithi uzosala uqoqa.” 

“Angithi uyamuzwa?” UDubazana wayebuzwa 
uMaMlambo egexise ikhanda. 

“Ngiyezwa.” 

Wasukuma uDubazana waphephuka eseyoziqoqa 
engazi nokuthi wayeyozifaka kwamabani izimpahla. 

75 

7 
ntambama lalinesibhengubhengu somoya, 
ilokishi lishunqa izintuli ezibomvu ezazibukeka 
sengathi zazilixhophile ilanga elalilengele phezu 
kwezintaba. Namafu ayehlobe ngayo imikhwazi. 
UMaZondi wayelinganisene noMakhosazana nomshayeli 
emhlahlavini weveni owawudlikizela wonke sengathi 
wawuzovele uhlakazeke. Wayengezwa, engaboni nakuthi 
naveni leyo yayibathwele nje ibasusa emalangabini 
babeyogazingwa kwenjani imbuthuma. ODubazana 
noNkosana nebhungwana elalinensila ngisho ebusweni, 
lidatshukelwe emahlombe, babehlezi ngemuva, 

benamathele ewadilobhini, befifiyela. Konke uDubazana 

ayekubuka wayekubona kulotshwe usizi. 

Umshayeli, eyindoda eyayisemashumini ayisithupha 
nanhlanu eminyaka, elingene nje ngesidumbu, ezigqokele 
i–ovalolo eyayinamafutha azo izimoto, wayishintsha imoto 
waze wagxuma ingangeni egiyeni. Lathi lapho liyongena 
khona, washaya isikhwehlela wathi, “Safa yizintuli 
ezibomvu. Mina–ke angizwani nelanga nenyanga ebomvu 
ngoba umkhulu wayehlala engitshela ukuthi kusho impi. Ake 
nilibuke nje ilanga! Likhala igazi.” Ngobuso obabumnyama 
bunezezelwa nangamafutha, nentshebe eyayingakanyiwe, 
inezingubo, yababuka ingezwa mpendulo. Yethuka lapho 
oMaZondi nendodakazi beyibuka ngayekhala igazi 
qede beyithela ngomvimbi wezinyembezi. AkaMaZondi 
ayenemikhwazi yokuhlupheka nokushaywa. 

Njengoba umgwaqo ababehamba ngawo wawusunqamula 

76 

imijondolo, umshayeli wawelukisela kuyo amehlo. 
Wayebuka izimanga zalezi zindlu ezazakhyiwe 
ngamakhathoni otshwala besintu, ngothayela abase 
babola, ngodaka, nani nani okunye okwakungase kumiswe 
ngakho amadlangala. Imvamisa yalezi zindlu yayitshekile. 
Zaziminyene, emagcekeni kuxhutha. Lwalungabuzwa 
usizi, lufundwa kubantu abadala nezingane ezazibonakala 

kumangalise kuleso siminyaminya sezindlu ukuthi 
ompompi, imigwaqo nezindlu zangasese kwakungabonakali. 

Ibhungu elalihlezi noDubazana, lithunywe uyise ukuba 
liyobalayela umjondolo ayebaqashisela wona, layishaya 
inhloko yeveni eyayivele izibolele yaze yabhodloka. Yalisika 
isandla elasinikina sesivuza igazi. Wema umshayeli, 
lamchazela ukuba achezuke emgwaqeni. 

Nempela iveni yanhlanhlatha ezikhotheni yaye yema 
kuleso sibhicongo sempilo. ODubazana nebhungu behla, 
walandela nomshayeli. Ibhungu labaholela egcekeni 
elalinendlwana eyayiwuhhafudakana owawutshekile, 
wakhiwe ngodaka, wafulelwa ngothayedlana owawugqwalile, 
unezimbobo. Amafasitela ayemancanyana, engenangilazi, 
kungamapulangwe wodwa, ayemabili, ephahle 
umnyango owawutshekile, ucakathisiwe nje emafulemini. 
Kwakungahluthulelwe nakuhluthulelwa. 

Ibhungu elalizethule ngokuthi lalinguMkhumbane igama 
lalo, lasichiliza isivalo savuleka, bangena. Kwakungekho 
lutho phakathi olungako. Phansi kwakubomvu igazi. 
Lapha nalaphaya kwakunezinqamu zogwayi nensangu, 
namaphepha okhasino, onhliziyo nompukane. 

“Owu! Uthi umuntu uyolunga lapha ebingelelwa yigazi 
engena ngakho kodwa nje?” Wayebuza uDubazana eqikileka 
ethuka. 

“Kanti baba unganaki. Yizinto zakhona lapha emjondolo,” 

77 

kusho uMkhumbane engagqizi qakala. “Ngiyabona 
ukuthi izigebengu lezi bese zithole indlu yokushovela 
amaphepha. Kodwa–ke uma usungenile, ngeke zisondele.” 

“Kungcono ngoba uzofihla ikhanda endlini noma 

kuthiwa ayishudiwe,” kuphawula umshayeli. 

Kulo lonke usizi lwasemjondolo, baziduduza ngokuthi 
lwaluzoba ngcono kunababekubone emakamelweni. 
Njengoba lapha kwakungekho mfula nampompi 
ababengakha kuwo amanzi bageze igazi phansi, bazidiliza 
izimpahla evenini. Kwabanjiswana ngazo zibekwa 
phezu kwalo igazi. Selibomvana ilanga liwucezu ngale 
kwezintaba, yafulathela iveni ibashiya esidlavaleni. 

Alizange liye eziko ngalelo langa. Nasebusuku 
ukubuthi quthu pho! Ubusuku bonke indlu yayizungezwa 
abantu ababehhomuzela benxapha, bethetha, bethuka, 
bewundondonya nangezibhakela umjondolo. Kwasa 
abakwaDubazana behlezi bemaphaphu aphezulu. 

Ngokusa kokuqala besemjondolo, besaba ngisho 
ukuphumela emnyango sebebone omunye womakhelwane 
wabo owayengakwesokunxele. Kwakuwumuzi wezingane 
ezase zizelene. Ebaleni base bezibonile izingane 
ezintathu, kungamantombazane amabili nomfana 
oyedwa. Zonke zazomelele, zimiboqwana, zinezinwele 
ezazilele, zizinde, namapaklaklana ezisu. Zazihlubule, 
zilingana, zibukeka sengathi zazishiyana ngesikhathi 
esasingaphansi konyaka. Onina noyise, owesimame 
eseminyakeni eyayiyishumi nesishiyagalombili, owesilisa 
iyishumi nesishiyagalolunye, babeyizinti zokuvungula 
ezazisindwa amakhanda. Bobabili babengasebenzi, 
beyimikhiqizo yobandlululo nezinkubela zomzabalazo. 
Lalishone elangayizolo, kuse nje, kumhlophe imilomo, 

78 

bengabonaze bakuthi mbibi. Babebabuke ngamehlo 
ezingwe ezilambileyo. 

Ngemuva kwamadina ngoMgqibelo bathelekelwa iqulu 
lentsha. Kwakungabafana, amabhobhodleyana nezinsizwa 
kanye namantombazane ayesemancane nayesekhulile. 
Phakathi kwalo kuthe gqwa gqwa amakhosikazi 
namadoda. Ababefana ngakho bonke kwakuwukuhlubula, 
ukuhloma ngezikhali ezazinhlobonhlobo, nokuthwala 
amehlo ayebomvu, ehlaba, elambele ukudla, ukufukutha 
nokuphuza igazi. AbakwaDubazana, bebabona bethi 
memfu emnyango, basho umthandazwana omncane 
ababecabanga ukuthi kwase kungowokugcina. 

Bangqongqoza, kwathiwa abangene. Bangena 
bagcwala indlu. Abanye bahlala naphezu kombhede 
okwenza ukuba abakwaDubazana abathathu babe 
yinqwatshana emsamo laphaya, ekhoneni lombhede. 
Ngaphandle kukaMakhosazana owavele wazishutheka 
ngaphansi kwawo umbhede lowo. 

Wababingelela uDubazana ebabuka ngamehlo 

79 

ayenezinyembezi zokwethuka. Kwavuma olunye 
uhalakasha lwendoda olwalufana nomakhelwane wabo. 

“Ngiyezwa bakithi.” Washo uDubazana luthi damu 
uvalo ngokuzwa elalithi babengezile ngempi. 

“Awuzisho–ke nsizwa ukuthi uwubani, wakuphi, 
nokuthi uyiliphi,” kusho lona uhalakasha lolu lumbuka 
ngokumlambela. 

Wachaza ukuthi wayengowakwaDubazana, ezalelwephi, 
esebenza kuphi, eganwe umabani, enezingane ezingaki. 

“Awukasho njalo ukuthi uyiliphi. Ukuba 
bekusezinsizweni bengizobuza ukuthi uviva naziphi.” 

Wadideka uDubazana, wabakaza ethi, “Mhlawumbe 
kukhona lapho engingezwisisi khona. Ezweni phela 
abantu sebalandela iNkolo yamaKhrestu. Mhlawumbe 
nibuza ukuthi ngisonta kuphi?” 

“Awusiyeke ngendaba yamakholwa. Mnumzane, 
wazenza umuntu ongaphili nje kuleli izwe? Angithi uyazi 
ukuthi lapha ezweni kunamaqembu ezombusazwe?” 

Wavuma uDubazana. 

“Uyazi ukuthi emaqenjini enkululeko yomuntu 
omnyama kunamabili kumanje abangayo, aqedana 
ubusuku nemini?” 

“Yebo ngiyazi.” 

“Thina singelinye–ke lawo. Njengoba usibona nje 
silapha besiyibambile eyomzabalazo womuntu omnyama. 
Siyidungulile. Uzibona nje izibhamu zisashunqa umsizi. 
Nezinkemba zisaconsa igazi.” 

Nempela wazibuka uDubazana ezazilele phambi 
kwabo zisemanzi yigazi. Kunembazo eyamhlasimulisa 
umzimba, inobuchopho. Ucelemba wawunomnkantsha: 
hhayi wesilwane — womuntu. 

80 


“Ngeke sihlale nomuntu singamazi. Sisheshisele! 
Zisho!” 

“Siyakuzwa lokho,” kwagasela abanye. “Sonke silapha 
emjondolo nje ngoba singenamizi. Kodwa noma kunjalo 
asikhohliwe yimpi yenkululeko. Uma ngabe ufihla ukuthi 
uzwelana naliphi iqembu, siyeke sikukhiphe inhliziyo 
siyifunde.” Amehlo ayesalotshwe izidumbu ayesanda 
kuzigingqa ambuka afisa esakhe. “Lapho obukade uqashe 
khona kade beyini?” 

“Bantu bakithi, bengiqashe emzini wabantu besimame 
abakade beziphuzela nje, benganake lutho.” 

“Pho, waxoshwa yini khona?” 

“Kube ukungezwani nje kokubanga ibhodwe.” 

“Benipheka ndawonye, bengasakhokhi?” 

“Impela, sengathi uyazi.” Wavumela phezulu 
uDubazana. 

“O, uyile nhlobo yomuntu esilwa nayo. 

Uyindlayodwana. O, sengiyabona.” Uhalakasha 
lwalunqekuzisa njalo ikhanda. “Namanje awukafuni 
ukusho ukuthi usha nabaphi?” 

“Ngicela ukuba nkonzonye nani.” 

“Kulungile. Uzosinika kuqala inombolo yalapho 
obuqashe khona, sihogele umkhondo ngawe. Uyokhonza 
nathi uma sesenelisiwe ukuthi uyiliphi ngoba asifune 
mpimpi lapha esizothi siyibambe nayo beyikhohlisana 
ihlomile. Okwesibili, kuzodingeka wazi ukuthi lapha 
kuyaliwa. Ezinye izitha zethu ezinkulu yilaba bantu 

81 

baselokishini abangaphesheya komgwaqo abangavumi 
sikhe amanzi kompompi babo. Thina–ke asizukulwela 
inkululeko yakho wena ube usonge izandla. Siyezwana?” 

“Unezingane ezingaki?” 

“Zimbili.” 

“Ziphi?” 

Nangu umfana ngemuva kwethu. Intombazana 
yethukile inibona, yacasha ngaphansi kombhede.” 

“Itshele iphume!” 

Waphuma uMakhosazana, watholoza encika ngonina. 

“A, kanti usunentombi engaka! Bonke nonina 
banonophele. Bayabonakala ukuthi balala kwezifudumele 
bedle izambane likapondo ngesikhathi thina silambile, 
silele ezikhotheni silwela inkululeko yabo. Namhlanje–ke, 
nakulo mfana wakho kufanele kucace ukuthi kuphelile 
ukuba umnqolo gombotsheni umachoba izintwala 
zikanina. Siyakhempa lapha. Siyalwa. Sizokwazisa 
ngosuku lwekhempu. 

“Okunye futhi okufanele ukwazi ukuthi awuzukuthutha 
lapha singakabuyi sizokutshela ukuthi sizwani ngawe. 
Uma sike sakubhadama uthutha, nango wena, nanto ithayi 
entanyeni!” Bengasavalelisanga nakuvalelisa, basukuma 
babashiya kanjalo bedidekile. Yize babelambile, kwaphela 
lokho kulamba nokoma. Umzuzu nomzuzu base belindele 
amathonsi abanzi. 

Ntambama ngesonto abakwaDubazana bezwa kukikizwa 
phandle. Kwathiwa abesilisa bonke abahlome, kuqhutshwe 
abesimame nemigqomo bayokha amanzi ngenkani 
kompompi bemizi yonke eyayingaphesheya elokishini, ibizwa 
ngeyabalandeli belinye iqembu. UDubazana engenakubuza 
ukuthi imizi yayingaba eyeqembu elilodwa kanjani yonke 
abantu bengayi nganhlanye bengemanzi nje, wathatha 

82 

imishizana yakhe. 

“Ngixoleleni bantabakababa. Bengiwuphum’ engena, 
ngiqasha emizini yabantu. Uyazi–ke nawe ukuthi emzini 
womuntu akungenwa nezikhali.” 

Yanxapha insizwa yathi, “Phambili! Sengathi ngalesi 
sibhamu ngingavele ngikuhlahlele lobu buchopho 
obunobuphukuphuku. Mina!” Yahosha insabula 
eyayiyinamathelise khona esibhamini yamnika. 
“Ngiyakubona ukuthi kule nhliziyo yakho ufuye 
ubucwicwicwi obufukamele uJesu. Ngifuna namhlanje 
lo Jesu wakho ukumbona ephuma eqhasha enhliziyweni 
yakho. Uma ngithi, “Mbulale!” Umbulale. Kusemjondolo 
lapha. NoMfundisi wakho usuyomtshela uma ekunquma 
ebandleni ukuthi uJesu wasala emjondolo.” Yamhlinela. 
“Uma ungambulali, kufa wena nomuzi wakho.” 

OMaZondi, oMakhosazana, amanye amakhosikazi 
namantombazane bathi nikilili nemigqomo, nezindishi, 
amabhakede namasosipani imbala. Yalandela kancane 
eyesilisa. KuyiSonto ntambama abantu bezibusela, bathi 
bebona babethi memfu abesimame nemigqomo. 

Bathi bayabuza ukuthi kwakwenzenjani, kwakukhala 
umpompi ngapha, kwakukhala omunye futhi ngale. 
Beyifunda ivaliwe abantu abadala ukuthi babecushiwe, 
bawuhlaba inhlali. Baqala abanye ukuqoqa ababengase 
bakuqoqe, bakulayisha ezimotweni. 

Izingane lezo ezingabuzanga nakubazali bazo ezacosha 
amatshe zabajikijela ngawo abamabhakede. Yenzeka 
indaba! Abesilisa beza bengasanyatheli phansi, sebendiza 
emoyeni. Ngokuphazima kweso bagaleleka emagcekeni. 

83 

Kwaba ubuwelewele. Kwaqhuma inhlamvu, kwadla 
umkhonto, kwahlahlela imbazo, yatshuza egazini 
intshumentshu. Babaleka ababaleka, abanye basala 
enkundleni. 

Wamsukela uDubazana. Ngokuphazima kweso 
wayesehefuzelela emahlombe akhe. Wamuthi jeqe 
umuntu wesifazane, wakhala. 

“Maye! Hawukela izingane zami mntanomuntu!” 
Wema, waphenduka wambuka ngamehlo ayehlengezela 
izinyembezi. “Kodwa ubulalelani kungakufanele 
nakangaka ukubulala?” Watshekisa ikhanda emncenga 
ngamehlo. “Ungibulalelani ngiwumuntu wesifazane, 
ngikuzala ngiphinde ngibe isithandwa sakho futhi?” 

“Akumina engithanda ukukugwaza. Uyezwa nje bethi 
bazongibulala uma ngingakugwazi.” 

“Kulungile impela ungifele. Nami ngike ngikufele uma 
ngibeletha.” 

“Manje umeleni? Baleka Nkosi yami ngisale ngikufela– 
ke!” 

“Ngiyabonga.” Waphenduka wabaleka. “Ubodlula 
kwami ngelinye ilanga uma usindile!” Wamtshela 
inombolo uDubazana angayizwanga. 

Kwakusheshwa laphaya. Kwangenwa ezindlini, 
kwatatshwa izingubo, ukudla, omabonwakude, imishini 
yokudlala izithombe, nokunye okuningi. NoDubazana 
esecwilise insabula yakhe egazini lenye insizwa eyayisilele 

84 

ungolala, watapa, waqiqinga naye. Yakhukhula iphinda 
emuva. 

“Ngimgwazile. Angazi noma ufile yini.” 

Yamvuthela ngamehlo ayeyigazi ithi, “Kade 
ungamdlokodli ngani inhliziyo umbone ukuthi ufe 
ngempela yini?” 

Sezifuna ukuphuma kuDubazana ekubona ukufa, 
wancenga ethi, “Ngicela ukukhuluma iqiniso mfowethu.” 

“Ufuna ukungibhedela! Iqiniso lani?’ 

“Uvele waphenduka lowa nkosikazi, wangibuka, wase 
engibuza ukuthi ngimbulalelani eyinzalabantu efike 
ingizale ibuye ibe yisithandwa sami. Uma ngimtshela 
ukuthi ngisempini, nginokubulawa uma ngimdedela, 
ungiphendule ngokuthi kulungile ngimfele ngoba nabo 
bayasifela uma besibeletha. Angehlulile bantabakababa 
lawo mazwi, ngamdedela nenxeba lelo elilodwa ebese 
ngimgwaze lona esiphangeni.” 

“Awuthi ngibone insabula yami ukuthi inalo yini igazi!” 

Wayinika uDubazana, yayibuka yalibona igazi. Yabuka 
abanye, yabuza yathi, “Nithi angimenze njani madoda, 
noma le nsabula ngiyiphelelisele enhliziyweni yakhe 
ngigwaze uJesu?” 

Zabukana izinsizwa. Yindoda eyayisiqinile, impunga, 
isigqigqi nje eyaphumela obala, yathi, “Myeke nsizwa ngoba 
uyambona nawe ukuthi usenobuntu. Akakakwejwayeli 
ukubulala. Enhliziyweni yakhe unoxolo; uma enoxolo 
unokuthula.” 

“Anginamsebenzi nakho lokho Ntshingwayo. Ngithe 
kuye akobulala uma ngithi akabulale.” 

“Ubuvele udlala ngaye Njayiphume uma uthi akobulala 
uma kuthanda wena sengathi yena akanangqondo 

85 

nanembeza.” Wanikina ikhanda okwakuthiwa 

nje ukuthi zonke lezi zigidi ngezigidi zabantu abayizizwe 
ngezizwe, nezinhlanga ngezinhlanga; nalabo othi wena 
ulwela inkululeko yabo bavundla eziswini zabesimame? 

Njengoba uthi ababulawe kalula nje, kuke kukufikele 

kodwa ukuthi bezwa izinseka nokuthi, njengoba nalowaya 
eshilo, basuke bengafa noma yinini uma bekhulelwe?” 

Wathula uNjayiphume ubuso bakhe bunyakama. 
Uthe ethatha wayethi kuDubazana, “Kulungile nhliziyo 
kaJesu. Ngelinye ilanga uyokuvakashela uSathane 
azokutshengisa ukuthi akusibo bonke abathi ‘Nkosi 
Nkosi’, kule nkolelo yakho.” 

Washingila nesibhamu nensabula yakhe, eshiya 
abalandeli bakhe bekhononda bethi, “Sengathi leli kholwa 
alizile ukuzogcwalisa, kepha lizochitha.” 

Ngalelo langa lashona abakwaDubazana bebhocobele, 
beshayekile nasemoyeni. Empilweni yabo babeqala 
ukuhlasela imizi yabantu, babaphange izimpahla 
zabo nokusho! Nanku umsakazo omkhulu uDubazana 
ayephoqeke ukuba awebe. Wawuhlezi lapha endlini 
bengenawo nagesi namabhetri okuwudlala. Kuphela 
wawuyisishayo sonembeza nobufakazi ngomuso 
obabuzobabhadlisa emajele. Kwakumthuthumelisa 
uDubazana ukuthi wayephoqekile ukuba akhiphe 
isidumbu ngoba nje kuhloswe ukuba abulawe unembeza. 

Okwakubamangazile lapha emjondolo ngesikhathi 
kuhlaselwa, ukubona omalokazana nabakhwenyana, 
amakhosikazi namadoda ayeseqinile impela, abanye babo 
benesizotha futhi, bephuma kodwa kula maxhokovana 
ayimijondolo. Ngoba naba nje nabanye abantu babehlezi, 
okusho ukuthi nabo babengazama. Ukuqhaqhazela 
kusengokwethuka kwenkonyane isisinga. 

86 

Impi yayibenze bazejwayeza namadoda namakhosikazi 
ambalwa ayentanganye nabo. Babewezwe nawo 
engundaza ebalisa ngokucekelana phansi kwabansundu 
bodwa belwa izimpi zokuzinqoba, ukuziphakula amandla, 
ukuzigwaza ngokwabo nokuzidlisa ubomi. 

Izinkinga zabajamela ngoLwesithathu, lapho kuthi 
hwalala nje, esanda kubuya emsebenzini uDubazana. 
Emnyango bezwa ngequpha elalingqongqoza sengathi 
lalizowugqobhoza umnyango. 

“Ubani lowo?” Wabuza uDubazana ethwala amehlo. 

“Yimina uNjayiphume. Vula!” 

Babukana nomkakhe, wavula, amehlo akhe ezithela 
kuye uNjayiphume ehamba nomhlambi wezingane, 
amantombazane, amabhobhodlana nezinsizwa. 

“Selufikile esasikhuluma ngalo lwekhempu. Aziphume 
izingane Dubazana!” Kwakusho yena uNjayiphume 
ebabuka oDubazana nomkakhe sengathi wayefunda 
okuthile ebusweni babo obabunokumangala. 

“Nkosi yami, besebancane kangaka!” Wazikhalela 
uMaZondi. 

Ngokumcasukela wambuka uNjayiphume wakhomba 
emhlambini wathi, “Zingakanani lezi?” Wabuza 
ezikhanyisa ngethoshi. 

Bazibuka oDubazana. Kwakukhona ngisho 
amantombazanyana ayeseminyakeni eyishumi. 

“Kodwa Nkosi yami …!” Wakhala uMaZondi. 

“Thula!” Wamsikaza ngempama uNjayiphume. 
Wathula. “Ziyahamba izingane noma nenqaba 
nazo nizuze umvuzo wenu?” Waphenduka wabheka 
emhlambini. “Sikhathele abantu esithi silwela inkululeko 
bebehonqa obudala. Sondelani bafana!” 

87 

Abafanyana ababili, beseminyakeni eyishumi, 
baphuma emnyameni bangena endlini. Bajama 
emnyango namathayi amabili. Bababuka abazali babo 
ababengoMaZondi noDubazana ngamehlo ayekhala igazi 
okwase kukade kwasa eliphuza, sebenequnga. Kubo 
ukushiswa komuntu kwase kwaba umdlalo. Ukukhala 
kwakhe eyobayoba evutha babekubiza ngomculo 
nomdanso. 

“Hhawu we ma wami! Ngiyesaba ma!” Wakhala 
wawuhlanya uMakhosazana ecasha ngeziketi zikanina. 
Indaba eyayihlasimulisa umzimba ngamakhempu lawo 
wayeseke wayizwa ixoxwa abangani esikoleni. 

“Kungasa sincengana nani! Animuzwa uyihlo ukuthi 
uthi asihambeni!” UNjayiphume welulekela kubo, 
wabacaphuna ngamahlonjana wabachilizela phandle. 

“Ngilamulele baba!” Wakhala emnyameni uMakhosazana 
ngesikhathi uholobha nabo umshungo uhamba. 

“Bayoganga ngabo Dubazana abantabami! Ngiyeke 
ngiyofa lapho befela khona!” Wakhala uMaZondi etibula, 
noDubazana ezabalaza embambile encenga. 

“Hlala phansi bandla sithandwa sami. Uma 
usuziphonsa ekufeni nje, awusaboni ngani ukuthi 
uma bengaqalanga ngokukugaxa ithayi, bazodlala 
badlale ngawe bese beyakubulala.” Wahlala embhedeni, 
wamgona, wamanga emesula nezinyembezi ngobuso. 

“Uyangilahla unembeza Dubazana. Awuvumi 
mntakwethu ukuba nginikele ngabantabami. Ngokuba 
uziyantunta nje ngincenga indawo yokuhlala sengingaze 
ngilahlekelwe amagugu ami wonke enginawo! Zolo lokhu 
kwaMlangeni bekufanele ngibekezelele ukukubuka 

88 

uqatshulwa ngoba ngincikiselwa ngomuzi. Maye babo!” 

Wayengezwa nakuzwa uMaZondi. Waqhubeka 
esikhihla ethi, “Nawe uziqhayisa ngami nje Dubazana 
ngoba uyazi ukuthi wangithola endaweni yakithi 
ngeshelwa, ngizizwa ngiziqhayisa ngomzimba wami 
wobuntombi. Ngikugane nje angiphoqwanga, kepha 
kwasukela othandweni. Inhliziyo yami ngayitshela, 
yakwamukela ukuthi umzimba wami nowakho owomuzi 
wethu. Namuhla kuyodlalwa ngomntanami egameni 
lenkululeko ukuze ngomuso ethukwe yibona kanye futhi 
abesilisa.” Wakhala wamthela ngezifudumele izinyembezi 
uDubazana. Wayesebhonga emswaneni. 

Izingane zaziholobhiswe njalo zayofakwa mjondolo 
thize owawuwuhhafudakazi owawutshekile, 
umakamelokazi amane. Wawubhekwe amabhungwana 
amathathu nomasihlalisane bawo, nezingane zabo 
ezinhlanu. Nabo bahlangana khona lapha emakhempini, 
nemilanjwana yazalwa ngenxa yawo. Umniniwo 
ngempela, nomndeni wakhe, inkosikazi namadodakazi 
amane babeqothwe bonke ngezinhlamvu ngenxa yokuthi 
babesolelwa ebumpimpini. Yindodakazi eyayibayalile 
ngokuvumela inkululeko yenhliziyo, iqome iphoyisa. 

Yikuwo–ke lo mjondolo lapho bahlaliswa 

khona phansi ababekhempile. Ababeqala ukufika 

batshelwa ngemithetho yendawo. Okokuqala nje, 
lapha enhlanganweni yenkululeko intombazane 

89 

yayingavunyelwe ukuba iqome umuntu wenye 
inhlangano noma iphoyisa. Yayingaqoma uma ijutshwe 
abaphathi ukuba iqome owenye inhlangano noma 
iphoyisa ukuze ibayengele ophathe, noma–ke uma 
kuhloswe ukuba iphoyisa lizuzwe ukuze lizwelane nabo. 
Inhloso yalokhu kwakuwukuba amaphoyisa ezwelane 
nabo, noma sekuliwa alamule isilamulakanjani, noma–ke 
athalalise uma kunabazomangalela inhlangano. 

Lapha ekhempini kwakungekho nazifundo 
ezazimayelana nezepolitiki, umnotho wezwe 
nokuphathwa kwalo. Kwakuba yintshumayelo 
ngemithetho, bese kuhutshwa amahubo ezomzabalazo. 
Kwakuthethwa namacala alabo ababebizwa ngezimpimpi, 
begwetshwa intambo bengekho. Kwanqunywa nokuba 
labo ababebonakala bengazimisele ukuxhasa umzabalazo 
babizelwe ezinkantolo. Kwakuphunywa kungenwa, 
kuhuqwa nomthunzi wezinkukhu. Sekuhutshwe kwaze 
kwabuhlungu imiphimbo, kwacishwa. Emnyameni 
izigilamkhuba zingasabonwa nokuthi zazingobani 
zazenzela. Iziqhwaga zazikhethela kwababefika bebizwa 
ngabasha. Kwathi kuqambe kukhanya zase zizilalele 

90 

engxenye. 

“Ubani lowo?” Kwakubuza uMaZondi ebuka umnyango 
ngamehlo ayezinyembezana. Izwi lowayekhala 
laphendula ngokuthi, “Yithina mama!” 

“Abantabami Nkosi yami!” Wagxuma esukuma 
eyobavulela. Phose waquleka ebona isimo ayeyiso 
umntanakhe. 

Ngendlela umoya kaDubazana owephuka ngayo, 
zamshisa wehluleka ukuzibamba. Zagelezisa okwezengane. 
Waphuma weduka nangengqondo. Kusemnyamana ekuseni 
ngoNhlangulana isigodi sasemjondolo wasibona sengathi 
sasivutha sonke. Ababengenamaphulamastofu naphalafini, 
nazindawo ezazenele ukuphekela base bebase phandle 
belungiselela ukuya emsebenzini. Kwakubomvu imililo, 
kushunqa. Akumfikelanga ukuthi naseningini lale mizi 
kwakubehlele okwakumehlele. Kanti–ke kwabanye kwase 
kwaba amahlalakhona, namahlaya asekhempini ngegciwane 
lengculaza esalala insila. Lalibaheqeza. Wabuyela endlini, 
wafica kukhala wonke umuntu. Yeka ukubalisa! 

“Ngicela amanzi mama ngigeze.” 

“Akangagezwa nina ukuze sithi uma sesimusa 
emaphoyiseni singasolwa.” Kwakusho uDubazana esaba 
ngisho ukuwaphimisa la mazwi. 

“Nike nilubhade phela emaphoyiseni nizobona 
kahle!” Kwakusho izwi ngemuva kwendlu. “Kade 
nitshelwa ukuthi lapha emjondolo eBusani akungeni 
veni namaphoyisa. Uma ningayinqamuli le milomo yenu 
emide, kukhona okuzonithulisa. Niklifilika nje angazi 
nokuthi nifelwe yiliphi izwe. Noma mhlawumbe yiyona 
ndlela eniyithela ngayo ngamashwa ikhempu?” Labuza 
lowo mbuzo lathula isikhathi. “Emaphoyiseni phela! 

91 

Nango nina, nanto ithayi!” Lasho ngesikade laphelela 
lapho ababe besazi noma umninilo wayesacuthile yini. 
Bakhala buthule. 

Siqhwaga leso futhi sakwabuthongo esayilamula 
entambama endala. Bonke balala obokufa. 

Baphaphama lapho kuthi zibaba phandle. Babevuswa 
ukuhhomuzela nokubabaza kwabantu, abesimame bekhala 
ngo ‘Maye!” Bakhanyisa ikhandlela qede baphumela 
phandle. 

“Yini, kwenzenjani ntombi?” Behlahle amehlo 
oDubazana bebona ezweni kushunqa izintuli, uMaZondi 
wayebuza komunye wesimame owayengabonakali nakahle 
emnyameni. 

“Emhlabeni mntanomuntu!” Yena lowo owayebukeka 
eseyinkosikazi esencane wayebabaza ngokwesaba. 
“Nivela kuliphi nina eningayizwanga intsha nabaphathi 
bayo bedlula lapha manje beshudula, behuba?” 

“Besisazunywe yisithongo ntombi. Phela izolo 
asilalanga silindele izingane ebeziye ekhempini.” 

92 

“Kanti–ke nkosikazi ningabobuvumela ubuthongo 
kule ndawo enje. Ngelinye ilanga niyofa nilele. Bedlule 
manje beqhuba ibhungwana abangene nalo laphaya 
kwaBiyase. Bafike khona bathatha indodakazi yakhona 
baya nayo esigcawini, empelandaba ngaphansi 
kwesihlahla. Ngishiye besaquliswa amacala okuthi 
umfana uwumngane wephoyisa nokuthi intombazane 
iqome lona. Kuthiwa babhadanywe kahle esiphingo bemi 
nalo, kuxoxwa, kuhlekwa, kuhleshulelwana nangenhlanzi 
ethosiwe.” 

“Maye babo! Maye we ma! Ngilamulele we 
ma! Ngasha! Ngicishe ma!” Kwakumpongoloza 
izwi lentombazane ibaleka iza ngakubo. Memfu, 
kwaqhamuka ubulangulangu bamalangabi elanguka 
elithika, umuntu evutha umzimba wonke nethayi 
entanyeni. Kuyisimangaliso ukuthi leya ntombazane 
yayisabona kanjani ekhaya kulokho kulanguka. Yaqonda 
ngasenkosikazini eyayishaye izingubo ezimnyama 
ihamba izihola, ikhathele, ithwele isikhwama 
esasinamaphakeshana empushana, ushukelana, isinkwa 
nosu lokuba kulalwe kukhohliswe umlomo. Yayikhathele 
ngakhona. Yayiqale nini, kuse nini iwasha, i–ayina, 
ipheka esilungwini? Ibona ilangabi liyiqonda, yethuka 
yalidedela, yabuza ledlula ithi, “Kodwa Nkosi yami 
owakuphi lo mntanabantu owenziwa nje? Yeka unina!” 
Isabambe amakhala izwa ukunuka kwenyama yomuntu, 
yababaza futhi isithi, “Wenzani lo muntu! Nangu engena 
endlini yabantabami nomlilo!” 

“UThenjiwe MaSangweni!” Kwakumemeza izwi lenye 
inkosikazi emnyameni. 

“UThenjiwe wakwabani Nkulunkulu wami?” 

93 

“Hhawu, MaSangweni mntanomuntu! UThenjiwe 
wakwakho!” 

“Ukuphi kodwa Nkulunkulu? Uthuleleni weNdodana 
yaseZulwini umntanami esha kanje?” Wakhubeka wavuka, 
wavuka wakhubeka. “Kodwa Biyase wathula lapho 
ukhona, awabe usangelekelela olakeni lwasemhlabeni 
owangishiya kuwo ngingenamuzi? Maye babo!” Washo 
eziphonsa phakathi emalangabini, elandelwa yisivalo 
kwasona esase sivutha. “Maye! Maye Nkosi yami! 
Ngelekeleleni bakithi! Nakhu ngifa nomntanami! Saze 
safa kabuhlungu mntanami! Kazi yithina yini esasiqale 
ubandlululo?” 

Umlilo owawungene nendodakazi wawufike wathungela 
impahla endlini. Ungena nje unina sewala ukhasha. 
Wamnompela sasondelangange. Intuthu imfusa, 
imxhopha, akabange esawubona umnyango ayengene 
ngawo. Ngokushesha okumangalisayo wamshwabadela. 
Okufike kudabukise du, ukuthi emshungwini 
wentsha eyayisecaleni likaThenjiwe, kwakukhona 
nabafowabo okwathi noma sekukhishwa isigwebo sakhe 
ababengenakusiphikisa, kwathiwa sasikhishwe ngo– 
elethu. Ungqongqa nje umuzi wakwabo kwakusahlekwa 
ibhungu elalibizwa ngempimpi liza lilanguka nalo 
nelalo ilangabi lizowela bude buduze noDubazana. Bathi 
bethuka, beqambe belishiya yayiwohlokela phezu konina 
indlu. Kwangqongqa ndawo zonke, kwagcina sekushunqa 
kunuka usi lwabantu. Nkathi leyo, indoda thize 
eyayibone isikhwama sikaMaSangweni yayisisicoshile 

94 

yayosithukusa ekhaya. Wayezothi esashunqa, 
okwakuphakathi bese ikugxabhisela abantwana. 

“Uma kwenzeka ngishiswa MaZondi, ngicela ungisize 
ngokuba nginele ngivuthe nje, ungigwaze ungiqedele 
ngingakabuzwa kakhulu ubuhlungu.” 

“Kahle Dubazana ukukhuluma kanje.” Waphihlika 
wakhala uMaZondi. “Wazi ngani noma mhlawumbe 
namuhla elami lamanqamu? Nakimi uma kwenzekani, 
ngicela ungibhekele abantabami Dubazana.” 

Indlu yakakwa, kwagcwala nasemnyango. Bangena 
abanye indlu yonke yanuka intuthu nenyama eyosiwe. 
Babuka oDubazana ngamehlo ayelokoza umlilo kusengathi 
ayezithwebulile izithombe zababeshisiwe. Bengakakhulumi 
nje, baliphephetha ikhandlela, balicisha. 

“Yingoba ndoda uzibona ubungcono yini kunabanye 
abazali njengoba ezakho izingane uzifuye endlini, 
zithe bunyalala embhedeni ngesikhathi ezabanye

UMakhosazana wayenele wakhubeka emgwaqweni, 
wawa, wayibuka sengathi wayephupha imoto yamaphoyisa 
okuphepha iphonseka ngapha nangapha kwakhe imvika. 
Wayevuke wazibeletha ephonseka emnyameni. Ngeshwa 
futhi wakhutshwa ngakuzwa kusanqwaba esikhotheni. 
Wawa wabhabhalala phezu kwakho. Kwakuyisidumbu 
sendwandlela yendoda eyayisashisa, isanda kukhuthuzwa 
yabulawa iphuma emsebenzini. Wethuka esethe, “Maye!” 
Wazikhuza. Selimbhece wabomvu igazi, wavuka wathi

kube nokuzithela emhhumeni wezinye izingonyama. 
Engemuva ngasekhishini, wathi qala, qala, wabona 
umgqomo wezibi. Waphakamisa isivalo washo phakathi, 
wayesezivalela. Yekanini ukunuka kwenkucunkucu 
eyayilapho idabula isifuba! Ukuze aphile, wayibekezelela. 
Empeleni kwayena wayezizwa eyize lezibi zezwe, 
umfanele nalo mgqomo. 

Walizwa igazi lomufi lomela ebusweni, wacabanga

9 
ekuseni, ngezithuba zehora

nabakhwenyane, nabazukulu. Ngisho kambe lapho kulalwa

108 

ukuba zizilolongele impumelelo empilweni? 

“Kulesi simo sombusazwe, lapho izingane 
seziphendulwe izikhali, ungasifundisa kanjani isikhali

Ngiyabuza, ngithi kulesi sikhathi lapho kubuthwa khona 
intsha kuthiwa isiwa emakhempini, ifike ixhashazwe, 
inukubezwa, ikhulelwe ekhulelwayo, kugiye amagciwane 
ezifo kwezinye, nilindeleni? Izingane zinukubeziwe 
emakhempini, emahositela, emiqashweni, ezindaweni 
ezixhixhayo ezihlala kuzo, nasemizini egcwele ichichima. 
Lezi zingane ziphelelwe amathemba ngempilo. 
Ezindlebeni zazo nokulungileyo ezikufundiswayo 
sekungena ngakule ndlebe, kuphume ngakuleya.” 

“Ezinye izingane esizifundisayo sezike zakhipha 
imiphefumulo. Ezinye zazo ziyikhiphe ngolunya 
oluhlasimulisa umzimba, zashisa abantu, kambe 
izidalwa eziyimifanekiso kaNkulunkulu. Lezo zingane 
uthi ufundisa zibe zikubuka ngamehlo akhala igazi 
nalokoza imililo. Ezinye zazo zikwenza lokhu zibhenyiswe 
izidakamizwa. Nithi asenzenjani?” 

“Senzenjani uma lezi zingane zingaphumeleli qede 
zingqokloze othisha ngezibhamu, njengoba kwenzeka 
kulesi sikole ngokuqala konyaka, nakwezinye 
eziningi?” Wazikhumula futhi izibuko, wacikica 

109 

amehlo, wayesezibuyisela eqhubeka. “Ngokubona 
ukuthi nokufundisa kothisha kulesi sikole ukudulela 
nje, bese ngicele abezenhlalakahle ukuba kebazoxoxa 
nalezi zingane ezididekile. Umbiko wabo osungidida 
kakhulu othi kwabona kubadidile ukudideka kwezikole 
zonke. Sekuyangicacela ukuthi kwamina ngididekile, 
nothisha bami kanye nabo abezenhlalakahle badideke 
ngokufanayo nezingane njengoba nabo bekhulele kulesi 
simo sempilo.” 

Laba bantu bayahlupheka, 

Kwasho inyoni ihlezi phezu kwejele. 

“Ukuze ngingaboshwa, kufanele ngiwahlanekezele la 
mazwi, ngithi: 

‘Laba bantu bayabusa, 

110 

Kwasho upholi ehlezi endlini yesicebi’.” 

“Uma kunje, sikuphi bakithi?” 

Inkulumo yayibathintile abazali. Kwake kwathuleka 
kwathi nya, bebodwa ababesula izinyembezi emehlweni, 
abanye bewacikica, abanye benamahloni, begobodisile 
ngoba unembeza ubakhumbuza ukuthi babelindele 
amasheke ngoDonda. 

Wabuka iwashi futhi uDonda, akaba nasinqe. 
Wasukuma, wazulazula futhi ehholo sengathi igazi lakhe 
lalimtshela okuthile. 

“Hhayi,” kwakusho yena ebamba isisu, “uma 
ngicabanga indaba yokuboshwa, ngisuke ngizwe 
ngixhuxhunyelwa yisisu. Ngisathi tshobe endlini 
encane. Uma bekhona abangifunayo, nibacele balinde, 
bangangiphazamisi.” Lwaphe, uThishomkhulu, akabange 
esaphuma nangomnyango. Weqa ngefasitela kwaqhewuka 
imiqhewu yebhuleza ebambe isisu eyongena endlini 
yothisha yangasese. Wazivalela eshiya abanye abazali 
sibahlekisa isenzo sesisu. 

Lukhona uhuntshu lwemoto emnyama olwaluthe 
memfu, lwabuye lwanyamalala. Dukuduku 
kwakubonakale amadoda amabili, isikhasakhasana 
nongqwazi, eshaye izigqoko ezimnyama, amasudi 
nezicathulo ezifana nawo amasudi, nezibuko zelanga. 
Ayekade ecathama ngezindonga, kepha anele aqhamukela 
ngasehholo, agqawuzela. Angena ehholo, abingelela, acela 
ukubonana noThishomkhulu uDonda. 

“Nkosi yami, uphethwe yisisu. Usaphuthume endlini 
yangasese,” kusho inkosikazi eyayihlezi emabhentshini 
aphambili, impofu, iziphihlile, ishaye nezibuko 
zakwanokusho. 

111 

“Ungene nini khona?” Kubuza ungqwazi 
olwalungasethulile isigqoko yize selusendlini. 

Isikhasakhasana sathi, “O, ngoba usebona thina, 
usekhishwa yisusu! Iphi yona leyo ndlu encane angene 
kuyona?” 

Bakhonjiswa. Ungqwazi lwagqawuzela isikhasakhasana 
sikhasazela phambili. Bema ngakuyo indlu eyayikhonjiwe, 
yaze yaphela imizuzu emihlanu uDonda engaphumi. 
Yenyuka yayishumi, yaba amashumi amabili. Basondela, 
bangqongqoza. Phinde ukuvula uDonda. Umnyango 
bawukhahlela salahleka laphaya isivalo abangena naso. 
Sengathi babehlangane nemamba, baphuma bendiza, 
bayizungeza indlu encane, qede babuyela phakathi kuyo 
baqalaza naphezu kwesigubhu samanzi. Basishaya naso, 
kepha phinde uDonda ukuphuma kuso. Babuya bevutha 
ehholo, bethi, “Khulumani nina! Uphi uDonda? Asimtholi!” 

Ihholo lonke lamkhomba endlini yangasese. 

“Nx, le nja!” Lwathula ungqwazi lufunda oqwembeni. 
“Iphethe ifaka isizwe umoya omubi! Abantu bahlupheka 
uma kwenzenjani?” 

“Amazwi ale nkondlo uwabhaliswe ukuchwensa ngoba 
uyazi ukuthi yavalwa.” Isikhasakhasana sadumela 
ibhulashi lokusula, singafinyeleli naphezulu. Sagxuma 
siwesula la mazwi, sishiya okwakuthiwe akapholi 
esawakhomba sithi, “Nanti iqiniso!” 

Lahlokoma lonke ihholo lithi, “Nizosisiza–ke nikhokhe 
umnyango wesikole sethu eniwubulele!” 

“Asinamsebenzi nalokho! Singabomthetho thina! 
Ibalekile le nja!” baphuma ngamajubane, balanda abanye 
ababesemotweni, wathungathwa isikole sonke uDonda 
waze wabhekwa ngisho emabhokisini oshoki. Phinde! 
Yaphuma imoto kwakliwula amathayi iyombheka kwakhe, 

112 


ekhweni lakhe, nasezihlotsheni. Phinde! 

Umzuzwana nomzuzu, izimoto ezazinikezelana 
ngoDonda zazimsondeza ekuweleni umngcele wezwe 
ayezofika kulo angene endizeni eyayizomedlulisela 
ezizweni. 

*** 

“Izolo bengisemjondolo, egatsheni elisha elisanda

Bengithokozile ngibona abantu begcwele indlu

waphakade.” 

“Bekungaleso sikhathi–ke lapho ngizwe indlu

ukukholwa okuyikho esigqilini esilanjisiweyo, sibuka 
isicebi sidla size sifinye ngendololwane, izinsalela

na embusweni wezulu?” Umfundisi uMbambo 
wayeyilanda le ndaba emi epulpiti lasesontweni khona 
eMlazi. Kwakugcwele, kukhona ngisho umqangabhodwe 
womfundisi omhlophe waseDashi umnumzane Fanie 

113 


Pienaar. 

“Esimweni esinje, isizwe ngizosishumayeza kanjani

“Ngelulekeni bakithi, ngokuthi ngizobashumayeza

114 

abakhulelwe nabakhulelisile ebandleni, ngithi

Esontweni kwathula cwaka umoya owawunomunyu. 
Umfundisi Pienaar, ehlezi phansi, emise izindlebe

Inkemane isizenzela kuthiwa abantu baqala ukudlana

“Mina ngiwuNdabazabantu efemini. Mihla namalanga

emsebenzini. Imizi abanayo. Izingane namakhosikazi abo

“Mfundisi!” Washo nomfundisi uFanie Pienaar 

116 

esukuma eyoma epulpiti, eduze kukaMbambo. “Isikhathi

Bengingazi ukuthi kanti isizwe siphekwe ngogalaza. 
Sengizobuyela ebandleni labamhlophe edolobheni 
nombuzo othi, kambe umbhalo wawuthini ngokuthi

Mhla inkungu yokungazi yasanguluka emakhanda, boswela

“Esengikubonga kakhulu kini ndlu emnyama,

Qiniselani kokuhle bakithi ngokuba ngemuva kwalo

kwalokho izikhuthali ezobe sezikhululekile emaketangeni 
ziyothokomala emafutheni.” 

117 

Isonto laphuma, ibandla lema phandle layizixukwana

nami!”

ngiboshelwa ukuphila. Kwanga lokho kuphila kunga 
okuphakade!” Washo engena emotweni bemkaka. 

Ibandla lisamangele, yasuka izithonto imoto, yalishiya 
nezintuli noMfundisi uPienaar eliqoqa, lihlabelela 
limthandazela uMbambo. 

Bekhala abanye, abanye behluleka nokukhuluma, 
zizehlela, balifulathela isonto. Abanye banyathela 
kancane beya ezimotweni zabo ababezimise imvamisa 
emthunzini wezihlahla. Nomnumzane Thabizolo 
Thabekhulu, uswazi lwensizwa eyayinethambo, ikhanya, 
impandla iqala ukwenyuka ngamanhlonhlo, imashumi 
mane eminyaka, wawunyathela ngokuwuhlonipha 
umhlaba esesudini eyayisibhakabhaka. Ngesinye 
isandla wayephethe iBhayibheli, ngesinye ebambe 
umkakhe uMaDlamini, uZamaSwazi owayesemashumini 
amathathu eminyaka ayeva ngesikhombisa, ewugamfu 
lwakwabo olwalukhanya, lushaye isiketi nebhantshi 
okwakufana nokomyeni. Babeqonde ocingweni lwemoto 

118 


yabo eyayiwuhlobo lweToyota Cressida eyayifana 
nezingubo zabo. UThabekhulu wayethi umvulela isivalo 
umkakhe lapho ezithela enkosikazini nendoda ababehlezi

Wathula uThabekhulu wayibuka le nsizwa nomndeni

“Usibona nje mntakababa sesihlupheke kangangokuba

enkolo engcwele. Mhlawumbe singake sihlangane nomuntu 
onobuntu, sithi noma simzekela le nsumansumane yethu 
abone ukuthi uthathani uhlanganisa nani.” 

Wayilanda ukusuka nokuhlala indaba 
yezigigaba ezazibehlele besemjondolo. Balapha 
nje, babeqe khona entathakusa, bephelele 
Ababenakho kwakungokwakusemzimbeni kuphela, 
nomashayandawonye usebhokile. Bacela noma ucezu

“Konje Nkosi yami sizonishiya kubani noMfundisi

10 


imoto yakwaThabekhulu yehla yenyuka nemithambeka 
nemimango yaseMlazi isuka esontweni ibabele emzini 
wabo owawusemaphethelweni esigceme sakwa–E, 
khona eMlazi. Wawungomunye weyayilengele phezu 
kwawo umfula uMlazi. Yayize yapatalala imoto ngemuva 
kuminyene uDubazana nomndeni wakhe. Kubo 
wayengekho owayekhulumisa omunye, kuyilowo eqhatha 
umunyu womzwangedwa. Kumbe abanye babelalele lo 
mculo owawumnandi, upholile, usholo phansi kule moto 
eyayingeyabahlanzekile, kwayona ihlanzekile, inuka 
amakha amnandi. Imoto yaye yema phambi kwamasango 
omuzi wakwanokusho owawubiyelwe ngofenisi oluhlaza, 
wona upendwe ngokwakuliphuzi, ufulelwe ngamathayela 
ayebomvu. Wawusanda kunwetshwa. 

UThabekhulu wehla wavula isango elikhulu negalaji. 
Wabuyela emotweni, wayifaka egalaji. Behla bonke, 
walivala igalaji, babahola. UMaDlamini wavula 
umnyango abangena ngawo bazithela endlini yokudlela 
eyayinetafulakazi elide lezimali ezishisiwe. Izihlalo 
ezazihlotshiswe ngezimbali, zaziyisishiyagalombili, 
nekhabethe lezitsha. Odongeni kwakulenga iwashi 
elalimanyazela sagolide. 

Bathithiza abakwaDubazana, sebesaba nokunyathela. 
Imizi enje babeyejwayele kwabamhlophe kuphela. 
Balandela abaninimuzi ababaholela endlini yokuphumula. 

“Hlalani bantu bakithi, nazi izihlalo,” kusho 
uThabekhulu emi kuyo leyo ndlu ababethe uma bengena 
kuyo izinyawo zacwila kunomfonomfo wokhaphethe. 

120 

Wayebakhombisa izihlalo zesikhumba esiphambili 
esasinsundu. Bahlala kuzo bacwila, nemiphefumulo 
bayizwa iphumula. Wahlala naye kwesinye esasilingene 
abantu ababili ngesikhathi umkakhe eshayela phezulu 
edlulela kwamanye amakamelo. 

“Sibonga umusa wakho Thabekhulu.” Wayesho 
uDubazana kungamkhululi neze ukuhlala kulo 
muzi ayewubona ungamfanele. Wayezizwa exhutha, 
nakhu namanzi wayesekade awagcina. UThabekhulu 
wabavulela umsakazo omkhulu, igumbagumba nayo

Nakalokhu, lapha endlini, kwabakwaDubazana, 
akekho owayekhulumisa omunye. Babesele bodwa nje 
babencishana amehlo, bajeqeza. Abanye babezibukela 
usilingi yakwaThabekhulu owawuyipulangwe 
elalipendwe ngevanishi lahlotshiswa ngongoti bakhona. 
Kwakunjalo phezulu endlini yokuphumula nakweyokudlela. 
Amalambu ogesi ayelenga phezulu ayeyizihlekehleke 
ezazinogesi ababefana namakhandlela. Kwakukhona 
nabanye ababenamathele ezindongeni ezaziluhlaza 
ngombala. Kuzo lezi zindonga kwakunepulangwe 
elihle elalizizungezile, kulo kulenga izithombe 
okwakungezomshado kaThabekhulu nomkakhe. Ezinye 
kwakungezendodana nendodakazi yabo oThabethule 
noThabisile, ezinye kungezomhlobiso nje. Afike wagxilisa 
amehlo kuso kakhulu uMaZondi kwakungesabo 
abaninimuzi behlezi esihlalweni sinye, bebambisene 
ngesitsha sokudla, bedlela kuso ndawonye ukudla 
ababekucozululelana. Umsakazo lona owawububulela 
phansi wawungowohlobo lwe–Hi–fi ephambili, usekhabetheni 

121 

lembuya elalizibukobuko, ligcwele udonga. 

“Enhlekeleleni eyehlele abantwana ongixoxele ngayo 
Dubazana, angazi noma kungangenwa yini emanzini 
kungakayiwa kwabomthetho nodokotela?” 

“Mntakababa,” kwakusho uDubazana ephunga 
impukane yokuqala ayeyibona ngaye lapha endlini, 
“sengingabe ngibezwisa ubuhlungu kwabona abantwana 
uma ngizobedlulisa benjengoba benje. Okwesibili, 
kulokhu kudideka abadideke khona, sekungaba 
ukubaxhopha umoya uma ngibasa emthethweni lapho 
bezobuzwa lokhu nalokhu, nokuthi pho sithi abenzenjani 
uma sesizomangala ngemuva kwesikhathi eside kangaka. 
Uma kungase kutholakale amanzi mfo wakithi, 
sengingazibongela, ngibabongele nabo.” 

Ngemuva kokubonisana kwaqhamuka uMaDlamini, 
wacela ukuba uMaZondi ayongena endlini yokugezela. 
Ephihlika izinyembezi uMaZondi wasukuma wamlandela. 
Bakhombisana indlu yokugezela. Wangena uMaZondi 
esetshengisiwe nezingubo ayezebolekwa, ezoshintsha 
ngazo. Wazivalela, wema wayibuka le ndlu eyayinobhavu 
wakwanokusho, nezitsha zokugeza izandla nezokuzikhulula. 
Kwakukhona neshawa, nezibuko odongeni, nekhabethe 
elalinezimfanelo zokugeza. Kwakuhlanzeke kangangokuba 
umuntu wayengalinga nokudlela kuyo ngaphandle 
kokunyakama kwenhliziyo. Wakhumula, wangena 
ebhavini, wageza. Wazibhucungisisa, waphuma, wazesula. 
Ukukhululeka komzimba akakuzwanga. Wazizwa exhutha. 
Isithombe sokwakumehlele sasibhadekeke engqondweni. 
Wayethukuthele. 

Waziqhola, waxubha, waphuma izinyembezi ezithwele 

122 

ngezinkophe, waphindela endlini yokuphumula. 
Kwalandela uDubazana, wageza naye, waphuma 
eseshaye ezikaThabekhulu, wabuyela kusofa. Kwangena 
uMakhosazana, waphuma nentukuthelo yakhe eshaye 
ezikaThabisile. Kwagcina uNkosana owaphuma elabhuzela 
ngezikaThabethule ezazizinde kunaye. 

“Impela Dubazana ngizizwa nginidabukela,” kusho

“Usizi lokuntula izindlu lolu ngolukhungethe izindimbane

“Kunjalo impela Thabekhulu.” Wamvumela uDubazana

usehlupheke lapha emhlabeni ehamba ekhosela waze 
wadakwa usizi. Ekuqasheni lapha iphuma kwamsokoci 
ingene kwamsokoci.” 

“Iqiniso elimsulwa lelo Dubazana. Imvamisa yabantu 
abaqashisayo nayo ngesuke ivele izihluphekele. Manje 
umuntu unele akubone unotho uyisiqashi, acabange 
ukuthi usuzenza ngcono emzini wakhe. Kuqala lapho–ke 
ukuchukuluzana. Ngikwazi kahle lokho Dubazana. Nathi 
silapha nje, saqala khona. Uke uphume kweminye imizi 
lapha nezimpahla zakho zingasaphelele. Khona uma 
umkakho kuthiwa uyabukeka nje, O!” Washaya izandla 
wazichitha, wabheka le, “isuke isiyenzekile indaba. Kanti 
kwawena futhi ndoda uma uke wangobukekayo, ufunwa 

123 

ngamnyama.” 

“Bangenzani phela okunye Dubazana ngaphandle 
kokuba bakukhuthuze imali? Emalokishini lapha 
kuhlushekiwe.” 

UMaDlamini wakhothama eceleni komyeni wakhe, 
wacela ukuba bangene endlini yokudlela. Nempela 
uThabekhulu wabacela, kwangenwa. Babingelelwa yitafula 
elase lidekiwe, amakhala ashaywa yiphunga lezibiliboco. 
OThabekhulu nomkakhe badonsa izihlalo ngasechopheni 
letafula, bahlala bancikana ngesikhathi abakwaDubazana 
besathithiza, benhlakanhlaka ezingqondweni. Bahlala 
nabo, indodakazi eceleni kukanina, nendodana ngakuyise. 
Wathandaza uThabekhulu, kwabhekwana nokudla. 

Abanye bakwaDubazana besakubuka ukudla, abanye 
besakukhophozelela, abakwaThabekhulu baxoxela phansi 
njengentombi nensizwa. Balekelelana lapha ezitsheni, 
omunye ephakela omunye. Badla, babuye bancozululelane 
nenyama, bafunzane. Babekwenza lokhu bebeba ngeso 
abakwaDubazana. Ngakulolo hlangothi inkosikazi yayiphakele 
izingane zayo nendoda qede wadla uNkosana akazithela 
ngabandayo. Laba abanye bathi choko choko, bekuhlafuna 
sengathi kwakunobomi, bakugwinya sengathi babephethwe 
uzagiga. Basheshe bakuyeka, bakudla ngamehlo. 

“Siyabonga Thabekhulu,” kusho uDubazana sekuqediwe, 
“lokhu kungibutha ongibutha khona mntwanawabantu, 
singazani nakwazana, sengiyokubongelwa oPhezu kwakho 
konke.” 

“O, hhe, mntakababa, kuthiwa ukusiza umuntu 
ukuzibekela.” 

124 

Baphuma endlini yokudlela babuyela kweyokuphumula 
lapho abakwaDubazana bashiywa khona, base 
belekelelana abakwaThabekhulu beqoqisana izitsha, 
belekelelana ekhishini, omunye ezigeza, omunye ezesula, 
belu bengalibele ukubukana nokwangana. Sebeqedile, 
babuyela koDubazana. 

“Ngiyezwa Thabekhulu.” 

“Sesithe–ke uma sikhuluma noyiwele nami, safinyelela 
ekutheni kesinikhoselise amakhanda lapha ekhaya 
okwesikhashana nisazifunela–ke nani engxenye.” 

“Thabekhulu! Nomashengela kaMfuzana owafuza 
imifula! Siwela! Nina enehla ngesilulu!” Wasukuma 
ehlala uDubazana, ethopha uMpanza. 

Kwasukunywa bakhonjiswa ikamelo. Kule ndlu 
eyayisanda kunwetshwa lona lalishaya umoya, lingakabi 
nampahla. Lalidle nje kuphela ngokuhlanzeka, lisanuka 
nopende, lisho ngamakhethini amahle. 

“Nangombhede ningakhathazeki. Okwamanje sizoke 
siniboleke wona owezingane.” 

“Kodwa Thabekhulu uzikhathazelani ngombhede ngoba 
thina sifanelwe yikhona nje ukubhuquza phansi? Ungaze 
usho–ke lapha endlini kukhona nokhaphethe!” 

Wanikina ikhanda uMpanza wathi, “Dubazana, akekho 
umuntu ofanelwe yimpilo yezinga eliphansi. Wena–ke 
nokusho awuzenzanga. Wenziwa yisimo sempilo.” 

NoMaZondi esebabonge ngokubathela ngezinyembezi, 
abesimame babuyela endlini yokuphumula. Abesilisa 

125 


babambisana ngombhede newadilobhu bekuthuthela 
ekamelweni elisha lakwanokusho okwase kuyilona 

yabakwaDubazana ngemuva kokuqhwagwa isithunzi 
sobusha nesomshado. 

Kwakukade kuduma okuhambayo naphakathi 
kobusuku, kepha hhayi njengasentathakusa. Isitimela 
sezwakala sikhalisa okwengane, insimbi edla ezinye igida 
ingidane ngakoZwelethu, koMnyandu naseLindokuhle. 
Amabhasi abubula, amatekisi abaphaphamisa abasebenzi 
ngamahuthi. Ngokugamanxa kwehora lesithathu

kungelokubavusa abaninimuzi. Nempela bavuka, ukukhala 
kwamabhodwe nezindishi kwezwakala. OThabekhulu 
nomkakhe babelekelelana. Waliphunga eliphephetha itiye 
uThabekhulu isaduma imoto eyifudumeza. Wangena kuyo, 
zaya, kuba yilapho umkakhe ebuyela embhedeni futhi. 

Ukuvuka kwabakwaThabekhulu kwakubaphaphamisile 
nabakwaDubazana. Indoda nenkosikazi babephaphame 
qede bahlahla amehlo. Imiqondo yabo yayilahlekile. 
Ukuzwa izigi zabakwaThabekhulu kwakubethusile, 
kube sengathi babezwe lezo zezinswelaboya. Kwakhona 
ukuphaphama amehlo bewaqhunsulele isibani sikagesi 
ababezumeke bengasicishile kwabadida. UDubazana 
wayegcine emajalidini ukulala emzini onogesi. UMaZondi 
wayengakaze. 

Ukudideka okwakudla umunyu phakathi kwabo 
kwakubalalise ngokwahlukana. Namuhla uDubazana 
wayelale phansi kukhaphethe. Ngale kombhede, 
phansi, kwakunguNkosana. Embhedeni kwakulele 
uMaZondi nendodakazi. Khona manjalo, waphihlika 
wakhala uMaZondi. UDubazana wamncisha amehlo, 

126 

akaze amesula nazinyembezi lezo. Waphenduka khona 
phansi, walala wamfulathela. Kwakungamkhanyeli 
ukuthi lo mphefumulo ayewufulathela wawumdinga 
kangakanani, nokuthi lezi zinyembezi ezaziyimifula ebilayo 
zazidinga ukuphoziswa nokwesulwa nguye. Kwakulalwe 
engakhulumisani nomkakhe; kwakusa nje ingqondo 
yakhe yayisajiyelwe. Okwakukukhulu kunakho konke 
enhliziyweni kwakuwukuzibona ephoxekile njengendoda. 
Iso lengqondo lalibhajwe emfanekisweni wokubanjwa 
komkakhe esikhundleni sokuyiqhamukela inkinga 
ngokuyibuka ngeso elinzulu labansundu. Lelo lokwazi 
ukuthi inkosikazi iwumuzi, hhayi womyeni wayo nje 
kuphela, kepha wamadlozi aleso sibongo, nesizwe jikelele. 

“Mayelana nani MaZondi?” 

Wambuka umkakhe wamthela ngezinyembezi. 
Wathi, “Yise, uyazi ukuthi ngikuthanda kangakanani. 
Engikucela kuwe–ke mntakwethu, ukuthi ngezikhathi 
zobuhlungu obungaka emoyeni nasemzimbeni wami, 
ungaqhelelani nami, kepha usondele eduze. Uma uqhela, 
njengoba wenzile nje, umoya wami ngiwuzwa ugodola, 
ungembethe. Ngicela uwembese.” Mihli, wamthela 
ngesiphihli sezinyembezi ebalisa ethi, “Angazi noma 
ukuphila kusangifanele yini? Umoya ushayekile; 
umzimba udungekile.” 

Esadidekile, edangele, edikibele uDubazana, wavuka 
wahlala ebuthe izabutha. Wayezama ukukhuluma, kepha 
izwi lala libindwe yizinyembezi. 

“Ngibuzile yise kaMakhosazana kuwe baba 
njengenhloko yekhaya, ukuthi mina mkakho 
nabantabakho, njengoba sesinjena nje, usikhipha kanjani 
kulolu bishi?” 

Balushuka udaba. Okokuqala nje babengenayo 

127 


nemali yokuya emaphoyiseni nakodokotela lapho. 
Noma–ke kuthiwa imali babenayo, yeka lobo buhlungu

ezazizowanaphaza emaphephandabeni amagama abo. 
Uma babezodalula amagama ezinye izinswelaboya 
babenokubulawa, kushiswe nomuzi wakwaMpanza. 
Njengoba vele kwase kubehlele, bakubona kungcono khona 
ukuba kebazame ukufela ngaphakathi nalobu buhlungu. 

Isikhathi sokuvuka kwezingane okwakufanele ziye

“Nokuveza ubuso lobo Dubazana angiboni ukuthi kuzosiza

Kulesi sigigaba esibehlele abantabethu, okwanamuhla 
abakabi nayo ingqondo edingeka esikoleni.” 

Ngaleyo ndlela bahlala bonke abakwaDubazana

Wathi ukuba angene, wakhala ngoMaZondi. 

“MaZondi! Ngisize ntombi!” 

UMaZondi owayengasazi lutho emhlabeni wethuka

128 

ngakhona. Wamethula umthwalo ayewuthwele. Kwaba

“Yinina enijabulayo bakithi. Ukuzama akufani nokuhlala.”

Waqeda, wabonga kuMaZondi, wayesefudumeza ukudla

Wanikela ehositela labesilisa elalingakwaMnyandu

nabazongeboleka imali ezalayo.” 

129 

UDubazana wageza, waphuma ngazo izingubo 
zikaThabekhulu washaya unobhanqa. Wayenyathela

“Ngiyaxolisa impela mfowethu. Bengingazi ukuthi 
kanti ubuya ngalesi sikhathi emsebenzini.” 

“Ngiphuma emini nje, ngiyavuka ekuseni.” Wakhumula 
ijakethe yakhe wayijika kusofa, wayesekhipha iduku

“Isizungu sesikubulele,” washo ehlala phansi. “Awuvuli 
ngani umsakazo lona uzilibazise ngawo?” 

“Ngesabile Thabekhulu.” 

Wamamatheka uThabekhulu, wathi, “Kanti 
uma ulapha ekhaya ubokhululeka MaZondi, mina 
ungithathise okomfowenu enizalana naye, nomkami 
umthathise okukadadewenu. Nathi, nilapha nje 
sinithathisa okwezingane zakwethu.” 

Ngomoya owawuphansi uMaZondi wathi, “Ngiyabonga 
mfowethu.” 

130 

Wambuka uThabekhulu, wabufica ubuso bakhe 
buhluneme. Amehlo akhe ayecwayizisa okwemibani. Ubuso 
bakhe babubukeka buthwele umvimbi owawuhambisana 
nenkanyamba. Akabange esanda namazwi. Wakhululeka 
uMaZondi, wabuyela ekamelweni eyobamba impi yakhe 
yomzwangedwa. 

Eseqedile, wadumela iphephandaba ayefike nalo, 

walifunda waze wozela. Wangena ekamelweni labo, 
wacambalala edimede ebuka iwashi, ebala amahora 
ayesasele ngaphambi kokubuya komkakhe. Ihora 
lesine lashaya. Wasukuma, waphondla wangqongqozela 
uMaZondi emazisa ukuthi wayesathi shelele eyolanda 
umkakhe. Waphuma, wangena emotweni, zaya. 

Babuya ngelesihlanu. Engena nje uMaDlamini 
endlini wavulela amanzi ashisayo ebhavini, washo 
phakathi. Umyeni wakhe owayeseseduze kwakhe, 
njengenhlalayenza, wathatha indwangu nensipho, 
wambekela isineke, emgcoba ngamafutha ayenamakha 
ayenuka izimbali. 

Baphuma ekamelweni, baba sekhishini bobabili. 
Ngesikhathi omunye ebeka amanzi etiye, omunye 
wayelungisa izinkomishi. Babekwenza lokhu bexoxa, 
behleka uhleko oluncane. Izimfanelo zetiye zabekwa 
etafuleni, kwaba yilapho uThabekhulu ekhipha iphakethe 
lamazambane athosiwe nenyama yenkukhu yodumo 
lweKentucky, konke ekuphathele umkakhe. Kwaphakwa 
puletini linye, badla. Sebeliphungile netiye, basukuma 
bagezisana izitsha. Ngemuva kwalokho bahlala bobabili 
endlini yokuphumula. Owesimame wanikeza owesilisa 
inoveli ayekade ezifundela yona emini. Owesilisa wanikeza 
owakwakhe iphephandaba ayeselifundile. 

Ngemuva kwesikhathi basukuma, omunye walungisa 

131 

igceke, omunye ezinye izimfanelo zasendlini, eqeda 
epheka. UMaDlamini wabaphakela abakwaDubazana, 
base bengena kwezokuvakasha nomyeni wakhe. Yaduma 
imoto, zaya. Yibo labaya edolobheni besayozichwathikela 
ezihlabathini zolwandle bebambene ngocikicane. 
Babuya kuhwalele, bangena embhedeni, baxoxelana 
beshiyelana nangemibono ngababekufunde enovelini 
nasephephandabeni. 

Ngehora leshumi nanye wangqongqoza uDubazana. 
Watatabuka umkakhe wamvulela. Wethuka uMaZondi 
embona engeDubazana owayejwayelekile. Namuhla 
wayeshaye i–ovalolo ayesebenza ngayo namadadla 
ayemnyama, konke kudabukile. Ayehambe ezigqokile 
wayezigodlile. Nokuphuma kwakhe emnyameni wokuhlwa 
engena ekamelweni kwakusewukungena osizini. 
Kuleli kamelo amathuba okwelapheka komshado wabo 
ayelahleka umzuzu nomzuzu. Esikhundleni sokuba 
ngabe babesondelana kakhulu, omunye acamelise ikhanda 
komunye, amkhalele, aduduzwe, lalingekho nalelo thuba 
kulelo kamelo kubo elase liwumuzi uphelele. 

Izinyanga ezintathu zaphela isimo siya ngokuya siba 
bucayi usuku nosuku. Isibindi sokuba ofelaphakathi 
sehlulwa wumzwangedwa. Bazidela amathambo 
bayobika emaphoyiseni nakodokotela. Bagqigqa 
begqigqile bebuzwa amanangananga amaningi behlolwa 
bethathwa negazi. UMaZondi wayesindile. Kwatholakala 

132 

ukuthi uMakhosazana owayesezithwele, wayenalo 
negciwane lengculaza. Kwaboniswana nangekhambi 
elaliwukuwukhipha umbungu. Wala waphetha 
uMakhosazana. 

“Ngiyazisa ngomntanami ompilo isiphahlazeke 
enhlekeleleni yobunhlwa engasayizwanga nenjabulo 
yobuntombi!” Ngesikhathi ebalisa engaqedi uMaZondi 
umyeni wakhe wayebancenga ukuba bakhale bezesula. 
Le ndaba kwakungafanele bayithi vu, kwaThabekhulu, 
funa baphelelwe nayindawo yokuquba.
