11 


UmNdeNi kaDubazana wawusuyiwo ngezidumbu, ubhubhe 
emoyeni. Unina wezingane wayesengenelwe ukuzenyeza 
nokungazethembi. Wayezizwa enganakiwe, engathandwa. 
Nendaba yegciwane yayimethusile, engethembi ukuthi 
ngempela wayexhegulile kulo. Ukungenwa yilesi sifo, 
nobuhlungu bokuthwala isixhwala sombungu owawuyise 
engaziwa nokuthi wayengowakwabani ezalwa wumabani 
wakuzwa sengathi kwakukuye. Zazike zibe khona 
izithuba lapho ayethi uma eyibona indodakazi imphihli, 

ingasafundi, ishabalalelwe wugqozi, afise ukuba naye 

ukufa kusheshe kumaphule ekudabukeni. UNkosana 
nakuye esasingedluli isilo sengubo ayesenziwe, 
wabuyela esewuNkosana omusha, unyube wasesikoleni. 
UDubazana wayebabuka bonke aphenduke isiduli nje 
esasicabanga singaqedi. Yikho lokhu kuthula kwakhe 
okwakunezelela enkathazweni yomphefumulo womkakhe 
nasekuzizweni enganakiwe, engathandwa. 

Ngokuqhubeka kwezinsuku inkinga kaMaZondi 
yathanda ukumhlala enhliziyweni uThabekhulu. Emini 
lapho ebuya emsebenzini wayethi uma engqongqoza 
kuvame ukuba uMaZondi owayemvulela qede ambuke 
ngamehlo esiguli ayekhombisa izinyembezi ezazisanda 
kwesulwa. Nasemzimbeni wayehusheka ngokushesha 
njengendodakazi yakhe eyayingasalubhadi esikoleni. Kazi 
yayingasafundi ngani? Nakuba wayekubona konke lokhu, 
waqale wanamahloni okubuza. 

Izinyanga eziningi befikile zaphela benje 

134 

abakwaDubazana. OThabekhulu bayifunda ivaliwe, 
baqala nomkakhe ukuyingqumuza embhedeni. 

Wavuma umkakhe ngokuthi, “Empeleni abakaze 
baswabuluke selokhu bafika. Kube kufanele–ke khona. 
Lukhulu olwabehlela.” 

“Ngibona sengathi kufanele sibasize kule nkinga 
ababhajwe kuyo.” 

“Singabasiza kanjani nje kodwa yise kaThabethule?” 

“Ngokubaxoxisa nina kaThabisile. Uyazi, umuntu 
noma enenkinga, imicabango ike ithi damu, uma 
inkinga yakhe eyibonisane nomunye. Ngakho–ke 
ngicela sibakhiphe ekamelweni, sihlale nabo endlini 
yokuphumula. Mina ngizothi ngibuyisa ingqondo 
kaDubazana, nawe ube ungamlibele umkakhe.” 

“Kanti ukuba uyazi ukuthi sengazama kanjani, 
ngehluleka ngoba uvele angincishe amehlo nje.” 

“Wenziwa yiyona impela inkinga emphethe.” 

Imizamo yabakwaThabekhulu yokuqhumbuza 
ithumba yaphelela emoyeni. AbakwaDubazana base 
bejwayela ukuzivalela ekamelweni, bengahambeli muntu. 
Nokubaxoxisa kwakuba sengathi kwakuwukubahlupha 
nje. Noma sebehlezi nabakwaThabekhulu babengagudli 
nakugudla emzwangedweni owawubaphethe. 

Kwaze kwathi ngalanga limbe uThabekhulu engqongqoza 
ebuya emsebenzini, wavulelwa uMaZondi namuhla 
umunyu owawumxine kangangokuba wayezesula zedlule 
zigeleze izinyembezi, ewadonsa ewadonsile namakhala. 
Wangena uThabekhulu, wavala, wayesembuka 
isikhashana. 

“MaZondi, ngisacela uhlale phansi, uke ungichathazele 
nje ukuthi ngabe yini lena engedluli, elokhu yakwephula 

135 

umoya.” 

“Akusizi ukuba ufelaphakathi. Usungaze umelwe

Wambekela isineke emncenga. Wagcina ehlezi uMaZondi 
kusofa. Naye wahlala komunye babhekana. Ngaso isineke 
wamxoxisa, emba imfihlo yenhliziyo. 

UMaZondi owayefundiswe ukuba izinkinga zomuzi

thina sodwa.” 

“Uma kuyinkinga ongafisi ayazi, ngeke ngimtshele.” 

UThabekhulu wazizwa edabuka embuka ekhedamisile. 

Wammisa idolo ngokuvaleleka kwemfihlo. Ngakho–ke, 

uMaZondi emethemba, wayibhoboza. 

Zehla izinyembezi ethi, “Ngicela ungayilokothi eyesifo

“Angingakufaki ezinkingeni mntanomuntu. Sengesaba 
nokuthi nakimi isifo silotshwe ebusweni.” 

“Qha, kuthiwa asithathelwana ngezinyembezi. Mina 
ngikubona umsulwa nje.” 

“Umyeni wami yena wesaba ngisho ukungithinta 
ngocikicane.” 

Lamethusa lelo uThabekhulu wathi, “Ngabe nakuwe 
latholakala yini?” 

“Balilandula, kepha akakholwanga. Ukungakholwa 

136 

kwakhe sekungenze angazethemba. Angazi ukuthi ubani 
ongake akhanyisele uDubazana ngezeluleko.” 

“Uzothi uzwe ngobani?” 

“Sizonicela nje nizosihlalisa endlini yokuphumula, bese 
kuba yilapho–ke engizosigaxelisa khona isihloko sodaba 
lwabaganeneyo. Isihloko sengculaza sozingenela sona. 
OMaDlamini noDubazana boze bayingene leyo bengazi 
ukuthi sesike sayidingida sisobabili.” 

“Ukuxoshwa esikwesabayo.” 

“Kanti mhlawumbe beningathi uma nishiyelana 
ngemibono nonina kaThabethule, uthole ukuphila.” 

“Kanti futhi kunokwenzeka athi sizomthelela 
ngezintwala zasemjondolo. Njengoba sivumelene, uma 
wena ukuxolela ukusigcina sinengculaza, makube wulwazi 
lwethu sodwa.” 

Behlukana uMaZondi esezisola ukuthi wayeze 
waphahlukelani. Kanti noThabekhulu, ngale ekamelweni, 
wayekhathazekile ngabakwaDubazana. Wayezazi izikhathi 
ezibuhlungu zezivunguvungu zomshado lapho umkhumbi 
owumuzi unqwamana khona neziphepho nezintaba 
zamadlambi, nalapho izikhulu zalo mkhumbi zidukelana 
khona nokuhloniphana, nokuthandana nokwamukelana. 
Nakubo nomkakhe babeke bahlangabezana nalezi 
zikhathi. Ubuhlungu ayebazi bubuhlungu kunabo bonke 
emshadweni, obokunganakani kufanele ninakane. 

Wacabanga abehla ubuthongo ukuthi wayengahle 
abasize kanjani. Wakhumbula ukuthi nabo nomkakhe 
babeze banamathela enkonzweni nje ngenxa yomunye 
umzalwane owayebavakashele ngelinye ilanga, wabafica 
sekwaba yizinyanga baxhukulelana. Uye umzalwane 

137 

mumbe lowo owayebahlalele phansi, wabakhanyisela 
ngokuthi umuzi wabo wawusemnyameni nje ngoba 
wawedukelene nelanga eliyisibani somshado esiwuMdali 
wesintu ngomgcagco. Uma oDubazana babengazimisele 
ngokuya enkonzweni, wakubeka emahlombe akhe 
ukuvuselela kubo umoya womshado. 

“Imizi eminingi bakithi ayibhidliki ngoba 
sekuganenwe. Indaba yonakala kuseshelwana,” 
kusho yena uThabekhulu kusihlwa bebonke endlini 
yokuphumula bebuka umabonwakude. 

Wabuza umkakhe wathi, “Indaba yonakala kanjani 
kuseshelwana?” 

“Indaba bakithi yonakala mhla umuntu eqala nje 
ukunweba izindebe zakhe zomlomo ethi uthanda omunye 
engazi nakuthanda lokho ukuthi kusho ukuthini. 
Sikhuluma nje, mfo kaDubazana, kukhona abantu 
abaganene kumanje, abazi ukuthi bayathandana 
bengathandani.” 

“Angiboni kunjalo Thabekhulu,” kuphika uDubazana. 
“Angiboni ukuthi ukhona umuntu ongababala omunye athi 
uyamthanda, aze amcele, amlobole, alahlekelwe ekhipha 
izibizo, ehlaba, eganwa, kepha abe engamthandi.” 

“Abanjalo yibona abaningi Dubazana. Uma ngingase 
ngibuze nje kuwe, usuke uqonde ukuthini uma ubelesela 
umuntu umeshela? Yena–ke usuke eseqonde ukuthini 
uma esekuqoma?” 

Wathula uDubazana. Kwakukade kwasa eshela 

138 

enziwa yisithukuthezi sothando. Wayengakaze kodwa 
azibuze ngenjula yokuthi wayesuke eqondeni ngempela 
ngelokuthanda omunye umuntu ngale nje kokukhangwa 
ubuhle bakhe. 

“Ngangiqonde phela ukuthi ngimthandela ukuvusa 
umuzi kababa.” 

“Lihle nalelo Dubazana lokuvusa umuzi 
wabakwaDubazana ngoba nenkosikazi ingeyabo. 
Kodwa–ke, umbuzo wami uthi, uma umsukela nje 
umuntu wesimame umeshela, usuke uqonde ukuthini, 
singakayiphathi nje eyokwakha umuzi?” 

“Hhayi, mhlawumbe simsukela ngemizwa engefani. 
Mina ngakolwami uhlangothi sengichazile. Awusho nawe 
wethu.” 

“Mina Dubazana ngakolwami uhlangothi ngithatha 
ngokuthi usuke umcela owesimame ukuba akwamukele.” 
Wabuka omkabo, wabuza wathi, “Mhla nisiqoma, 
naniqonde ukusitshela ukuthini makhosikazi?” 

Babukana oMaZondi noMaDlamini. Ngokokuqala base 

belokhu bafika kwaMpanza, wabonakala emamatheka 

uMaZondi. 

“Awusho wena MaZondi. Mhla usuchobozela, 
usumqoma uDubazana, wawuqonde ukumtshela 
ukuthini?” 

Wachobozela futhi uMaZondi, wathi, “Ngangiqonde 
ukumtshela ukuthi, ezeshelini zami zonke, njengoba 
naye ubengomunye obecula ngokuthi uyangithanda, 
uyena kuphela empilweni yami engicela angithande. 
Selokhu–ke saqomana noDubazana angiceli lutho olunye 
kuye ngaphandle kokuba angikhombise ukungithanda 

139 

ngezenzo.” Wambuka wambhansela ngalawo mehlo akhe 
ayezothile, ensundu. 

“ElikaMaZondi elami yise kaThabethule. Lapho 
kuthiwa kunothando khona, nendlela ikhona. Kunye 
engikucela kuwe Mpanza — uthando. Uma lukhona, 
empilweni yami yonke ngizimisele ukulucentela, 
ngiluchelele ukuze luzithelele izithelo.” 

Amazwi ayemphathe kwamancane uMpanza. 
Emamatheka wabuka uDubazana wathi, “Uyabezwa 
kodwa Dubazana ukuthi bacelani kithi?” 

Ngezwi lowayeshayekile uDubazana wavuma. 
Wawetshisa amagama uMpanza ethi, bathi: 
“Sengiyakwemukela–ke. Nawe–ke, njengoba uthi 
uyangithanda, sengicela ungisize, ungithande. Okufike 
kudabukise–ke Dubazana kulezi zikhathi zanamuhla, 
ukuthi zithi zibekwa nje phansi lo muntu ocelwa ukuba 
akhombise uthando ngezenzo, uqala ukubhala ecisha. 
Engakathathi ngisho esokuqala isinyathelo sokukhombisa 
uthando, uyothi umbona, nanguya usekhonjwa engxenye, 
nakhona uyeshela. Ngamanye amazwi ucela nakhona 
ukuthanda lokhu angakwazi. 

“Leli lokwamukela nokuthanda lihamba indlela ende, 
Dubazana. Lize lifakazelwe nayiNcwadi yeZincwadi lapho 
ithi, ‘Madoda thandani omkenu. Makhosikazi, hloniphani 
amadoda enu.’ Elokuhlonipha mina ngilihumusha 
ngelokwamukela, ngoba umuntu umamukela ngomoya 
omuhle ngoba umthanda, umhlonipha. Nemizi eminingi 
ize iphihlizeke nje ngoba kusuke kwehlulekekile 
ukufezwa kwalezi zicelo ezimbili. Ekhaya omunye kumbe 
elule izingalo elindele ukwamukela ukuze athandwe, 
kanti uzelulele ukubiphelwa. Omunye eze emagange ethi 

140 


uzokwamukeleka, okulindeleke ukuba amemukele amfice 

abaqomene bafinyelele ezingeni lomshado,” kuqhuba 

uMaDlamini. “Yileli zinga–ke elingenza ngizibuze ukuthi, 
kusho ukuthini ukuganana? Lo mbuzo bakwaDubazana 
sake sazibuzabuza wona nomyeni wami ngesikhathi nathi 
sesidukelene enkungwini yokuganana kwabantu bengazi 
ngempela ukuthi kusho ukuthini ukuganana. Ngikholwa 
nawukuthi baningi impela abaze bachithane bengakaze 
bahlale phansi bobabili babuzane ngokuthi sebekuliphi 
izinga asebelichitha. 

“Ekuzibuzabuzeni kwethu ngomshado, sathola 
impendulo ewukuthi umshado awuzona nje kuphela 
lezi zidumbu zethu esasiklolodelana ngokuthi noma 
sasingehlukana, babengazibuka abanye bazithande. 
Sathola ukuthi kunomoya womshado; umoya womuzi. 
Sathola ukuthi umshado kufanele uphefumule umoya 
wempilo. Umoya bakwaDubazana empilweni yezizwe 
ngezizwe zomhlaba siwubona ubaluleke ukwedlula konke. 
Siphiliswa umoya, Manzima. Izinqola eziningi nezindiza 
esihamba ngazo, zihamba ngomoya. Kuthiwa ngisho 
uMdali wamdala umuntu wayesemphefumulela ngomoya 
wakhe. Umuntu uthandeka ngomoya wokuthula noxolo 
anawo.” 

“Imisebenzi yomoya,” uMpanza wamelekelela 
umkakhe, waqhubeka wathi, “uma sesiyinakisisa, 
siyithola iyisimangaliso. Uke uthathe incwadi uyifunde, 
ikufake usikisiki, nomoya wayo ukwenze umkhonze 
umlobi wayo ungamazi nakumazi. Abaculi abadumile 
emhlabeni jikelele, abanye ongakaze ubabone ngisho 
kumabonwakude, uke ubakhonze uze ube umlandeli 
wabo, ngomoya nje womculo, qhwaba. Ngokunjalo 

141 

nasemshadweni, kubusa umoya womshado. Yiwona lo 
moya obenza abantu bangathathani ngabuhle nangcebo. 
Yiwona lo moya odudula umuntu acele engasaboni, 
azishaye ezakwabo ezibongela. Yiwona futhi lo moya 
obusa endlini yabaganeneyo. Kukangaki ngizwa amadoda 
ethi uma engena endlini inkosikazi ingekho awabe 
esasibeka naphansi isinqe ngoba ayizwa indlu ibanda, 
yomele ukufudunyezwa wumoya womshado. EsiZulwini 
sasingekho isahlukaniso njengoba babazi ukuthi lo moya 
womshado awube usehlukana nezithunzi zabaniniwo. 
Kwala umuntu esehlukanisile noma eshonelwe, 
umoya wokuthi ungumkabani, noma umyeni kabani 
awushabalali. Kwanga, kusukela namuhla singalala 
sibhangqwe yilo moya ongcwele.” 

“Awuzwe–ke izwi lendoda. Indoda iyindoda ngenkosikazi.” 
Kwakwenanela uThabekhulu. 

Sekwehlukanwa ngamakamelo oDubazana nomkakhe 
bamangala bekhonjiswa elinye ikamelo, kuthiwa 
okwesikhashana izingane zingakabuyi babengahlala kulo. 

142 

Bangena ekamelweni elalihlanzekile, linombhedekazi 
owawendlalwe ngezintsha izingubo ezazisanuka isitolo. 
Bageza, wangena embhedeni uMaZondi, wahlala phezu 
kwawo uDubazana, wakhedamisa ebambelele esihlathini. 
Umkakhe owayekade exoxa besenabakwaMpanza, 
eseyizwile nenjabulo yemfudumalo yengxoxo, kwabe 
uyadulela ezama ukuyivusa ngokuthi: ‘Hhayi, 
bayakhuluma abantu bakwaThabekhulu. Futhi 
banezeluleko ezakhayo njengoba nabo basinda emlonyeni 
wengonyama eyisahlukaniso.” 

UMaZondi wabuyela ekukhumeni umzwangedwa. 
Ikamelo nobuhle balo laba nawo umoya womshado, nokho 
ngaleso sikhathi owawungaphefumuli, ungavunguzi. 
Kwakuba sengathi kwakuheleza unyela lobufelwa 
nobufelokazi. Waqwasha uMaZondi. Phose kwasa 
enomndanana wokwamukela nokuthandwa. 

Ngokuqhubeka kwezinsuku nomoya wokufelwa 
nobufelokazi kwabakwaDubazana, kwabuyela kokudala, 
lapho wayethi uma engqongqoza uMpanza, uMaZondi 
amvulele qede ambuke ngobuso obabugcwele ngci, 
isangci. Ngokumbekela isineke kukaThabekhulu, 
emxoxisa, emhlekisa ngokumncokolisa, wagcina 
uMaZondi esezizwa enomngani owayenezaluleko 
ezakhayo. Nakuba wayeyisinteli, likhona isela elase liqale 
ukumcathamela enganakile. Kunokufika kukaDubazana 
owayezobamba isihlathi, wethatshiswa ukungqongqoza 
kukaThabizolo. Kulokho kuncokola uThabizolo 
wamethembisa ukumelekelela uMaZondi empini 
yokuzuza uthando lomyeni. 

143 

Kwaqhutshekwa ntambama, kwahlaliswana, kuxoxwa, 
kubukwa nomabonwakude. 

“Umuntu, Thabekhulu, uma enibona nizihlalele 
nje, ngeke aze acabange ukuthi nake nedlula ezihibeni 
ezinjalo,” kusho uDubazana. “Kwase kwenzenjani?” 

Esitsheni esasiphambi kwabo, sinezithelo, 
uThabekhulu wathatha ihhabhula, walisika phakathi, 
ucezu olunye walukhangeza umkakhe. UDubazana 
esevele eziphathele elakhe ihhabhula, nomkakhe 
ezicoshele iwolintshi, wasibuka isenzo sikaThabekhulu 
washayeka. 

“Okwakubanga ukuba singezwani, Dubazana, 
kwakuwukungazani nokungazi. Ngangingamazi umkami, 
naye engangazi. Sasiganene nje, sasingakaze sihlale 
phansi siziphenye imiphefumulo ngokuthi, ngempela 
ngempela kuyini ukuganana, nokuthi ukuba owomunye 
kusho ukuthini komunye.” 

UMaZondi owayelihlafuna kancane iwolintshi, 
ewesula ngesineke namanzana alo ayemnandi, wayilalela 
ngokuyithakasela ingxoxo. Wabuza wathi: “Nathola yiphi 
impendulo ekuziphenyeni kwenu?” 

“Ngicela kube uwena omchazelayo MaDlamini,” kusho 
uThabekhulu. 

“Ziyisimangaliso ntombi izimpendulo esazithola. 
Sabukana, sathola ukuthi omunye wethu komunye 
uwumhlaba wakhe okulindeleke ukuba awudavuze 

144 

izinsuku zakhe zonke zokuphila. Ngaleso sibonakaliso 
kwahlaluka ukuthi njengoba ubuntu nentokozo kuzuzeka 
kumuntu ngokuwuthanda nokuwuhlonipha umhlaba 
aphila kuwo, nathi ukuze sinqobe, kufanele sihloniphane 
sithandane. Umhlaba ophila kuwo–ke uwuthanda 
ngokuwakha, uwulime, uchelele, uvune. Sathola futhi 
ukuthi akuthandwana nje kuphela ebuhleni, kepha 
kubanjiswana nasezinsizini.” 

“Kithi sekwaphela ukuthi okwami okwami; okwakho 
okwakho. Sesinokwethu, komuzi,” kwenanela uMaDlamini. 

Kwaxoxwa eside isikhathi kwaze kwahlukwanwa 
ngamakamelo nangezenzo. Ngesikhathi abakwaThabekhulu 
bethabile, kwelabakwaDubazana wayekhala uMaZondi. 

Elinye ikhambi lokwelapha lo mshado 
wakwaDubazana abalicabanga, kwaba wukuba 
ngomunye uMgqibelo kebabavakashise nje, babashayise 
ngomoya. Babonisana nabo, uDubazana wavumelana 
nombono, inqobo nje uma wayezothola ithuba lokuthenga 
okokwembatha kokuhamba. Kanjalo, ngoMgqibelo 
thize, bobane bangena emotweni beyidlile indwangu. 
Isho kancane, kamnandi ingoma eyayipholile, yanyelela 

145 

imoto yangena umgwaqo. Ingoma yothando yenza 
ababengaphambili emotweni bathintane ngezandla. 
ODubazana belinganisene ngemuva, umkakhe wayizwa 
ingoma wazisondeza kakhulu kumyeni wambamba 
isandla esaba wugodo. 

UDubazana wathi: “Kufanele Thabekhulu. Izwe 
liyanyakaza.” 

Imoto yathi ukuba iphume eMlazi omdala yangena 
imigwaqo eyayiyitafula, ingemigodigodi. Kusemnandi 
yagaleleka enhliziyweni yedolobha. Galaji thize 
bayishiya kwelenyoni. OThabekhulu nomkakhe 
babambana ngezingalo nangocikicane behambe 
bema emafasiteleni ezitolo bekhombisana izimpahla 
ababezifisa. NakoDubazana kwavukavuka okudala, 
babambana, nokho ngokwesaba. Kwakwazise ukuthi 
babengakwejwayele ngempela ukutetemuka ezitaladini 
bebambene. 

“Sinenhlanhla bakwaDubazana ngokuba abashadikazi 
okushaya lezi khathi kuyimpelasonto besakwazi 
ukutetemuka ndawonye. Abanye abasaboni. Uma 
ungase uhambe ubuza wonke amadoda ukuthi akugcina 
nini ukuqabula omkawo, nokuthi abanga kangaki 
ngonyaka, ungathola isimanga. Abanye bagcina mhla 
beshada betshengiswa wumthwebuli wezithombe ukuthi 
abenzenjani.” 

146 

Yahlekwa indaba kaThabekhulu yayihlaya elalinqumela 
enhliziyweni kuDubazana. Kwakuba sengathi kwakugconwa 
yena. Yedlula leyo kwachwathikwa kwangenwa emagcekeni 
ehholo yedolobha. Ayekhanya klelele, emahle, ehlotshiswe 
yizihlahla, izimbali nongwengwe kwezinye izindawo 
okwakulotshwe ngalo iminyaka enemilando yedolobha. 

“Siyabonga bakwaThabekhulu ngokuba kenisivakashise 
nje, umuntu ake abone umhlaba nokuphila kwabantu 
bawo. Sonke isikhathi lesi sihlupheka, bese ngilibele 
du ukuthi khona lapha enqulwini esilungwini kuphilwa 
komunye umhlaba. Ngakho–ke, akungabazeki ukuthi 
njengoba kukhona osekukhanyeni nosemnyameni, 
kukhona osemsamo nosemnyango.” Kusho uDubazana. 

“Nathi siyabonga Dubazana uma nikuthokozela 
ukuvakasha. Njengoba usho nje mfowethu, uthi 
kunabasemnyameni, kunabantu thina okufanele 
nanininini sihlale ngokubadumisa ngezenzo 
nangezinhliziyo.” 

“Kusekhona ukudumisa bantu kodwa Thabekhulu uma 
isimo sisidida ingqondo kanje?” 

147 


“Noma kunjalo Dubazana, kulokho kudideka 
kukhona amaqhawe akhona. Usuke ewumhlobo wakho 
ngeqiniso umuntu ofa lapho ufa khona. Thina sibe 
nenhlanhla ngokuba nabantu besimame abasithande 
ezikhathini ezibuhlungu zobandlululo. Ngabe akubuntu 
ukungabadumisi belamba lapho silambe khona, 
siquba nabo emadlangaleni abizwa ngemijondolo. 
Singebadumise ngani besikhonzise okwamadoda ngisho 
izenzo zasezweni zisenza amadojeyana emehlweni 
abo? Kufanele sibadumise Dubazana ngokuthi 
abathathekanga amagolide namadayimani abelenga 
ezinjingeni. Basizalele, bakhulisa kulowo mnyama. 
Uwufakazi Dubazana ngokuthi bahlukunyeziwe. Nakuba 
kunjalo, basenobuqotho bobukhosikazi base–Afrika. 
Okuyisimangaliso ngala makhosikazi ethu esikhathi 
sobandlululo, Dubazana ukuthi, nakuba egajwe usizi, 
kuthi nje gqwa, gqwa edidekela ekubulaleni abayeni 
bawo. Namanje, MaDlamini noMaZondi, nani nonke 
makhosikazi ethu esikhathi sobandlululo, nginethulela 
isigqoko!” Washo eyimisa imoto phambi kwegalaji 
lakwakhe. 


12 


NgokUgqigqa kukaMakhosazana esibhedlela nasemnya– 
ngweni wezeNhlalakahle wakhona, unonhlalonhle 
wavama naye ukubahambela abakwaDubazana. 
Ngale nje kothando lomsebenzi, entokazini lena 
kwase kukhuluma negazi. Yebo, uDuduzile Mwelase 
wayeyintokazi ziphelele, enethambo, lunyathela luzizwe 
ugamfu lakwabo. Ngale nje kokubhekana nokududuzeka 
kwabo wayeyigugu abakwaDubazana ababezizwa benalo. 

Inyanga yokuphela konyaka yafika uDuduzile, 

njengegama lakhe, esemduduze uMakhosazana 
waze wabuyelwa yisithunzi sakhe. Wayezoze azeye, 

azisole nje ngoba wayoneni, kubani? Nokuzifihla 

wakubona kuwukufa nezifundo zomhlaba. Wazimisela 
ngokuba kowawuzokwethwasa abuyele esikoleni 
ukuze athole ithuba lokuthintana nenye intsha 
ezikoleni ngezikole. Wayephokophelele ukuba nalabo 
ababevumelane ngokushayana ngezingane zenziwa 
izikhali bamuzwe, basho–ke ukuthi uma kwase kunjeya, 

kwakwenziwanjani. Ngobunjalo bakhe wayefisa 

ukuba nesililo sababentula izindlu, kudlalwa ngabo 

bengomagumangithole, sifinyelele eziphathimandleni. 

Zavalwa izikole ethandazela ukuba litholakale esaphila 
ikhambi lokwelapha lolu bhubhane. 

Ngokusondela kwezinsuku zikaKhisimusi kwehliwa 
kwenyukwa, bebodwa ababephikelele emakhaya, abanye 
bevakashela emadolobheni. Nezingane zakwaThabekhulu 

zafika, oDubazana nezakhe baqoqana ekamelweni 

149 

elilodwa. Yize kwakuyizinsuku zomunyu iningi labantu 
lawuthokozela umgubho kaKhisimusi. Kwababefana 
noDubazana nje, kwasuku lolo abazanga nakuthi lwalusho 
ukuthini. Nansimbi zoNcibijane bazizwa bengazizwa, 
kowawufa nowawethwasa bengalindele mahluko. 

“Ngenkolo yethu bansundu, mfowethu,” kwakusho 
uDuduzile, “inkosikazi ifana nendlu enkulu okuthethelwa 
kuyo intando yamadlozi ukuba umuzi wawo ume, ungawi. 
Idlozi–ke alithethwa wumuntu onamafundululu enhliziyo. 
Nasenkolweni yamaKristu kuthiwa umshado ungcwele, 
nomzimba wabaganeneyo uyisidlo esingcwele kubo. Isidlo 
esingcwele umuntu akasilokothi esenhliziyo ifukamele 
imidlinzo.” UDuduzile wayedulela kumfowabo owayezwa 
engezwa. 

Nakuba imizamo yoDuduzile nabakwaMpanza 
yaphumelela ukubaxebula oMakhosazana nonina 
ezinkingeni ababedlule kuzo, umqondo kaDubazana 
wasala unamathele. Okwase kumqedela du, kwase 
kuyimidlinzo. Ezindaweni eziningi ayekade ephuma 
engena kuzo nomkakhe babevame ukumqambela amanga 
uMaZondi ngokuthi wayezama ukugaqela izimali zabo. 
NakwamMlangeni kwakube njalo. Babelimise ngembaba 
elokuthi wayekade ezama ukuyenga uQumbisa. Kwabona 
abasemjondolo, ngaphambi kokuba bamthele phansi 
ngesimolontshisi uDubazana, wayelizwile elalithe umkakhe 

150 

wayeyintombi yomunye, ethathe imali yakhe emini. 
Inkoloze yokuhabula imimoya yokuba uphumengena 
uDubazana yayisimdida, ingase imlahlele okukhona 
ngokungekho. 

UMakhosazana wathengelwa inyumfomu, wabuyela 
khona eMzuzwana lapho avama khona ukuqeketha 
ngesifo esasimphethe, nokuthi wayesithole kanjani. Unina 
wavama ukusala yedwa endlini ezibuza eziphendula. 
Ingqinamba eyayisamkhungethe yiyo yokuthi lapha endlini 
ukubuya emini kukaMpanza owayemphumuza emunywini 
ngokumxoxisa eneme kwakusawuthokozisa umoya wakhe 
kunokubuya kukaDubazana owayewuhlaba inhlali esineme. 
Naye uThabizolo wayesenemfihlo ethile enhliziyweni. 
Wayesenokukhathazeka okuthile ngoMaZondi, 
esemdabukela, emzwela. Wayesezamile ukumsiza 
ngokubonisa uDubazana. Wayehlulekile. Lezi zinyembezi 
uMaZondi ayemthela ngazo mihla lapho engqongqoza 
wayengasazi ukuthi wayezomesula kanjani. Yebo, buthule 
ezinhliziyweni zabo izulu laqala ukuhloma. Usuku nosuku 
omunye waqhubeka nokukhumbula omunye. 

KungoLwesithathu emini, esanda kuhamba 

uDubazana eyongena ngehora lesibili, wafika uMpanza 

kwakhe, wangqongqoza njengokwakwejwayelekile. 
UMaZondi wamvulela, wambingelela, wayesembuka 
ngalawo mehlo okukhathazeka nendumalo. Ngalolo suku 
akabanga nasinqe. Washeshe wabuyela ekamelweni 

151 

abase bebuyiselwe kulo noDubazana. 

Uma esesephasijini, iso lakhe wathi uma eliphonsa 
ngaphakathi ekamelweni elalilala oDubazana, waqikileka 
emangele. Wayemangazwa ukubona uMaZondi ezenwaya 
ngokuzikhuhla echosheni lewadilobhu. Ngcono amsize … 

Sagcina isandla senwaya, sachilizwa, sabuyiswa, 
sabanjwa, kwacinyezwa … 

*** 

Lase lidume ledlula koMaZondi noThabekhulu. 
Yilowo nalowo wayesezicambalalele ekamelweni lakhe. 
Bobabili babecambalele nje babeluzwa lungena lushweza 
unyela lokuzishaya, uvunguza ngamandla nomoya abake 
bakhuluma ngawo. Lase libacacela iqiniso eliwukuthi 

152 

umshado kwakuthiwa owoMdali nje ngoba ufana neso 

ngakuhlukanisa nakufelwa. Lihlala njalo likhazimula 
ngemisebe yalo kunembeza. Eziphambukweni azenzile 
oshadileyo kuba sengathi aganene naye uyambuka. 
Ngisho kwasebahlukanisa, noma omunye esadlula 
emhlabeni, lowo ochwathika nesithandwa esisha kuba 
sengathi liyambona iso lomphefumulo. Yingakho nje 
emasikweni ase–Afrika ongena emzini wowashonayo 
ebikwa kongasekho. 

UThabekhulu wayesefana nomuntu owayelale 
esuthi amponjwana, ingqondo yakhe isibuya kancane, 
ezibona izigemegeme azidale engasabonisisi kahle 
ngeso lenyama nelengqondo. Wayesezibuzabuza ukuthi 
kodwa kwakwenzenjani, ngoba ngisho nangezinsuku 
zobunzima emzini wabo nomkakhe wayengabonaze abe 
nothando lowesithathu. Nakhu, namuhla, ngokuvaleleka 
ndlininye nenkosikazi yowayesezinkingeni zokuntula 
umuzi, wayesewile. Washayeka eshayekile emoyeni. 
Ngale nje komkakhe, wayebuzwa ubuqotho bakhe 
behlile kuMaZondi. Wayeyophinde ameluleke kanjani 
ngobuqotho emendweni? Nomkakhe wayesemenze 
ize emehlweni enye inkosikazi. Wayeseyothi noma 
eziqhayisa ngomendo wakhe, imhleke usulu. Kazi– 
ke yena uDubazana wayesayombhekelwa ubani? 
Yayingasaphathwa phela eyomkakhe! Nakalokho iso 
lomshado kwakungathi lalisambuka ikakhulukazi 
njengoba nasesithombeni sawo esasilenga odongeni 
wayebukeka emuthe njo, umkakhe. Zaqala ukunyakaza 
izindebe eshaya umthandazwana omncane ecela 
intethelelo. 

UMaZondi ngale wayethe cu, ngesisu embhedeni, 
ikhanda elithe mbo, ezandleni ayezicamelise emqamelweni. 

153 

Nazo zazimanzi nte, yizinyembezi. Wayeshayekile 
emoyeni. Isehlo esasibehlele noThabekhulu wayesifanisa 
nezulu elase lilelese isisa uMaDlamini ayewubusise 
ngaso umndeni wonke kaDubazana. Zaziqathaka 
ubuqathaqatha izinyembezi. 

Iwashi elalisodongeni endlini yokuphumula 
lanqenqethisa okwensimbi yesonto lapha lishaya ihora 
elithile, lilibala. Lashaya nehora lesine, leva ngemizuzu. 
Enyobozela uThabizolo, wedlula kuye uMaZondi emcela 
ukuba aqaphe njengoba wayesathi shelele nje, elanda 
umkakhe. Nalelo lokulanda umkakhe lamshayisa ngovalo 
uMaZondi. 

Ngalelo langa uMaDlamini akambonanga 
uMaZondi owayezigqume ekamelweni. Wabuya 
noDubazana wamfica ezinyembezana. Izwi ayelilambele 
kakhulu, nelalingawududuza umphefumulo wakhe, 
ngelikaDubazana elithi wayesamthanda. 

Ezinsukwini ezalandela samshuka isazelo asamnika 
sithuba. Wajiyelwa ukuthi wayezoxolisa kanjani 
kuMaDlamini ayesesaba ngisho ukumbheka. Ngisho 
sebehlezi bobane endlini yokuphumula, bexoxa, 
isazelo kubo noThabekhulu sahlala emehlweni. Izinga 
lokudideka kwabo lenyuswa ukubona uMaDlamini 
noDubazana bekhululeke ngaphezu kwabo lapho 
kuxoxwa. Babehleka baze baveze nelomhlathi abantu 
bakhona bengagqilazwe nembeza. Nawo lawo omhlathi 
ayesephenduke isishayo. 

154 

UMaZondi wagcina ezidele amathambo, wazicelela 
kuMaDlamini ukuba bahambisane nabo lapho beya 
ezinkonzweni. UDubazana waqale waphambana nalesi 
sinyathelo. Elalimcika kakhulu ezintshumayelweni 
zasemasontweni ngelalithi abantu bayoba munye 
eZulwini, phezu kwenqubo yokucwasana eyayiqhutshwa 
ezweni yibo kanye ababefike kuleli nenkolo yaseYurophu. 
Nokho, embekele isineke uMaDlamini, emncenga, 
wagcina elandela, nakuba wayemadolonzima. Yena 
wayengazi nasonto lelo, azikhulelela emapulazini lapho 
izinsizwa zazihuba khona, zinegoso; nasemajele lapho 
kwakuhlukunyezwana khona kulinywa amazambane. 

emadolonzima, wayephuma eseqine idolo. Kuyo wayefike 

waphakelwa ukuphila komoya owawulambile. Wezwa 
ukuvuselelwa konembeza, uthando noxolo. Isonto 
nesonto engena kule ndlu, wayezizwa ephuma ezelwe 
busha, nenhliziyo yakhe eyayinamafundululu namahlule 
ihlanzekile. 

Kwamcacela lapha ukuthi kanti umsebenzi wezinkonzo 
ngowokubuyisa yona imiphefumulo edukileyo, 
nokuthambisa zona izinhliziyo eziyitshe nezicwasanayo. 
Kancane, kancane, nakuye ingqondo yabuya, ulaka 
lwehla, nenhliziyo yathokomala ekuthuleni. Inhlansi 
yokukhanya isalokoza emzini kaDubazana, pheliyane 
amandla okuya ezinkonzweni kumkakhe. Uyena owaqala 
wamadolonzima, wagcina engasalubhadi. Nokuhlala 
kwabo bobane endlini yokuphumula kwaphela, umkakhe 
wagcina eseyinto yombhede. Wayekhala imini yonke 
uma engena emini, nobusuku bonke uma ekhona noma 
engekho esebenza. Nakuba uDubazana, ngemuva 
kokuya ezinkonzweni, wayeqalile ukukhululeka 
emoyeni, uMaZondi wayesabhocobele. Wehla umdlandla 

155 

nakuDubazana, izinkonzo zagcina sezihanjelwa yibo 
oMpanza nomkakhe, behambisana noMakhosazane 
noNkosana ngamanye amasonto. 

“O, hhe, mntanomuntu! Ungaziqeda yini izindaba 
zemizi yabantu.” Waphelela lapha uuThabekhulu. 

“UDubazana uma umbuza wena, uthini?” 

“Uyazithulela uDubazana. Uyazi nawe MaDlamini.” 

“Hhayi, angiyazi mina le ndaba. UMaZondi ubukeka 
ethukile. Kunele kuhlangane amehlo ethu naye, ethuke 
ome, ngesinye isikhathi athuke esexolisa ngingazi ukuthi 
uxolisa oneni.” 

Wasishayela phansi isikhwehlela uThabekhulu, 
waziphinda kaningi zimbinda. 

*** 

“Ukhona yini omunye onombuzo?” Wabuza 
uMakhosazana emi phambi kothisha nezingane 
ezazigcwele swi ehholo lesikole, eManzolwandle 
lapho ayehambele khona. Nonina wayekhona, ehlezi 
emabhentshini ayephambili nothisha, esonge izandla. 
Wayembukela umntanakhe ephume impi yokukhanyisela 
ontanga ngenhlalo yesintu enesandla ekubhebhethekeni 
kwezifo. Lona lelo thuba wayelisebenzisela nokuqoqa 
izimali zesikhwama sezintandane zengculaza. 

Saphakama isandla. Kwakungesentombi 

156 

eyayiseminyakeni eyayingamashumi amabili. 
Wasikhomba, wasukuma umniniso waphefumula 
wathi, “Makhosazana, dadewethu, siyayizwa indaba 
edabukisayo osusilandise yona. Kunendida nokho 
engididayo. Ngiyaye ngizwe kuthiwa umthetho 
uyabavumela abezempilo ukuba bamkhiphe isisu 
osibambe ngokugcwelezwa. Engingakuqondi–ke ukuthi, 
ngabe umthetho wenqaba yini ukukusiza?” Yahlala 
phansi intombazane, yabuye yavumbuka yathi, “Ngicela 
bandla umbuzo wami ungakuphathi kabi.” Yacwila futhi. 

“UBongiwe Mbongwa, dadewethu.” 

“Okokuqala nje, Bongiwe, angikukhanyisele ukuthi 
umthetho unemibandela yawo. Kunamaphuzu amisiweyo 
achaza ngokuthi kuyini ukunukubezwa, nokuthi 
ummangali uyokwemukeleka kwabomthetho edluliselwe 
nakwabezempilo uma emangala ngemuva kwesikhathi 
esingakanani egcweleziwe. Sinenkinga kulesi sikhathi 
esiphila kuso, lapho umuntu egcwelezelwa kwabo, ahlale 
kuphele unyaka engamangele ngoba kuthiwa alubhadwa 
emaphoyiseni ngisho kubulewe umuntu. Kulukhuni kabi 
ukuchazela abomthetho ukuthi wagcwelezwa ngenyanga 
ethile, njengoba uzobika namuhla, mhlawumbe sewaze 
wabeletha nokubeletha. 

“Esami–ke angisiyekiswanga yimicikilisho yomthetho. 
Ngisiyekele ukufakazisa ngaso kubabusi bezwe 
neziphathimandla ukuze bazibonele ukuthi ezweni 
eliphethwe budedengu isizwe sakhona sibhujiswa kanjani

luhlaza.” Wasithinta. Sasibukeka singasasalelwe masonto 
mangaki asibeke phansi. Nonina wasithinta esakhe, 
wahlina sengathi sasimluma. Wazisusa kuso izandla, 

157 

wavala amehlo ezama nemizamo engaphumelelanga

“Uma abaphethe izwe beliphethe ngokwenza 
izakhamuzi zalo zizibone ziyize, nazo zigcina

ishibhile. Uma sekushibhe impilo–ke unembeza usuke 
usufele ngaphakathi, isidumbu sesiwumoya womungcwi. 

“Esinye futhi isizathu esenza ngehle ngenyuka

eminye yemiphumela yokwenziwa isizwe esingabizwa

kababa umuzi ongenanxiwa, umuzi wezikhonzi eziphuma 
zingena. Abanye abafana nathi sebehlupheke baze

aboguqa bathandazele kuyo, izintshumayelo ziyoba 

158 

ukudulela nje esizweni esiyobe singasenamithetho

nje.” Wazishaya isisu. “Sinje nje nje, akuntando yethu,

Nonina wasibuka esakhe, wankenywa oluncane

“Ningabe nisangikhalela mina. Nokho insindiso mayibe

uKaManzini! “Oshaka bayazenzela! Sisemanzini olwandle

yizigcwelegcwele zasolwandle.” Zaqathaka wazesula;

13 


NgemUva kwamadina, kungoLwesibili, uThabekhulu 
owayesehosheke ngezinsukwana nje, waphuma 
egaraji, wazihola, wangqongqoza kwakhe. Dukuduku, 
njengenhlalayenza, wamvulela uMaZondi owabe 
esephephukela kusofa naye, ehlala ekhedamisa kuwo, 
emthela ngezinyembezi. Wabuyisela emnyango uThabekhulu, 
wahlala kusofa owawubhekene nokaMaZondi. 


“Yini, kwenzenjani wangibingelela ngezinyembezi?” 

“Sengathi Thabekhulu sesifikile manje isikhathi 
sokuba ngizibulale. Angisaboni ngempela ukuthi manje 
yikuphi okuthokozisayo nokungiduduzayo engingathi 
ngiyakuphilela. Umntanami uMakhosazana engikhuluma 
nje, uyagula, ulalisiwe esibhedlela. Ukhulelwe 
umntanomntanami ongasekho engakazalwa. Umntanami 
uNkosana usephenduke isidindi nje esesihlala sithule, 
singasadlali nantanga yaso. Ngike ngithi ngiyamumemeza 
noma eseduze kwami, angangizwa. Kuyangicacela ukuthi 
ingqondo yakhe yedukile. Yithina ngapha nomyeni wami, 
sesihlupheke saze sadideka izingqondo, sedukelwa 
nawuthando olwalusihlanganisile. Namuhla ngithe shi, 
emahlazweni, ngivele ngobuso.” Wasidinda kakhulu isililo. 

Ngalelo langa lalishisa likhipha umkhovu etsheni. 
Nokho, uThabekhulu ezwa liqina elamahlazo, waqhuqha, 
wabuza sasiguli ethi, “Mahlazo mani osungene kuwo?” 

“Njengoba Thabekhulu ngike ngakutshela ukuthi 
ngizizwa ngingazizwa, wanginika imali wathi angiye 
kudokotela, ungena nje, sesicishe sangenisana. Ngivela 

160 

kuye.” 

“Amazwi akhe ahamba ezinsolweni zami.” 
Wabibitheka. 

“Hhawu, hhe!” Wazikhalela uThabekhulu. Wathi 
uyabuza wabheda ethi, “Uthi ukhuleliswe ubani kodwa?” 

“Akazange asho Thabekhulu. Yithina sobabili esaziyo.” 

“I!” Wanikina ikhanda uThabekhulu. “Saze sangena 
emahlazweni! Sekuwukubhidlika kwemizi njalo 
nokuphelelwa wukwethembeka emphakathini?” 

Ukubalisa kukaThabekhulu kwawathunuka amahlaba

“Namuhla ngikhulelwe ingane ethukeka ingakazalwa, 
ezobizwa ngevezandlebe nomenzelwa, engathandwa 
nawuyise ngoba iyisichithamuzi. Kuzomehlisa nesithunzi 
emphakathini ukuzalwa kwayo. Ngamanye amazwi 
ngikhulelwe uQedukuthula, uDaluqhekeko.” 

“U…u…u…” Wangingiza uThabekhulu ebopheka ulimi 
eqalwa amalimi ayengenawo. 

“Nakhu manje ngihlezi phambi kwakho. 
Uyaqhaqhazela, uyangingiza ngoba nakhu ngiyinkinga 
ongazi nokuthi uzoyithini. Ngiyisilingo esakulinga, 
nesichitho. Nkosi yami! Angazi ukuthi ngangize 
ngaphilelani uma ngiphilela ukuhlupheka okunje?” 

UThabekhulu wayejulukiswa, evevezeliswa wuvalo. 
Wayesaba lokhu kuzamazama okwakuzozamazamisa 
umshado wabo abase bewushayelele iminyaka, 
nezibhidi zodaka ezazizowuthela. Yekanini ukuphoxeka 
komphefumulo womkakhe mhla waziveza ungiyosho! 
Yekanini ukuchochobaliswa yichilo! Kazi izwe namakholwa 
ayelandela nawo ayeyoyizwa le ndaba ambheke athini, yena 
awabukelwe wubani? Kazi–ke uDubazana wayeyothini, 

161 

kambe yena Thabekhulu ezomtakula ngandlelani 
uMaZondi ukuba angachithekelwa wumendo? Uma 
umchithekela wayezombutha ambekephi nengane? 
Engqondweni yakhe uThabekhulu imicabango 
yaphambanisa okwemibani. Ngokokuqala ngqa esendlini 
kwakhe, wezwakala esewushayela phansi umlozi. 
Yayixakekile indoda. 

Wazishayela phansi izikhwehlela uThabekhulu zimbinda 
ezama ukuthi, “Unembeza wami uyangilahla MaZondi. 
Ngeke kuphume yena. Yimina esengoba usehlasenyuka 
nemigwaqo.” 

“Noma singakubhekisa ngaphi, konke kumchilizela 
osizini. Noma ungaphuma wena, ukumshiya ekukhonze 
njengoba ngazi, kuwukufa kuye.” 

Waphefumulela phezulu futhi uThabekhulu. 
Okwakumephula umoya kakhulu ukuthi, kuhlala

“Imvamisa yabantu basezweni bakuthanda uma 
kusesebuhleni. Uma ususodakeni bema qekelele 
ngentaba.” 

“Ubani osemi ngentaba MaZondi?” 

“Uyazi Thabekhulu ukuthi ngake ngakubikela ukuthi 
umyeni wami akasenandaba nami. Esikhundleni sokuba 
kube uyena ongiduduzayo akasanginakile nje. Namuhla 

162 

ngikolunye ubishi engifakwe kulo yileso sizungu engisenaso 
nginaye. Nawe usuhambela kude nami. Ungiqhelela 
ngomele ukududuzwa.” Wasukuma ekhala. “Isimo 
sempilo yami sesingibeke ekubeni nginukele izwe.” 
Waphephuka wayongena ekamelweni labo. 

“Ngiyazi phela ukuthi njengoba senginje nje Thabekhulu, 
sengizonukela lonke izwe. Umunwe imvamisa uphakama 
kalula uma ubeka umuntu wesifazane amabala. Umyeni 
wami uzonele angibone, abone isoni. Emzini bazobona 
isikhohlakali senkosikazi. Ngisho kwethu lapho ngizalwa 
khona, umama uzovele achithe izandla. Ngabe kungcono 
ukuba mhlawumbe ubaba usaphila, ngoba yena kumbe 
ubezoke angibuzele ukuthi kuze kube nje nje, kusukaphi.” 

Uzwelo lumbulala uThabekhulu, wamdonsa uMaZondi, 
wamvusa, wamesula futhi izinyembezi. Wamgaxa, 
wasondeza ubuso kobabumanzi bahlangana, bamanzi te 
bobabili yizinyembezi zomunye, bangana. 

“Angazi Nkosi yami ukuthi ngangiweswelelani 
umuzi ngize ngingene ekulingekeni okungaka!” Washo 
ephefumulela phezulu kumshayisa uvalo okwakwenzeka. 
“Umyeni wami ngiyamthanda, nempilo yami iyindumalo 

163 

ngaphandle kwakhe. Nokho, Thabekhulu, ngiyaxolisa 
ukuthi sengize ngalingekela ekubeni ngikuthande. 
Angizenzi. Ngenziwa ukuthi ngaphansi kwephiko lakho 
ngizizwa ngithokomele ngaphansi kophahla lwendlu 
nolothando. Ngeshwa–ke, le ndlu sesiyasha nayo. 
Okudabukisayo yikho ukuthi uma indlu yomshado isisha 
iwela phezu kwabaningi, nezinhlansi zayo ziyaphephuka 
zithungele neminye imizi.” 

Phezu kokududuzana koThabekhulu noMaZondi 
besebobabili, banele behlukana, kwayilowo wahlala 
yedwa emakamelweni ababeke bathi ayevunguza umoya 
womshado. Abajamela amaqiniso awukuthi njengoba 
lalixhoshwe libhekile nje kubo beshadile, base belahlekelwe 
okwakukhona ngokwakungekho. Noma babengaganana, 
umuzi wabo wawungaxhwala. Izindeni zezinhliziyo 
zazazi ukuthi ukuphela kokwethembeka kubo kwakuqede 
nokwethembana. 

Izinsuku zaqhubeka. OMaDlamini noDubazana 
ababengashiswa sazela baya ngokuya nabo bengenwa 
yisifo sokukhathazeka. Babekhathazeka ngakhona uma 
laba bantu ababebavalela bobabili emini sebebukeka 
bewohloka, bephelela emehlweni usuku nosuku. Kwakwala 
uThabekhulu esemphathela umngenandlini uMaZondi, 
inhlanzi namazambane athosiwe, upholoni noshizi, ethi 
uyamduduza, phinde ukududuzeka kwenhliziyo. Ukufa 
komuntu kukabili — ukuya emgodini, nokufa uphila 
usufelwe yisithunzi sokwethembeka. 

Abuya kuDubazana amathemba nothando 
olwalulahlekile. Phezu kwendumalo ayehlangabezane 

164 

nayo empilweni, wabuya umdlandla wokwakha umuzi. 
Abantu ayebabona betibula engcindezelweni, bakha 
imizi kanokusho, njengabo oThabekhulu, baba wugqozi 
lwenqubekelaphambili kuye. Ukuze akwazi ukuthenga 
isitende, akhe, kwakudingeka imali. Wabhunga nomkakhe 
owayesemncisha amehlo. Ngezimpelasonto ezalandela, uma 
engasebenzi, wabonakala ehla enyuka nemigwaqo edayisa 
izindwangu zokugeza ubuso namathawula ayekutitiliza 
mbonini thize. 

ayekwenza wayekuthanda, efisa nokumelekelela. 

Intshisekelo yokumsiza yayishatshalaliswa yimibono yeso 
lengqondo. Laliyibona imizamo yomyeni ifana neyomholi 

owayehola ababeguduza ehlane, ezofinyelela ezweni 

lesethembiso eseyedwa, akade ebahola sebexhoshwe yizintuli 
zogwadule bedukelana naye. UThabekhulu ngakolwakhe 
uhlangothi, wayazi ukuthi uMaZondi kwakumxhwalisa 
ukunganakwa, evama ukusondelana naye amduduze, 

amfunze nomngenandlini ayemphathela wona. Emfihlweni 
yenhliziyo wayefisa ukuba ayesembiza ngesithandwa sakhe 

kumchithekele ayekuthwele kunokuchithekelwa yimizi. 

Ukudideka kunje emagcekeni akwaThabekhulu, 
uMakhosazana wayishaya phansi esibhedlela indodana 
ayetha ngelikaSibonelo. ODubazana nomkakhe baba yinala 
esibhedlela, bemthanda umzukulu wabo owayebafuzile. 
Bahlala ethembeni lokuthi kumbe laliyosheshe litholakale 
ikhambi lokwelapha lo mqedazwe wesifo isaphila indodakazi 
nomzukulu. 

Esayigonile, eyibuka eyiqabula uMakhosazana eyakhe 
yendluzula, unina wasala eyithwele eyakhe inhlekelele 
yempilo. 

** * 

165 

Impahla eyayidayiswa wuDubazana yayithengwa 
ubuthaphuthaphu, imali isimenza azincishe nethuba 
lokuphumula. NangaMgqibelo thize emini kwaba 
wukubuya nje emsebenzini, wathi qu, waphuma

Esibhabhadlolweni selanga wayehamba ebuka eminye

nabo nomkakhe babeyokuwa bevuka, baphethe benawo. 
Nokho, imijuluko yamphazamisa, wacimeza. Wawabeka

zimkhombisa ukuthi zazingaphethe lutho. Zamcela 
ukuba aphakamise izandla, akwenza, zapeketula zadela. 
Zapetulula emithwalweni yakhe. 

“Hhayi, akukhona okwami!” Wayebabaza ethwala 
izandla engawakholwa amehlo eyibona iyimidumba 
yemihwebesha phansi kwamathawula. Phaqa, 
zamkhalela. UmaZondi umbiko wawuthola ngocingo 
olwaluphuma ophikweni lwamaphoyisa ezidakamizwa 
lumtshela nesiteshi umyeni wakhe ayetokele kuso. 

“Lokhu engikuzwayo ngiyakweshwama. UDubazana 
angikaze ngimbone ephethe ngisho umlotha wayo.” 
Kwakusho uMaZondi kuqathaka izinyembezi phambi 
kukaThabekhulu nomkakhe. Bobabili uMaDlamini 
wababuka.

“Ngelinye ilanga niyongikhumbula ngokuthi ngake

Wayemthanda. Itshe elalibehlele noThabekhulu lalehle

Kanti ngakolwakhe uhlangothi naye uThabekhulu

Wayesehlala edikibele, ebalisa buthule engaqedi. 
Maningi amafundululu ayizimfihlo ayephenduka egxabha

okokuqala, ngoba kuthiwa wayelandelana nendoda,

izinyembezi lapho esekhumbula izingane ezilahliwe

Ngokwehluleka kukaThabekhulu ukuthutha

Ngokokuqala ngqa empilweni yazo zafikela ekhaya 

elaliphithene, kumabhekedwane. Noma onina noyise

lapho uMaDlamini abhadama khona umyeni wakhe 
etheleka noMaZondi emini, ibhashile imoto negilosa.

Wayethule sengathi wayengekho endlini besabambisana,

14 


kUhlale kuthiwa okwehlula amadoda kuyabikwa. Isuke 
ingazekeki eyehlula inkosikazi emzini wayo. 

UMaDlamini wayekade evevezeliswa yizinsolo, 
kepha ngokumbona uMxolisi ekhula, eba umyeni 
wakhe efulathele, wajika, wathuthunyeliswa wuvalo 
lokubhidlikelwa wumuzi. Okwakusiqedela isimo esasibucayi 
ukuthi wayenesithombe somyeni wakhe esemncane, egaqa. 
Uma ebuka sona wayebona uMxolisi njengoba enjalo. 
Nokunxoma kwabantu ababefika lapha ekhaya kwakubuye 
kuwuvuthele umlilo. Kwakuba ukuyibona nje ingane, 
noma igaqa, bababaze umhlola, babuze kuye uMaDlamini 
ukuthi kodwa wayeyibelethe nini le ngane eyayiwuyise nje 
uThabizolo? Wayesimuze ankwankwaze nje. 

Abanye omakhelwane ababevele uMaDlamini 
bemzondiswa ukucabanga ukuthi wayezithwele, bavama 
ukuvakasha bezobona lo mboniswano. 

“Kukhona ukufana kwabantu!” Babembulala inhliziyo, 
bekhuluma baze bachithe izandla. “Kanti nihlobene 
nonke yini lapha endlini?” 

Babemshiya edangele, elele embhedeni, ekhala 
ezimathonsi. 

“Kodwa Thabekhulu uyabezwa bonke abantu abafika 
lapha ekhaya ukuthi babaza, babuze bathini ngale ngane 
kaMaZondi?” 

“Basuke bebheda nje ngoba nawe uyabazi abantu 
ukuthi bayathanda ukuzibhedela.” 

“Awukhulume iqiniso kanye nje njengomuntu efa. Yona 

179 

yenziwa yini ngempela ukuba ikufuze kangaka?” 

“Ithini–ke eyinsambatheka impendulo?” 

Wehlisa isikhwehlela uThabekhulu wathi, “Uthi naye 
akazi ukuthi kwenziwa yini, kodwa ucabangela ekutheni 
isizathu singahle sibe ukuthi wayethandiswa ukungibuka 
esakhulelwe.” 

“Akenizwe nje amashwa ami! Khona sekuthiwa 
wayethandiswa, wayeyekelani ukuthandiswa 
amapentshisi namantongomane, azothandiswa 
wena? Ngizoke ngihambe–ke azothola ithuba elenele 
lokukuthandiswa.” 

Igama lomuzi laya ngokuya lihuduleka odakeni. 
Omakhelwane abathile ababengakafundiswa ngokuhlalisana 
nokuphathwa komoya wabantu ababenegciwane 
lengculaza baqala ukuwukhomba ngeminwe umuzi 
kaThabekhulu. Bawubiza ngowemikhuba, bandisa nehaba 
lokuthi wonke umuntu owayephila kuwo wayenalo leli 
gciwane. Inyama yakhona, ikakhulukazi ekaMaZondi 
owayephila ngokuyidayisa komakhelwane, bayipha iso 
ababe besayithenga. Wawa, wahlala phansi wabheka 
uThabekhulu emehlweni. 

Babuya bebuyile abebandla bethi bazovuselela, nabo 

bafike bashaywe amahloni ngokubona uThabekhulu 

wakwasiqashi egaqa ebaleni. Wathi uMaDlamini eqambe 
ebanekela isifuba wawusumkhulu umonakalo ekhaya. 
Bawa phansi bakhuleka, bemkhalela ngababembiza 
ngoSathane owayemcuthele emasangweni esonto 
wamhlangabeza khona. Babemduduza ngokumnxusa 

180 

ngokuba angabe esakubheka okwasemhlabeni, kepha 
abheke phezulu eZulwini. 

Okwalandela kwaThabekhulu kwaba wukuba 
uthando olwaluke lwaphuma endlini lwahlala emnyango, 
lwabaleka nakhona. Esikhundleni salo, sacambalala 
sanja eduze komnyango isehlukaniso. Ukwehluleka 
kokuzelapha kwenyanga kwabonakala lapho. Amazwi 
ajulile ababelapha ngawo abakwaDubazana eduka 
nokudideka. Leso sixhwala senhliziyo yomkaMpanza 
owayesehlala ethithibele sasiguli, sathinteka. Asibange 
sisazi nokuthi kwakufanele senzenjani lapho lezi zingane 
ezimbili, uSibonelo noMxolisi bevama ukuya kuye, 
omunye entenga, omunye egaqa. Babefika baziphonse 
ezingalweni zakhe. Okukanye uma engamnakile 
uMxolisi, amkotele bese embuka emamatheka. 
Ingenacala ingane, wayimoyizelela ekubibithekeni. 

NgoMsombuluko ekuseni, esecabange kwaphela 
ukucabanga uMaDlamini, wanele wahamba umyeni 
wakhe, wabutha izimpahlana zakhe ezithile. Washiya 
engasavalelisanga nakuvalelisa. Amabombo wawabhekisa 
kwabo eChesterville ezethembisa ukuthi wayesayophumuza 
ingqondo. Ihora leshumi lamshayela esebhasini elalibheke 

181 

ekhaya, lihaza naye ngoBooth Road. Lalinqamula phakathi 
kwamahlashana, amaqele namagqunyana ayesaphenduka 
ihlane ngemuva kokuthuthwa koMkhumbane. 
Kwakumnyama amehlo. 

Washaya insimbi, wehla, wahamba ephephuka waze 
wayongena kwabo. Wayengasindwa yimithwalo, kepha 
esindwa amahloni okubuya emendweni. Ngemuva kokuba 
engqongqozile, kwaba yisikhashana, kwase kuvula 
intokazi eyayikhanya, ibukeka, isemashumini amathathu 
nento. 

“Awu, kanti nguwe dadewethu?” Yambuza imoyizela, 
imbuka ngemahlo ayedangele. 

“Yimina mkamfowethu.” Wangena wahlala kusofa, 
umthwadlana wakhe wawubeka phambi kwakhe, wesula 
ubuso obase bujuluka. Babingelelana noMaMngoma 
owayengumkankosana yakwabo uVusumuzi. 

“Usaphumule namhlanje MaMngoma?” 

“Umuntu usaphumule kulesi sitolo sethu umuntu 
asebenza kuso nangezimpelasonto.” 

182 

Baxoxa eziningi okwagqama kuzo usizi 
olwalukhungethe lo muzi. Olwalugqame kunazo zonke 
olokugcwala kwendlu. Odadewabo abane nabafowabo 
ababili base bezele bagcwalisa indlu. Kubo bonke 
babili kuphela ababesebenza, oGugulethu noVusi, 
kanye–ke nonina. Insebenzo yalaba abanye yayingacaci. 
Babebamba namuhla bayeke ngomuso. 

Esenamahloni uMaDlamini ngokuzibona ezoba 
omunye umthwalo, wamduduza uMaMngoma ngokuthi 
wayezoxoxa nabo. Umalokazana wakwabo wasukuma, 
wamenzela itiye, emgcobela nezinkwa. Baliphunga, 
wayesexolisa emshiya eyohlanza izingubo. 

Wasala yedwa endlini yokuphumula ehlezi nemithwalo 
yakhe ayengazi ukuthi wayezoyifaka kuliphi ikamelo. 
Nokho, wagcina eyithathile wayifaka ekamelweni 
likanina athi uma esebubukisisa kahle ubungako balo, 
linemibhede emibili, newadilobhu, akaze ayibona eyakhe 
indawo. Wahlala yedwa enesizungu kwaze kwantambama 
lapho babuya khona oThokozile, oNtombifuthi, 
oThembeni, nonina uMaMbonambi ayemfuze 
beyizithupha. Bahlanganisa–ke amakhanda ekamelweni, 
bakhalelana. Abanye babekhala ngomkamfowabo 
owayebabalisela ngokubondlela izingane. Abanye bekhala 
ngomfowabo uVusi ababemusho ukulungisa okwemvu, 
emthobele umkakhe ngoba nakhu wayesamshaya 
ngaphakathi wamqeda ngentando. Nonina wakhala 
ezimathonsi, ebalisa ngokufelwa umyeni. Wabalisa 
akaqeda futhi nalapho inkosazana yakwakhe isimxoxela 
ukuthi yayihlezi emanzini, iziveza kancane izinkinga 

183 

zomuzi, kepha iwafihla amahlazo awo. 

Kwaphekwa, kwadliwa, kwalalwa, unyawo ungeke 
usalufaka ngisho ekhishini. UMaDlamini wazumeka 
kusa, ikade ingamshiyi imicabango imbekela imifanekiso 
yokwakwenzeka kwakhe. Kwakukade kukhona 
nethenjana lokuthi umyeni wakhe wayezofike ashayeke, 
angene emotweni azomfuna. Nalelo themba laliye 
ngokushabalala ngokukhala kwamaqhude okusa. 

Yize uThabekhulu wayefike watshelwa uMaZondi 
ukuthi umkakhe wayeqoqe okunye okungokwakhe 
wahamba, wahlalela ethembeni lokuthi uzobuya. Lathi 
lapho liyoshona ilanga, kuthi zibaba, indoda yase 
ilunguze ngefasitela yaze yakhathala. Yayisize yema 
phandle ithalaza ubala. Wabuyela ekamelweni labo 
alizwa namuhla libanda, lishweza unyela losizi. Empeleni 
indlu yonke yayibanda ilambile, yomele ukuthokomaliswa 
yinkosikazi yamathongo akhona. Ukuhamba ngale 
ndlela komkakhe ayesehlale iminyaka ngeminyaka naye 
kusukela ebusheni babo, kwayibibithekisa izinyembezi 
inhliziyo. Wahlala wathi khovololo, embhedeni, eseyizwa 
inhliziyo imenekela amaqiniso okuthi wayemthanda 
engazenzisi umkakhe. Kwakusabhoke nomcabango 
wokuba avele angene emotweni anikele ekhweni 
ayombheka ngesikhathi ehluleka ukuzibamba, 
umzwangedwa umphahlukisa, ezishaya idolo ekhuluma 
yedwa, ebalisa. 

UMaZondi owayekade edlula ngasemnyango ngesikhathi 
ekhuluma, wema walalelisisa indlebe eyinamathelise 

184 

esivalweni, ezwa izigi zenhliziyo yakhe igida.Wanele 
wathula, wamngqongqozela kancane. 

“Uthini–ke MaZondi?” Wabuza lumshaya uvadlwana. 

“Hhayi, angisho lutho yise kaMx … baba Thabekhulu. 
Bengizobuza nje ukuthi, hhawu, kanti kwaba njalo?” 

Wathwala amehlo uThabekhulu wathi, “Angiqondisisi 
ukuthi uthini. Uthi kwaba njalo uma kwakwenzenjani?” 

“Qha, bengizokuncoma nje ngokuthi, kwaze kwakuhleke 
Thabekhulu wazisholo wena, mlomo wakho ukuthi 
uwena owabophisa umyeni wami. Udonsa nje ngoba wena 
wawuphephisa umuzi wakho eziphepheni eziyimina.”

“Uma ngabe ukhona omunye ohlezi naye lapha endlini, 
uyena osho njalo. Ngangithi uyakwazi ukumela iqiniso. 
Sekwenzenjani manje?” 

Wabakaza uThabekhulu, wamisa nezindlebe sengathi

“Ngisayolanda uMxolisi yise ukuze uzongicacisela

“Ngicela uvule isifuba sakho yise, ungitshele ukuthi 

185 

ubani ngempela owabophisa uDubazana?”

“Mina angikwazi ukuqamba amanga Thabekhulu, 
nengane futhi uyayibona iyazisho.” 

Sengathi wayesefuna ukukhala uThabekhulu,

Ngamehlo ayelokoza ngale kwezinyembezi wambuka

“Ngabona khona ukuthi ngangizochithekelwa yikho

Akaphendulanga uMaZondi esasikhihla.

Manje uma ekubuza ngoyise kaMxolisi, usungabika

“Okwasemhlabeni! Ukuze kuphephe umuzi negama

186 

phezu kwalo.”

“Njengoba sengike ngasho, mntakababa, uyazi ukuthi

Ngesinye isikhathi isihe siyisife.”

187 

“Sengobonga lokho yise okungasiza ekuwuphephiseni 

nothando. UDubazana useyophuma azibonele naye ukuthi

Wathatha umntanakhe waya ngasemnyango.

ngilitholephi ikamelo.”

Nakwamabili, ngesikhathi intombi yakhe nayo 
ngale eChesterville ingabuthi quthu, nakuye ngapha 
babungehli. A, inkumbulo yomkakhe! Naye kwamsobozela

Kambe uma kwakuqhubeka kanje, okwakwenza

Wayethandazela nokuba kusheshe kuse, nokuba athi uma

Kwasa wasebenza engazizwa nokuthi wayenzani, elokhu

“Ungangishiyi bo, Mondise!” Indoda ayeyiqhweba 

isiphuma ngesango yayimfishane, imakhwembana,

188 

buzidlubha.

Ungaze ungibone ngihamba nje, kanti izinto zingitshekele.” 

“Akusho wena Thabekhulu, kusho ubuso ukuthi 
awumnandi neze.” 

UThabekhulu wamholela emotweni yakhe lapho

Ekamelweni elincane ngiqashisile, nasekhishini 
futhi. Edaningilumu, nakuba esekhona oqashile,

189 

uMondise. Indlu yayingenye yezaziyimihubhe eyayimumethe

Egwinya izinyembezi uMaZondi yabubula naye futhi

Ihora lesihlanu ntambama ngoLwesibili lashaya 
imoto yoThabekhulu ibubula kuye uBooth Road. Umculo

UMaDlamini owayezihlalele endlini yokuphumula 
wayibona, inhliziyo yakhe yagxuma, yathuka ukwethuka,

ngasemnyango sangane eyayinamahloni.

190 

“Hlala kosithandayo isihlalo Thabekhulu.”

yise kaThabethule.” 
Wambuka ngayemangele uThabekhulu, wabuza wathi:

191 

“Kanti njengoba sengike ngasho nje, thina

NgolWesiNe kusihlwa, ligamenxe ihora 

lesishiyagalolunye, isitimela esasivela eGoli silibangise 
eThekwini saphuma eMgungundlovu sekumnyama. 
Sanyathela kancane sigudla intaba, sizibuka amanxa, 
seqa umgwaqo oya eYideni, sibhekana nesiteshi 
iPentrich. Sedlula nakuso ngesizotha qede saholobha seqa 
imifula nemihosha, izintaba sizithubeleza emathunjini. 
Izihambi ezazikulesi sitimela zase zikhathele, eningini 
lazo kungasekho nakubuka ngamafasitela. Kwakufanele 
ukuba eziningi zilale njengoba zase zizilalele, zilolozelwa 
umculo wamasondo ensimbi edl’ ezinye igadula 
igid’ ingidane. Sasilokhu sisuke ngayizolo kusihlwa 
eGoli. Imini eningi sasiyichithe simi ezinkangala 
ngaseMatiwane lapho kwakwenzeke khona inhlekelele 
yengozi ngokuphaphalaza kwesitimela esithwala 
impahla. 

Ususithele uMgungundlovu, isitimela sesidukuza 
emnyameni, siwedlula uMlazi, iNkambathawini 
neKitolishi, ephasijini lezinye zezinqola kwakumi 
uDubazana owayephuce ikhanda. Wayegqoke izingubo 
nezicathulo okwakusolisa ukuthi ngahle ukuba 
kwakungokwesiboshwa. Isitimela sedlula koGeorgedale 
nakoHammarsdale, sibuka amadwala eCliffdale, 
wayelokhu emile, ejolozele umnyama. Wayeyibuka 
phambili inhloko imise izimpondo, ivuke uhlanya 
sandlondlo enogedla, ithungatha uThungulu. Nempela 
wayephuma khona ejele, eKandaspense. Wayemi laphaya 

194 

nje wayenesizungu nokuzenyeza. Abantu abambalwa 
ayesele nabo kukhophathimenti wayebashayisa ngomoya, 
ebaphumuza nasekuhlahleni amehlo bambuka sasilahlwa, 
bengamethembi. Nemithwalo yabo babeyibambele eduze. 

Wayezibuza eziphendula nje, umkakhe wayelele 
zu, ekamelweni amshiya kulo. Engalweni yakhe 
kwakuqamele uMxolisi ayengamazi yena uDubazana, 
kepha eze waba uMxolisi nje ngoba kuzoxoliswa kuye. 
Wayekhathele umkakhe, ehlale imini yonke esibhedlela 
lapho ayekade ephuthumise khona uMakhosazana 
nomntanomntanakhe uSibonelo ababehlatshwe 
umkhuhlane. Nabo babegcine ngokulaliswa esibhedlela. 

195 

UNkosana owayenganakiwe kangako wayethe cu, 
embhedeni elele. Owayengazumekile uThabekhulu 
owayecabangana nomkakhe. Wayebala izinsuku 
ezazisele anduba athuthe uMaZondi kubuye umkakhe 
ayemkhumbule ngalobo busuku kangangokuba wayeze 
waqamela ephinifweni lakhe. UThabekhulu wayezizwa 

Ujantshi ezinkalweni wawusaqhuma, noDubazana 
elokhu ewujolozele umnyama ecabanga. A, wakhumbula. 
Kambe kwakuyiso lesi sitimela ayefike ngaso eThekwini 
evela emakhaya. Kwakuyiso futhi ayenyuke ngaso 
kaninginingi eseyisiboshwa esendelwa emakhaya. 
Kwakuyisona nesasike samthwala efake ozankosi, 
eqhutshwa eyodonsa iminyaka eMazambaneni. Namuhla 
wayebuya ekudonseni eminye iminyaka ngamaphilisi 
ezidakamizwa ayekade engakaze awabone ngisho 
kwaMadala eJudeni. Namanje, njengoba sase sehlisa 
ijubane nje, simpongoloza eJongishani sibona iTheku, kazi 
wayeyophelelaphi kulo mnyama, kuse edwanguza kuziphi 
izinkalo?” 

Sekuya kwamabili isitimela sema nse, eThekwini 
esiteshini. Wehla watholoza engasenathemba lokuthola 
esasiya eMlazi. Engakalindeli, saqhamuka esokugcina. 
Basho phakathi kwasuka amaphepha. Kwathi 
sekukwamabili sabhobokela eMlazi. 

Wehla uZwelisha esiteshini eZwelethu. Kambe izwe 
lethu lelo elalinezidlidli zezindlu okwakulala izinyokotho 
kuzo, kungekho ngisho indawo yokuphenduka. Isimo 
sasiphambene nemithetho yempilo, nokulunga, namasiko. 
Kungasekho bhasi natekisi, walishaya phansi esezidelile 
nasezigebengwini. 

Kwase kwesabeka phandle, namafu emkhathini 
eseziphendula imifanekiso ethile eyayingamabhayi 

196 

ayelenga emazulwini. Esewele umfula iMfongosi 
inyanga yamlunguza kancane ngaphansi kwamafu, 
isilengele ezintabeni. Kwasuka nomoya, wahamba 

Ngenhlanhla isango elincane lalingahluthulelwe. 
Eseshaywa wuvalo lokuthi kazi umkakhe nabantwana 

wayesayobafica yini, benjani, wanyonyoba wazungeza 

indlu. Wayesaba nokukhuleka ngaleso sikhathi sobusuku. 
Wema maqondana nekamelo ayeboshwe esabhace kulo, 
wangqongqoza kancane efasiteleni. 

UMaZondi owayelele obokufa wakuzwa kancane, 
saphushana lokho kushayeka kwefasitela sengathi 
lalithelwa amathonsi emvula. Ngokuphikelela kwequpha 
waphaphama, wathwala amehlo. Esaba ngisho ukubuza 
ukuthi wayengubani lowo, wathi lacu esukuma. Wayithi 
thasi ingane waphuma endiza ekamelweni wayongena 
nezivalo kwelikaThabekhulu owayevele naye emise 
izindlebe. 

“Yini, kwenzenjani?” Wabuza ethuka. 

“Kukhona umuntu okade engqongqoza ngale 
ekamelweni.” Wayehleba. 

Wahleba naye uThabekhulu ebuza ethi, “Uthi uwubani?” 

“Ngesaba ngisho ukumbuza.” 

Washaya futhi umunwe efasiteleni, usuqala ukuqinisa 
kancane. Wabheka iwashi engalweni uThabekhulu wathi, 
“Futhi ngeke kwaba uDubazana ngalesi sikhathi sosuku. 
Ake sizwe.” Wamhola, baphuma bangena kwayebaleke 
kulo eselandela. Wabuza uThabekhulu eqinisa izwi ethi, 
“Ubani lowo?” 

“Yimina uDubazana mfowethu.” Laphendulela phansi 
izwi lowayeshayekile. 

“Hhawu Nkosi yami! Hhawu we Ma! Nangu 
uDubazana! Ngaze ngafa namhlanje! Ngizoya ngicashe 

197 

kwamabani bakithi?” Wayevevezela esephumile 

uma uDubazana wayezovulelwa ngasekhishini, yena 
wayezophulukundlela ngomnyango owawungaphambili. 

“Kulungile–ke Dubazana, yiya emnyango ongaphambili 
ngizokuvulela.” Washo uThabekhulu ngemuva kokuba 
elembule kancane ikhethini waqiniseka ngokuthi 
kwakunguye ngempela. 

“Ngizothini ngoMxolisi?” Wabuza bedideka ephasijini, 
beshayisana bobabili. 

“Uma ekubuza, ushone ngapha nangapha, umphendule 
ngezimpendulo ezingezwakali.” 

“Ezingezwakali kanjani?” 

“Ngakutshela nje ngathi ubothi uyise umuntu 
ongamazi owakukhohlisa awaphinde wambona,” washo 
emshiya eqonda emnyango. 

“Kodwa ngizowaqamba kanjani amanga ngingakwazi 
Thabekhulu?” Wabuza esesele yedwa ephasijini. 
Ngokudideka ayeseyikho, waphenduka watatazela 
wangena ekamelweni lakhe uThabekhulu. Emi ebakaza, 
kwamfikela ukuba ingane ayishiye khona ekamelweni 
likayise ukuze iphephe, aziyele kumyeni wakhe emsulwa. 
Ngesikhathi ephuma ekamelweni likaThabekhulu, 
eseyishiye embhedeni ingane, amehlo akhe azithela 
kwawomyeni wakhe owayesanda kuhlala kusofa endlini 
yokuphumula, maqondana nephasiji. Wakhutshwa 
wubala, phose wavuma phansi. Ezizwa efikelwa yisinxi, 
waphephuka, wantingaza endlini yokuphumula. Amehlo 
kaDubazana elokhu egxile kuye engasuki wamesaba 
elahlwa nawunembeza. Wazethuka esehlezi sihlalweni 
sinye noThabekhulu, belinganisene bebuka uDubazana 
owayekwesasibhekene nabo. Naye uDubazana ebabuka, 
wadideka uqobo lokudideka. 

198 

“Siyakubingelela Dubazana.” Wayebingelelwa 
uThabekhulu embuka ngamehlo ayegwajaza. 
NoDubazana ecwayizisa awakhe ayethuswa yizindonga 
ayengasazejwayele, nokwenza kwakhona kumthunaza, 
wavuma. Babuzana impilo baba ngababephila bonke. 
Khona manjalo ekamelweni likaThabekhulu yasho ingane 
ngengila. Babukana futhi oThabekhulu noMaZondi 
bejiyelwe ingqondo. 

Bamupha amehlo ayemzekela ubuze babo. 

Yabelesela ingane ikhala ayanqamuka, kepha 
nonina wabekezela engasazi nokuthi wayebekezelele 
inini. Kwaba ukukhala kwayo isixhilwa okwamenza 
wasukumisa okwezeze, wandiza eyongena ekamelweni 
likaThabekhulu. Wayifica isikhiphe amehlwana wayithi 
thasi, waphuma nayo endiza, wafike wema nayo phambi 
kukayise ethi, “Nkosi yami, yise, nansi ingane yami 
ixhilelwa ukufa!” Washo eyiphephetha. “Phaphama 
mkhulu! Phaphama Thabekhulu.” Wayithakazela. 

Ngesikhathi unina nendodana bephephethana bejuluka, 
uDubazana wamfoma. Wathi uyayesula imijuluko 
yageleza ngenkani yamxhopha. Abuya amehlo engane, 
yambuka unina yamumoyizelela, qede yakhala. 

“Thula baba khulu.” Wahlala phansi unina eceleni 
kukaThabekhulu, wakhipha incence, wayincelisa. 

UThabekhulu weswela umgodi wokucasha. 
UDubazana wawacikica amehlo, wawesula, wakubukisisa 
okwakwenzeka engaphuphi. Edidekile, wabuza wathi, 
“Angedukile nje? Ngikhona impela kwaThabekhulu lapho 
engaboshwa ngiqashe khona, nalapho engashiya khona 

199 

isithandwa senhliziyo yami esiwumkami?” 

“Ngiyabuza bakithi, ngicela impendulo. Uma ngempela 
ngisemzini engiwushoyo, ngicela ukubona umkami 
osekukade ngamgcina. Sengimkhumbule.” 

Amehlo kaDubazana awashayisa sambani 
akaThabekhulu, wabakaza umninimuzi wathi, “Ukhona 
impela kwaThabekhulu. Umkakho osumkhumbule uye 
impela lona.” Wamkhomba ngekhanda. 

“Thabekhulu, ngizwe ngingezwa uma ekubiza ngoyise 
wengane ebixhilwa, eyithakazela ngoThabekhulu. 
Thabekhulu, ngibona ngingaboni ukuthi ngabe uye 
ngempela lona oncelisa umntanakho!” Avutha umlilo 
amehlo akhe, ahlengezela izinyembezi. “Uwena uyise?” 

“Buza kunina.” 

“Ngisho ngoba ngimbone eyilanda ekamelweni lakho.” 

“Ungene khona naye nezivalo ngoba ethuswa uwena 
umngqongqozela kwamabili.” 

“MaZondi, nkosikazi wakwaDubazana, nina 
kaMakhosazana noNkosana, owakwabani lo mntwana

Kwashuba umoya endlini kubukwana ngeziqu 
zamehlo. KuMaZondi zabe sezigeleza izinyembezi 
ziqathakela kumntwana ayemncelisa. 

“Musa ukungithela ngezinyembezi MaZondi. Bengibuze 
nje kuphela ukuthi owakwabani umntwana onceliswayo?” 

Wagwinya amathe uMaZondi, wankwankwaza ethi, 
“Oka … owakwa … ngicela ungixolele Nkosi yami bandla 
Dubazana!” Kwehla imvula yazo. 

“Ungakulindela kanjani ukuxolelwa iqiniso 
ungakalikhulumi? Ngiphendule, ngibuzile.” 

Phinde impendulo. 

“Cishe sengenza iphutha ngokukubuza izindaba zomuzi 

200 

wethu endlini yokuphumula, siphambi komninimuzi 
nokusho. Ngicela siyozixoxela ekamelweni le… uThabekhulu 
asisiza ngalo.” Wasukuma. UMaZondi, ehlezi ephelelwe

Sengathi babetshelene noyise kaMxolisi, izikhwehlela 
bazishayela phansi baziphindelela kanye kanye. Kwathi 

sasiyilona lulimi ababetshelana okuthile ngalo. Ingane

uhlwitha itshwele ephikweni lesikhukhukazi. 

Wakhala uMaZondi elula izingalo ethi, “Dubazana, 
ngiyavuma, ngonile, kepha ngicela ungangibulaleli ingane 
yami!” 

Wambuka ngamehlo ayelanguka umlilo uDubazana 
wathi, “Aliphume liqhasha iqiniso eliyisiqiniseko sokusinda 
kwengane!” Wayibukisisa ingane. Yambuka nayo ingazi 
nokuthi lalidumephi. 

“Ngishilo nje Dubazana ngathi eyami.” 

“Uyise?” Wayibukisisa futhi kwamsolisa okwakuke 
kwasolwa nangabaningi. ‘Noma uyena uThabekhulu lona?” 

Wawabona amehlo omyeni wakhe esefana nawebhubesi

“Yebo, Dubazana kunjengoba usuzibonele.” 

Wayibukisisa futhi uDubazana. Nakuye, njengoba 
yayike yenza nakuMaZondi, yambuka yamumoyizelela. 

“Hhayi, sidalwa seNkosi esingenacala, ngingaxabana

Wamamatheka naye anduba ambuyisele kunina uMxolisi. 

Nalokho kumamatheka kwakhe kwamthinta emoyeni 
uMaZondi, wamemukela umntwana ebonga, akwabe 
kusavuma nokuba ahlale naye phansi. 

Ubuhlungu bokuzibona engasenamuzi uDubazana 
bamephula amalungu kwaxega amadolo, wahlala phansi. 

201 

“Sekuyangicacela–ke ukuthi ngize ngiboshwe nje 
kwakusukelephi.” 

“Lelo phutha ngiyalemukela Thabekhulu. Nami 
sengingedwa kwalasha enangiphonsa kuwo ngalibona

phutha.” Wambheka ngamehlo ayemncenga. “Angazi

“Oxolisayo uyaxolelwa Dubazana. Ngiyakuxolela impela.” 

“Ngiyabonga. Iphutha lami kodwa lalingasho 
ukuthi ngothando lwenu ngibophiseni, ningingcwabe

Wakhungatheka uThabekhulu enamahloni

“Wazicoshela owesiqashi, isihlupheki. Wazitapela efeni

Esamile uMaZondi eshushuzela umntwana ayesamgonile,

bani ngokuqina kokushuba kwamazwi phakathi kwala 

202 

madoda amabili. Ngokwenaba kwenkulumo ukuphehlana

kuThabekhulu. Akabange esamthatha nangamankomane,

Izwa ubuhlungu indoda yabubula ithi, “Impela nawe

“Angikudayisi yise kaMakhosazana kepha

Wayekhuluma ehefuzelela phezulu engasazizwa nokuthi 
wayethini. 

UDubazana wawezwa evutha amehlo sengathi

203 

esathuswe amandla ebhubesi ayewabone kumyeni wakhe,

“Qha, uphele inkani manje. Ngeke esaba nempi. 
Mdedele!” 

Okungahle ukuba wayeseyalela uDubazana, wajanquza,

“Myeke Thabekhulu! Ngadela ikwethu ngaye lo

Njengomuntu ebuyisela itshe elinemamba,

“Dubazana! Dubazana! Hhawu, we Mkhululi wami 

204 

ngiboniswani emhlabeni!” Wawa ngamadolo waguqa

UThabekhulu uvalo lwamshaya lwameqa wathi

“Yise kaMakhosazana, vuka yise wabantabami. 
Vuka phela mntakababa.” Wayesaguqe eceleni kwakhe

Wafola, wamesula ubuso, wabanga. Wathi ukhihla isililo,

“Qinisela nina kaMxolisi. Kube yiphutha nje lamawala

“Kodwa yise kaMxolisi usale usuqinisa isandla nje

“Ngicela ungabe usakhala singakahlanganisi ukuthi

beke bakuzwa ukhihla isililo, siyobe sesiboshiwe. 

205 

Ngiyakuncenga, thula.” Wamesula izinyembezi 
ngeminwe. Waphefumulela phezulu uMaZondi esivalela

noma ngingafa ukufa kungifanele. Ukufa kwakho 
kungadala izintandane ezingenabani.” 

UDubazana wayesathambalele phansi. Ukuba 
wayengaphinde avuke, aphinde ahleke nje impela 
nabo, wayengabe ugila iziga. UThabekhulu wayesagone 
ikhanda lomfelokazi, umbulawa emjolozele ngamehlo
