umhloniphise ngokumcimezisa.” 

“Ngimcimezise uma kwenzenjani kodwa Thabekhulu?” 

“Ngiyaxolisa MaZondi. Ngibona sengathi akasekho.” 

“Akasekho uma eyephi?” Wasukuma waphephukela 
kuyena, wabhabhalala phezu kwakhe, wamphathaphatha 
ubuso. Wayeseqala ukubanda. Wabalisa akangaqeda. 

“Ukubalisa ngeke kusasisiza MaZondi. Uma sekunje, 
ngicela udele, uqinisele, umcimezise.” 

“Hhawu, nsizwa kaDubazana, ngaze ngabuzwa 
ubuhlungu ngawe namuhla emhlabeni! Angazi ukuthi angifi 
ngani manje ngilale nami ngilinganisane nawe!” Esemanzi 
te, uDubazana yizinyembezi ezaziqathakela ebusweni 
bakhe, umkakhe wayibeka iminwe emehlweni akhe. 
Wazivala phaqa izahluko zempilo ngokumcimezisa. 

Wasukuma umfelokazi ephephukela esihlalweni. 
Bathwala amehlo bobabili bethuswa ukuvuleka kwesivalo 

206 

sekamelo elalilala uNkosana. Kanye kanye bamkhaca 
esaphuma ethi uyongena endlini encane bethi, “Emuva 
wena!” 

“Cishe le ngane ibonile.” Washo uMaZondi ehefuzelela 
phezulu engqondweni yakhe uhlaluka umfanekiso wokufa 
kwabo belenga ePitoli. 

“Noma ubengebe nasiqiniseko sokuthi uyise ushonile, 
uzosoliswa yilezi zinyembezi zakho esengike ngakukhuza 
ngazo nakuqala. Ngizocela–ke manje uzesule zome geqe, 
uma usathanda ukuphilela abantabakho.” Wathetha. 

Wazesula zaphikelela zageleza. 

“Kunganjani sicishe lapha endlini, bese simdedela lo mfana 
wakho angene endlini encane, bese simkhiyela esebuyele?” 

Bavumelana, uThabekhulu wasukuma wamhudulela 
endlini yokudlela uDubazana, wayeseqonda ekamelweni 
elalilala uNkosana. Walunguza emtshela ukuthi 
wayengakhululeka angene endlini yokuzikhulula. 
Nempela, uNkosana owayehlezi embhedeni, ebambelele 
esihlathini, wasukuma, waphuma, wangena. Wabuyela 
ekamelweni angena kulo qede zamkhalela izihluthulelo. 

“Kuyasa khona manje. Asingabe sisachitha sikhathi!” 
Wahleba uThabekhulu esebuyela khona endlini yezidumo. 
“Awuthathe itshali lakhe umembese ngokushesha, 
sibonisane ukuthi simenzenjani?” 

Walabhuzela uMaZondi, wawalanda amabili. 
Elinye wamembesa ngalo umyeni, elinye walithi bhu, 
emahlombe, walembatha. UThabekhulu wawacisha 
wonke amalambu ayesakhanya ngaphakathi, wahlala 
basondelana noMaZondi, bahleba. 

“Alikho elinye icebo elingacishe lisisindise ngaphandle 

207 

kokuba manje simthwale, siye naye hlathini thize. 

ejele. Kungcono ngoba akananxeba. Noma angatholakala 
ngandlela thize engakonakali, nodokotela kahulumeni 
phose adideke ngoba kadeni ufe ngokuklinywa. 
Useyohlawumbisela. Angazi ukuthi ubona kanjani?” 

“Ngiboneni mntanomuntu ngingakaze ngibulale muntu 
selokhu ngazalwa?” 

“Nami angikaze. Ngiyaqala nje. Nacebo leli 
engilicabangayo angazi noma lizosikhuba yini.” 
Lalimenyelisa elokubulala. Kwathuleka sebethuswa 
nayikhasi elalihashaza phandle. “Ayikho enye indlela. 
Angifune ucingo ungibambise.” 

“Ngingakusiza kanjani kodwa ngoba uma ngishiya 
ingane lapha izokhala ibe wuhlanya? Ngeke futhi 
kwalunga uma ngingena nayo emotweni ihogela umoya 
womuntu ongasekho ingaka.” 

“Ayikho enye indlela. Namhlanje izongena naye. Nawe 
futhi angisakwethembi. Uma ngikushiya wedwa lapha 
endlini, ungahle ungidonsele amehlo abantu ngesililo. 
Kungcono umntwana akhale emotweni sihamba naye.” 
Iqunga laqala ukuzisho, amehlo kaThabekhulu afana 
nawohlanya, alokoza umlilo. Uye lowaya ephuma engena 
egalaji, ebuya nocingo. Kwadingeka ukuba akhanyise 
endlini eyayilele isidumbu anduba asiqalange ngalo 
ucingo. 

“Ngicela ungibambise–ke simfake emotweni.” 

Lahlala phansi itshali kuMaZondi, wabamba imilenze, 
uThabekhulu emahlombe. Basilahla phansi bethuswa 
ukukhala kweqhude phandle. 

“Nx, yileli qhude nje! Ngibambise,” kusho 
uThabekhulu. Kumnyama emehlweni bamdidizelisa. A, 

208 

ukusinda kwensizwa ishone isashisa! Baphephuka naye 
bangena egalaji, wafakwa ebhuthini. Bayivala babuyela 
ekamelweni likaThabekhulu lapho uMaZondi athatha 
khona umntwana. Kwaba yizithuba eziningana ezama 
ukuyibeletha ingane, phose ayibuthe phansi. Wagcina 
eyisongile, baphuma, bahluthulela, bangena emotweni 
eyangena umgwaqo lapho inyanga ishona ithi gqwambi 
ngale kwezintaba. Waqale wayinyonyobisa uThabekhulu. 
Ngokudeda kwayo komakhelwane, zaya kakhulu idukuza 
umnyama. UMazondi uMlazi owayewazi ngaleyo ndlela 
nje, emini futhi, wagcina engasazi ngempela ukuthi 
yayisidukuzaphi. Yagcina iphumile elokishini yadukuza 
endaweni eyayingasenagesi, inomnyama owawukhasa 

leli. Yewukela, yaphuma emgwaqweni, yanhlanhlatha 
isibhekene nokwakusantabakazi emnyama. Yaye yema 
bude buduze nomfula owawucwebezela enzansi. 

“Asimqukule simshiye ehlathini.” 

“Awu bakithi! Yihlathi leli elimnyama kangaka? Kodwa 
asizukucandwa yizindlondlo nje lapha?” 

“Ngabe nazo zisisizile zasiphumuza kulobu buhlungu 
bamalahle esiwathwele ngezinhliziyo. Asisheshise kungaze 
kukhanye.” Washaya ijazi lakhe, wakhipha nethoshi 
emotweni, walifaka esakeni lekhukhu laleli jazi. 

“Ingane izosala nobani lapha emotweni?” 

“Noma ingakhala, uma sivale amafasitela, angikholwa 
ukuthi kulo mhlaba esikuwo ukhona ongayizwa.” 

Sebehlile, babambisana. UThabekhulu wahefuzelela 
phezulu wazama ukuluqukula uthathamela lwesidumbu. 
Yibo labaya nalo uMaZondi ehamba ekhutshwa wubala, 
ewa evuka. Baze bangena esinindolweni sehlathi 
lapha abaqala khona ukubona ukukhanya. Bethuswa 
wukukhanya lokhu kukakhanyikhanyi. Bekhathele ulimi 

209 

lulenga, isidumbu abasibekanga phansi, saziwela. 

Nempela wasiqukula, senyuka kancane esehline 
eyingolovane uThabekhulu egatsheni. Kwathi phazi, 
sadedeleka, samdudula uMaZondi. Wathi ethi fofobala 
phansi, sasiwela phezu kwakhe. 

“Hhawu kodwa Nkosi yami! Dubazana ngenzeni?” 

“Yeka ukubalisa njalo! Uzoze usibophise!” Wafutheka 
egxumela phansi. Wasivusa futhi isidumbu esase silele 
mbo ngekhanda esifubeni somkaso, wasidudulela eceleni. 
Babonisana, wamelekelela uMaZondi wamqukulela 
egatsheni ayekade ehlezi kulo. Watibula, wasiqukulela 
phezulu. Sesiwudedele impela umhlaba wathi, 
“Usungabopha–ke!” 

Wabopha uMaZondi, salenga. Wagxumela 
kuThabekhulu owamuthi qithi phansi qede wacaca 
wayosiqalanga egatsheni ngendlela ayethemba ukuthi 
yayingezukubanansolo kwezikadalawane. Esenelisekile, 
wagxumela phansi naye, base bephakamisa ubuso 
besibukisisa isidumbu esasilokhu siphenduphenduka 
kancane sabhantshi lenekwe ngekhothenga ocingweni. 
Enkumbulweni kaMaZondi ayelokhu ethi bani … bani … 
amazwi kaDubazana lapho ethi, “Hhawu, kodwa ngawe 
MaZondi mkami ngikuthanda kangaka uyangidayisa?” 
Zamfinineka izinyembezi. 

“Engingakuqondisisi kahle ukuthi konje uma 
umuntu ezibulele uyacimeza noma uyawaqhunsula 
yini amehlo?” Wathula ecabanga uThabekhulu. 

210 

“Kodwa kufanele ukuba uyawaqhunsula ngoba asuke 
ezocinyeziswa wubani?” Wacaca futhi, wazama imizamo 
engaphumelelanga yokuwavula. “Nk,” washaya 
amankanka, wehla, wathatha ithoshi, wakhanyisa phansi 
ebheka okwakungase kube nobufakazi obabungaholela 
ezikadalawane kubo. Esezenelisile, wabuka unina 
kaMxolisi, wayesethi, “Sesingahamba–ke.” 

“MaZondi!” Wamgaxa. “Ngicela kesibuyele ekhaya 
siyobonisana bese siyamlanda–ke noma ngomuso 
ebusuku.” Wamdonsa. 

Bahamba uMaZondi esekufisa ukufa ethi, 
“Akusaqhamuki nabhubesi kodwa lingibulale?” 
Phinde! Wukhanyikhanyi kuphela owabaphelezela 
ebaneka, wabazungeza wabashiya ngasemotweni 
wayeseziphindelela lapho ababevela ngakhona. 

Sebesemotweni, uThabekhulu wayicaphuna ingane 
wayigonisa unina. Wayidumisa imoto yaphindela 
ebukleleleni bamalambu akwakhe, emshiya uDubazana 
emnyameni kuzosa agcagcazwe yizimpukane eziluhlaza. 

“Kazi Nkulunkulu wami izingane zami seziyothi 
uma zingibuza ukuthi uyise washonaphi, ngiziphendule 
ngithini?” Wawubuza lowo mbuzo imoto isijamelana 
nesango lakwaThabekhulu. “Ngangena naye kula 
magceke. Namuhla, zandla zami, uthando lwami 
ngilungcwabe esihlahleni.” Wathela umvimbi 
wezinyembezi. 

211 


16 


UkWesaba ukuthi uMaZondi wayengahle alile 

ampongoloze, noma azibulale, kwamphoqa uThabekhulu 
ukuba angene ekamelweni labo noDubazana. Ngalokho 
kusa wahlala wenaba uMaZondi embhedeni, wancikisa 
ikhanda epulangweni, zehla zalandelana izinyembezi. 
Wasondela uThabekhulu, wahlala eceleni kwakhe, 
wambambela eduze. Wayezama ukumduduza, 
emncengela nokuba akwedlulise okwakubehlele. 
Wawuzwa umzimba wakhe uvevezela, uqhuqha. 

“Musa ukungithinta!” Wasichilizela laphaya isandla 
sakhe. 

“Ngenzeni? Usuyangenyanya yini MaZondi?” 

“Ngicela ungangithinti. Njengoba ngihlezi nje, iso 
lomshado wabansundu elingozeli, elingalali, elingaxhoshwa, 
elingacimezi, elingafi, sengathi liyangibona. Njengoba 
ngihlezi nje, igazi lami liyethuka, lizwa sengathi 
uDubazana uhlezi ndawana thize lapha endlini, 
uyangibuka.” Wathuthumela kakhulu umzimba wakhe. 

“Ukuze nomfanekiso wakhe wedlule engqondweni, 
ngicela kesithuthele kwelami ikamelo.” 

Nakuba wayengavumi, wamncenga. Nokwesaba 
kwamvumisa. Wambamba ingalo wamtatamisa, wamfaka 
ekamelweni. Wambeka embhedeni ngobunono, wamcikisa 
nangemiqamelo. Wasondela futhi eduze kwakhe ethi 
uyamduduza, kepha kwaphinda sona esasike senzeka, 
sokuchilizwa kwesandla. 

“Sekwenzenjani–ke manje? Nalapha lisakulandele yini iso 

212 

likaDubazana?” Wabuza kugxilile kuye ukukhathazeka. 

“Angisazi ngempela MaZondi ukuthi kufanele ngikwenze 
njani manje. Izinyembezi zakho zingamaketanga 
amaningi abopha inhliziyo yami. Angisale sengiboshwa, 
ngiyolengiswa. Inhliziyo ngendlela eqaqanjelwa ngayo 
ubuhlungu, ngidinga umduduzi eceleni kwami. Umduduzi 
wami kungabuye kube ngubani–ke ngaphandle 
kowesifazane ongithandayo? Kepha uma ngizisondeza 
kuwe, uyangichiliza. Angazi ukuthi uthi angibe 
ngokabani ngemizwa nangomphefumulo.” 

Sagcina simbambile isithongo uMaZondi, wozela, 
wazumeka. Ukusondela kukaThabekhulu, encika ngaye, 
naye kwamthelela ngabo ubuthongo. Yozi, wazumeka zu. 
Inhlansi yokukhanya yasondela bekwelamaphupho. Nge, 
kwasa beyibhudla imbudlane. Ngehora lesishiyagalombili 
waphaphama uThabekhulu, wethuka, wadonsa amathe. 

“A, emsebenzini!” 

Wethuka noMaZondi, waphaphama. 

Okwake kwenzeka kuDubazana esaba ukumshiya 
umkakhe emjondolo ngoba esaba nokuthi wayengahle 
azibulale, kwamehlela noThabekhulu. Wancama 
ukungalubeki emsebenzini encenga umoya kanina kaMxolisi. 

“Osekungethusa kakhulu emoyeni yile ngane evele 
yavula umnyango uyise esadindilize phansi. Mhlawumbe 
imbonile. Uyofika udadewabo imxoxele.” 

“Zama ukuthola ingqondo yayo. Uma ike yabuza 
uyikhohlise ngokuthi obedindilizile ubeyisivakashi sami 

213 

ebese sehlulwe ukudla. 

Wayehlezi embhedeni uNkosana, esonge izandla. 
Inhliziyo yakhe eyayiya ngokuya iqina wayibona 
uThabekhulu ngesikhathi kuhlangana amehlo, embuka 
ngeso lengwe enamanxeba. Lapho iphuma indodana, iwathi 
nhla ekamelweni likaThabekhulu elalivuliwe, imbona 
unina enebe embhedeni, yamuthi klabe. Yageza, yagqoka, 
yaphuma ingacelanga kudla, ingadlanga, ingavalelisanga 

— zaya. Basala endlini bebulawa isazela, bezibuza 
beziphendula. 
Impelasonto yonke uThabekhulu wayidla emelusile 
umfelokazi, emduduza. NgoMsombuluko, ebuyele 
emsebenzini, wabuya uMakhosazana egone uSibonelo 
owayeluleme okungatheni. Naye wathi engena ngakho kodwa 
nje endlini wayebabaza ukuphelela emehlweni kukanina. 

“Bese ngimangazwe nawukuthi ubungasasivakasheli 
ngani sisesibhedlela. Sekuyazisho–ke manje ukuthi 
kungani.” 

“Bengixinwe yisifo mntanami,” ekhulumela phansi, 
eyibuka indodakazi ngawo amehlo ayeseneziyingi zesazela. 

“Kade ngihlushwa yiphupho elibi kabi ngobaba 
ngisesibhedlela. Anikezwa lutho ngaye ejele?” 

“Lutho, Makhosazana mntanami.” Wesula amehlo 
ayehlamba, wayeseziphephetha. 

“Kulokhu kusuke ngoLwesihlanu ngiphupha ubaba 
emile, egebise ikhanda endaweni esemnyameni, ehlengezela 
izinyembezi ethi, ‘Makhosazana mntanami, angiyithandi le 
ndawo engikuyo. Ngincengele kunyoko bangilande’.” 

“I, Nkosi yami! Kazi waphelelaphi noDubazana 
engasasibhaleli nencane nje incwadi?” Lwehla unyembezi, 

214 

waphuma wangena endlini yangasese, wazidedela 
zageleza ngenkululeko. 

“Yini mntanami?” Wabuza esekhishini. 

“Besikhuluma ngobaba nje izolo kanti sesizwa incwadi 
yakhe ebisisendleleni. Ubaba usaphila! Nansi incwadi 
yakhe!” Wamnika emoyizela. 

“O, Nkosi yami uDubazana!” Wayemukela, 
wayibukisisa. Kwakuyisandla sakhe impela. Watatabuka 
nayo wayohlala kusofa, wayivula, wayifunda. Enhla 
kwakubhalwe ikheli lasejele ayekade edonsa kulo enhla 
nezwe, nenombolo yendlu ayevalelwe kuyo. Yayibhalwe 
emasontweni amathathu ayedlule. Wadonsa amakhala 
efunda, ecwayiza engaqedi: 

MaZondi, sithandwa sami, 

Umoya wami uphatheke kabuhlungu kabi 
ngokungangiphenduli kwakho phezu kokuba 
sengikubhalele izincwadi eziningi kangaka. Mhlawumbe 
wenziwa wukungazi ukuthi ngikuthanda, ngikukhumbula 
kangakanani. Ukunganginaki kwakho, sithandwa 
senhliziyo, njengoba ngibhadla ejele, kumbe kubangelwa 
ukuthi nami ngacabangela uhlangothi lwami ngedwa. 

215 

Angilunakanga olwakho ngemva kokuba ugcweleziwe. 
Sikhathi sonke manje, lapho ngicabanga ngawe, 
ngikukhumbula ezinhlungwini nasenjabulweni, lihlala lithi 
bha, engqondweni iphutha lami. Sengihlala ngibala imizuzu 

ngikuthande, ube umkami, ngibe umyeni wakho. 

Emoyeni wami angisafisi lutho olunye ngaphandle 
kokuthula noxolo. Nanjengoba ngizophuma nje, sengathi 
ngingahamba ngokuphepha ngize ngifinyelele kuwe 
zandla eziphephile ezifudumeza impilo yami. Ekuphumeni 
kwami, ngizoqala phansi futhi, ngidayise, ngigudluze 
noma ngqinamba zini ezingaba yisithiyo sokwakha umuzi 
wethu wenjabulo esingaseyukugcwelezwa nakuboshiswa 
muntu kuwo. Luyeza lolo suku lapho emzini wethu siyoba 
njengezithandani eziqomene izolo, zinjengabaphupha 
besezweni elisha. 

Ngicela ungikhonzele kubantabami, oMakhosazana 
noNkosana, nomzukulu wami uSibonelo. Ungalibali 
ukufukamela imiphefumulo yabo ngothando ukuze 
bakhohlwe nayinhlekelele eyabehlela siphuma singena 
emiqashweni. Ubatshele ukuthi ngithe kubo, noma umuntu 
angabhajwa ngemilenze nangezingalo esidakeni somhlaba; 
noma kungathiwa ukufa okungaphunyukwa sekumcuthele 
sangonyama, yinye iNkosi abangayethemba. Yileyo eyadala 
iZulu nomhlaba nakho konke okukulo nakuwo. 

Sala kahle–ke, Thuleleni, ntombi yami! Noma singehlukana 
ngenyama, sisemunye uma sisabambene ngomoya, ngawo 

216 

kuyilowo nalowo kithi ephilela omunye ngokuphiliswa umoya 
womunye. Ngiyayivala–ke manje le ncwadi amehlo ami 
ngiwabhekise kulolo suku lapho siyoba njengasebebonana 

zentethelelo. Ngaphandle–ke uma isandla esangibophisa 

sesingibona singibulala singakaxhawulani, ukubonana 

kwethu sekoba semuseni weNkosi! 

Yimina oziqhenyayo ngawe 

Umyeni wakho 

uZwelisha 

Ngemuva kokugula imini yonke, wanele wafika 

uThabekhulu wamkhombisa yona. Wamkhalela ezibuza 
ukuthi lalimfanele ngaphi elithi wayeyizandla eziphephile 
ngokufudumeza impilo yomyeni wakhe ayembulele. 
Wavuma ukuthi naye wayebe nesandla ekubulaweni 
kukaDubazana ngokumcindezela esiswini ngenkathi 
encishwa umoya. O, izinyembezi ezazingasanqamuki! 

Zaqhubeka izinsuku. Lapho liwushuza umoya, noma 
limakhaza, noma liyidliva, enhliziyweni kaMaZondi 
nozwelo sengathi zonke lezi zimo zezulu zazizenzela 
kuDubazana owayesaphila, ezwa ubuhlungu. Lapho izulu 
liduma liqhaqhabula, lalihaqhabula ocabangweni libaneka 
kwamancane. Lathi liyohlangana ishumi lezinsuku 
emizimbeni babezingubo zixhonywe konongekleni. 
Babeqedelwa kakhulu nayindodana kaDubazana 
eyayingabavezeli zinyo ngisho beyincokolisa. Yayibapha 
kuphela amehlo engonyama eyayibabeke umkhusu. 

217 

UThabekhulu okwakumcacela ukuthi lase liphihlizekile 
ithemba lokuthi wayeyobuye aphilisane nomkakhe 
waphuma emsebenzi ngenye imini wedlula ezitolo, 
emakethe nasesilaheni. Wakhithiza eyozixolisela. 
Sebehlezi bexoxa nomkakhe ekhweni, wayelokhu 
ekhononde njalo umkakhe ngokuthi amehlo omyeni 
ayefana nawombulali. 

“Asazi ejele.” Wayebalekisa lawo mehlo ayemceba. 

“Zozwakala Thabekhulu. Angisayikholwa nale 
nsumansumane ongethela yona yokuthi awungilandi 
nje ngoba usafunela uMaZondi indawo. Ngisola 
sengathi nididwe indaba kaDubazana osithunzi sakhe 
sihambisana nawe.” 

Washeshe wavalelisa, watshovoza wayongena 
emotweni esephindela kwakhe eyolindela amathonsi 
abanzi. 

Ekupheleni kwesonto lesithathu alengiswa 
uDubazana, ukushaya komoya owawuthubeleza ehlathini 
elaliphezu komfula uMlazi kwaba yinkinga emakhaleni 
ababakhe emijondolo eyayingalapho. Bahlaba umkhosi 
emaphoyiseni. Azidela amathambo, angena ehlathini 
ayobheka. Ayeyombheka ambuka engasabhekeki. 

KuDubazana amaphoyisa ayelutholile uqwembe 
olwalunemininingwane yakhe. Ngalo ayewulandele njalo 
umkhondo owawuze wawafinyelelisa kwaThabekhulu. 
Ayenele ambikela uMaZondi wazibhonqa kaningi phansi, 
ekhala ebalisa. Ayemfake emotweni wayozibonela 
mathupha emakhazeni kahulumeni imiphumela 
yensebenzo yezandla zabo. Wayeyofa engakukhohlwanga 
ayekubone emakhazeni. 

UThabekhulu owayebuye emsebenzini isililo sesidla 

218 

umunyu kwakhe wagwajaza. Omakhelwane nabanye 
bebandla ababazi indaba kaMxolisi bazingqumuza bethi 
indaba wayeyazi. Iminwe yamkhomba yamnamathela. 

Okwakumudla ngaphakathi uThabekhulu kwamenza 
wazama ukulutha amehlo abantu ngesihe, ethi, 
“Sengizosale sengenzela iNkosi nje bakithi. Nakuba ngazi 
ukuthi anginakukhokhelwa, kepha uma abazali bale 
nsizwa bewabonile nje amathambo engane yabo, ngiyobe 
ngikhokhelwe impela. Ngizodela imoto yami, nobuthongo, 
ngiyobabikela, ngibuye nabo futhi.” 

“Ubudoda yibo lobo Thabekhulu!” Wayetuswa impandla 
yakwaMthimkhulu eyayiwumakhelwane, imbuka ngeso 
elalidlinza. 

UThabekhulu wagcina eyithele umgwaqo imoto eyathi 
itheleka nabakwaDubazana, yayikhala ithayi futhi 
ilanda abakwaZondi eNkumba. Bonke babuthana kulo 
muzi owawunamakhosikazi omakhelwane emabhodweni 
ayezihleba zingalali endleleni. Zazithi lapho ziyoshayeka 
ezigujini zezindlebe zabasemzini nabasekhweni, 
balambelane bodwa. 

Inkonzo yomngcwabo kaDubazana yaba ngoMgqibelo, 
ngehora leshumi esontweni khona eMlazi. Kwakunohide 
lwamabhasi ayeqashwe ngeminikelo yamalungu 
enhlangano ethize yamalungelo esintu. Ngakho–ke, 
endlini yokukhonza eyagcwala yachichima ngesikhashana, 
kwakufunjathwa izibhakela, kukhuzwa iziqubulo, 
kuhutshwa awezombangazwe nawezenkolo. OThabekhulu 
noMaZondi ababengabonaze bamphuphe uDubazana 

219 

engcwatshiswa okwesipheshethwa kanjeya, batshoda 
bevele behwabhekile. 

UBhekizizwe wawulanda–ke umlando wokwazana 
kwabo noDubazana kusukela bebonana emhlanganweni 
owawuseMbalasi, ehlangana naye nasezinkantolo 
ngamacala ezidakamizwa, nasempilweni. “Kunomyalezo 
nokho le nsizwa ewushiyele izwe ngokufa kwayo. 
Umyalezo uthi, nakuba ababusi bazama ukuyingcwaba 
inkinga ngokunigqiba iminyaka eMazambaneni; nakuba 
banithutha bayonifihla ezintabeni nasemaweni, sisondele 
isikhathi lapho amafuku eyoqhumisa okwamakhowe 
phakathi emadolobheni. Njengotwayi obelufihlekile 
seluziveza eminweni yencwasimende, ayovela abe 
yiBhabhiloni.” Inkundla wayishiyela uMfundisi uSokhela 
owayibamba inkonzo kwathula umoya. 

Izinsizwa zakwaboZwelisha ezazizinde zilaphaya, 
oMahambehlala, oMjijeni, oCalaliyaphikwa, oMsobo 
noMasobozela zabambisana ngaye zaphuma nebhokisi. 
Zazithela kuThabekhulu ezamkluluza ngabomvu amehlo 
amthinta isazela wahlengezela izinyembezi. Ewabalekisa 
awakhe ebhokisini azithela kwawomkakhe owayemile 
ekhala, embuka. 

220 

“Xola mkami.” Wazizwa eseshilo. 

Yamehlula impendulo. 

Izingqinamba zajiya emangcwabeni. Umfundisi 
esephathe eyothuli othulini, esebize nezihlobo ukuba 
zizophonsa inhlabathi, uMasobozela wawubhebhezela 
umlilo ngokubuka uSokhela ngayeyigazi amehlo qede 
athi, “Siyezwa Mfundisi ngezethembiso zezwekazi elihle 
elizayo. Ngeshwa, sengathi thina asiseyukulibona uma 
umntakamama enje, eyinkilivane nathi esehluleka 
ukuyichaza. Ubulawe abantu abakhona mhlawumbe lapha 
phakathi kwethu, okumanje nje bachiphiza izinyembezi 
zengwenya.” Wabheka ngakuMaZondi, wakhomba. “Wena 
MaZondi, uzolihlanza ulibeke lapha iqiniso! Usho yona le 
ndoda enihlangene nayo, uzoyikhipha uyibeke lapha!” 

UMazondi wabuna ngaphansi kwetshali ayegubuzele 
ngalo. UThabekhulu washwabana ensudini emnyama. 
Waqalaza emuva kwathi akathi galo yephuka. Wazikhuza 
esaba amehlo abantu. Ngeshwa labo futhi, kanye kanye 
amehlo abo ahlangana nakaNkosana ayengawengwe. 
Baluhlafuna balugwinya ubala. 

“Konke asisale sesikubeka eNkosini!” Wayeshweleza 
uMfundisi ethalaza eminye imigodi eyayihlala isimbiwe 
kula mangcwaba ayaziwa ngelaseSeventini. 

UMazondi wathi uyayibamba ngesasinedumbe 
yachitheka yonke inhlabathi. Wagcina ephonse ize. 
UThabekhulu wachilizwa esewela emgodini. Amakhanda 
ayezululekiswa yinzululwane. Balandela nabanye, 
noMaDlamini, bayiphonsa bafulathela nezinyembezi. 
Kwaqalwa kwagqitshwa. Ngesikhathi inhlabathi ikhala 
phezu kwebhokisi, yakhala nasezindenini zezinhliziyo 
zoMjijeni noCalaliyaphikwa nabanye. 

“Ngeke Nzima! Ngeke Khondlo! Uma baba singase 

221 

sibukelele umfowethu egqitshwa yedwa, basale ababulali 
bekhona, ngabe awuzele zinsizwa mfo kaKhalalempi,” 
kusho uMjijeni eyeka ukugqiba, ema nehalavu. “Phakathi 
nawe mka mfowethu ukuze uzwe ukuthi kunjani 
ukugqitshwa!” Wayesemdumele, wamdonsela phakathi. 
Wehla nenhlabathi uMaZondi wakhala nayo phezu 
kwebhokisi. 

“Nawe phakathi!” Wamkhomba kanye 
uCalaliyaphikwa, wagxala eya kuye. 

Wahlehla uMpanza engasajeqezanga nasemuva. 
“Maye!” Washo ekhalakathela engcwabeni elase limbiwe 
ayehlehlela kulo. 

Ngokuxolisa kweningi, kukhuza nabazali, abhodla 
amadodana akwaDubazana, abadedela oMaZondi 
noMpanza. Bemthuqusana, bexhoshiwe, becwayiza 
bengaqedi, balabhuzela. Baze bayosithela bebukiswa 
okwezoni. Kwasala kuqhutshekwa nomsebenzi, 
wangcwatshwa uDubazana. Kanjalo neyakhe indunduma 
yasala neziningi iyisikhumbuzo. Kwahlakazekwa. 
KwaThabekhulu kwabuyela kuphela unina kaMaZondi 
owayephelezela izingane. 

222 


17 


NTAMBAMA ngemuva kwezigigaba zasemangcwabeni, 
imoto yema phezu kolwandle eSiphingo. Bahlala 
bawabuka amagagasi evuka indlobane eba bulawu 
buphehlwa. Iminjunju yobuhlungu enhliziyweni 
kaThabekhulu yayinezelelwa nayizinyembezi 
zikaMaZondi. 

Ngezwi elalivevezela uThabekhulu wathi, “Noma 
ngilele, angikaze ngiziphuphe ngizibone ngisemahlazweni 
nasemachilweni anje, ngicashele izwe, njengoba senza, 
ngoba ngiwumbulali. Nami, mhla ngiqala ukunibona 
bakwaDubazana ngangithi ngiyasiza. Namuhla kepha 
sengiwumbulali, ngiyafunwa, ngibalekele umuzi wami 
kwawona osubhidlikile.” Lwaduma ulwandle lwatheleka 
emotweni. Phezu kwalolo lulaka, izinyoni ezimhloshana, 
amavubu andiza phezu kwalo. Nomkhumbi owawuntanta 
phakathi wabonakala luvinjwana ofasimbeni lwalo. 

Ebambe ukumpongoloza emotweni uMaZondi, 
waqhumuka wakhala. 

“Iphutha okungafanele ulenze MaZondi elokuthi uma 
sekunje uzisole, uzibhixe ngokuzethwesa icala lokuthi 
mhlawumbe kunje nje ngoba kunguwena owangilinga. Neze 
neze, awuzange ungilinge. Isimo sempilo esisihlanganisile 
sisibeke esimweni esikuzo.” 

“Ungcono wena mntanomuntu. Nakuba umkhumbi 
ukucwilela usenaye umaqondana osenokuxolisa kuye 
akuxolele. Okwami okwezandla. Sengiyoxolisa ngale 
kokufa uma sisahlangana. Ukusuka manje Nkosi yami 

223  

angazi ngingokabani?” Wavala amehlo wasidinda. 

“Nalowo mshado angiboni ukuthi ungaba yimpumelelo. 
Njengoba nawe usho nje, ngeke ungithathe ngothando 
kepha ngephuzu lokwenzekile. Nomkakho angifisi 
anyathele emalahleni ebenginyathela kuwo okungabi 
namuzi. Naphezu kwakho konke lokho, iqiniso nje 
elimsulwa ukuthi asithandani, futhi asikaze siqomane. 
Nokwasehlela kwaba yisehlo nje sangalolo suku. 

“Yise kaMxolisi, ngicela ungithathe ungiphuthumise 
kwethu lapho ngizalwa khona. Kungcono bayongibulalela 
khona kunokuba ngizoba yisidumbu esiyinkinga 
emzini wakho. Nawe uzibonele ukuthi abafowethu 
bakwaDubazana banjani. Siyabhubha phela manje.” 

Kwaze kwaswelela bedidekile, bexoxa ingxoxo 
eyayingahlangani. Ukuhlwa kwabaqoqa, yasuka yatotoba 
imoto isiphindela kwaThabekhulu. Bafika khona, 
basinga emnyameni imoto beyicishile. Kwakumnyama 
phandle, kungabonakali mfanekiso wamuntu. Endlini 
kwakukhanya. Yanyonyoba imoto, yangena. Wehla 
umninimuzi wayongqongqozisa okwesoka emzini 
wakhe. UMaMbhele, unina kaMaZondi waphendula, 
wazichaza noThabekhulu ehleba. Wamvulela, wangena 
wabuza ukuthi kwakuphephile yini. Nakuba uMaMbhele 
wayengenasiqiniseko sokuphepha kepha abakwaDubazana 
babephume emngcwabeni bashaya bachitha ababe 
besedlula lapha. Nakudla okwakukade kuphekelwe 
abantu, kwakugcwele amabhodwe ekhishini, kungabange 
kusedlula muntu. Wayifaka egalaji imoto, behla 
noMaZondi bangena bezobhekana namaqiniso empilo. 

“Namakhosikazi abengiphelezele ngiwakhululile 

224 

bantabami ngathi awahambe ngoba bengilambele ithuba 
lokuxoxa nani,” kuhleba uMaMbhele egone uMxolisi, 
endlini yokuphumula. “Ake ningilandise nje ukusuka 
nokuhlala kwendaba. Kwenzenjani?” 

Kwabhuduzelwa kuqoqwa, kulayishwa. Kuqathaka 
izinyembezi kugogo wabantwana, endodakazini 
nakubazukulu, yaphuma ngomnyama imoto yazifuna 
lapho zazingakhona izintaba zangakubo kaMaZondi, 
oNomandamfu nomfula uMkhomazi ogcwala ngomoya, 
nePholela. 

* * * 

UMaZondi wayesahlala ehluneme. Wayedidwa 
yizinkulumo zabantu. Isigodi sonke sasibingelelana 
ngendaba yakhe — intombi kamasibanibani eyayibulele 
indoda eThekwini. Wayethathwa njengomuntu 
owayeyisibonelo esibi entsheni yendawo. 

Wayedikibaliswe ukuhlupheka nendlala, nezingane 
belala bevuka ngamanzi. Ngokufa kukaDubazana 
nokubaleka kwabo eMlazi nezingane unyaka uphakathi, 
wawuphele zingasafundi. Wawuqale omusha wabhukula 
unina eyobabhalisa esikoleni. Yayibe yinye, zambili 
izinyanga befunda, wadideka waphela uNkosana, 
wamadolonzima ukuya. Wagcina ezihlalele phansi 

225 

nobujaka ayeyibo. Usizi lwalungasamhlafuni, lwase 
lumququda. Wayedangaliswe uNkosana owayesehlala 
ethule, ebhocobele. Kwakwala noma ethi uyamncokolisa, 
asimze azidle izindebe, amncishe amehlo. Ingqondo yakhe 
yayisihlala ididizela, yethukela, yethuswa yizithunzi 
zikaDubazana ayezibona emini nasebusuku. Wayengabuthi 
quthu ubuthongo amaphupho. Umfanekiso womyeni 
wawulokhu wathi bhade engqondweni ewubhambalala 
phansi. Nalapho sebelekelelana bemlengisa, 
kwacaca kwathi bha. Okwakuyinkinga kakhulu kuye 
eseNkumba, nakuThabekhulu engale kwezintaba, phezu 
koThungulu, kwakuwukhanyikhanyi owawuphume 
nabo ehlathini, wabazungeza sebengasemotweni, baze 
bawuphunga bobabili. Nakalokho wawusabazungeza, 
imini nobusuku behlala bechitha izandla bephunga ize. 
Wayekhala kuze kuse exolisa kuDubazana. Okwase 
kumehlula kunakho konke yindlala, ukoma nokuqaleka. 
Wayelambile, elambele uthando. Wayomile, omele 
izwi elingamanzi enduduzo. Wayeqalekile, eqalekele 
ayezoshiyelana naye ngomlilo wezifuba owawulanguka 
ubashisa. Owakhe wezifuba ayengake ahlebe naye 
kumbe idambe imbuthuma yenhliziyo wayeyedwa. 
KwakunguThabekhulu qhwaba. Kwakungelona uthando 
olwalumkhumbuza uThabekhulu, kepha kwase kuya 
njengesisho samaNgisi lapho ethi, “Izinyoni ezifanayo 
zindiza ndawonye.” 

226 

njani. Ngisho esengena ngaphakathi kwezindonga zawo 
kwakuba sengathi wayengena emakhazeni ayenesidumbu 
sikaDubazana. Umbhede wakhe, yize kwakungowezimali 
ezishisiwe, ewendlala izindwangu ezazizinhle zivutha 
zithi bhe, wayethi uma esengena kuwo, kube sengathi 

Umkakhe wayesasebenza, ewumdayisi kwesinye 
sezitolo zengqephu ephambili edolobheni. Wayesaqasha 
mzini thize esigcemeni esasikude nakwakhe, khona 
eMlazi. Kwakuqasha lokhu kwakuyenza inhliziyo 
kaThabekhulu ihlale yaba nesilokozane esasingapheli 
ngezingane zakhe ezazihlala ekamelweni nonina. 
Nazo zase zamesabela kude ngokuzwa elokubulala. 
Nomoya wakhe wazama ukuthola umthunzi nophahla 
enhliziyweni kaMaDlamini, kepha wafica sekwaba 
nameva okuphoxeka. Wase washa nomthombo wamanzi 
ayewomele okucisha amalangabi enhliziyo. Umkakhe 
wayemtinyela ngentshumayelo yesono sokubulala ayethi 
sasingasoze sathethelelwa. Ngokumesabisa ngalelo, 
wamesaba naye, wahambela kude naye okwelanga 
lasebusika. 

NgoMgqibelo thize, emini yantambama, ezihlalele 
yedwa endlini uThabekhulu, ezibukela ezemidlalo 
kumabonwakude, wabona ngoyise nonina sebetheleka 
ngemoto yabo entsha ababesanda kuyithenga. Nakuba 
wababona kwathi akababalekele, kepha ayesemphelele 
nasozwaneni amenza wahlala kusofa sengathi 
wayebanjwe yinomfi. Uyise owayenethambo njengayo 
indodana, eyingengelezi ekhanyayo, eqatha, waba 
mude emnyango, engqongqoza. Yasukuma indodana, 
yabhucabhuca izandla ibulawa amahloni, ithi abangene. 
Bangena. Unina uMaMgobhozi owayengakhulile kangako, 
empofu, eshaye isiketi nebhantshi okwakuluhlaza 

227 

sasibhakabhaka, wahlala wayibuka indodana qede 
amehlo acweba izinyembezi. Kwabingelelwana qede 
abazali abachitha sikhathi. UThabizolo bambuza 
uMaDlamini nezingane, oThabethule noThabisile. 
UThabizolo wabika imibiba, wabika ibuzi. 

“Impendula mntanami engephule umoya,” unina 
wayesho echiphiza izinyembezi, evula isikhwama 
ayesiphethe, ebuya nencwadi eyayibhalwe yisandla 
sikaMaDlamini, “ethi wena usumxoshile umkakho 
wazihlalela nomfelokazi othe eqambe eshonelwa 
wayesevele egone umzukulu. Kunensolo neyokuthi 
indoda ikobandayo nje ihambele ezandleni zakho. 
Mntanami, uyazi ukuthi eMnambithi abantu 
basihlonipha kangakanani, nokuthi balindele nenzalo 
yethu ukuba ibe yisibonelo esihle ezweni njengoba 
besifundisa isizwe sobabili. Ungasithela kanjani kodwa 
ngechilo lokukhipha umphefumulo kaNkulunkulu 
esidalweni asikhonzile esiwumfanekiso wakhe?” 

Amehlo kaThabizolo akhama, waliphika wema 

228 

ngentaba elokubulala. Wenaba nodaba, eyichaza 
ukusuka nokuhlala eyokubonana nokuhlalisana 
nabakwaDubazana. Wasivuma isehlo esasibehlele 
ngokuzalwa kukaMxolisi. Wagcizelela nokuthi babeze 
bametha ngoMxolisi nje ngoba bezishaya emoyeni, 
bexolisa becela intethelelo. 

Yalidukuza ilokishi imoto, uThabizolo elokhu 
eyikhombe ngapha nangapha. Wagcina eyikhombe 
egcekeni lomuzi owawumakamelomane, ungawazi upende, 
negceke lakhona lesabeka. Wawungeminye eyayibhekene 
nemijondolo, umniniwo azithathela impesheni wawushiya 
nendodana eyayiwuqashise wonke. Yona yayizidlela 
ugavini ilala ingasaboni ngisho emehlweni efukwaneni 
lomjondolo eyayiwakhe khona egcekeni. 

Bangqongqoza, edaningilumu bavulelwa yinkosikazi 
eyayingangothi lokuvungula, igqoke isiketshana nejezana 
okwakumnyama, kuphuphaphuphile. Yababuza ukuthi 
babekhala ngobani, bayitshela. Yathi abedlule khona 
ekamelweni eyayiliqashile bayongena kwelincane 
elalihlala uMaDlamini. Bangena, bedlula kungekho 
ngisho indawo yokufaka unyawo. Kwakugcwele 
amantombazane ayesekhulile, egone abazukulu 
bale nkosikazi nendoda eyayihlezi phezu kombhede 
ilinganisene nawo. Yayibeke amabhodlela kabhiya 
etafulaneni elaliphambi kwabo. Yababuka indoda ngeziqu 
zamehlo ibona ingqephu ababeyishayile. Yabahola 
inkosikazi ephasijini, yaye yabakhombisa umnyango 

229 

wekamelo elincane eyangqongqoza kuwo qede savuleka 
isivalo, kwavela ubuso bukaMaDlamini. 

“Bandla, Nkosi yami, ningivakashela ngiwubani kodwa 
baba nomama?” Wabheka ekamelweni akaze ayibona 
indawo ayezobahlalisa kuyo. Kwakukhona umbhede, 
ngenhla kwawo kunekhabeshana elalithi alilingane 
nawo. Phezu kwalo kwakulele iBhayibheli. Odongeni 
olwalungasemnyango kwakumi itafula elalilayishe 
amabhodwe, izitsha nephulamastofu. 

Wabangenisa. Wasukuma uThabisile, wabaqhelela 
bahlala bonke embhedeni. Kwabingelelwana, 
kwabuzwana impilo. Impendulo kaMaDlamini kwaba 
yizinyembezi. Nendodakazi yabo eyayikhulile, impofu, 
ibalande bobabili yampheleka unina. Kwezwela 
nakuninazala, zaqathaka. 

“Angithandi ukukubona mntanomntanami ukhala 
kanje. Awuthathe lesi sikhiye uyozihlalela emotweni 
kamkhulu sisaxoxa.” Umkhulu wakhe wamnika 
uThabisile, waphuma evale amehlo. 

“Bantabami, kuhle ngoba nizibonela nina ukuthi le 
mpilo esiphilwa umuzi wenu iqonde kusiphi isibhicongo. 
Uma kunje–ke, malokazana, nilale kanjani nonke 
nabantwana?” 

“O, hhe, baba, siyazama.” UMaDlamini wayesho 
ecikica amehlo. “Mina nendodakazi silala embhedeni, 
indodana yona ilale lapha phansi.” Wakhomba. 

“Eyami indodana iphenduka kankulungwane igunquza 
yodwa endlini eyikhaya lenu nonke. Nokho–ke, namuhla 
angize ngamacala. Kuphela nje malokazana sizocela 
ukuba ube nathi laphaya kwakho ngomuso sihlanganise 

230 

amakhanda sonke nomlingani nezingane zakwenu 
esesiphuma kubo manje. Nabo bavumile ukuba sibalande 
kusa ngomuso.” 

Sebephuma bedlula ekhishini nalo elaligcwele, 
kuqashiwe. Embhedeni omfishane wezinsimbi 
kwakuhlezi indoda eyayimnyama suce, imfishane, 
imboqwana, imehlwabomvu, ingangothi. Yayiphefumula 
sengathi yayibanjwe yiphika. Yayinamashumi 
ayisithupha eminyaka. Eceleni kwayo kwakuhlezi 
intombazane eyayiminyaka iyishumi nesishiyagalombili, 
nayo yomelele, imboqwana, idonse amehlo. Yayigone 
udwamba lomfana owayeneminyaka emihlanu, ehlubule. 
Yayimkhulelwe ineminyaka eyishumi nantathu, khona 
emijondolo eyayingaphesheya lapho okwakubanjwe khona 
oMakhosazana ngendlela efanayo nayo. Indoda lena 
uMsulele Mbanjwa yayiyicoshe ingane le isakhulelwe, 
iyintandane, abazali bayo babhuqwa ngenhlamvu, ibuka. 
Yayisiwumasihlalisane wayo. Okwakungaqondakali 
kahle ukuthi igciwane lengculaza babelicoshephi bonke. 
Okwakuyiqiniso elimsulwa ukuthi njengoba laligcaluza 
egazini labo bobathathu, lase lingenele namakhosikazi 
amabili ayeyisithembu sikaMbanjwa emakhaya, nabanye 
abaningi ababegcatshwe ngansingo nye ngezinye 
zezinyanga ezazizama ukubelapha. 

Lapho abakwaThabekhulu bedlula, akakucabanganga 
uyise, kepha kwazenzakalela ukuba avele akhiphe 
amashumi amabili amalandi anikele kuMbanjwa. 
Akazange akhulume uMbanjwa. Wawemukela, 
waphakamisa izandla sakukhuleka, wayesekhwehlela 
undendende. Sebengenile emotweni, yaphenduka, zaya 

231 

onina noyise bakaThabizolo besathuthumela. 

Impendulo kwaba ukushaya isikhwehlela nokugwinya 
amathe, kuhambisana nokuziluma ulimi. 

Ngomuso ekuseni laqulwa libomvu elikaThabizolo. 
Inkulumo yoThabizolo nomkakhe yase inohlalwane 
yenziwa uthando olwase lunezisihla namashanda. 
Lwalunezisihla zokuthi uThabizolo uMaZondi 
wayesembiza ngonina womfana, linamashanda okuthi 
wayesebulele, nokusho indoda eyibulalela umuzi wayo. 
Nalapho, nakuba uThabizolo wayeliphika elokubulala, 
waxolisa waze wahlanganisa izandla esifubeni 
ngelengane. Kumnyama kunjalo, baciciyela abazali waze 
wathamba uMaDlamini. Wethembisa ukubuyela kumyeni 
ukuze bazame ukuphemba busha, bavuthele umlotha, 
inqobo nje uma bobabili babezokhombisana ngezincwadi 
zodokotela ukuthi babemsulwa egciwaneni lengculaza. 

“Akusho wena mntanami,” kusho uyisezala, “kepha 
kusho izikhathi nempilo yabantu baso.” 

Kwagcinwa kwehlukenwe. OThabekhulu nomkakhe 
baphindela eMnambithi benethemba lokuvuka komuzi 
wabantababo phezu kwalolo ngabazane lwegciwane. 

Esebuzwe kahle ubuhlungu bokugunquza yedwa 

endlini uThabekhulu, wavukela kwadokotela, wafike 

wathathwa igazi. Wacelwa ukuba abuye ngosuku 
oluthile azokuzwa imiphumela. Waphindela amaphaphu 
ephezulu. Wayemsulwa. Wabuyela kwakhe emagange, 

ezofike athi qu, edlulele edolobheni kumkakhe 

eyomkhombisa ukuthi wayephila njengenhlanzi 

emanzini. Efika kwakhe imoto akayifakanga ngisho 

232 

egaraji. Wangena endlini. Esavule iwadilobhu ebheka 
okungcono ayengase akugqoke, wezwa sengathi kukhona 
okwakunyakaza phandle egcekeni elalingemuva. 
Waqhawuzela, wavula umnyango wasekhishini. Wethuka 
waqikileka sengathi wayebanjwe wugesi, wahlahla 
awesikhova. Wayebona uMaZondi nendodakazi yakhe 
uMakhosazana behlezi phezu kwamabhokisi amabhodlela 
kanamanethi, bobabili begone amadodana abo oMxolisi 
noSibonelo. Bembona ethuka engaswabuluki, nabo 
bambuka ngawabo bedideke bandwaza. 

OMaZondi nendodakazi base bagqunqa bamnyama 
suce, ikade ibazuka indawo yasemakhaya nentuthu 
bengasayejwayele. Amazinyo abawaveza akubange 
kusacaca noma kwakungawokumamatheka noma 
kwakungawokunyewuka yini. Bazinyakazisa izingane 
abase bezigone zaze zalala, bazimisa. Bazidonsa 
zinwabuluka bangena nazo endlini. UThabekhulu 
esavala umnyango wasekhishini, bona bedlulela endlini 
yokuphumula angena kuyo uMaZondi kwakude ukuba 
ahlale phansi. Umfanekiso womyeni wakhe ethe ja, phansi, 
wawumbuyela unjengoba wawunjalo. 

“Nk, Nkosi yami!” Washo lawo nje wahlala 
esenamahloni omntanakhe owayembuka emangele. 
Wangena noThabekhulu, wahlala kusofa owawubhekene 
nayehlezi kuwo. Beqala ngqa ukubonana kusukela 
ngosuku lomngcwabo kaDubazana, babukana 
ngezinhlansi zamehlo ayebanekisa okukakhanyikhanyi 
lowo. Wababingelela ngesizotha somuntu eqala 
ukumbona nokumbingelela umfelokazi selokhu 
ashonelwa. Kwabuzwana impilo. 

“Akukho mpilo etheni lapha Thabekhulu. Ungibona 

233 

ngilapha nje, ngilethe oMakhosazana nomntwana 
esibhedlela. Umntanomntanami njengoba umbona 
ethambe enje, akamnandi neze egazini.” Waphunga 
ukhanyikhanyi. 

“Uphi kodwa uMaDlamini, akazukusishaya nje esibona 
sesigcwele umuzi wakhe?” 

Wamchazela uThabekhulu ukuthi nakalokho umkakhe 
wayengakabuyi. 

“Nami Thabekhulu sebenele bangenzela usiko 
ekhaya, bangigeza, ngahlala nezingane ngizibuka 
zibhuquziswa yindlala, ngaze ngabona ukuthi alikho 
elinye ikhambi ngaphandle kokubuyela eThekwini 
ngizofuna umsebenzi. Engicela–ke ukuba mntanomuntu 
ungisize ungibhekele lapho ongase ungifihlise khona 
ikhanda. Noma kusehhokweni lezinkukhu, noma 
egoqweni noma kungaba sesithumbanjeni nje kulungile. 
Ungibekele nendlebe lapho kuqashwa khona.” Wambuka 
wamkhophozelela. Kwaqala olulodwa unyembezi, 
lwageleza ngesineke anduba luphelekwe olunye. 
Wambuka wadabuka uThabekhulu, wayesephunga 
ukhanyikhanyi. 

“Umfana wakho lona omunye, uNkosana, 
nimshiyephi?” 

“UNkosana simshiye ngoba singasasiboni isizathu 
sokumletha lapha eThekwini njengoba umntanami 
usaphenduka imbodla nje engasafundi.” Wakhala kakhulu. 

234 

UThabekhulu kwakungumuntu wokuqala ayengase 
amkhalele enethemba lokuthi wayengase amzwele 
njengoba emakhaya wayethi uyalubika usizi, abhinqwe 
ngomzenzisi owayebulale indoda. Uzwelo, uthando, 
nokunakwa nokududuzwa wayesekomele emizweni 
nasemphefumulweni. 

“Asale nobani uMakhosazana mntanabantu ngoba 
phela akuphephile lapha?” 

“Njengoba sengike ngakuchazela, kuphephile impela. 
Yitshele nje kuphela ingane ukuthi sisaya esitolo.” 

“Ngizoke ngiqale ngigeze nami. Ngijulukile, kade 
sihamba.” 

Wasukuma waqalaza imithwalo yabo. Kwaba yila 
ebonayo ukuthi babeyikhohlwe phandle. Waphuma 
wayilanda. Wangena ebhavini, wageza, washaya ezakhe. 
Zaziseyizo ayezithengelwe uDubazana, zimthunaza nje 
kuphela ngokuthi zazilengiswa ukwehla komzimba. 
Esemtshelile uMakhosazana ukuthi babesaya esitolo, 
baphuma belandelana. UThabekhulu wamvulela isivalo 
semoto, wangena. Yaphuma yanyonyoba, zikhalela phansi 
izingoma. Yabashiya omakhelwane ababengonondaba 
bebambelele okhalo, emadandeni noma beqhwebana, 
okukanye bevakashelana bayoshonisa ilanga ngokuzixoxa 
nokuzinonga. 

Yalishiya ilokishi yaphikelela edolobheni. Yahahalaza 
phezu kolwandle yaye yayongena edolobheni eMhlanga. 
Yema phambi kwehhotela lakhona elaliphambili, 
iCabana. Wehla, wamvulela, balinganisana emkhombisa 
iminyango yakhona ababezongena ngayo. Bangena 
ebucwazicwazini, bedlulela endlini yokudlela lapho 

235 

uThabekhulu amkhombisa khona izihlalo. Bahlala 
babonisana emoyeni owawupholile. Intokazi yomlungu 
eyayishaye ezokuweta yeza kubo, yabingelela, yabuza 
ababengakuthanda. Walifaka uThabekhulu i–oda 
leziminzi, lapho okwakuthiwa umuntu uzitika kukhathale 
izinyo, kukhononde ithumbu. Umuntu engadekelwa, 
ezibonela, namapuleti nazo zonke izimfanelo zokudla 
ziphambi kwabo, zathelwa zayekwa kwamaziqokele. 
Kwakuwukuthatha ipuleti, uzidikele, noma ukhombe 
okuthandayo, iziteki, inyama epholile, njalo njalo, 
ugebhulelwe amaqa. 

“Kanti, ngale nje bandla Dubaz… njalo Thabekhulu, 
kwemicabango ngokwenzeka, nendawo efana nalena 
esikuyo namuhla ngiqala ngqa ukungena kuyo empilweni 
yami. Mina indlu engiyaziyo kuphela eyasemakhaya, 
eyaselokishini emakamelo mane ebesiqasha kuzo, kanye 
neyasemjondolo. Angikaze ngilubhade endaweni enje, 
ngisho nokulunguza ngakuyo.” 

Wambekela isineke uThabekhulu ezama ukuba ingqondo 
yakhe ikhululeke ekwesabeni okwakumkhungethe. 

236 

Wamtotobisa bandla nakulokho kwesaba kwakhe ngisho 
ukuhlafuna phambi kwabelungu. Wayedla eshalaza, 
nomlomo ewesula njalo. Okwakungamkhululekisi 
du, ukuthi kuleli hholo lendlu yokudlela 
kwakungenamfanekiso womunye omnyama njengabo 
owayezokudla ngaphandle kwabo. Ababefana nabo 
kwakungababesezimbizeni, nabasizi babo, kanye noweta, 
nabaphaki. Waze wakhululeka ngokuhamba kwabelungu 
ababeseduze kwabo, nasehholo kusala idlanzana elalithe 
gqwa, gqwa lapha nalaphaya. Wakwazi nokusukuma 
ayocela impinda. 

“Nina kaMxolisi.” 

“Yebo Thabekhulu.” 

“Namhlanje ngicela ungitshele futhi igama lakwenu.” 

UMaZondi wambuka kancane, wayesebuza ethi, 
“Ngoba?” 

“Uma usungitshelile ngizokuchazela.” 

“Hhayi–ke, kulungile, noma ngingasejwayele nje 
ukubizwa ngalo. NginguThuleleni.” 

“Mina nginguThabizolo.” 

‘Ngiyalikhumbula, nakuba ngingasoze 
ngalisebenzisa. Ekhaya ngafundiswa ukuthi umuntu 
wesilisa esesinengane naye angombiza ngebizo 
lengane yokuqala yethu. Nokho–ke, ngoba libizeka 
kamnandi ake ngicele ukulizama nokulinambitha 
kanye nje.” Laphephezela iduku ekhanda embuka 
elindele impendulo. 

“Libize.” 

Wabala izinhlamvu ethi “Tha–bi–zo–lo. Abazali 

237 

bakuqamba lona walilandela.” 

“Ngoba selokhu wahlangana nami ukwethaba kuwe 
nomuzi wakho sekungokwayizolo.” 

“Uma kunjalo, uwena ozokwenza ukuthokoza 
kwayizolo kube ngokwanamuhla nangomuso.” 

Wakhophoza uMaZondi, akangazi ngempela ukuthi 
wayezophendula athini. Wambangcaza ethi, “Kodwa 
Nkosi yami ngoba uganiwe nje, nomkakho ngiyamazi?” 

“Umshado kubantu ababili kufanele uthi noma uke 
wahlatshwa yisiqubu sokugula, uxhegule. Akufuneki 
uquleke umlibe.” 

Ebusweni uMaZondi wezwa eshaywa elalipholile 
ihelehele lasolwandle, ezibilini kwashweza kwamancane. 
Phezu kwetshe, ezihlabathini zolwandle, babambelana 
eduze, bangana phezu kwezethembiso zokuba abangani 
nezithandani emshikashikeni wothando nempilo. 
Nalapho sebesukuma, bagaxana. Labashaya ihelehele 
lasolwandle lisiphephetha kancane isiketi neduku 
lasekhanda likaMaZondi. 

Imoto yawubamba umgwaqo owawuphinda 
kwaThabekhulu ivungazela umculo owawupholile. 
Babengakhulumi isikhathi esiningi, izingqondo umculo 
ziwusheba nonembeza. Bafika ekhaya, bazindezindela 
besindwa ukuvula umnyango wekamelo likaMaDlamini. 
Ekugcineni wangena unina kaMxolisi noyise kaMxolisi 
ngokokuqala ngqa, bethandana. 

“Ekabani le ncwadi kadokotela?” Wayebuza 
uMaZondi emile eyibuka iphezu kwekhabethe lezingubo 
elalizibukokazi. 

“Eyami.” 
“Ngoba isanda kubhalwa nje?” 


238 

“Impela. Bengisaye kodokotela ngithi ake bangihlole 
nje wonke umzimba. Hhayi–ke, njengoba uyibona nje, 
isho ukuthi ngimsulwa nasegciwaneni lengculaza.” 

Sakuncokola uThabekhulu wathi, “Esinalo thina 
igciwane elengculaza yenhliziyo.” 

Isixhwala esasiwumshado woMaDlamini 
noThabekhulu okwakugingqika izincwadi zodokotela 
emakhabetheni nje ngoba kuzanywa ukuba selashwe, 
ekugcineni sabhabhalala, kwasala umndondo. 

239 


18 


iNtUthU eyayikade ishunqa iminyaka, ivuthelwa, 

yagqamuka amalangabi alanguka abhadlisa izwe lonke. 
Imithetho eyayikade ingamaketanga ayevalele isizwe 
ezindaweni ezazibizwa ngezabelo yagqabuka. Abantu 
batheleka okwezikhukhula emadolobheni qede kwaqhibuka 
inkowankowane yamadlangala ayewumlahlathemba. 

Efiphele amathemba, abantu sebephenduke inhlanganisela 

yendikibalo nenzondo, baqembukelana. Owayengenatho 
nowayenomnotho walumela komunye. Lwabadida 
usizi abantu baba maqembuqembu ezombangazwe 
ababengaqondi migomo namithethosisekelo yawo. 
Bangqubuzana, izwe labuswa ngobomvu tebhu umbala 
womlilo negazi. Awubonaze usizwe esinjeya nesingakaya 
isililo! Sibambene isizwe, sibhoxa sishelela egazini, 
singqongqa emalangabini, isisi sabosi nesomantshu 
samangala nakuMvelinqangi. Ingomuso laphenduka 
umlotha, nezingane zawohlokela enqwabeni yezinkubela 
ngengqondo ezazizokhubaza ikusasa lezizukulwane 
ezazizolandela. Sekunje, ithemba labe selibekwa 
emahlombe ezitha zenqubo ezazikade ziyilwisa ngolaka 
lwamalaka nakwezaziyibhodlele umlilo wamabhosho. 

OMaZondi noThabekhulu basibuka lesi simo 

esasibuhlungu baso babebuzwa emizweni. Bafisa 

ukuxolisa emphakathini ngokuwusebenzela. Bazimisela 
ngokubhukula baqale izahluko ezintsha zempilo lapho 
impilo yayingaseyukuba ngeyabo, isiyoba ngeyesizwe. 

“Yize nathi sibhoxile emaxhaphozini empilo endala, 

240 

asikhumbule, sixolise kuDubazana ngokusebenzela 
uxolo” Wakhala wazesula uMaZondi. “MntakaMpanza, 
asicele neNkosi isiphe amandla. Asibe mndenimunye 
nesizukulwane esisha ngezinhliziyo esizokuba yibhuloho 
loxolo phakathi komgwaqo omdala womusi nomusha 
womusa.” Bawa ngamadolo bakhuleka. 

“Njengoba sengichazile, Mfundisi, asibonaze sithandane. 
Laxhoshwa libhekile. Kwathi kunjalo, umyeni wakhe 
waboshelwa ukudayisa izidakamizwa, wadonsa iminyaka. 
Ngokuboshwa inhliziyo yakhe yephukile ngomkakhe, 
mhlawumbe wathi nalapho esekhululwa, akafisa ukufika 
kwami abone egone leyo ngane. Mfundisi, wazibulala.” 

UMfundisi uLangalamalanga Langa, owayeyindoda 
eyayisiqinile, enethambo eqatha, empofu, enonwele, 
nentshebe icwalwe kahle, wababuka ngezibuko. 
Wazikhipha wazesula, wazibuyisela wababuka. 

“Wazibulala kanjani?’ 

“Watholwa elenga esihlahleni, phezu komfula uMlazi.” 

“I!” Waquma uMfundisi, wabambelela esihlathini. 

241 

Zacweba nakuMaZondi, waphihlika wakhala. 
“Umkami,” Kwakuqhuba uThabekhulu, ‘kuyamcasula 

esenengane ethi baba kimi.” 

“Bakithi,” kwakusho uMfundisi, “okumcasulayo ake 
singakubuki ngamehlo ethu, kepha ake sikuthathe, 
sikuphendule, sikubuke ngamehlo akhe. Ake sithi 
okwanehlela kwaba yisehlo esehlela yena noDubazana. 
Ukuba uDubazana usewumfelwa, unomntwana 
kumkakho, umkakho uqobo ushayela uyise womntanakhe 
uDubazana indesheni kuwe ucela ukuba umfihlise 
ikhanda, ubungakwenza?” 

Washaya isikhwehlela uThabekhulu, wabakaza. 

“Uthini mfo kaMpanza?: Wambuza ngomoya ophansi 
uLanga. “Nawe Mfundisi uyasazi isisho esithi ‘Izinkunzi 
ezimbili azikhonyi sibayeni sinye’. Indoda enye, 
njengoDubazana nje, yiyona okufanele izakhele umuzi, 
hhayi ukuba ilindele ukuthi izokwakhelwa ngenye 
indoda, noma ishayelwe indesheni yinkosikazi.” 

“Ngahle ukuba umkakho akanikelanga nangolunci, 
noma akaphonsanga tshe esivivaneni sokwakhiwa kwalo 
muzi wenu?” 

Wacwayiza ecwayizile uMpanza, wagwinya amathe, 
wathi, “Mfundisi, ngathi ngizilahle ngecala, wangichitha 
nawe?” 

“Angikuchithi mfowethu, kepha ngizama ukuba 
ucacelwe ukuthi indlela eya embusweni ongcwele 
weNkosi ayinhlanhlathi. Kuyo akushaywa 
ngezamawuba, kepha ithe qekelele, iyakhanya. 
Thabekhulu, uyakwazi ukungena izulu ngezamawuba? 
Kungukuthi usuphendukela eNkosini ushiya ze le ngane 
eniganene nayo isakuthanda, ikhala ngawe amemeza 
ehlane.” Wabuka uMaZondi wayesembuza ethi, “Ukuba 

242 

ubuwumkaMpanza, ubungavumelana yini nesicelo sakhe 
sokukhoselisa inkosikazi ewunina womntanakhe emzini 
wakho?” 

“Okusho–ke ukuthi ngokwasemhlabeni 
siyathetheleleka isenzo somkakho Thabekhulu?” 

“Uyathetheleleka Mfundisi ngoba ngeke salindela 
ukuba yena yedwa akubekezelele sesivumile sobabili 
ukuthi kungasehlula. Umkami, mfo kaLanga, 
ngiyamthanda, futhi angisoze ngehlukanisa naye 
ngokwami. Uyena ongangifakela isahlukaniso. 
Sengimncengile, ngisazomncenga futhi. Kepha engicela 
Mfundisi ukuba ukuzwisise kahle ukuthi, izinhliziyo 
zethu noMaZondi zilambele umthunzi wokulunga, 
uxolo nentethelelo. Sobabili asiwutholi. Isenzo sethu 
ezinhliziyweni zabantu abaningi ababesazi safana 
nokungcolisela izihlahla ezinomthunzi ebesiphumula 
kuwo. Usibona nje, simanaphanapha, sinukela izwe. 
Njengoba usibona sihambisana nje, akungangoba 
sihlanganiswe yinyama, kepha sibhangqwe umoya 
okhathazekileyo. Enhliziyweni yalo mntwanawabantu 
umoya wami unendawo. Umoya wami olambele 
ukulunga, uyaphakelwa. Umoya wami owomele 
uxolo uyaphuziswa. Inhliziyo ebese ilahle ithemba, 
iyalifumana. Umoya wakhe ungamanzi kimi, uwukudla 
nophahla oluyisiphephelo somphefumulo. Konke lokhu 
kuyahlangana kube uthando olusondeza umphefumulo 
wami kuNkulunkulu. Ukuphuma kwakhe emzimbeni 
kuwukuphuma komphefumulo nokufa kwesidumbu sami 
siphila, siba yingcwaba laphezulu.” 

“Okusho ukuthi uma sesikhuluma iqiniso nje, ukuba 
wawuhlanganiswe ngokomshado wosiko, ubungaganwa 
nawuMaZondi?” 

243 

“Mfundisi, ibutho lamadoda awontanga yethu ngiyaye 
ngithathe ngokuthi lehlukaniswe izigaba ezimbili. 
Elinye elabazingeli, elinye elabavikeli. Elabazingeli 
lithatha izithembu ngoba libesabone muntu wesifazane 
limsukele. Obambekayo limephula intamo liyomdicilela 
ekhaya, libuyele enkundleni liyozingela. Eyami inhliziyo 
eyomvikeli nomsizi. Size sihlwathize emathunzini 
omnyama nje, ngoba ngangithi ngimvikela ebuhlungwini. 
Namanje ngisacela ithuba lokuba sisizane. Ukuphendula 
umbuzo wakho–ke Mfundisi, ukuba kuya ngami, impela 
ngabe ngiyamthatha.” 

“Esikucelayo Mfundisi,” wesula amehlo uThabekhulu, 
“wukunikwa ithuba lokukhonza iNkosi nokuzixolisela 
kuyo ngokuyisebenzela nesizwe sayo. Engqondweni yami 
nginesibonakaliso Mfundisi.” 

“Esithini?” 

“Esithi, nakuba indlela esihlanganisile iyiphutha, 
kepha uma ngingamlahli emaweni njengoba uke washo, 
kodwa iphutha silenza isifundo, sibambana, ukuthula 
komphefumulo sikucela ngqo kowasidala, siyoba 
njengabaphuphayo sesifela emuseni wakhe.” 

Wababuka uMfundisi, wakhipha izibuko wazesula. 
Wazibuyisela, wababuka, wathi, “O, hhe, nakuba 
ngingumalusi, kepha angiyena umahluleli wesizwe 
seNkosi. Uma nizicelela ukungena endlini yakhe, 
ngenani, njengalokhu nayo iNkosi isho ithi, ‘Vumelani 
abantwana beze kimi, ningabenqabeli ngokuba umbuso 
wezulu ungowabanjalo?’ Ngokuzinikela kwezinhliziyo 
zenu iyozithatha izisebenzisele ukuzuza abanye. 
Mhlawumbe ngamandla ayo insebenzo yakho yobuhle 
iphinde ikuhlanganise nomkakho, uwuzuze futhi umusa 

244 

nothando lwakhe.” 

“UmntakaDubazana encwadini ayibhala 
esezozishonela wathi. ‘Emoyeni wami angisafisi lutho 
olunye emhlabeni ngaphandle kokuthula noxolo’. Kwanga 
lokho kuthula noxolo kungaba yifa alishiyela ukudliwa 
yizinhliziyo zethu.” Kwakusho uMaZondi bengena 
emotweni, ziya kakhulu. 

Abachithanga sikhathi. Ukungena ezinhlanganweni 
zokusiza isizwe baqala ngokuba munye nezebandla, 
basungula nezinye sebebambisene noMfundisi. Izikhwama 
zababengasebenzi, bebulawa umphangazane, zasungulwa. 
Abase bekhulile, abanye babo bengondingasithebeni 
bemukeliswa ngesobho nezinye izidlo. Khona ebandleni 
basungula ikwaya yomculo wezokholo eyaqopha namaculo. 
Kwakukhalwa ngawo, seyaziwa. Baphuma bengena nayo 
emabandleni ngamabandla bewanxusa ukuba aphonse 
izandla ezikhwameni ezagcina sezibe yimpumelelo 
kangangokuba azibange zisaba ezebandla elithile, kepha 
sekungezamabandla ahlangene. A, oMaZondi noThabekhulu 
sebemi belinganisene, beyiphakela indlebe ngokudla kwayo, 
babeze bacelwe impinda. 

Esikhathini eside uMaZondi ehla enyuka, ephuma 
engena noDubazana, engenakusebenza ngoba ekhutshazwa 
yimithetho yamapasi nezipesheli, wayeseze wagcina 
esebukeka sasithingathingana nje esasilele inkungu 
ekhanda. Kanti umuntu wayejiyezekile nje, engenakuphonsa 
nasandla empilweni yabo nomyeni, wayeke wahlala 
edeskini waze waphothula ibanga lesishiyagalolunye. 
Babonisana noThabekhulu, wamfunela umsebenzi 
bhange thize aqashwa kulo ewumpheki wetiye. 
Bayishabalalisa inkungu ekhanda, nothuli baluthintitha 
ngokugqugquzelana ngokuba aqhubeke ngokufunda ngasese 

245 

athole isitifiketi sebanga leshumi. Wakwenza lokho, 

Wayenqobe phezu kwezingqinamba uMaZondi. 
Esanda kungena ngakho kodwa nje emsebenzini, abazali 
bakaThabizolo babebuye bagcwala umuzi, banxusa 
indodana ukuba yehlukane naye. Nakubo indodana 
yayichiphize ezimathonsi, yatibula ngeyayizabalaze ngawo 
nakuMfundisi. Bageza izandla, bashingila bahamba. 

Enye yezingqinamba eyayimcabangisa ubusuku 
nemini angaphumi nakhambi, yayinoNkosana. Nakuba 
wayengasafundi, wayekade emthumelela unina 
imali yokumondla. Uma eke wathi uyamvakashela, 
kwakuba sengathi umxoshile ekhaya. Wayebuyela mhla 
ehambile. Wayengasazi nokuthi wayezoxolisa athini. 
Ukuvula nje kwakhe umlomo, kwakuba ukufulathela. 
Wayesethandaze waze wagcina esekhuluma yedwa. 
Muva nje wayesethole umbiko owawuthi iNkosana 
wayenyamalele emakhaya, ebonakele nokho engena 
emathekisini ayephikelele eMgungundlovu. Yase yaphela 
iminyaka emibili ethungathwa engatholwa. 

Nakuba kunjalo, yaphikelela phambili impi yamabutho 
okuthula. OMaZondi noThabekhulu base bebambisene 
namanye amadodana namadodakazi esizwe amnyama 
namhlophe, akhanyayo nangamunwe, njengabanumzane 
oBhekizizwe Zulu, oThisha uDonda, oMfundisi Mbambo 
noPienaar, nabanye abaningi. Impi yabo bayenabisela 
ezikhungweni zokondla izingane ezaziwuvanzi ezitaladini. 
Izizathu zokuba uvanzi kwazo zaziningi njengokuba 

246 

nhlakanhlaka kwazo. Kwakunezazibulawelwe abazali 
bazo emajele ngoba belwa nenqubo yababusi. Ezinye 
zaziyimiphumela yokuhlakazwa kwenkambiso 
yesizwe yinqubo yombuso. Ezinye kwakuyizintandane 
ezazibulawelwe abazali ababebhecwa ngelobumbuka 
nezimpimpi ezimpini zomzabalazo. Kambe abanye befele 
insebenzo yabo. Abanye babebulawelwe imizi, abanye 
izimoto, abanye ububona. Zasungulwa nezikhwama 
zezinye izibhicongo zempilo, njengezababebhuqwa yisifo 
sengculaza nesezintandane zaso, simelwe ikakhulukazi 
uMakhosazana. 

Naphezu kwempumelelo ekutakuleni umphakathi 
osizini, naye uThabekhulu wayenesilokozane sendumalo 
enhliziyweni. Inhlalo yomkakhe ngokuqasha yayimkhubaza 
emoyeni. Nakuba wayesakhosela nezingane emzini 
owawungumazakhele, ungowomfelokazi owayethe thuthu 
kunaye ngeminyaka, wayenesazelo sokuthi uze abe efihla 
ikhanda nje ngoba bona noMaZondi benqwahe nomuzi 
wakhe. Lolu daba base beludingide kaningi noMaZondi 
owayecacelwa yisenzo sabo esasiyiphutha. Emsebenzini 
wayesazama ngisho nokuboleka izimali zokwakha, 
wazithola. Njengokwakuyinhlalayenza emalokishini 
abomdabu, naye wayengalitholi inxiwa. Wayesakhuluma 
nenkampani thize eyayisazoqala ukwakha izindlu 
eyayizozidayisa ngebomvu imali. Babethe besayixoxa 
le ndaba kuwuMgqibelo kusihlwa, kuhushuza umoya 
kaNtulikazi, udosi lokubhidlika komuzi lwatinyela 
lezwela kuThabekhulu. Ucingo lwalukhale lwabelesela. 
Wayelubambe yena uqobo uThabekhulu. Lwalushaywa 

247 

umkakhe owayemkhalela ezimathonsi emnxusa ukuba 
aphuthume, eze kuyena. 

“Umntanami nangu efa! Sebemgwazile uThabethule! 
Nangu nje edindilize phansi. Ngicela uphuthume 
uzomusa esibhedlela angaze angifele!” 

“Yini kodwa, kwenzenjani?” 

“Umntanami nangu efa!” Lwavaleka. 

Kumnyama emehlweni, waphuthaza ubala efuna 
izihluthulelo zemoto. NoMaZondi ethukile wabuza wathi, 
“Kwenzenjani Thabekhulu?” 

“Umntanami uThabethule sebemgwazile! Ingabe 
zikhiye nikuphi ngiphuthume?” Izikhiye ayezifuna 
zazisephaketheni lebhulukwe ayeligqokile. Watatazela, 
wangena emotweni, wayishaya yazula. 

“Wenzeni kodwa umntanami?” Wayebuza uThabekhulu 
ehla egxuma emotweni, isivalo sisala sizishayekela 
sivaleka. Wema dlengelele ezwa ubumayemaye 
kukhuzwa, kuphungwa insizwa eyayiphakamise 
umhebhe owawuconsa igazi, ikhuluma ithukuthele 
ithuthumela ithi, “Ngibafuna bedindilize phansi bobabili 
nengoduso yami! Mina ngiyajuluka ngiyasebenza, 
ngiyalobola, yena unesoka endlini!” 

“Abathandani mntanami!” Kwakukhala unina 
wentombazane emnyameni. 

“Yini engingayethemba uma ingoduso yami ivalelwe 
nensizwa ndlininye? Nasemini laba bantu ngike 
ngibelamele bevalelwe bobabili, bemamathekelana. 
Kade ngangithi hamba lapha, kodwa wenqabe ngoba 
ungehlukane nengoduso yesiphukuphuku!” 

“Njengoba uzwa–ke nje Thabekhulu ukuthi 
umntanami ufelani. Abathandani nakuthandana. Ufela 

248 

ukuthi akanalo ikwabo.” UMaDlamini wayesho isoka 
lentombazane selithe galo yephuka ngokubona iveni 
yamaphoyisa izedlulela ngomgwaqo. “Ngiqukulise yise 
simfake emotweni, simbalekise.” 

“Angabe esasala uThabisile umntanami. Ngeke 
ngisamshiya nina. Akangene emotweni sihambe!” 

“Shaya imoto sihambe yise kaThabethule. 
UThabisile yise naye akekho ekhona. Isihlobo somuzi 
sabhadanywa yisoka lakhe sesikhiphe nesikhali sizama 
ukumgcweleza. Selamthatha layohlala naye kwabo.” 

“Lingalobolile nakulobola kodwa nina?” 

“Kwabonakala ukuthi njengoba singasenamuzi nje, 
kwabo soka yiwona muzi ongcono umntanami ayengase 
abhace kuwo.” 

Wayisusa uThabekhulu imoto, yabamba umgwaqo 
amabombo ebheke esibhedlela. 

“Yaze yabuhlungu inhliziyo yami ngabantabami 
namhlanje. Awusangitsheli nokuthi umntanami 
ukipitile. Usengaze akhulelwe nje ngoba umfana 
ezitholele ifa lezwe,” kusho yena uThabekhulu ejolozele 
umgwaqo emnyameni. 

“Kuba njengoba ubona nje Thabekhulu uma indoda 
isakhohlwe owayo umuzi, isahlenga eyabanye. Ithi 
ihlenga ngapha, kwayo bekuba nhlanga zimuka nomoya. 
NoThabisile lowo okhuluma ngaye ngikhuluma nje 
usevele ukhulelwe. Ingane angayishaya phansi noma 
nini.” 

UThabethule waphaphama esezinxakanxakeni 
zemishini yasesibhedlela. Wayengasophinde asukume 

249 

azimele, noma aphinde eme qingqo, azihambele. 
Wayeseyoba yisigoga sesihlalo esinamasondo, eseyohamba 
ngokududulwa kwaso. 

250 


19 


Wayeshayekile uMaZondi ngokuphelela endle komndeni 
kaDubazana. Wazinikela enkonzweni kangangokuba 
nasemgwaqweni wayethi noma ehamba yedwa ezwakale 
evuma ingoma yokholo. Nomfutho wokholo lwakhe 
wezwakala. Amanye amakhosikazi aze amncengela 
ukuba avume ukuba ngenye yawomthandazo. Wagcina 
evumile. Nokuvuma kwakhe lokho kwaqala impikiswano 
eyacishe yawenza aqembukelana amakhosikazi. Amanye 
ayengavumelani ngokugcotshwa kwakhe esahlala 
kwaThabekhulu. Aludingida amakhosikazi udaba. 

“UThabekhulu akafune kwehlukanisa nomkakhe. 
Nosiko lwesiZulu olungenasehlukaniso luyamvuna. 
UThabekhulu akathandi ukulahla umntanakhe 
ezintabeni. Uyafisa ukuganana noMaZondi. Umthetho 
wesilungu awumvumeli ukuba aganwe engahlukanisile. 
UThabekhulu usezamile ukuphatha eyelobolo kwaZondi 
nakwaDubazana. Kuyo yomibili le mizi abafunwa nalapho 
behambe khona. UMaZondi–ke manje ucela ukungeniswa 
emndenini kaNkulunkulu. Sekukunina–ke bathandazi 
ukuba ninqume mayelana nokuthi niphikisana nosiko, 
nithi uThabekhulu akehlukanise nomkakhe, noma 
nithi ababe yiziboshwa, bashadane phezu komunye 
umshado wesilungu. Kukinina, noma nithi abehlukane, 
ingane ikhule ingenayise, noma niyamvumela abe 
mndeni munye nani emzini kaNkulunkulu onentethelelo 
kwabayicelayo?” Kwakusemhlanganweni wamakhosikazi, 
kubuza umphathi wawo ekulungisa ekuphindelela 

251 

ukuhlala kwezibuko ebusweni bakhe obabumpofu. 

“Impendulo eyiyo ngeyeNkosi esiyilandelayo okwakuthe 
kuqulwa icala lenkosikazi yakuloba emhlabathini eyakusho 
kubamangali. Yathi lowo owayengenasono phakathi 
kwabo wayengaqala ayijukujele ngetshe. Baphuma 
belahlwe yizinhliziyo zabo, iNkosi yathi enkosikazini 
yayingayilahli. Yayiyala ukuba ihambe kepha ingabe 
isona. Ake sizwe kini–ke bathandazi bezwi leNkosi ukuthi 
thina–ke sithini.” 

Iningi lagcina livumelene nokuba agcotshwe. 

Wazishaya zaphelela ezejoyini ezazingamabhantshi 
amhlophe, neziketi ezimnyama. 

Bobabili, uThabekhulu elokhu enyela lokho 
ngokulinyalelwa yindodana isifunda eTheknikhoni 
nokusho noMaZondi edidekile ngokudukelwa eyakhe, 
baqhubeka nemisebenzi yomphakathi sebezizwa 
beyizahluleki kokwakuqondene nabo. 

Kwaze kwathi ngalanga thize, kuwuKhisimusi, 
oMaZondi noThabekhulu bezishayelwa umoya ebhishi, 
bamelamela uNkosana emhlambimunye nezingane 
ezaziwuvanzi edolobheni, nezazinabazali sezithatheka 
njengezazingenabani. Bamcela uxolo, ngenhlanhla 
wavuma. Wayesaba yibhobhodleyana elase lafaka 
amabhulukwe amade, namateki, limadlodlombiya 
ekhanda. Bambingelela, wavuma ebancisha amehlo. 
Ayethi lapho eke ababheka, ahlangana, kube sengathi 
awabo ayekade exhonxwa ngezinsungulo. Kulelo 
thutshana abanika indlebe ngalo, abamncenganga, 
baphose bamguqela phansi ngedolo. Babemncengela 
ukuba abuye bazomfundisa. Nasenhliziyweni 
kaThabekhulu kwakungaba yisishayo esibuhlungu ukuba 

252 

umntakaDubazana aphelele emnyameni wokungafundi 
ngoba nje ashonelwa uyise. 

“Njengoba ekuyala nje umama mfana wami, ukutshela 
iqiniso. Imfundo iyikhona kuqhakaza kwengomuso 
lomuntu.” Wathintitha umoya noThabekhulu ewubona 
ukhanyikhanyi umzungeza. Wathula nje uNkosana 
wababuka emangele. Aduma, abhonga, ahaza, abubula 
amagagasi olwandle. 

UNkosana wagcina evumile ukubuyela ekhaya. Wacela 
ithuba lokuvalelisa kubangane bakhe. 

“Kulungile mkhulu, valelisa kubangani bakho,” kusho 
unina ngelalincenga. “Ubatshele nokuthi abafana nabo 
izinhlangano zethu zibathanda impela. Sethemba ukuthi 
ngelinye ilanga uyosiholela kubo nabo sibasingathe 
ngezandla ezifudumele uthando.” 

Wadeda uNkosana, bema buqamama nabangani bakhe 
bexoxa ngolimi olwaluyisishalambombo. Wabuyela kubo 
abazali. Wacela ukuba bamlinde njengoba wayesayolanda 
izimpahla zakhe. Kwavunyelwana, washishinga 
nomhlambi lowo. Wabashiya onina, balinda kwanethunzi. 
Baze bathi sebelahle nethemba, sebethi bayahamba, 
waqhamuka ephethe uphephabheki owawunezidwejana 
zakhe. 

Kwabacacela ukuthi wayelambe kome umlomo. Bangena 
kwelinye lamahhotela ayeseduze, bamthengela ukudla. 
Nawabo amapuleti bawabiza. Badla engadli yena ewolela, 
edimede ebaklabela ngelokuhlola insimu. 

Wafika kwaThabekhulu uMakhosazana wagxumagxuma 
emthakasela, kuba sengathi wayebuyelwa yizwe 
elalimfele. Ngesikhashana nje ebuyile uNkosana, 

253 

wethuka udadewabo embona engaseNkosana 
ayemejwayele. Nalapho emphakela, wayebibela nje, adle 
aze akhothe amapuleti. Baqala nonina ukuba nezinsolo 
zokuthi kumbe wayedla izidakamizwa. Laphela isonto 
ethukela ubala, ecula engezwakali nokuthi wayethini, 
evungama. 

NezikaMakhosazana izinkinga zazilokhu zabajamela 

njalo. Bamfica ngomunye uMgqibelo kusihlwa ehlezi 

kusofa, elusizana, ebukela umabonwakude ebona 
izintombi emkhosini woMhlanga ziyizintombi. Yena 
wayegone ingane eyayikhala ngoyise. 

“Nginenkinga mama.” 

Unina owayesanda kuhlala eceleni kwakhe wabuza 
wathi, “Nkingani?” 

Inkinga enginayo mama ekaSibonelo. Njalo nje, 
ikakhulukazi njengoba esehlala ngokuxhwala, uhlala 
ekhala ngoyise ethi, ‘Baba’. Sengizibuzabuze kaningi 
ukuthi lo yise engingamazi nakumazi ngizomtholaphi, 
nokuthi lumfanele yini uthando lokukhonjiswa ingane 
yakhe.” 

Zahlengezela kunina, akaze azi ukuthi 
wayezophendula athini. Yaqhubeka indodakazi 
yamkhulula enkingeni yempendulo ngokuthi, “Ngibona 
kufanele ukuba uyise kaSibonelo owangibhaxabula 
ngebhaxa elinameva mina ngimshaye ngokumxhawula 
ngezifudumele uthando. Ngicela ningisize, ningiphelezele, 
sihambe siyomthungatha. Ngifisa simkhombise 

254 

imiphumela yempi yabo okwakungasempi yenkululeko 
eyayiliwa nesitha esiwubandlululo, kepha eyase iyinxeba 
lemikhuba. Mhlawumbe lesi senzo singalekelela 
nasekubaduduzeni abanye abanalesi sifo emjondolo, 
benganakwe nakunakwa, bengelashwa, bengahanjelwa, 
bengavuselelwa muntu.” 

“Konakala okonakala mama. Igqubu alinazithelo 
zenkululeko. Ngemuva kwesibhicongo, ukuze kube 
khona inkululeko nenqubekelaphambili, konke kumele 
kuqale oxolweni. Njengegama lakhe umntanami, 
uSibonelo, ngithanda ukwenza isibonelo kuyise 
ngokumxolela.” 

OMaZondi noThabekhulu bavumelana nombono 
wendodakazi, udaba balwedlulisela kuMfundisi 
nasebandleni. Semukeleka isiphakamiso, athintwa 
namanye amabandla. Ngakho–ke, ngelinye isonto, 
licwathule nasebukhweni bezinja, amabandla 
ayesehlangene asusa izintuli eshaye ujenga eyongena 
emjondolo ababeke bakhosela kuwo oMaZondi. 

Isimangaliso esacaca ngesikhathi kungenwa, 
ukuthi abanye abantu ababehlala elokishini 
elaliwumakhelwane wale mijondolo, empeleni sekuke 
kwaliwa ezibomvu izimpi kubangwa amanzi nezinye 
izakhamuzi ezazincikene nayo, babengayazi impilo 
yakhona. Abanye babengakaze balubhade nakulubhada 
khona. Yingakho nje kukhona abawabona la madlangala 
ayeminyene bakhala ngeBhabhiloni, abanye ngeSodoma 
neGomora. Babodwa abashaywa yingebhe, bafaka 
umoya wokuba kuphindelwe emasontweni. Abefundisi 
bawuhola umshungu, bashaya ingoma, badabula 
phakathi kwezindlu ezazingenamagceke. Izingane 
nabazali, abanye kungabantu ababehloniphekile 

255 

impela, babemi bencike ngezindlu ezazakhiwe ngothayela 
ababegqwalile, ngodaka, ngamakhathoni omqombothi 
nokunye. Lapha nalaphaya kwakumi amaloli amasotsha 
amanye ayehlezi phezulu, ephethe izibhamu, amanye 
enqike ngawo amaloli, ebukeka elahle ithemba, 
edangele. Impi yayikade yayibambana emijondolo. 
Ukudideka kwesintu kwakusixabanisa sodwa, sesibizana 
ngezinhlangano zombusazwe ezazalana, sesibhubhisana. 

Phihli, yabakhalisa ezimathonsi abanye imiphumela 
yenqubo yombuso. Bathatha ihubo oMaZondi 
noThabekhulu, kwakhonzwa kwathandazwa. Lazingena 
izwi ezinye izingane, zasondela zazofakaza. Zazizibika 
ubuze, zibala izigigaba ezazizilethe laphaya. Ezinye 
zaziyizintandane, ziboshwe emzabalazweni, zaphuma 
emajele sezabulawelwa abazali. Ezinye zaziganiswe 
ngodli. Nakuba zase zaba yizixhwala zengculaza, namanje 
zazisagcwelezwa. 

Wakhuluma uMakhosazana ezikhumbuza ukuthi naye 
walimala khona lapha, wangenwa yigciwane ayelithelele 
nomntanakhe. Wayebanxusa ukuba, naphezu kwenzondo 
ababekhuliswe ngayo, bona izwe balikhombise uxolo 
nothando. Wabatshengisa nengane yakhe, ebazisa ukuthi 
wayelaphaya nje wayezoyikhombisa uyise ayengamazi 
kwayena ewunina. Wayecela ukuba ababekhumbula 
nababeyazi imfihlo, bayidalule. Ngenhlanhla babesekhona 
ababesakhumbula nababelazi ishoshozela lomgawuli 

256 

wentsha. Nabanye babebelethe izingane nje, ezinye 
sezashona, kwabona babelinde ukufa, ngoba bagcwelezwa 
uyena. 

O, hhe, zaphephuka izingane zabantu, ezinye 
zisatetene, zabahola abefundisi nebandla ziphahle 
uMakhosazana owayeqhuba uSibonelo. Kwaculwa, 
kwakhala amagade phansi nezikhotha kuqondwe 
mjondolo thize. 

Kwafinyelelwa kuwo, kwavulwa. Kwakuyiyona impela 
indlu yezigameko. Yayisemakamelo amane. Kwelokuqala 
okuyilona elavulwa, wadudulwa umnyango qede abefundisi 
ababelandela bethuka, bahlehlela emuva. Babeshaqiswa 
ngababekubona. Indoda eyayingasenamilenze, inemiphini, 
amehlo eyizinhlansana ezingoxweni, empeleni umphefumulo 
usuhlezi emathanjeni, yayilele inqike ngodonga. 
Yayilinikina lusizana ikhanda elalinobuso obabuqaqelwe 
yizimpukane. 

“Nangu–ke!” Amkhomba amabhungwana kwawona 
ayemehlo ayekhala igazi, esakwejwayela ukuphila 
nokufa, nokunuka engasakugqizi qakala. 

“Ningabaleki befundisi!” Wayethi uyamemeza ehleba. 
“Ngicela nisale seningibulala. Kade ngangibacela ukuba 
bangiqedele, abafuni.” 

“Engubani kodwa yena lo muntu weNkosi?” Wabuza

ngeBhayibheli. 

“Uyena uNjayiphume.” 

“Uyena lona osenje?” Bethuka boma oMakhosazana 
nonina. 

“Njengoba nimbona nje befundisi, wayezibeke yena 

257 

waba umphathi wentsha ayeyibuthile. Wayiyekisa 
nezikole ethi ulwa nengcindezelo. Yena futhi 
wayiphendukela wayigqilaza ngokuyigcweleza. Izingane 
eziningi lapha zazibelethene nje ngenxa yemisebenzi 
yakhe nabangani bakhe ababezinyonyobela emnyameni 
baziqhwage ubusha, anduba baziqhathe nabafana. 
Umngani wakhe ababengcole naye samphendukela, 
samgaxa ithayi, yena samshiyela ukuba ayibuke 
imisebenzi yakhe.” Kwakusho elinye lamabhobhodleyana

“Unengculaza naye nimbona nje; empeleni uyisiphethu 
sayo.” 

“O, Mdali wezulu nomhlaba!” Wajuluka wamanzi 
te uMfundisi. Wabuza kuye uNjayiphume wathi, 
“Kwenzenjani mfowethu?” 

“Abakushoyo kuyiqiniso Mfundisi.” Wayephendula

yiphika. “Nami angizenzanga.” Wakhwehlela. “Angazi 
ukuthi ngazalelwaphi, ubani. Ngizithuke sengiwumfana 
nje okhulele ezitaladini zeTheku, ngihlukunyezwa 
nangokocansi. Ngabe sengitholwa wumnumzane 
Naidoo nabanye ababengiqasha ngibadayisele izithelo

ngiboshelwa amapasi nezipesheli. Ejele ngangivalelwa

Ukuthi omunye umuntu uke abe nesihe komunye, yinto 
engingayazi.” 

Wanikina ikhanda uMfundisi Langa, waqhweba 
uMakhosazana nomntwana, wayesebuza ethi, 

258 

“Uyamkhumbula lo mntwana?” 

“Uyakukhumbula okwayehlela le ngane?” 

“Yebo, Mfundisi. Yimina mathupha engamlanda kwabo

esengiqedela.” Wakhala. Ngamathambo ayeyizandla 
wazama ukwesula ubuso. 

“Qha, baba, ngeke ngikubulale. Mina nginaso isihe lesi

“Njengoba usuzivumile izono zakho, kunjengoba usho

“Senizongibopha Mfundisi?” 

Waphendula uMakhosazana wathi, “Asizile baba

Ngeshwa, umntanakho ngeke usakwazi nokumgona

“Kungcono mntanami ungishaye noma ungibophe

“Ngizobe angisahloniphi uma ngishaya abantu 

abadala. Ngiyakuxolela. Ngifisa ukwazi ukuthi mina

Wabuka uSibonelo, wambamba isandla, wayesezikhomba

Emamatheka uSibonelo welula isandla ethi. “Ba … ba, 

259 

babe, baba.” 

“O, Nkosi yami!” Wawa ngamadolo uMaZondi. 
“Ukusukela kuleso senzo sakho mntwanawabantu

“Uyangithethelela kodwa sihlobo sami?” 

“Nakuba ngisezinhlungwini, ngiyakuthethelela

“Okubuhlungu ezweni uma uxolo lungekho, ukuthi

“Mfundisi ngeke! Akafe eyibuka insebenzo yakhe!” 
Aphikelela ngalokho amabhobhodleyana. 

“Kanti bantabami akufanele nilibale wukuthi ukuba

nehlise umoya, ningaphindisi okubi ngokubi.” 

Yagcina yehlile imihlwenga. Abizwa amasotsha,

namasha ayesazokwenzeka. Emuva emjondolo njengoba 

260 


babeshiya kufiwa nje, phambili elokishini kwakushunqa, 

“Umntanami uMakhosazana wenze isibonelo esihle 
soxolo.” UMaZondi wayesho kuThabekhulu bezihlalele

UThabekhulu wambuka ngelalidabukisa, limdabukela,

omkhulu ngothi uzomngena ngaliphi?” 

“Ngale ndlela umntanami uMakhosazana enze ngayo. 
Ngizocela abathandazi nawe ningiphelezele.” 

Wabacela, nesicelo sokubonana noMaDlamini 
ngaMgqibelo mumbe, ngemuva kwamadima semukeleka. 

Nempela, lipholile ngosuku ababevumelene ngalo, 
oMaZondi nabathandazi bangena becula emzini thize 
owawuyindlu eyayejwayelekile emalokishini, imakamelo

yindlala kwakubonakala nangegceke okwakungangenwa 
ngasango kulo njengoba lalingabiyelwe nakubiyelwa nje. 
Esikhotheni kwakungavuka indlondlo ibhubhise abantu. 
Izindonga zakhona zazingakwazi ukupulasitelwa, izitini 

261 

zizimbanjana ezazibomvu, sezagqunqa. Yayizonakwa 
ubani njengoba iziqashi zazithezisana ngokuhlanza 
igceke, nabaniniyo ababegananele ukuzithola 
beseseMkhumbane sebaba yizimba zasematshwaleni. 

Nakhona lapha, njengasemjondolo, kwaculwa, 
kwathandazwa kucelwa lona uxolo. Noma sebesukuma 
abanye behlala, uMaZondi wasala eguqile phambi 
kukaMaDlamini ethi, “Mntakamama, noma ngingebe 
yisiboshwa phambi komthetho wasezweni, kepha 
ngizizwa ngiyisiboshwa phambi kwakho, naphambi 
koMdali nezithunywa zakwenu. 

“Bagcwele bechichima nje endlini, sengibachazele 
ukuthi ukweswela umuzi kwangidudulela kanjani 
kwakho, nokuthi wasicosha sinqunu emzimbeni 
nasemphefumulweni. Ngingelande lutho ngoba indaba 
uyazi ukusuka nokuhlala. Nabantabakho banjenje, ngenxa 
yami.” Wasidinda. “Ukuze umoya wami ube nokuthula, 
ngicela uxolo kuwe. Ngiyazi ngakona, noxolo lwakho 
alungifanele.” 

Baqala phansi ubuhlungu kuMaDlamini, wasikhihla 
naye esimathambo esathinta umoya womyeni wakhe, 
izandla zakhe zejwayela njalo emehlweni, namakhala 
wawashaya ewashayile. Kwaba muncu endlini lapho 

262 

namanye amakhosikazi eseshaya ijoyini esililweni 
edangaliswa nawukubona undanda lukaThabekhulu 
luyisimbelambela esihlalweni. 

“Kanti imoto yenu isincikwa yishwa.” 

“Nawe mntwanawakwethu wafika kwami kumnyama 
amehlo wena nomuzi wenu nonke nikade nidlala 
izwe. Sobabili ukungabi namizi kusenze asabe sisaba 
amakhosikazi, sagana. Asaba nangane sizele. Ngalawo 
mazwi ngizwakalisa ukukuxolela mntakababa. Akukho futhi 
okunye esingaphinde sikwenze ngaphandle kokuxolelana 
ngezenzo esingazenzanga ngabomu nanganhloso.” Welula 
izandla, babambana, bangana ezihlathini. 

“Ngicela ukuxolisa nakumntanami uThabethule.” Washo 
uMaZondi ehuduleka, egaqa, eguqa phambi kwakhe. 
“Ngiyaxolisa mntanami.” Wayesho eluleka, emanga 
emthela ngezinyembezi. “Ukuba umoya wokuhlupheka 
awungidudulelanga kwenu, ngineqiniso ukuthi ngabe 
awunjena. Ukuzwa nje eliphuma emlonyeni wakho lithi 
liyangixolela, liyowukhulula umoya wami.” 

“Ngiyakuxolela mama, nakuba ungenzanga lutho olubi 
kimi. Nawe ngicela ube noxolo.” 

“Ngixolele bani kuyimina soni?” Wakhala. 

“Uxolele labo abona bengakwazi ababekwenza 

263 

ngokukududulela ezilingweni zempilo ngokugweva 
namalungelo akho okuphila. Siyobe sixolelene uma 
ubaxolele.” 

“Uma unoxolo–ke, unokuthula. Uma unokuthula, 
usunqobile empini yenhlalakahle.” 

“Nami ngicela nisale seningiphuzisa noma iconsi nje 
kuleso sitsha somoya woxolo,” kuncenga uThabekhulu 
enamahloni. 

“Phuza Thabekhulu!” Kusho umkakhe. 

“Phuza baba!” kunanela indodana 

Wabonga uThabekhulu ngokuthi, “Ngiyabonga 
bakithi.” Wabanga. 

UMaZondi wabuyela eceleni kukaMaDlamini, 
waguqa ethi, “Sengilindele ukuba banginike isikhiye 
sendlu esengiyithengile dadewethu. Ngokwami ngabe 
angisekho endlini ukuze ukhululeke kulokhu kubopheka 
obopheke khona emakamelweni ngenxa yami. Uma 
kunjani sengizoziphonsa nasemafulethini edolobheni, 
nakhu besethembisa ngokuthi ukwesulwa kwemithetho 
ebisenqabela sekusezithebeni.” 

“Kwangathi nomoya kaDubazana lapho ukhona 
ungakwelekelela. Nawe uke uzwe nje impilo yokuhlala 
nabantabakho emzini ozobizwa ngomyeni wakho 
owaboshwa edayisa ezama khona ukunakhela.” 

Kwaphinde kwaculwa, kwathandazwa, kwase kuxoxwa 
ezinye zasezweni. Kwavaleliswana, kwehlukanwa. 
OMaZondi noThabekhulu base bezizwa belula kusengathi 
babekhululwe emaketangeni ayekade ebagoge izinhliziyo. 
Base beyolala nobuthongo ukuba akumfanekiso 

264 

kakhanyikhanyi ababewubona ugqamuka umlilo obomvu 
tebhu noluhlaza cwe naphezu kwemiqamelo ebusuku. 
Wawuhambisana nelibomvu iso likaNkosana nemvunge 
yakhe njengoba wayehlala evungama, ecula ezimungunya 
izinhlamvu zehubo lakhe. 


20 


Ngambon’ ubaba, 
Engumalunguza, 
Ephuma nath’ engena 
Emizini yabantu. 


Babedlala ngaye 
Abansundu nabamhlophe, 
Babezixhaphazel’ 
Abanye bezibophela. 


Ngabon’ indoda, 
Ikanye nesithandwa sayo, 
Bemengem’ ubaba, 
Owayekhihliz’ amagwebu. 


Ngathi ngiyalunguza, 
Bangikhaca kabi, 
Beth’ emuva le nto, 
Ayiphind’ ekamelweni! 


Kwathi kus’ ubaba, 
Wayeleng’ emthini: 
Babulali ngiyanazi, 
Ngomphindisela! 


Ngokokuqala ngqa uMakhosazana wamuzwa umnawakhe 
eyihaya eyiphimisela le ngoma yakhe ayekade eyihuba 

266 

eyimungunya. Wayehlezi eceleni kwakhe uNkosana, 
khona ekamelweni ayelala kulo. Wayeseze watshekisa 
nekhanda elusizana, ezinyembezana seliyoshona. 

“Mntakababa,” wayemupha iso elalibomvu, 
“njengamanje nje, ngeke ngibadalule. Mhla ngabadalula, 
koba mhla besheba umlilo namalahle?” 

“Ngeke mntakamama ngikuvune kulokho. Ukushebisa 
abantu umlilo namalahle ukubulala. 

Angazi noma uyakhumbula yini ukuthi ngomzuzwana nje 
oqala ngawo umcabango wokubulala usuke usuyintshinge 
kude laphaya inhliziyo yobuntu, usuzixhume eyobulwane. 
Angazi mntakamama noma ngiyaphosisa yini uma 
ngithi, okhiphe isidumbu ngenhloso akabe esavama 
ukuba nezinhlanhla. Izinto azibe zisamhambela kahle 
empilweni. Nebezikade zimkhanyela ziyafekela, zigcine 
ngokucisha.” 

“Konke lokhu okushoyo Makhosazana kuyinkolelo yakho 
kuphela. Kimi akusho, nolunci. Ngesikhathi abesilisa bedlala 
ngami emjondolo akekho owangizwela nowangikhombisa 
ngisho obuncane ubuntu lobu ongitshela ngabo. Namuhla 
owesilisa nowesifazane bebulala ubaba, akekho namunye 
kubo owake wangicabangela ngokuthi wayengemuka ubaba 
engimthandayo, nangokuthi wayengingcwabela ingomuso. 
Ngakho–ke, nami anginasihe esintwini sonke; angikhathali 
umuntu owesilisa noma owesifazane. Munye kuphela 
umphako engiwubekele sona — ipuleti lamalahle nomlilo.” 

“Ukuzonda isintu ukuzizonda ubuwena mfowethu. 
Funda ngami. Wawukhona kudlalwa ngami emakhempini, 
nokusho ngidlala amadoda ayelanywa ubaba. Noma 
sobabili nomntanami silindele ukufa, mina angibazondi 

267 

abantu besilisa ngoba ngiyazi ukuthi abababi bonke. 
Ngikholelwa ekutheni inhliziyo enenzondo ihlale 
igqamuka amalangabi. Ipheka imbubhiso njengoba 
nawe uyipheka ngeyakho, usophe ukubashebisa abantu 
amalahle ngamalangabi. Angithi wangibona ngisukuma 
nomntwana ngiyothungatha uyise?” 

“Njengoba mfowethu uzibiza ngomuntu 
osemzabalazweni nonesikhundla emakomitini owabiza 
ngawenkululeko yesizwe, kufanele ngabe uwena uqobo 
okuqonda kangcono noshumayeza izwe ngokuthi lize 
lilwe kanje nje, ngenxa yayo inzondo, nokuthi alisoze 
labusa kusabusa yona. Konke okwakubhidlizwe 
yinzondo akukezukwakhiwa kuvuswe kuvuke uma 
abantu besahlalele ovalweni lokuphakelwa uphuthu 
olungamalahle nesobho eliwumlilo. Kepha izwe liyovuswa 
livuke mhla baba semseni woxolo.” 

“Kungasa liphinde lishone silalele izintshumayelo 
nemizekeliso yoMakhosazana. Ngisaya emhlanganweni.” 
Wasukuma, waphuma edlula endlini yokuphumula 
okwakuhlezi kuyo uThabekhulu, nasekhishini 
okwakumi kulo unina. Wayelicula ivesi eqinisa 
izinhlamvu lapho ephatha elokubona indoda imi 
nesithandwa sayo bephahle uyise owayekhihliza 
amagwebu. Wayesale uThabekhulu eshaya intamo ethi 
wethusa umfanekiso kakhanyikhanyi owawugqamuke 
oluhlaza umbani. UMaZondi wayesale ehlengezela 
izinyembezi. Wayilandelisa ngazo indodana yakhe yaze 
yaphuma anduba aphakamise izandla naye ephunge 
ukhanyikhanyi. 

Ngalobo busuku bangoLwesithathu uThabekhulu 
akalalanga yiphupho elalimkhalisa, enklinkliza aze 

268 

azame nokuphakamisa ingalo ethi uyaqhweba. Kwasa 
ebhocobele, igazi liphansi kungavumi nokuba aye 
emsebenzini. Nempela akayanga. 

“Igazi alisho, nephupho lasebusuku alingiphumuzi 
emoyeni.” Wamlandisa lona. 

UMaZondi wamduduza ngokuthi iphupho kumbe 
lalingabiki lutho olubi. Kwakunokwenzeka ukuthi 
wayekade elele ebheke phezulu. Esayogeza wamenzela 
ukudla abuya wakuthi choko choko kungavumi nokwehla. 

“Uma amaphupho enje, akufanele umuntu alale 
engambonanga uMaDlamini, achaze, aphinde axolise 
uma kuxoliseka.” 

Nempela sekuyoshaya ihora leshumi wagalela isudi

bayikhetha naye uMaDlamini. Wavalelisa. 

“Njengoba kungoLwesine nje yise kaMxolisi, ngehora 
lesibili sizohlangana kwaMfundisi nabanye abathandazi, 
bese sisukela khona–ke sesihambela imizi ethile. Okusho 
ukuthi uma kukhona okuphuthumayo ongangidingela 
khona, uyongithola khona.” 

Bavumelana. Wayesephuma uThabekhulu ngesikhathi 
lukhala lunqenqetha ucingo. Walubamba, wahlala kusofa 
owawuseduze kwalo, wabingelela. 

“Mfowethu,” lalisholo phansi izwi lenkosikazi. 

“Yebo dadewethu.” 

“Bengicela ukukhuluma noThabekhulu uqobo.” 

“Uye nezinqotho lona okhuluma naye.” 

“Mina–ke ngiyinkosikazi ongeke mhlawumbe 
wayifanisa noma ngingazichaza. Nami ngikwazela 
nganhlanye. Kunemfihlo engifisa ukukuchathazela yona. 
Ngicela ungazihluphi ngokungibuza ukuthi ngingubani 

269 

wakwabani, ngoba ngeke ngikutshele.” 

“Ngishaya nje ngoba ngizizwa ngikudabukela. Ngizwe 
kuthiwa emhlanganweni wentsha obubanjelwe ngaphansi 
kwesihlahla kwaNozililo izolo kusihlwa, kunqunywe 
ukuba ulandwe kwakho uyothethiswa icala ngaphansi 
kwaso isihlahla sezililo.” 

“Hu!” Waphefumulela phezulu uThabekhulu. “Kuthiwa 
ngizolandwa ngoba ngenzeni?” 

“Kuthiwa uyazi nawe ukuthi wabulala bani. Engisho– 
ke mntanomuntu ukuthi noma ngingaluzwanga usuku 
lwecala, kodwa sona isigwebo sesivele siyaziwa. Ukuba 
bengiwuwena bengizogcwala izinkalo namhlanje.” 

Emile uMaZondi wambuka uThabekhulu ewathwala, 
ewalahla, ewaphonsa ngapha nangapha amehlo, 
wazibonela ukuthi kwakonakele. 

“Bathi sigwebo sini?” Wabuza uThabekhulu ephunga 
ukhanyikhanyi. 

“Ngizwe sengathi yisona esejwayelekile, sesicathulo 
semoto.” 

“Hhawu Nkosi yami!” Wazikhalela. “Kodwa uzwe 
ngobani?” 

“Njengoba ngithe ngeke ngizisho nje ukuthi 
ngingubani ngoba ngihletshelwe umfana wami obekhona 
emhlanganweni. Uma ngizidalula izozwakala indaba, 
isicathulo semoto sibe yisithandwa sentamo yakhe.” 

“Okusho ukuthi sengifana nosefile?” 

“Uma ngabe awubaleki njengamanje, cishe ukuba 
usekhona nje ngoba sekusele umzuzu. Usale kahle.” 

“Ngiyabonga. Awusho ukuthi ngihambe kahle?” 

“Uma kwenzeka, nami ngiyakuthandazela 
kuNkulunkulu. Ngicela akuthethelele amacala akho, 

270 

nomoya wakho awemukele ngomusa.” Ngalawo mazwi
