walubuka isikhathi eside. Kwathula cwaka endlini 
uMaZondi esambuka ngokushaqeka. 

“Kuya ngalo elezigameko zephupho lami. Angisekho.” 
Walubeka endaweni yalo ucingo, wamlandisa esembuka 
emshalazelela. 

“Kuhlupha ngoba usehambile lo mntwana. Uma 

kunjani ngizoya esikoleni, ngifike ngimcele kuye 

uThishomkhulu uDonda, ngimqonde ngqo, ngimtshele 
ukuthi akehlukane nale nhliziyo yakhe ebolile. 
Angingabazi nakungabaza ngokuthi ishoshozela elikhulu 
lalo mlilo uNkosana.” 

“Nathi sengathi senza iphutha nina. Nakuba saxolisa 
kuMaDlamini sakhohlwa wukuxolisa kumntanami. 
Angazi ukuthi ngingambona kanjani ngixolise.” 

“Uxolise ukuthini?” Waqalaza uMakhosazana. 
Wayengekho eduze. Wahleba ethi, “Phela uma usuxolisa 
uyoqala ngokuvuma ukuthi sambulala uyise. Ngeke 
ulokothe wenze iphutha elinjalo Thabekhulu ngoba phela 
ngabe sesiboshiwe. Ngabe sekuwukulahleka komsebenzi 
wami nokushiya abantabami beyizintandane ezingenabani. 
Imfihlo yokubulala uDubazana ngicela siyembule phambi 
koMdali, necala silithethe phambi kwakhe kunoNkosana 
ozohlekisa ngathi asisasazele nangenja ebomvu.” 
Wachiphiza izinyembezi. 

“Angazi nina kaMxolisi. Imvamisa umzimba awuvumi 

ukuya ngaphansi kwenhlabathi nezimfihlo. Yikhona 

okukade kungikhalisa ngokunginklinklizisa ebusuku.” 

“Ngeke wehlelwe lutho namhlanje Thabekhulu. Uma 
kunguNkosana umholi wababulali, ngizomkhuza angizwe 

271 

umntanami. Ngeke angangilaleli ngimzala.” 

Wamlanda unina ezidlalela phansi, wamanga uyise, 
wayeseqabula nakuye unina, esethi, “Ngisahamba. 
Ngizosheshe ngibuye ngiqoqe okunqoqekayo bese 
ngigcwala amahlathi uma lolu lungemuhla wokuphela.” 

Bangana futhi, balandelana bayongena egalaji. Wangena 
emotweni uThabekhulu, wayidumisa, wayikhipha 
wayimisa egcekeni, wayesephuma ema, ewubuka umuzi 
wabo, enikina ikhanda. Wabuyela emotweni. Wayethi 
uyikhipha ngesango ngesikhathi unyawo lonke lushona 
phansi, inqanyukelwa yintambo yesipuni. 

“Konke namuhla kuyenqaba. Okusho ukuthi sekuyikho 
ukunqamuka kwezindlela,” wayesho ephuma ephunga 
ukhanyikhanyi. Wayizama imoto, ayabe isaduma 
nakuduma. Balekelelana bayidudulela egalaji, bayivalela. 

Ilanga selishisa likhipha umkhovu ematsheni, 
uThabekhulu washaya kancane ebheke emathekisini. Waze 
wasithela uMaZondi elokhu emile embuka. Naye ephunga 
owakhe ukhanyikhanyi, wabuyela endlini, wangena 
ekamelweni labo, wathi cu, phezu kombhede, wakhala. 

Ihora leshumi nanye lashaya uThabekhulu enyathela 
kancane ngoWest Street. Waye wangena esitolokazi 
sezingubo esasisebenza umkakhe. Izintokazi zimile, zidle 
ingqephu, zidayisa phakathi kwemvunge emnandi yomculo 
eyayisholo phansi, wanyobozela uThabekhulu washona 
kweyakhe nayo intokazi eyayizishaye ibukeka. Yayidle isudu 
eyayifana neyakhe. UMaDlamini esambuka umyeni wakhe 
esebuqamama, wethuka efunda ukukhathazeka ebusweni 
bakhe. Emi eduze kwentokazi eyayibunjiwe, igqokiswe 
imvakazi, ilinganisene nomyeni wakhe naye owayebunjiwe, 
ezishaye ziphelele ezosuku, uMaDlamini wambingelela 

272 

umyeni, babuzana impilo. Bobabili baba ngababengaphilile 
emoyeni. Nakuba izivunguvungu zezwe zazibahlukanisile, 
kepha wawungaphika uma ubona ukuthobelana kwabo 
lapho behlangene. 

“Kungenzeka kanjani lingabi nandawo yakho wazi kahle 
kamhlophe Thabekhulu ukuthi ngiyakuthanda, nokuthi

angiguqula isibongo ngaba ngowakwenu?” Wabuka intokazi 
eyayifake imvakazi, wabuka nensizwa eceleni kwayo,

umuzwe umuntu uma ethi angisoze ngazikhohlwa lezi

“Yebo, ngihlale ngibezwa.” 

“Nami ngisho njalo kuwe. Ngithi angisoze ngazilibala 
lezo ntaba ezinguwena ngoba kuzo kwawela inkaba 
ewubusha bami.” 

“Laze lahlala kamnandi lelo.” Wagebisa ikhanda, 

wamanga. “Ngizokwenekela izimfihlo zami. Angazi 

ukuthi singahlalaphi sixoxe?” 

Intokazi yomlungu eyayisikhulakhulile, iyimeneja 
yalapha esitolo, uMaDlamini esake wayichathazela 
ngezinkinga zomendo, yayibabukela esithe bangana. 
Yakuthokozela lokho, yayisisondela kubo, imbingelela 
uThabekhulu. Yamcela uxolo uMaDlamini. Sebethe 
qekelele bobabili, yamnika ithuba lokuba ayobonisana 
nomyeni, aze abuye sebeyiphothulile ingxoxo ayethemba 
ukuthi yayingeyokubuyisana. Wabonga uMaDlamini, 
wathatha isikhwama sakhe, wasigaxa, wacela ukuba 

273 

bahambe. Bashaya kancane okwenza enye intokazi 
ize ibabuze ukuthi babeyoshada yini. Bamamatheka, 
baphuma esitolo, bashaya ngaye uWest Street, behla 
beya ngasolwandle bebambene ngocikicane. Bawuwela 
umgwaqo uGardiner, bedlula eposini elikhulu ledolobha. 
Bangena epaki eyayibude buduze nalo, incikene 
nezinkimbinkimbi zesonto laseSheshi. Ngaphesheya 
nomgwaqo kwakungezinye izinkimbinkimbi ezaziyihhlolo 
lalo idolobha. 

UThabekhulu wamxoxela. “Ngiphuphe singaphesheya 
komfula, simi silinganisene noDubazana emfundeni 
eluhlaza cwe yawo. Ngale komfula ebese ngiwuwelile 
ngibone isixuku sabantu simile, singunge isidumbu 
sami ebesisebhokisini ebeliphezu kwethuna. Kwabakade 
benganeno bekhala bezigingqagingqa phansi, ngikubonile 
nezingane zethu nabazali bethu. Okufike kwangephula 
umoya kunakho konke ukuthi, nakuba kade ngingaphesheya 
ngizamile ukumemeza, ngixolisa, nginitshela nezimfihlo 
obekuthiwa angizeneke. Izwi lami belingafinyeleli kini 
nakuba beningekude. Bengingasavunyelwe futhi nokuba 
ngiphinde ngiwuwele umfula ngizohlangana nani. 
Osekungiqedele du ngivele ngingasekho, ucingo olusanda 
kungena ekhaya sengigqokile nje ngithi ngiza kuwe.” 

Wavuka umkakhe wambuka ngayexwayile. “Beluthini, 
luphumaphi?” 

“Bengihletshelwa owesifazane ongathandanga 

274 

ukuzidalula. Uthi–ke emhlanganweni wentsha obubanjwe 
izolo kusihlwa, iphathiwe eyokuthi ngizolandwa 
ngiyothethiswa amacala ami ngaphansi kwesihlahla 
somdoni kwaNozililo.” 

“Ngithi angizokutshela ngisaphila nje ukuthi 
bekuthiwa angidalule ziphi izimfihlo.” 

“Yebo Thabekhulu.” Wavumela phansi umkakhe 
ikhanda eselincikise ehlombe lakhe. 

Wayizeka uThabekhulu umkakhe ayeyoyizekela 
amagwababa echobana. Ngokushuba kwazo wakhala 
umkakhe, wagcina esesukumile, ebabaza, ethwele izandla 
ekhanda. 

“Buya sithandwa sami. Musa ukungilahlisa ithemba 
kuwuwena engethembe ukuthi uwudondolo olungimisa 
idolo!” Wayephunga ubala qede elula izingalo emdonsela 
eduze. Wahlala umkakhe. Waphinde wasukuma futhi. 
Ngalesi sikhathi akabambelelanga ekhanda. Wagebisa 
ikhanda, wabambelela esihlathini. 

“Hlala phansi MaDlamini! Iphupho lithe angigeqe 
amagula.” 

Wahlala umkakhe walalela, wayesebuza ethi, “Zandla 
zakho impela yise kaThabethule?” 

“Impela nina kaMxolisi.” Wavuma enamahlonyana. 
Wakhexa umkakhe, wabheka phezulu esihlahleni. 
Ngaso leso sikhathi iwashi eposini elikhulu ledolobha 
lanqenqetha, labala kashumi nambili, lenanelwa 
yizinsimbi zasesontweni laseSheshi ezazihuba iculo. 

“Nomkakhe imbala?” Wathwala amehlo uMaDlamini. 
Wavuma uThabekhulu. Wathi eqambe eyiqeda indaba 
umkakhe wayesekhala, ethandaza emcelela intethelelo. 

“Yilokhu–ke mkami ebengifisa ukukwambulela khona 

engingakhathazeka kabi uma inhliziyo yami ingema 

275                        

ikumumethe.” 

“Bengingakuthokozela lokho. Empeleni ukuba imoto 
ayingifele, bengizonilanda mina njengoba kunenkinga 
kaThabethule ohamba ngesihlalo. Uma ilunga, 
ngizonilanda.” 

Ngehora lokuqala bangana, baphakama epaki, 
baphuma bebambene ngezandla. Behlukana wayidavuza 
indlela yakhe uThabekhulu sekumnyama amehlo, 
wanyamalala ezihlweleni. 

Ihora lesibili lagamanxa engena emagcekeni esonto, 
esejuluke emfoma. Waba nenhlanhla yokumthola uMfundisi 
uLanga ephuma ngakho kodwa nje emhlanganweni ayekade 
ewubambe nabathandazi. Wacela ithuba lokumbona ekanye 
naye uMaZondi. 

“Kodwa yise kaMxolisi wazi ukuthi umthethimacala 
wasemhlabeni akasoze asixolela, ubungelinde sisale 
sesilithetha enkantolo yokugcina?” Wambuza uMaZondi 
esaphumile uMfundisi ebashiya beguqe e–althare. 

“Alusekho olunye usuku nina kaMxolisi, nale ndawo 
akuyona eyamanga.” 

Wabuya uMfundisi, bavalelana futhi bobathathu 
esontweni lapho uThabekhulu ayilanda khona futhi 
eyephupho lakhe nocingo ayeluthole kusa. Walalela 
edabukile uMfundisi. 

“Ukuze–ke Mfundisi, uma kwenzekani, ngingabi 

276 

nenkinga yokufisa ukuhlambuluka ngingasenakukhuluma, 
ngithi angizokudalulela iqiniso esalifihla mhla siqala 
ukukwambulela izimfihlo zethu.” 

“Angikutshelanga Mfundisi iqiniso eliwukuthi 
uDubazana waboshiswa yimi. Ngashutheka izidakamizwa 
empahleni ayeyidayisa ngoba ngesaba ukuthi umkakhe 
wayezothi lapho esecindezelwa ngemibuzo, angikhombe.” 
Yilo leli elalibabazise umkakhe. 

Wagwinya amathe uMfundisi wathi, “Kwanga iNkosi 
inganithethelela ngoba vele senikhethe ukuxolisa 
ngokuzinikela kuyo.” 

“Angazi Mfundisi noma kukhona yini ukuthethelelwa 
komuntu onezandla ezinegazi lokukhishwa 
komphefumulo?” 

Ngomoya ophansi waphendula uMfundisi ngokuthi, 
“ngethemba kukhona ukuthethelelwa kophenduke 
esaphila, waxolisa. Wena ikakhulukazi wathelwa 
amachaphazelo egazi utakula abantu empini 
yengcindezelo. Akuvami ukuba umuntu osempini, 
nongumhlengi kuyo abe nezandla ezihlanzekileyo. Abahlala 
bengenamachashazi imvamisa kuba abasonga izandla 
nababavalela ngaphandle emizini yabo abangqongqoza 
benamanxeba. Wena wabavulela iminyango.” 

“Ngiyalibonga lelo lesethembiso, Mfundisi. Ngicela 
namuhla wazi ukuthi uDubazana wabulawa yimina, 
zandla zami.” Wazivula izandla wazibuka ngezinyembezi. 
“Ngangingahlosile. Ngisho umkakhe waba nesandla 
ethi uyangelekelela ngizivikela.” Wayichaza yonke 
leyo ndaba eyayisukumise umkakhe wabambelela 
ekhanda, wayesesehlisa isandla wabambelela esihlathini 

277 

lapho eselanda eyokubhadanywa kwabo uNkosana. 
Ngesikhathi eselanda eyokumthwala nokumlengisa 
esihlahleni, wayekhexile umkakhe, wabheka phezulu 
esihlahleni. UMfundisi yena wajamela isiphambano 
esasinanyathiselwe odongeni. 

Beguqe phambi kwakhe, uMfundisi wababeka 
izandla emakhanda, wabakhulekela. Eseqedile, bobabili 
bacela ukupholisa izifuba ngokwamukeliswa. Nempela 
wabemukelisa isidlo esingcwele. 

“Namhlanje angazi noma Thabekhulu ubungasivumela 
yini sikuvakashele nomthandazo?” 

“Ungaze ubuze Mfundisi! Uma ungethembisa, 
ngizophuthuma manje ekhaya ngiyonilungisela.” 

“Kulungile–ke. Amakhosikazi athe asayokwenza 
inkonzo yenduduzo kwaMsomi. Ngizowalanda lapho, 
siminyane emotweni, size ekhaya.” 

Wabonga uThabekhulu, waphuma elengise intambo 
yesipuni semoto ayedlule wayithenga edolobheni. 

“Yise kaMxolisi, angazi noma ufuna sihambisane yini?’ 
Wabuza esula izinyembezi uMaZondi sebesegcekeni. 

Wamamatheka uThabekhulu wathi, “Kulungile 
uhambe namanye amakhosikazi niyothandaza. Uma 
ukhanyikhanyi engagqamukanga umlilo wangibhubhisa, 
sizoficana ekhaya. Uma egqamuke amalangabi, 
ukubonana kwethu sekoba ngaphesheya komfula 
engiwuphuphile.” Wambamba isandla, wasiqinisa, 
wayeseqalaza, wasiphakamisa, wasanga, emqabula 

278 

nasesihlathini. 

279 


21 


Uthabizolo Thabekhulu wehla ethekisini wathalaza 
ubala ethuka izanya. Imizwa yakhe yayizwa sengathi 
ayekhona amehlo ayemnyonkoloza. Walathazela 
wathatha omunye wemigwaqo eyayiya kwakhe. 
Wayeseluphunga eluphungile ubala, ungamnike sithuba 
manje ukhanyikhanyi. Wayesezishiye ngemuva izitolo 
ngesikhathi ezwa imvunge yabantu becula. Waqikileka, 
waqhunsula amehlo, walalelisisa. Akezwisisanga. 
Wathatha izinyawo waqhubeka. Ngokuzwa ukuthi 
wayengase ahlangane nababehuba, wema futhi, 
wacija izindlebe. A, amazwi abesilisa nabesifazane 
ababezwakala sengathi babewulusha ayethi: 

Ngabon’ indoda 

Ikanye nesithandwa sayo, 

Bemengem’ ubaba 

Owayekhihliz’ amagwebu. 

Walazi lelo, wayesephakamisa izinyawo, ethatha 
ezazinqamulela egwegwesa kakhulu emgwaqweni. 
Wayeseze wanhlanhlatha lapho ebona ingane yesikole 
ifake inyunifomu. Eminyakeni eyayingaphambi kwaleyo 
ukuhlangana nengane yesikole kwakuwukhulula 
umphefumulo, kuvusa namathemba engomuso 
elikhanyayo lesizwe. Kepha ngalezo zinsuku zokuhuba 
kwazo okwakugqwegqisa uThabekhulu, zase zesabeka. 
Umuntu oshayisana nazo wayecabanga ngokufa 

280 

kunensindiso. Nengomuso umuntu ayeba nethenjana 
lokuthi laliyoke liqhakaze wayelibona lifuswa yintuthu 
namalangabi anuka usi lomuntu, izinyembezi 
zezintandane nemijuluko yesizwe sakha imizi, sithenga 
impahla nezimoto ezazisha zingqongqa. 

Ngathi ngiyalunguza, 
Bangikhaca kabi, 
Beth’ emuva le nto, 
Ayiphind’ ekamelweni! 


Zaqonda kuye, ziholwa uNkosana owayetshakadula 
nomjiva wejazi elimnyama, eqhuba okungabafanyana 
ababili ababeseminyakeni eyayiyishumi nambili. Bona 
bobabili babeqhuba amathayi ezimoto. 

Esikoleni uNkosana wayesaphenduka umholi 
okwakuthiwa wayehola intsha kuliwa nengcindezelo. 
Nokho, okubuhlungu nokudumazayo emizamweni 
yakhe yobuholi ukuthi, ngenxa yezinga lemfundo 
yakhe, nobungako ngeminyaka, wayengaziqondi neze 
ezombusazwe. Ngokwesabeka ayeseyikho esikoleni 
ngenxa yodlame ayenalo lubangwa yintukuthelo 
eyayimvuthela ngaphakathi ngenxa yezigigaba ezibuhlungu 
ayehlangabezane nazo ebuncaneni, bakhona abamthola 
esehlane. Ubuthakathaka bakhe babusebenzisela 
ukufeza izinhloso zabo. Babemlutha ngemali, kuthiwa 

281 

uyagqugquzelwa ukuba abe nomdlandla wokulwa 
nemfundo yengcindezelo ngokuba akhiphe izingane 
ezikoleni. Wayesenesigejana sezingane nazo ezazikhule 
ngokuhlukumezeka, bezikhipha izingane kwesabo 
isikole, bedlulele kwezinye, amanyumfomu agcwale 
imigwaqo. Ukuthi umcindezeli ezazilwa naye ngempela 
kwakungubani, kwakungaqondakali. Zaziphelela phansi 

abazali abathile ababephikisana nokukhishwa kwabafundi 
ezikoleni, bebizwa ngezimpimpi. Nempela babegwetshwa, 
babhaxabulwe esidlangaleni. Abanye babegwetshwa 
bengekho, babone ngoba sekuvutha imizi yabo uma 
kungavuthi bona. Yayinjalo inkantolo enkulu yabantu, 
kwaNozililo emdonini. 

“O, Nkulunkulu wami! Baleka muntu wabantu!” 
Egcekeni lomuzi ayedideka ngaphandle kwawo 
uThabekhulu kwakukhala inkosikazi eyayibukeka 
intanganye nomkakhe, ikhanya ezingutsheni ezimnyama 
zenzilo. Umyeni wayo wayesanda kudutshulwa. “Angazi 
ukuthi ubusayaphi ngoba bese ngikuhlebele ngocingo 
ukuthi baleka!” 

Esikhundleni sokuba abaleke uThabekhulu, wafikelwa 
yisinxi. Wambona futhi ukhanyikhanyi ekhafula imibani 
ebomvu neluhlaza. Wazululeka washaya uzamthilili 
ethi, “Noma bengingabaleka, kepha, uma kungiqondile 
bekuyonginqoba ngokuba, ngosuku lokufa, mntanomuntu, 
akukho okuyoba namandla empilweni yomuntu ngaphezu 
kwakho!” 

“Yiso leso isiboshwa!” Kwakumemeza izwi 
lebhobhodleyana. UThabekhulu inzululwane yamqinisa 
ngesikhathi abafanyana bamathayi bemzungeza ngawo. 
Lathi liqambe limqaqela iqulu wayesengoqulekile 
ngengqondo. Usushishinga naye umshungu wafana 

282 

nomuntu oselahlekelwe yingqondo ezungezwa amagagasi 
olwandle emlande engadlali, ekhukhula naye. Kwashunqa 
izintuli beqonde naye kwaNozililo, behuba beqa 
amagqanqu. Waye wamiswa esigcawini, ngaphansi 
kwesihlahla somdoni lapho inkosi yenkantolo yabekelwa 
khona ibhentshana elaliphuma khona emshungwini. 

Umshushisi ekhuluma ngesihosho wabuza wathi, 
“Angithi uyalazi icala obekwa lona?” 

“Beningakangitsheli bafana bami.” 

“Hhayi indaba yokuthi bafana bami lapha! 
Kusenkantolo lapha! Ubothi ‘Nkosi yeNkantolo’!” 
Wamqhunsulela amehlo ayegqamuka umlilo uMshayazafe 
owayeyindodana kaLindeni. 

“Bengingakatshelwa Nkosi yeNkantolo.” 

“Ungabosenza iziphukuphuku ngoba icala obekwe 
lona uyalazi. Angithi uyazi ukuthi ngomunye unyaka, 
osukwini esengilukhohliwe, wena lona, welekelelana 
nonina weJaji lale nkantolo, nabulala uyise walo?” 

“Ngiyaliphika icala.” 

“Uyeyisa–ke lo muntu!” Kwakububula abanye 
esixukwini. “Asazi ukuthi kusathethwa cala lani ingabe 
umuntu lona uvele agaxwe umgexo womntakwabo!” 

283 

“Uliphikelani uyise weJaji afa, esemangcwabeni 
sikhuluma nje?” Kwakubuza omunye umshushisi okhela 
ugwayi ebhema. 

Wagqamuka ukhanyikhanyi, waphunga ubala. 

“Uma ufakazi esukuma ethi uwena owamsukela, 
uzothini?” 

“Ngizokuphika lokho ngoba akubanga njalo.” 

“Uthi uyamazi ufakazi kuleli cala?” Wambuka futhi 
efifiyelisa amehlo abomvu, ebhema. 

“Angimazi.” 

Umshushisi wabheka umahluleli, wathi, “YiNkosi 
yeNkantolo, umlomo ongathethi manga. Uyafuna usukume 
ufakaze?” 

“Uma iNkosi yangibona phela ingasukuma.” 

“Uthi akusukume iNkosi yeNkantolo? Uyazi weyisa 
kabi lo muntu?” Elinye ibhungu laqhasha esixukwini, 
uyise uThabekhulu lamsakaza ngempama eyahlakaza 
amathe, wasala enambitha ubala. 

“Mhlawumbe wenziwa ukungeya ngoba nakhu 
engibona ngifake amateki. Uyakhohlwa wukuthi ngabe 
ngifake izicathulo eziphambili ukuba akangibulalelanga 
ubaba.” Wakhala, uNkosana ecula ephinda lona ivesi 
lendoda ayibona yengeme uyise ikanye nesithandwa sayo. 

“Uyezwa ukhalisa iJaji wena?” Amkhankatha amazwi 
amaningi esixukwini. “Uyalivuma noma uyaliphika na 
icala?” 

“Wafa ngizivikela bantabami. Ngangingenanhloso.” 

“Uma pho naningenanhloso, namkhipha kanjani 
endlini, namthwala ibanga elide, naze namlengisa 
esihlahleni esisemawolokohlweni phezu komfula uMlazi?” 
Wayikhipha ngomlomo nangamakhala intuthu. 

284 

Lamhila lelo uThabekhulu. Wakhwehlela, wabakaza. 

“Bantabami, ngaphambi kokuba sinonina weNkosi 
yeNkantolo sibuyele ebandleni likaNkulunkulu, saguqa 
phambi kwakhe, esontweni, okwenzeka konke sakudalula 
noMfundisi ezwa. Inhloso yona impela yayingekho. 
Ngendlela le ndaba esinda ngayo, bantabami, abantu 
abadala kuphela engingabachazela ngayo, bezwe. Ikude 
kabi nomuntu ongakaganwa nongakagani.” 

“Musa ukusibhedela wena lapha! Asikhulumi 
ngamacala asezulwini lapha. Siqula amacala asemhlabeni 
okusibulalela obaba!” Kwakuvutha omunye umshushisi 
naye okhela owakhe ugwayi. 

Wakhala umehluleli, wacula bempheleka abanye ethi: 

Ngathi ngiyalunguza 

Bangikhaca kabi, 

Beth’ emuva le nto, 

Ayiphind’ ekamelweni! 

“Uyabukhumbula lobo busuku mbulali?” Wayesebuzwa 
umahluleli esehlengezela izinyembezi. 

“Ngiyakhumbula mfana wami. Obaba nomama wakho 
lapho bekhona bayazi ukuthi kwakusukelephi. Ngicela 
ungixolele.” Wacweba izinyembezi, waphunga lapho 
ukhanyikhanyi ekhipha oluhlaza nomhlophe umbani. 

“Kungcono ngoba uzivumela ngomlomo wakho.” 
Wabuyela esihlalweni sakhe uNkosana, wayesebuza 
kubashushisi ukuthi babefinyelela kusiphi isinqumo. 
Babukana abashushisi. Abazange baphendule, 

285 

ngaphandle kokuba bedlulise iminwe ezintanyeni, 
okwakuwuphawu lokunqunywa noma ukulengiswa, noma 
ukulenga ithayi. 

Umahluleli wakhwexa amahlombe wayesethi, 
“Njengoba inkantolo uyizwa, ivumelana ngazwi linye 
ngokuthi uwumbulali. Obulala ngesandla, uyofa ngaso 
naye. Inja eluma ezinye iyofa ngokulunywa ngezinye 
nayo. Inkantolo ikuthola unecala. Asikho esinye isigwebo 
ebona ukuthi sikufanele ngaphandle kokuba ufe ngocu 
lomntakwenu. 

“Njengoba wabulala ubaba nje, ngikubona kungifanele, 
kungilingene futhi ukuba ngimphindisele. Ngihlala 
ngigweba nje, ngingabafaki mathayi zandla zami, wena 
ucu lomntakwenu uzolugaxwa yimina, mathupha, zandla 
zami.” Wazikhotha izindebe, wayesesukuma eseqhweba 
omunye umfana owayeseguqe eceleni kukaThabekhulu 
nethayi. 

“Ngiphe mfana siphethe umsebenzi zingakafiki lezi 

zinto ezingamaphoyisa!” 
Wasondela nalo umfana. 

“Phuthumani ingaze ifike leya moto ezayo! Mhlawumbe 

ngeyamaphoyisa.” Kwakuwiliza elinye izwi esixukwini. 

Waliphakamisa uNkosana ithayi, walehlisela 
entanyeni kaThabekhulu kancane eseyihubela phansi, 
abanye bemvumela: 

Kwathi kus’ ubaba 

Wayeleng’ emthini: 

Babulali ngiyanazi, 

Ngomphindisela! 

286 

“Mbhaveni!” 

“Ugwayi!” Kwakumemeza omunye. 

Waqhamuka umndweza kasikilidi, wabethelwa 
emlonyeni kaThabekhulu. Wanikwa nomentshisi. 

“Zokhelele wena, ubheme!” 

Ikhanda selingenhla kwethayi, waze walitshekisa 
uThabekhulu encenga ethi, “Kodwa mntanami 
awusakhumbuli nosuku enganicosha ngalo nincike 
ngemoto yami esontweni, ngayonikhoselisa ekhaya? 
Ngixolele ndodana!” 

“Mxoleleni bandla!” Intombazana eyayiseminyakeni 
eyayiyishumi nantathu yakhala yathwala izandla 
ekhanda. 

“Thula! Ufuna ukumendlalela yini?” Amehlo ayebomvu 
omshushisi ayigqolozela. Amanye amantombazane 
ayephoqiwe nokuba laphaya, ephikisana nokwakwenziwa, 
eyayikhala ayisindisa ngokuyibamba isamuku. 

“Bhema wena! Musa ukudlala ngathi lapha!” 
Kwakusho abanye besimame ungasazi nokuthi izinseka 
zase zashonaphi. 

Esathithibele uThabekhulu, nsi, yema iveni 
yoMfundisi eyayigcwele inyinyitheka abathandazi. 
Embona uThabekhulu eseligaxiwe ithayi, wehla egxuma 
uMfundisi Langa, sekuwubumayemaye bekhala bonke. 
Abanye abathandazi bathi bevulela ababengemuva, 
uLanga wayeseqhekeze iBhayibheli, emi phambi kolusha, 
encenga, ekhuza. 

“Suka lapha Mfundisi!” Amabhungu ayebambisana 
ngaye emchiliza. “Uma unenkani yeselesele, siyifaka 

287 

umlilo le veni yakho!” 

UMaZondi wehla evenini wahaqazela ngamadolo 
eshweleza endodaneni. Kwaba nhlanga zemuka 
nomoya. Esikhundleni sokumzwela uNkosana wahuba 
ingoma yakhe wamkhomba ethi, “Babulali ngiyanazi. 
Sengiyaphindisa! Mbambeni nangu umbulali! Icala lakhe 
selinqunyiwe. Liyefana nelosegwetshiwe!” 

“Sengingaze ngikhonjwe wumunwe wakho mntanami!” 
Wazama ukuzibeletha uMaZondi. Wawa, wavuka, 
wakhubeka, wabalekisa okomntwana. 

“Bulalani mina bantabami!” Waziphonsa kubo 
uMfundisi kwawubunikilili edonsa edudula abase

“Sibulaleni okungenani bantabethu! Lezi zingubo 
sizifakele khona ukulilwela nokulifela iqiniso!” Babesho 
abathandazi sebeyibambe nezingane zabo. 

“Sibambeni isiboshwa, nasi sibaleka!” Kwakumemeza 
abanye bembona uThabekhulu ebaleka nethayi besalibele 
uMaZondi. Esejikijelwa nangamatshe ekhala umzimba 
wonke, wema. Bambhubela bamphuzisa wona futhi 
uphetroli. 

“Yokhela umentshisi uwuphonse kuye!” Kwakumemeza 
izwi emazwini ngamazwi. 

UThabekhulu wambona futhi ukhanyikhanyi ushaya 
umbani owawubomvu tebhu. Kwahlwa engqondweni. 
Akalicabanganga ihubo alicula. Wazizwa eselihuba ethi: 

Lapho zingihleka izoni, 

Zingifak’ umqhel’ ekhanda, 

Zingifela ebusweni, 

Ngakukhumbula njalo. 

288 

Wo, angazi noma wena 

Kwashuba umoya ngesikhathi abathandazi 
ababehlengezela izinyembezi beyivuma naye, abanye 
besazilahlela ezinganeni bethi nabo azibashise. Umentshisi 
wokuqala ababewokhele bawujika buqamama oNkosana 
ababengasabhekeki wawucishile. 

“Oshayo oshayo!” Balinga ukuwokhela futhi omunye. 
Bahlakazeka abathandazi. UThabekhulu wambona 
futhi ukhanyikhanyi ugqamuka unyazi lokugcina qede 
wayikloba ngesikhathi, walithika amalangabi: 

Khona esiphambanweni, 

Ngibethelwe ngihlupheka, 

Ngibhotshozwa zipikili, 

Ngakukhumbula njalo. 

Lawo mazwi wawasho uThabekhulu esukeleka ngejubane 
emshwabadela emfobela amalangabi amanye elanguka 
ngomlomo. Waqonda ngqo kuMaZondi owayesekade emi 
buqamama ebukela ekhala. 

“Bayekeni! Bazothungelana!” 

Wawungathi babejahana, kungasacaci nokuthi 
uThabekhulu wayesambona ngani uMaZondi kulawaya 
malangabi. Wawa wavuka futhi uMaZondi, wavuka, 
wawa. Wavuka wabaleka akangazithambisa esekubona 
ngamehlo ukufa. Bakhala ubumayemaye abathandazi 
bembona uThabekhulu owayeselule izingalo 
ezazingamalangabi sekwala kancane ambambe. 

“Wo, angazi, noma wena 
Ungikhumbulile na? 


289 

MaZondi! Nangu uDubazana! Ngixo …” 

“Yebo, ngiyakukhumbula! Angibaleki! Sengifa lapho 
ofela khona!” Walahleka phansi naye. 

“Abokhelani! Mbambeni!” Yabhuza futhi intsha iya 
kubo. Muntu wabantu lowo, owamisa imoto, wasivula 
sandiza isivalo, waziphonsa phakathi uMaZondi qede 
yashaya yachitha naye. 

“Uwena lona ovikela izoni. Ngabe simbambile lowa 
mama!” Basho bebhodlela kuye uMfundisi owayebutha 
inhlabathi ezama ukucisha uThabekhulu owayengqongqa 
phansi. Babadudula bonke nabathandazi ababemelekelela, 
bavuma phansi. Bamhlwitha nebhayibheli ayeligodlile, 
baliphonsa emlilweni. Wasala enkemile. 

“Phonsani nezincwadi enifunda ngazo ezosheshe ashe 

aphele zingakafiki lezi ziphazamiso ezingamaphoyisa!” 

Nezingane ezazingahambisani naleso senzo, 
ngokwesabela impilo yazo zaziphonsa izincwadi 
emalangabini. Edelile uMfundisi wantenga, 
wayikhulekela inyama eyayisha. 

“Hhawu, bakithi! Ngizwa sengathi wuThabekhulu 
lona oshiswayo?” Wayetheleka egijima uBhekizizwe Zulu, 
esehefuzela. 

“Uyena impela, mfowethu.” Kwakuvuma uLanga. 

Wahuduleka uZulu waye waguqa ngaselangabini, 
wakhala eshaya inhlabathi ngezandla ethi, “Kodwa kukhale 
nyonini ezweni lakithi! Bantabami, njengoba sasishaywa 
nje, siboshwa, abanye bebulawa, sasingazinikeleli ukuba 
nizithathele umthetho niwusebenzisele ukubhubhisa 
izwe nesizwe. Sasilwela amalungelo nentando yokulunga, 
nenkululeko, nokushaywa nokusetshenziswa komthetho 

290 

ngendlela eyiyo. Sasishabashekela inhlalakahle; hhayi le 
nhlekelele eseniyenza! Nina seningqongqisa bona kanye 
laba bantu esasibalwela nesasibalekelela, abangabonaze 
bayizwe inkululeko empilweni yabo. Esikhundleni 
sengcindezelo yobandlululo nina nifaka imbubhiso yomlilo. 
Nkulunkulu, sicela isihe nomusa e–Afrika!” 

Laze laba bomvana ilanga phezu kwezintaba 
kusalindelwe abokugcinwa komthetho. Umlotha 
kaThabekhulu nogalo ababemnyama suce kwakusekhona 
phansi. Eceleni kwaleyo nqabakayitshelwana kwase 
kuguqe uMaDlamini owayefike ngesidumo wakhihla isililo. 
Wayebuye aduduze noThabisile okwakungasensuku zingaki 
abelethe enye. UThabethule wayehlezi esihlalweni sakhe 
esasinamasondo, ecwebe izinyembezi. UMakhosazana, 
ngokwesaba ukuthi umfowabo wayengafika ekhaya azobasa 
noMxolisi, wayenele wabona iloli lamasotsha wabalekela 
khona lapha kwaNozililo nabantwana. Naye wayekhala 
bemphahlile. Ingomuso labo nabo lalingacacile. 

“Zidalekile izixhwala nezigoga. Uma zingenakulashwa 
imizimba nemiphefumulo, nankululeko okukhulunywa 
ngayo iyoba ukubhongela emswaneni kwenkunzi enqundwe 

291 

amanqindi,” kuphawula uZulu. “Njengoba ubabona 
behlezi bedideke benje, ababona abakwaThabekhulu 
nabakwaDubazana kuphela, kepha bamele izigidi 
ngezigidi eziminziswe wuzamcolo wenqubo. Nalezi 
zingane ezimi laphaya zisisho ngenhlamba, zimele 
inkumbula eyakhishwa ezikoleni yakhulela emnyameni, 
isiyophinde izalele emnyameni.” 

waya emlotheni, wafike wadonsa amaphepha ezincwadi 

ezazishisiwe, wawathintitha, wawaphakamisela 
phezulu ethi, “sithintithe zona lezi zincwadi, ngolwazi 
olukuzo siwudedise umnyama. Ngazo likhona ithemba 
lokuthi uyodamuka, ngale kwawo kube nokukhanya 
nokuqonda. Ukubusa kwesizwe sisemnyameni 
nokungawondi, sibhujiswa yizifo, ububha, kunokukhala 
nokugedla kwamazinyo silwa sodwa, sizala siqhulula 
intululwane yezingane esingazidingi nezingenamondli, 
kuwukuzikhohlisa ngenkululeko esizweni esakhe phezu 
kwentabamlilo.” 

NoMfundisi Langa waguqa eduze kwawo umlotha 
wakhothoza imvuthu yeBhayibheli. Wayithola 
imvuthuluka, wayithintitha waphakama nayo 
eyiphakamisa ethi, “Ngamazwi alotshwe kule ncwadi, 
bonke abavutha ngezinhliziyo siyobaphozisa ngomusa, 
inqobo nje uma singacheme namaqembu ezombusazwe. 
Ngale kwesisi somusi kuyoba nesisa sobuntu.” 

Abathandazi babelokhu bemile, begebise amakhanda, 
bevule izihlabelelo becula. Imoto yamasotsha yayisemi 
buqamama. Nawo ngemuva ayebukeka edangele, 
edikibele nemibhobho yezibhamu ayeseyibhekise 
phansi. Kujana egqumeni yakhala yanqenqetha 
insimbi esontweni lamaRoma aKhatholika. Yathunuka 
inkumbulo kaMaDlamini, wakhihla uqanduqandu 

292 

lwesililo. Wayesekhumbula ukuthi emini yanamuhla, 
ngehora leshumi nambili babeke bahlala babambanela 
eduze nomyeni wakhe. Izinsimbi zesonto laseSheshi 
zazibakhalele zibaculela. UThabekhulu manje 
wayesethule, eshunqa. Nangalelo hora lesithupha 
izinsimbi zaseSt Paul zazisakhala zincencetha kuduma 
iTheku nezitezi namagagasi alo, zihuba zithi: 

Kuzakusa; 
Ngiphathe ngomusa 
Njengomntwana. 
Ngenhliziyo yami ngithi: 
Nkosi yami: 
Kuwe Nkosi yami, ngiza kuwe. 


“Ikhambi elinye,” kwakusho uMfundisi, “likubo 
abaholi nesizwe abozinqumela ukubuyisana 
nokusebenzisana ezinhliziyweni zabo bemumeme 
bamemukela uMdali wezwe nomusa nokukhalipha 
kwakhe!” 

Yaqhamuka ngesikade iveni indiza, yema kwashunqa 
izintuli. Njengesiguli wehliswa uMaZondi waphahlwa 
amaphoyisa ayephethe imigqonqo yezibhamu. Wahamba 
ephephuka ekhutshwa nangesinye sezicathulo 
esasiphume sisha kuThabekhulu. 

“Kepha, uma kusenjengoba sibona nje, ukufa 
sisaphila kuseyingxenye yempilo,” selisele ngocezwana 
ezintabeni, uBhekizizwe wababuka bonke abase 
beyizixuku bebukela. “Sikuphi bakithi kule nhlekelele 
yempilo?” 

Kanye kanye, sengathi babetshelene, baphendula 
kwababaza amagquma bethi, “ASIKHO NDAWO 

293 

BAKITHI!” 

Gqwambi, lashona ilanga. 
O, hhe, Nkosi yami! Mntanami, sasingasekho isikhathi 
esasisengcono!
